/ / khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang ngur smrig gi bla gos 'chang ba dpal gnas gsar pa chen po 'jam mgon bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa legs pa'i mtshan gyi zhal snga nas kyi rnam par
thar pa ngo mtshar rab 'byams zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /

rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag dpal ldan bla ma dam pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs la phyag
'tshal zhing skyabs su mchi'o/ /ngag dbang mkhyen pa'i chu gter rab yangs kun dga'i gsung rab snying po'i bcud/ /bsod nams ye shes legs pa'i rtser son yon tan rin chen 'byung
gnas che/ /theg mchog bstan pa'i klung rgyun cher 'babs rab snyan grags pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /dpal 'byor bzang po'i chu rgyun kun 'dus sngon med chos kyi rgya mtsho
rgyal/ /rab mdzes sku ni mtshan dpes yongs spras ngag dbang lha de ngur smrig 'chang / /sgra snyan gsung ni 'gro kun dga' mdzad legs par bshad pa'i 'byung gnas che/
/rab zab thugs ni theg mchog bstan pa'i nying khu bgrang

yas ting 'dzin mdzod/ /rab 'byams yon tan rgyal mtshan 'dzin mkhas dpal ldan phrin las bzang por 'dud/ /gsung ngag dbang bzhi'i chu rgyun 'bebs sogs 'phags bod paN grub kun
gyi dngos/ /dga' chen khyab bdag 'khor lo sdom sogs legs pa'i 'byung gnas rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /lung rtogs bdag nyid theg mchog bstan sogs zab dang rgya che dam pa'i chos/
/nyes kun las rgyal dge mtshan bsgrengs sogs tshogs mchog dpal ldan bzang pos skyongs/ /gdul bya'i 'dzin mar dbang bzhi'i rgyun 'bebs sku bzhi'i 'bras stsol sa skya pa/
/rdo rje 'chang dngos bsod nams rin chen zhabs dang rje btsun thar rtse mgon/ /bka' drin mnyam med nam mkha'i mtshan dang snyan brgyud mnga' bdag brag rtsa rje/ /blo gsal
ting 'dzin rgya mtsho la sogs gcig nyid tha dad bstan rnams bsngags/ /grangs med bskal par mngon par

byang chub kyang / /lnga bdo'i 'gro la rjes chags mkhyen brtse'i gter/ /dus 'dir ngo mtshar mdzad bzang bcu gnyis kyis/ /rnam grol lam ston shAkya seng ger 'dud/ /gang gi bstan
pa gsal mdzad byams 'jam dbyangs/ /rdo rje snying po dgra bcom nyan thos tshogs/ /rgyan drug mchog gnyis grub chen brgyad cu sogs/ /'phags yul ting 'dzin rgya mtsho
bsngags par 'os/ /gangs ljongs mtha' 'khob mun pa'i smag rum du/ /bstan pa'i nyi mas phan bde'i lam ston pa'i/ /rgyal blon lo paN mkhas grub ji snyed bcas/ /rim par byon
pa rnams la bdag cag dad/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag sa skya pa'i/ /gdung rabs rin chen phreng dang khyad par du/ /rje btsun gong ma dbang po'i grangs ldan la/ /bka'
drin dran pas grangs med phyag bgyi'o/ /des gsungs mdo sngags bstan pa rin po che/ /yongs su spel mkhas g.yag rong go shAka 'bum/ /ngor rdzong gong dkar zhes grags bstan
'dzin gyi/ /skyes mchog rim par byon rnams spyi bos mchod/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /snyan brgyud mdzod 'dzin bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / /kun spangs
rje dang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal/ /brgyud par bcas kyi rnam thar bsam bzhin dang / /rgyud sde'i nying khu yang phur bde kye gsang / /dpal ldan dus 'khor gshin rje'i
gshed dmar nag /tshe dpag med sogs lhag pa'i lha tshogs kyis/ /'phral yun thun mong mchog gi dngos grub stsol/ /rgyal ba'i bstan srung gur mgon lcam dral dang / /stobs
'phrog dbang po nor skyong

las mgon lnga/ /beg tse dkar bdud phur srung las gshin sogs/ /srung ma'i dbang pos byang chub bar du skyongs/ /dbang chen rig byed tshogs bdag 'dod pa'i rgyal/ /dgos 'dod char
'bebs rnam sras dzam la'i tshogs/ /nor rgyun dbyu gu mched sogs gter bdag gis/ /phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i dge legs stsol/ /de ltar rtsa brgyud bla ma yi dam lha/
/chos srung nor lhar bcas la gus btud nas/ /skyabs gnas kun 'dus drin chen rdo rje 'chang / /gnas gsar 'jam mgon legs pa'i mtshan can gyi/ /rnam thar yon tan rgya mtsho'i
klong yangs las/ /chu thigs tsam zhig dad pas rab blangs te/ /bdag sogs gdul bya'i bsod nams bgo skal du/ /legs par bshad kyi skal bzang dga' bas nyon/ /zhes phyogs bcu
dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa sras dang slob mar bcas pa'i snang brnyan tha dad du bstan kyang / gang thugs ye shes ngo bor ro gcig pa'i yul khyad par can rnams la mchod
par brjod pa dang bshad pa dam bcas nas skal bzang spro ba bskyed pa'i tshigs bcad cung zad tsam gyis sngon bsus te gleng bar bya ba ni/ gang gi sku gsung thugs mi zad
pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo'i gnas las brtsams te ngo mtshar gyi gtam mthong thos kyi legs byas phra mos kyang rgyal ba thams cad kyi ye shes gzigs pa'i rgyun yid la 'jug par mdzad
pa po ni mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i rdo rje slob dpon nyid yin la/ de lta bu'i yon tan gyi cha shas tsam bsngags pas kyang grangs med pa'i bsod nams dang ye shes kyi
tshogs

'phel bar 'gyur bas na/ rang nyid dam pa'i rjes su 'jug pa'i spobs pa dge ba khyad par can thob pa'i ched dang / rje bla ma gang gi gzhal du med pa'i bka' drin gyi phung po
mngon par dran pas dbang byas/ dad pa dang blo gros can gzhan dag kyang rmad du byung ba'i mdzad phrin gyi rjes su nges par 'jug grang snyam pa'i lhag bsam zla ba tshes
pa lta bus nye bar bskul te/ thos pa don dang ldan pa'i ngo mtshar can gyi gtam mtha' yas pa dag rang blos ji ltar nus pa tsam zhig brjod pa 'dir yang rdo rje slob dpon sogs
dam pa rnams kyi yon tan bsngags dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan dang / rgyu mtshan can gyi dam pa'i rtogs brjod dngos la 'jug pa gnyis kyi sgo nas bsnyad par bya ba las/ dang
po ni/ mdo las/ 'di ltar 'jig rten na rigs thams cad kyi bla mar gyur pa shAkya rnams kyi skyes pa'i rabs bzung zhing chub par byas nas gzhan la'ang rgya cher bsnyad na chos
dang mthun pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po dpag tu med pa 'byung la/ yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'phel bar byed pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu dang / rgyud las kyang
/ slob dpon yon tan gleng bya yi/ /skyon rnams nam yang ma yin no/ /zhes pa dang / skyon brjod pas ni dngos grub med/ /chu la 'o ma rang zhugs pa/ /de bton nas ni ngang

/ /ji ltar til mkhan mkhas pa yis/ /til

sogs mar khur 'gyur ba bzhin/ /bla ma'i yon tan gzhur la gzung / /skyar mos mtsho las nya len bzhin/ /bla ma'i yon tan rnam par gzung / /zhes pa dang / sangs rgyas dang byang
chub sems dpa' ganggA'i klung gi bye ma snyed la skal pa ganggA'i klung gi bye ma snyed du bsnyen bkur ba bas ni/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig la til mar
gyis byugs pas ches khyad par du 'phags so/ /zhes dang / lha sku bye ba stong bsgoms pas/ /bla ma dran pa bsod nams che/ /zhes pa dang / 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi rim pa lnga
pa las/ /mchod pa thams cad spangs nas ni/ /bla ma mchod pa yang dag brtsam/ /de mnyes pas ni kun mkhyen pa'i/ /ye shes mchog ni 'thob par 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs
pa mdo rgyud bstan bcos mang po nas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan brjod pa bas/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi yon tan gyi cha shas tsam brjod pa bsod nams che bar
gsungs pa yin la/ de'i rgyu mtshan yang / ba tshwa can chu klung gi mdo las/ lnga brgya tha mar gyur pa na/ /nga nyid slob dpon gzugs 'dzin te/ /nga yin snyam du yid byos
la/ /de tshe de la gus pa bskyed/ /ces dang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi rgyud las/ rdo rje sems dpa' lta bu yi/ /de ltar slob dpon gzugs 'dzin te/ /sems can rjes su

pha dang ma/ /'di nyid yid la bsam par bya/ /zhes pa dang / gang phyir ye shes rdo rje ni/ /mnyes pas myur du 'thob par 'gyur/ /de phyir slob dpon drung gshegs te/ /de bzhin
gshegs rnams phyag mdzad do/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa rgya cher gsungs pa ltar/ thar 'dod rnams la ma nor ba'i lam tshul bzhin du 'doms par mdzad pa'i bshes gnyen dam pa
zab mo'i smin grol gyi bka' drin stsol bar mdzad pa'i mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i rdo rje slob dpon dag ni ji ltar na mtha' klas pa'i nam mkha'i khyon gyis gzhal ba'i skye
rgu rnams kyi nyer 'tsho'i dbang por gyur pa/ gting dpag dka' ba'i thugs bskyed dang smon lam gyi chu mtsho las legs par 'ongs shing / tshogs gnyis rlabs po che'i dri bzhon

dkyil 'khor rmad du byung ba las/ ris med pa'i phrin las kyi 'od zer grangs med pa dus rtag tu 'phro zhing 'phro ba'i ngang tshul can gyi bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyi ye

dkon mchog gsum gyi

rtsa ba/ chos srung nor lha thams cad kyi mnga' bdag /mkhyen brtse nus pa'i gter chen/ chos kyi rje/ chos kyi rgyal po/ /chos kyi dbang phyug /chos dam pa'i 'byor pa zad mi

'dzin pa kun gyi gtso bo/ /bla na med pa'i thugs bskyed bzang po'i cha shas yongs su rdzogs shing / gzhan phan thugs bskyed kyi 'od dkar phyogs brgyar 'phro bas mkha'

par mdzad la/ zab gsang rdo rje gsum gyi rnal 'byor las 'khrungs pa'i nyams rtogs kyi ral pas mngon par brjid cing / dbang rgyud man ngag gi gad rgyang phyogs brgyar sgrogs
pa'i dus zhabs pa smra ba'i seng ge chen po/ /rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog gi bklag lung rnam par dag pa'i nor bu rin po che rnam dpyod brtson pa'i gru chen gyis legs

cad ga ya dha ra mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ /seng ge rgyal mtshan grub mchog yar klung pa/ /shangs chos mnga' bdag bsod nams bzang po dang / /rnal 'byor dbang mo
rnams la gsol

ba 'debs/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug tshar pa rje/ /blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ /dpal 'byor bzang po rdo rje 'chang chen po'i/ /rnam thar dran zhing
snying nas gsol ba 'debs/ /'khrul med ngo mtshar bcu gsum bstan 'gro'i dpal/ /slar yang bsam bzhin mchog gi sprul pa'i sku/ /'gro ba'i mgon po khyab bdag bka' 'gyur
ba/ /bsod nams mchog ldan zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /gzhan yang byin brlabs sprul pa'i rnam rol can/ /'phags pa'i dge bsnyen dharma tA la'i zhabs/ /mkha' 'gros rjes bzung rdo
rje dril bu pa/ /paN chen gang spel rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /kun mkhyen gnyis pa chos kyi grags pa dang / /slob dpon chen po'i thugs sras nam mkha'i snying / /byang chub
sems dpa' jo bo a ti sha/ /bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /rgyal sras sems dpa'i rnam sprul mtha' yas pa'i/ /gsang ba gsum gyi byin rlabs dbyer med pa/
/ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas mtshan/ /khyab bdag bla ma mchog la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar 'chad pa la/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
gis mdzad pa'i tshar chen gsol 'debs bkra shis mtshan bzang mar/ mgon khyod gdod ma'i dbyings su sangs rgyas kyang / /sna tshogs gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa bzhin/
/ngo mtshar skye ba'i zlos gar bcu gsum gyis/ /phan bde'i dga' ston spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dang / 'dar pa rin chen dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i tshar

chen 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs las/ mgon khyod 'og min chen po'i zhing khams su/ /sku gsum yan lag bdun ldan mngon gyur kyang / /zhing 'dir skal bzang 'gro rnams bsgral ba'i
slad/ /bgrang yas rnam sprul bstan la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dang / rje 'di'i sku bstod nged rang gis brtsams pa las/ 'og min zhing na sku lnga lhun grub/ /'phags pa'i yul
na zas gtsang sras po/ /gangs ljongs gnas gsar chos rjer gyur la/ /gsol ba 'debs so byin gyis rlobs shig /ces smos nas/ zas gtsang sras zhes pa'i mtshan du 'di ni kho bo
cag rang lo nyer gcig lon skabs kI la ya'i bsnyen sgrub kyi tshe dbo zla'i tshes dgu'i tho rengs rmi lam gyi snang ba las nges shes yang dag par rnyed do/ /zhes bkod pa
ni/ spyir so skye'i rmi ltas la tshad 'dzin ci la yod kyang / 'di skabs kyi snang ba 'di ni bla ma yi dam gyi byin rlabs dang / rang gi dad mos kyi dbang gis shar ba 'dra'ang
re zhig de skor gyi lo rgyus zhib par 'dri ma nus pas don gnyer can yod na kho bos gsang gtam logs su 'dri ba der gzigs shig /rgyu mtshan de nyid kyi phyir/ bdag cag
gi ston pa mnyam med shAkya'i rgyal po dang skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid dbyer med du bzhugs pas/ de'i dbang du btang na rang cag rnams kyi ston pa 'di nyid ni/ dang por
byang chub mchog tu thugs bskyed/ bar du bskal pa grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags/ mthar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te bla med ye shes mchog gi go 'phang mngon du mdzad
pa yin la/ 'di la'ang theg pa che chung

gi bzhed tshul mi 'dra ba yod kyang / 'dir theg chen gyi dgongs pa bla med 'khrul zad rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi bzhed pa ltar bshad na/ tshul dang po gsum mdzes par byed
pa'i rgyan las/ skyon med bla ma rnams kyi bzhed srol ni/ /grangs med bskal pa'i sngon du rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /zhes bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol du 'og min stug po
bkod pa'am/ rgya mtsho zhes bya bar sangs rgyas dbang po'i tog tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ slar 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir sangs rgya ba'i tshul tsam zhig bstan
pa yin te/ slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas/ dpal ldan stug po bkod pa nyid du don dam thugs chud cing / /dga' ldan skye bo'i don mdzad phyir ni dam pa tog dkar gyur/
/de nas 'dir ni 'gro ba'i don mdzad shAkya'i tog gyur gang / /'chi bdag las rgyal sgyu ma kun ston de ni rgyal gyur cig /ces gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i sangs rgyas de'ang
don dam par mkha' khyab chos kyi sku las g.yo ba med bzhin du longs spyod rdzogs pa dang / sprul pa'i sku ste/ sku gsum mam/ de'i khar kun khyab ngo bo nyid sku dang
shin tu rnam par dag pa ngo bo nyid kyi sku/ zhes sku lnga'i rang bzhin can du bzhugs shing / de'i nang tshan sprul pa'i sku'i skabs su/ rje btsun byams pas mngon rtogs
rgyan las/ gang gi srid pa ji srid bar/ /'gro la phan pa sna tshogs dag /mnyam du mdzad pa'i sku de ni/ /thub pa'i sprul sku rgyun mi 'chad/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ byang sems
dang mkhas grub sogs du ma'i tshul bzung bar mdzad pas na/ de las 'khrungs

rabs kyi phreng ba rim par byon pa ni/ de'ang 'og tu zhing khams brje kha ma'i mnal ltas la dpag na/ 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs 'di'i dngos bstan tshig zin la med rung / /mkha'
khyab skye rgu spyi dang / bye brag gangs can lha gcig spyan ras gzigs dbang sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs du ma dang ldan pa'i thugs rje'i gter chen de nyid las gud na
ma mchis shing / 'khrungs rabs kyi dngos bstan ngo mtshar sku phreng bcu gsum la/ dang po rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa ni rgya gar sman gyi dbang po'i grong khyer du rgyal
po gser gyi 'khor lo'i sras dngul gyi 'khor lo rab tu byung ba'i mtshan dpal ldan chos skyong / ye shes mkha' 'gros dngos su rjes su bzung nas grub pa brnyes te/ rang
nyid ngan par zhal gyis bzhes pa'i mtshan birWa par grags ste/ 'dzam gling mkhas grub kun gyi nang na 'gran zla dang bral ba deng sang yang swa ba nA tha na rdo sku'i tshul
du bzhugs pa de nyid dang / gnyis pa stha wi ra ni/ o Di ya na'i gnas su sku 'khrungs shing / rdo rje btsun mos rjes su bzungs la/ gnas lnga mkhyen pa'i paNDi ta/ rdo
rje gdan gyi mkhan po mdzad cing / brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mthar phyin pa de nyid dang / gsum pa dharma pA la ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs su sku 'khrungs pa lnga rigs mthar
phyin zhing / rlung sems dbang du 'dus pas sku tshe la mnga' brnyes pa lo chen rin chen bzang po'i dbu bla de nyid dang / bzhi pa ga ya dha ra ni/ bhangga la'i rgyal po
tsaNDa rU'u pa akSha'i yig mkhan gyi rigs yin pas ka phasthar grags shing / mtshan dngos ga ya dha ra ste sprin 'dzin nam sprin

gyi shugs can du grags pa/ birWa pa'i slob brgyud a ba dhU tI pa sogs kyis rjes su bzung zhing mkhas grub kyi sa la bzhugs pas 'brog mi lo tsA ba'i bla ma mdzad de/ ljongs
'dir gsung ngag rin po che thog mar spel ba de dang / lnga pa mkhas grub khyung po ni/ snye mo ra mangs su rigs khyung po las sku 'khrungs te/ bon dang gsang sngags gsar
rnying sogs gzhung lugs mang po la sbyangs pa mthar phyin/ bla ma brgya dang lnga bcu bsten/ khyad par ye shes mkha' 'gro ni gu dang / su kha siddhi las yang dag pa'i gdams
ngag khyad par can bzhes te mkhas grub kyi mdzad pa mthar phyin pa de dang / drug pa paN chen bsod snyoms pa ni/ kha che khri brtan du sku 'khrungs pa'i mtshan shAkya
shrI bha dra ste/ ma byon sangs rgyas gsum pa rab gsal gyi rnam sprul du grags shing / rje btsun sgrol mas rjes su bzung zhing 'dul ba'i bstan pa la shin tu bka' drin che
ba sa skya paNDi ta'i dbu bla de nyid dang / bdun pa sangs rgyas ston pa ni/ dbus kyi sa chab bsil ma zhes bya bar bon gyi rigs las 'khrungs shing / sangs rgyas kyi bstan
par rab tu byung ba'i mtshan brtson 'grus seng ge zhes theg pa che chung gi zab chos du ma dang / khyad par shangs chos kyi bdag por brgyud pa rin chen sna bdun gyi tha
ma de nyid dang / brgyad pa kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer ni/ myang stod gser sdings su 'khrungs shing mdo rgyud bstan bcos la mkhas par gyur pas kun mkhyen du grags shing
/ mtshan dngos chos kyi 'od zer la/ thugs rab shin tu che bas 'phags pa rin po ches chos sku 'od zer du gsol ba/ hor dmag byung

ba'i tshe mang po'i srog skyob pa sogs 'gro ba'i dpal mgon du gyur pa de nyid dang / dgu pa kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che ni/ shab smad sgom gnas su rnying ma'i brgyud 'dzin
zhig gi gdung du 'khrungs shing mdo sngags rig gnas dang bcas pa dang / khyad par dus phyis yo ga'i bstan pa la shin tu sku drin che ba de nyid dang / bcu pa yar klung
pa seng ge rgyal mtshan ni/ ldong gi rigs las 'khrungs shing / mkhas grub kyi go sar bzhugs te/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa de nyid
dang / bcu gcig pa pha rgod bsod nams bzang po ni/ gzhon nu nas dam pa'i rigs sad cing / man ngag rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag shangs chos bstan pa'i srog shing / rje btsun rdo
ring pa'i dbu blar gyur pa de nyid dang / bcu gnyis pa rnal 'byor dbang mo ni/ tshar chen rin po che'i sku zhang gi rigs su bltams shing / mkhyen pa'i yon tan rgya che
ba dang / rab tu byung ma'i brtul zhugs la shin tu brtson zhing / rlung sems dbang du 'dus pa de nyid dang / bcu gsum pa tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po ni/ yongs grags kyi
mkhas grub 'gran zla dang bral zhing / rang lugs rje btsun gong ma'i bstan pa'i srog shing de nyid de/ sku phreng bcu gsum po de dag gi 'khrungs rabs 'khrul med so so'i
mnal ltas sogs las nges pa rnyed pa'i lo rgyus dang / rnam thar mdor bsdus re ni gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa'i tshar chen rin po che'i rtogs brjod du'ang
gsal zhing / zhib par ni so so'i rnam thar las rtogs par bya'o/ /der ma zad 'khrungs rabs zhal gsungs ma'i tshig zin ltar/ 'phags pa'i

dge bsnyen dharma tAr yang zhal gyis bzhes te/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ skabs shig rmi ltas su gnas bcu'i thang sku shin tu ngo mtshar ba zhig 'dug par/ de'i gras dge bsnyen
dharma tA lar zhen chen pos bltas shing / 'di'i mdun gyi nam mkhar snang ba mtha' yas zhig kyang yod snyam pa de ma mthong yang / don la dge bsnyen des kho bo byin gyis
brlabs pa zhig yin 'dra gsungs shing zhal gyi bzhes pa ltar/ dharma tA la 'di ni dge bsnyen gyi cha lugs bzung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po zhig yin par bshad cing /
rgya nag thang gi rgyal pos gnas brtan bcu drug spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur mdzad pa'i tshe/ gnas brtan rnams nyin re bzhin ha la shan gyi ri la 'byon pa na/ dha rma tAs
phyags dar mdzad dus gcan gzan ma rungs pas 'tshe ba las zhabs pus g.yas nas stag sprul te ded/ sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas mdun gyi nam mkha'i sprin gseb tu bzhugs nas
byin gyis rlob par grags/ yang slob dpon rdo rje dril bu par zhal gyis bzhes pa ni/ kho bo dbus la phyi ma phyin skabs bkra shis chos sder gsung 'phros su/ skabs shig
rmi lam du grub chen dril bu pa'i rnam thar thang ka zhig gi khrod la 'gro ba snyam byed cing / grub chen de sdig chen rgyal po la thugs khros te/ rwa shor brdabs pas sa
gas nas chu thon te rgyal po 'khor bcas 'jig par nye ba na spyan ras gzigs la gsol ba thob cig gsungs pas/ chu dbus su 'phags pa rang byon de 'di'i thad na yod snyam bltas
pas/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sku zhig kyang mthong zhes gsungs pa dang / yang gsungs las/ 'khor

lo bde mchog 'di la bag chags chen po zhig yod par 'dug /'di'i bsgom bzlas g.yel na yang yang bskul ba'i nyams byed kyin 'dug gsungs pa dang / 'dar grong mkhan chen ngag dbang
shes rab sku drung na bzhugs skabs/ gsungs las/ bde mchog gi bsgom bzlas 'di la yang yang bskul ba zhig gda' ste/ kha sang nas kyang khams phrug zhig gis rgya mthongs
kha 'dir bde mchog gi rtsa sngags dag gsal 'don pa zhig byung gsungs pa sogs grub pa'i slob dpon chen po rdo rje dril bu par yang sku skye bzhes te/ de'ang slob dpon 'di
ni rgya gar shar phyogs bha randrar rgyal rigs su 'khrungs shing / rab tu byung ba'i mtshan blo gros snying po zhes yongs rdzogs kyi paNDi ta chen por gyur te/ mu stegs
kyi rtsod pa las rgyal bas dgra las rnam rgyal du'ang grags shing / dha ri ka pas rjes su bzung nas 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang dang gdams ngag gsan te bhangga la'i nags khrod
du sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe nam mkha' nas o rgyan du phag rdzi mos rjes su 'dzin par lung bstan gyi sgra byung bas der byon te/ phag rdzi mo dang mjal ba'i tshe ye shes
mkha' 'gro ma'i sku dngos su bstan te/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang dang gdams pa gnang nas/ o Di bi sha'i bas mtha' zhig gi nags khrod du sgrub pa mdzad pas bskyed rim mthar
phyin/ rdzogs rim rim lnga'i las rgyar slebs pa na/ yul de'i rgyal po nags khrod du ri dwags kyi rngon par byung tshe phyag dang zhes ma mdzad pas rgyal po khros nas/
chang 'tshong ma'i bu mo padma can zhig yod pa de dma' dbab tu btang bar/ las rgya mdzad nas rgyal pos bu mo la dge slong khrig shog byas

te/ grong gseb tu chang bum bsgrigs nas slob dpon byon pa'i tshe sprul pa'i sras dang sras mo g.yas g.yon du rgyug cing / jo mos chang bum bteg ste rwa bshor du blugs pa gsol
zhing byon pa na/ rgyal pos spyan drangs tshe mi 'ong / chang 'tshong ma'i bu mos bos na 'ong ba zhes thams cad kyis khrel btab pas rwa bshor brdabs pas rim bdun sa 'og
nas chu byung ste/ slob dpon nyid he ru kar byas/ jo mo phag mo/ sras rdo rje dang / sras mo dril bur bsgyur nas nam mkhar gshegs pa na/ kun gyis bzod par gsol bas thugs
rje chen po la gsol ba thob gsungs pa dang / de bzhin byas pas/ chu'i dbus nas thugs rje chen po'i sku rang byung zhig byon te/ de la chus bskor ba lan bdun byas nas chu
sa 'og tu thim/ yul phyogs de thams cad rdo rje theg pa la bkod do/ /yang paN chen gang ba spel du zhal gyis bzhes pa'ang / chu sprel lor 'dar grong chen du mkha' spyod
ma'i khrid sogs chos 'khor bskor tshe/ nyin gcig zhal slob kyi gras rdzong ri rab 'byams pa/ lha rtse chos sde'i dbu byed blo bzang 'gyur med/ sa dmar chos mdzad skal bzang
phun tshogs gsum la gsol ja dang gung tshigs gsol ras stsol skabs/ dbu byed des sku zhabs kyi rnam thar sku phreng gsol 'debs dang bcas pa zhig ljags rtsom zhus pas/
gsol 'debs 'ong min gyi lan ci'ang mi gsung bar/ rgya gar du mdzod la 'grel bshad mdzad pa'i slob dpon gang ba spel de yin pa gsal por 'dug gsungs nas/ rdzong ri rab 'byams
pa la spyan cher gzigs te/ ri bo che'i mkhan chen de la mkha' 'gro'i gsang lung mang po

pheb pa de na/ nga khyung po rnal 'byor yin gsung 'dug /des na tshar chen rin po che'ang de kha yin gsung zhing / de'i 'phros las/ lha sa'i nub ma gir bong bur skyes nas ngal
dub thang chad kyis nyal te mig btsums nas yod 'phror/ shar phyogs su bltas pas rkyang thang sgong skya chur re 'dug pa mthong bas sems skyo nas mchi ma brul byung ba
zhig gsal por 'dug gsungs pa dang / yang skabs shig kho bo la sa skyar bka' chos gnang skabs/ gsung las/ paN chen gang ba spel du skyes pa 'dra ste/ skabs shig rmi lam du
bkra shis chos sde'i sde yangs na khri chen po zhig gi steng du gang ba spel 'dren chas dang bcas par bzhugs nas mdzod kyi bshad pa mdzad cing 'dug pa la/ mngon pa'i bshad
pa de legs min ji 'dra 'ong snyam nged rang gis thog kha nas bltas pas/ rlung po zhig gis paN chen gyi sku pang de ling nger byas song ba na/ ngo tsha nyams byed pa zhig
byung gsung ba/ 'di dag la dpag na gang ba spel dang tshar chen gnyis char du zhal gyis bzhes shing / mnal lam du byung bar ma zad/ mngon par mdzod gyi phyag dpe 'bral
med lta bur mdzad cing / de'i tshig don la mkhyen rab phul du byung bas na/ de'ang slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi dngos slob mngon pa rang las mkhas pa blo gros brtan pa'i slob
ma mngon par la shin tu mkhas shing mdzod la 'grel bshad mdzad pa'i paN chen gang ba spel de nyid dang / dpal ldan chos grags kyi rnam sprul yin pa ni/ grub dbang thang
stong rgyal po'i dbon brgyud ri bo che'i mkhan rin po che blo bzang stobs

ldan dpal 'byor gyi dag snang lung bstan du/ sngon gyi dpal ldan chos grags de/ /mkhas grub mang po rim brgyud de/ /da lta kun dga'i mtshan can 'dir/ /tshad ma'i bag chags
mang du sad/ /sbyong mi dgos pa'i blo tshogs rgyas/ /shes bya rig pa'i gnas lnga la/ /blo stobs shes rab dpa' rtsal rgyas/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ slob dpon 'di ni rgya gar
lho phyogs rgyal dbang gtsug gi nor bu zhes par mu stegs kyi bram ze'i rigs su 'khrungs te/ chung ngu nas sgra mkhas par mkhyen/ zhang pos rab byung gi chas ma ster ba la
khros nas mu stegs pham par bya'o snyam ste nang pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung nas/ dbang phyug sde las tshad ma kun btus tshar gsum gsan pa'i gnyis pa la slob dpon las
kyang mkhas par gyur pas/ slob dpon gyis/ khyod kyis nga'i grub mtha' nor ba phyogs sngar bzung la kun btus kyi 'grel pa rtsoms gsungs/ chos grags kyis kyang grangs can
grub mtha'i gsang tshig shes ched/ zhang po'i chung ma'i g.yog byas te/ de'i ngag bzhin nyan nas gnad rnams dris pas mkhyen pa dang / mkhas pa yod na rtsod par byed do zhes
bsgrags pas phar cher bros/ rtsod pa byas pa rnams rig pas tshar bcad de chos kyi lam la bkod/ rgyal po me tog rgyas pas mkhas pa su yod dris pa na/ mkhas pa yod tshul
gyi tshigs bcad mthar/ phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba nga min su/ /zhes gsungs pas dad de sbyin bdag byas nas sde bdun dang rnam 'grel gyi le'u dang po'i 'grel pa mdzad nas
mkhas pa'i gral

'grims pas phal cher gyis ma shes/ shes pa rnams kyis phrag dog byas te/ khyi mjug la btags pa dang / rten 'brel 'dis nga'i bstan bcos dar bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs nas mnyes
so/ /rgyu mtshan de'i phyir bu ston gyi rnam thar sgra tshad pas mdzad pa las/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'di'i lho phyogs kyi rgyud phal che bar mkhas pa paNDi ta'i skye ba brgyud
mar bzhes nas/ phyi rol mu stegs kyi rgol ba thams cad rmeg med par bcom/ nang pa sangs rgyas pa'i bstan pa nam langs pa la nyi ma shar ba ltar mdzad nas bstan pa'i rtsa
lag chen por gyur/ ces gsungs pa ltar dang / yang nam mkha'i snying po'i sprul pa yin pa ni/ ratna'i spyi lung las/ nam mkha'i snying po'i smon lam sprul pa'i sku: /kun
dga'i ming can gtsang gi phyogs su 'byung : /zhes dang / chos mdzad ma a snying dpal mos zhus ngor stsal ba'i rje nyid kyi gsol 'debs zhal gsung ma las/ rgyal ba kun dngos
padmas rjes bzung zhing / /brtse chen chos kyi dga' ston 'gyed mkhas pa/ /legs pa'i blo gros rgyal sras rdo rje 'dzin/ /grub gnyis phan bde'i 'byung gnas zhabs la 'dud/
/ces dang / dag snang du grub dbang thang stong rgyal pos stsal pa'i zhabs brtan gsol 'debs las/ rigs brgya'i khyab bdag padma kA ra yis/ /tshe rabs du mar rjes bzung
'chi med kyi/ /rigs su bstan 'gro'i dpal du legs 'khrungs pa'i/ /'gro ba'i re gnas lo brgyar 'tsho bar shog /ces gsungs pa ltar/ dge slong nam mkha'i snying

po ni/ chos skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan gyi dbu'i bla mchod mkhan po bo dhi sa twa las so thar gyi sdom pa thob pa dge slong nam mkha'i snying po la sogs pa
mi lnga byung ba gser phye bre re dang bcas rgya gar du gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i chos 'tshol du mngags par mdzad pa bzhin pheb ste/ grub thob su yod dris pas/ ro langs
bde ba dang hU~M kA ra bzhugs zer ba bzhin/ thog mar ro langs bde ba'i drung du byon pas des bod 'dul ba'i dus la ma babs/ rgyal po ku ku rA dzar chos zhus gsungs/ de
nas rim bzhin gser brag bya skyibs tshal na hU~M kA ra bzhugs pa de rtse rgod nag po zhes bya ba zhig gis bstan te sku mdun du thal gyis byon pas/ thugs khros nas bod kyi
sdug 'dre sleb byung hU~M hU~M gsung zhing shangs nas me stag tsha tsha 'phros pas dge slong mi lnga dran med du brgyal/ nam mkha'i snying po thog mar thugs dran gsos
te/ bdag rnams 'dre min/ bod rgyal pos chos 'tshol du btang ba lags pas/ tshe 'di nyid la rig 'dzin gyi sar 'gro ba'i chos gnang dgos zhus nas gser rnams phul bas/ slob dpon
gyis ngas bod 'dul ba'i dus la bab min lha la 'dri'i gsungs nas/ dar cig dgongs par bzhugs nas dus la babs 'dug pas/ gsang sngags bshad sgrub byed pa la dbang thob dgos
gsungs nas/ dpal chen yang dag gi dbang bskur/ de'i bskyed rdzogs kyi man ngag las tshogs dang bcas pa gnang bas/ mi lnga'i nang nas nam mkha'i snying po sku bsod/ thugs
rab/ thugs rus rnams phul du phyin pas sa la phyag gang tsam ma reg par gshegs

te dbang phyug nyer gcig bran bzhin bkol/ ye shes kyi lha mo bdun dang dngos su sbyor ba'i grub pa brnyes/ de'i tshe bod kyi rgyal po la blon po rnams kyis snyan phra phul
ba'i yi ge rgyal pos rgya gar du dge slong mi lngar gnang bas na/ dge slong lnga dang slob dpon bka' bgros mdzad de yang dag gi sgrub pa btsugs par/ dpal gyi seng ges ma
gsan par nam mkha'i snying pos legs slob mdzad kyang bod du byon pas lam bar du klu'i bar chad kyis gshegs/ nam mkha'i snying po sogs bzhis slob dpon gyi bka' bzhin bsgrubs
pas grub rtags su mar me rang 'bar/ dpal gtor zhag tu 'khyil/ bdud rtsi'i snod bcud rnams 'phel zhing dpal chen yab yum gyi zhal gzigs/ de dus bod rgyal po bsnyun gyis
zin par/ nam snying ma gtogs gzhan sus kyang mi phan zer ba mo rtsis la babs pa bzhin/ myur du 'byon gsungs pa'i bka' shog gnang ba ltar bod du byon te/ rgyal po la byin
rlabs mdzad pa tsam gyis bsnyun las grol/ yang dag gi smin grol las tshogs dang bcas pa gnang ba na/ btsun mo dmar rgyan dang sdig blon rnams kyis chos min zhes skur pa
btab pas rgyal po the tshom skyes te lho brag mkhar chur spyugs/ der sgrub pa mdzad pas brag la sku rgyab kyi rjes dang phur pa btab/ nyi zer la chibs nas gshegs bzhud mdzad/
de nas ma 'gyangs par yang / rgyal po bsnyun thu mos zin pa na/ mo rtsis la nam mkha'i snying pos phan zer ba babs pa bzhin/ A tsArYa ye shes dbyangs dang gsal mchog
gnyis slob dpon spyan 'dren pa la btang

pas sngon la song gsungs/ bang phyin ma slebs par slob dpon bsam yas su byon nas/ rgyal po sku khams mi bde'am gsungs pas/ da shi ba la thug /'di la phan pa i yod/ yo byad
ci dgos gsungs pas/ slob dpon gyis phan thabs yod/ yo byad ci'ang mi dgos/ rgyal po rang gis gsol ba gang bzhes nga la drongs shig gsungs nas/ zas kyi rnal 'byor mdzad de
gsol ba tsam gyis cung zad bde/ de nas sum cha dang / sum gnyis dang / yongs rdzogs bzhes pa nas rim bzhin bsnyun las grol/ gsol ba'i lhag ma mdzo zho dang bcas par slob
dpon gyis zhal chab btab ste rgyal por gnang / nyi ma bzhud khar rgyal po'i dbu bsil ba na/ slob dpon gyis nyi grib mtshams su phur pa btsugs te nyi ma bzung / dbu skra
bsil tshar ma thag phyugs rnams ra bar chug cig gsungs nas/ phur pa bton pas nyi ma nub pa sogs thugs rje dang rdzu 'phrul la rgyal po thugs rangs nas za 'og gi ber sogs
phul/ slob dpon gyis bka' 'khor dam pa'i rgyud lnga dang / sme brtsegs me ltar 'bar ba/ 'jam dpal gsang rgyud/ gwa'u nag po/ ro langs gsang rgyud/ tsitta gsang rgyud rnams
bsgyur/ de nas sngar lo paN du mas chos bsgyur ba rnams la rab gnas mdzad pa'i tshe rgyal po dang nam mkha'i snying po gnyis khrom gseb tu phyag la ma 'chams pas/ nam mkha'i
snying pos rgyal po'i bla ma mi byed do gsungs nas lho brag mkhar chur 'byon par chas pa na/ lo paN gzhan gyis yon mchod gyi bar du mtshams sbyar te/ nam mkha'i snying
po bzhugs par/ phyi blon nang blon rnams kyis slob dpon

dkrong ba'i khrims bcas te lhog sgor khri gnyis brtsegs nas rgyal po dang slob dpon bzhugs su bcug /mda' mdung sogs mtshon gyi sbyor ba brtsams pa na rgyal po thugs skrag nas
sku 'dar/ slob dpon gyis gha Ta shag gsungs te thal mo phral bas blon po rnams kyis mtshon cha thams cad shor/ mgon po dang lha mo'i sku zhig yod par slob dpon gyi zhabs
rdo brgyabs nas ldongs gsungs pas slob dpon gyi rjes la 'brangs/ hU~M sgra drag por gsungs pas thog babs pa sdigs mdzub kyi rtse la dkris nas 'u shang rdo'i brag la brgyabs
pas dum bur bsnyil/ rgyal po la mi 'jigs sam gsungs pas/ gnam lcags kyi thog las kyang slob dpon gyi hU~M sgra de 'jigs so gsungs nas/ rgyal pos phyag phul ba sogs
mkhas grub kyi go 'phang chen po la bzhugs pa de nyid/ slar yang lho brag mkhar chur gshegs te mthar phung po lhag ma med par mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul ston par mdzad
ces bshad do/ /yang a ti sha'i rnam sprul yin pa ni/ phrin las kyi mgon po pu tra dmar po'i lung las/ ra sgreng phyogs su mchod 'bul gsol 'debs 'phungs/ /zhes dang / rje
'di'i zhabs brtan la dmigs jo bo'i sku bstod 'don dgos par gsungs pa sogs/ don gyi jo bo rjer lung bstan pa bzhin/ jo bo rje 'di ni bdag cag gi ston pa dang mnyam du thugs
bskyed cing / ston pa sangs rgyas pa'i tshe rgyal sras bzang skyong du gyur nas bskal bzang 'di la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa ston par bshad cing / thun mong pa'i rnam thar
ni/ shing glang lor dar mas bstan pa bsnubs nas lo don brgyad

song ba na/ shar phyogs bhangga la'i pho brang gser gyi rgyal mtshan du rgyal po dge ba dpal dang / btsun mo 'od zer can gnyis la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i/ bar pa zla ba'i snying
po 'di nyid chu rta lor 'khrungs pa'i tshe pho brang gi thog mtshams la utpal sngon po skyes pa kun gyis mthong zhing / rgyal bu la sgrol mas zhal gzigs te rjes su
bzung bar mkhyen/ dgung lo bcu'i bar du yi ge /bzo/ gso dpyad dang / lugs kyi bstan bcos sbyangs/ nyer gcig pa la sgra tshad/ sgyu rtsal drug cu rtsa bzhi/ zlos gar/ snyan
ngag /rtsis rnams mkhyen/ dzai tA ri sogs bla ma lnga las theg chen gyi chos gsan nas/ rgyud man ngag rdzogs par mkhyen te lo drug tu brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mdzad pas
yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs/ ting 'dzin dang mngon shes lnga thob/ rdo rje rnal 'byor mas dngos su dbang bskur/ gsang sngags kyi rgyud sde mang du mkhyen pa'i nga rgyal yod
pa na mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis rgyud kyi glegs bam du ma bstan nas thugs rgyal bcag /rtsod pa'i sgo nas mu stegs tshar bcad/ mnal lam du thub pa'i dbang pos bskul te dgung
lo nyer dgu la rab tu byung ba'i mtshan dI paM kA' ra shrI dznyA nar gsol nas/ zab mo lta brgyud/ rgya chen spyod brgyud/ nyams len byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa las 'ongs pa'i
sde snod mtha' dag gsan cing thugs su chud pas mkhas pa'i grags pas khyab cing / btsun pa'i yon tan so thar dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa 'ong ma myangs/ byang sems dang sngags
sdom la cung zad byung srid kyang de ma thag bshags te zhag tu 'grogs ma myangs gsungs

pa dang / rtogs pa'i yon tan byang sems dang ting 'dzin phun sum tshogs shing / spyan dang / mngon shes dang / rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab par mnga' bas paN grub
kun las ches lhag par mthong nas/ rgyal po dharmA pA las a ti sha zhes/ bod skad du phul du byung ba'i mtshan gsol te/ rgyal gar du bstan 'gro'i don dpag med mdzad nas
dgung lo nga bdun pa'am re gcig gang rung la lha btsun khu dbon gyis bod du spyan drangs te sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nam langs pa la nyi ma shar ba ltar mdzad pa de nyid
yin la/ gzhan yang chos rgyal dbang po'i sdes mdzad pa'i gter ston brgya rtsa'i gsol 'debs las/ rig 'dzin padma'i rnam sprul a ti sha /zhes gsungs par dpag na/ de gnyis
thugs rgyud gcig pas/ slob dpon chen po'i sprul par yang mi 'gal lam snyam ste/ skabs shig 'dar grong mkhan po zhal dkar rje drung la gsung sgros kyi mur/ nga tshe rabs
mang por slob dpon chen pos rjes su bzung ba zhig ni nges par yin 'dug pheb par/ de ji ltar lags zhus pas/ chung ngu'i skabs dbang lung gang yang ma thob pa'i rnying lugs
kyi nyams len zhig la brten nas rmi lam bzung bas/ bkra shis chos sde'i sgo 'phyor rab gsal gyi dpyang khar phyin pas g.yang za snyam gyis rkyen byas rmi lam zin pa dang
sprul bsgyur gyi snang ba'ang shar bzhin/ de mtshungs dbang lung dang bral ba'i pad gling nas brgyud pa'i tshe sgrub cig la nyams len bgyis nub/ de kha'i rmi ltas su/ tshe
bum gyi rtse rgyan tshe dpag med kyi sku yod par zil pa phrom phrom ba zhig gi zil pa

rnams 'jibs pas ro phun sum tshogs pa yod pa zhig byung gsung ba kun rdzob ltar snang du sku tshe 'dir gang zag gzhan las ma gsan yang / mnal nyams lta bur dag pa ye shes kyi
sku gang rung gis rjes su ma bzung ba'i nges pa med par ma zad/ sku phreng gzhan du gsan sgom gnang ba'i smon lam dbang bskur dang / bka' babs lung bstan lta bur yin pa
dang / nges don du gu ru padma nyid du'ang zhal gyis bzhes sam snyam pa'i khungs shin tu mang yang / re zhig yi ge'i dbang gis de tsam mo/ /yang skabs shig ngas bram ze
ta thA ga ta rakShi tar skye ba blangs pa zhig kyang dran gsungs/ ji ltar lags zhus pas/ rmi lam zhig la zhal bram gzugs kyi sku thang legs pa zhig 'dug pa'i gsham na 'di
ta thA ga ta rakShi ta'i thugs dam ma yin zer ba zhig 'dug par/ de nga yin snyam pa zhig byung gsungs/ rjes su 'khrungs rabs kyi ljags lung stsal ba'i tshe 'dir ta thA
ga ta rakShi ta mi snang zhus pas/ yod tshad ci la 'ong / dran tshad bris na bong bu zhig tu skyes pa'ang dran te/ de'ang rgod dkar la'i rtse 'og zhig tu bdag po rnams tsha
phog byed cing nyi ma dgong myur tsam la da dung la rtser slebs pa dka' mo 'ong 'dra snyam sems las dang bcas nyal nas yod pas mig gyen la blta ba zhig kyang dran gsungs
pa ni/ rje mkhyen brtses/ dag dang ma dag skye ba bcu gnyis mthar/ /zhes dang / bdag cag gi ston pas kyang / seng ge /glang chen/ ngang pa'i rgyal po sogs sna tshogs su
sku 'khrungs pa dang 'dra bar bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam thar du sems zhes zhal dkar ba gsungs pa dang /

sa skya'i rig 'dzin pho brang du bzhugs skabs shig /mnal lam du sa skya paNDi ta bzhugs yod dgongs pa la/ sa skya'i shar phyogs su mu stegs 'phrog byed dga' bo'i gur yin 'dug
zer ba'i gur mang po rmis pas/ sa paN gyi sku 'khor zhig gi skye ba yin tshod du 'dug ces rdzong rams par gsungs pa dang / khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog
ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam sprul yin pa ni/ grub dbang thang stong rgyal po dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang sogs kyi rnam sprul grub dbang sgro
lung pa chen po mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel dang / grub pa'i sar bzhugs dam can bran du 'khol ba'i khams ston chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho sogs dam pa du mas 'khrul
med du ngos 'dzin mdzad pa ni 'og tu gsal ba ltar dang / bsam yas chos skyong chen pos kyang gnas chung lcog tu rgya dar dkar po la yig brgya'i snying po bris nas phul
na bzang / zhes lung bstan gyi dgongs gzhi/ sngar gung thang du khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba dang gnas chung chos skyong gnyis la dam sel cung zad byung ba de zhi byed kyi lung
bstan 'khrul med dang / rje 'di nyid kyis kyang sngon gnas rjes dran gyi tshul gsal bar gsungs pa ni/ chung ngu nas dbus skad gsungs pa dang / rje ngag la/ bka' las/ dbus
'gro dang po'i nyer bsdogs skabs/ gong dkar chos sde dran gsos pa dang / gong dkar du thog mar slebs pa'i sna bstad klu dbang gling zhes khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba'i bzhugs
gnas der thug pa'ang de'i skye ba 'dra rung tsam yin 'dra pheb pa dang /

sman lung pa blo mchog rdo rjer/ gong ra ba rnams kyis thugs bsun zhus tshul dang / skabs shig shin tu bkren pas gtor ma'i mtheb skyu gsol dgos tshe'ang zhabs phyi der khyod
rang mang tsam zo/ nged a'u rtsi zhes pheb tshul spyan chab bcas gnang ba dang / zhwa lu mkhan chen gyi'ang / sku chas thams cad lan gsum dag par mdzad skabs shin tu bkren
par byung 'dug cing / de skabs shig khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba nged sdod sa 'di dang / mkhan chen de nyid da lta 'jam dpal sdod sa 'dir bzhugs nas gsung ngag slob bshad
rdzogs par gsan 'dug ces spyan chab mang po bsil mthar/ mkhan chen zhwa lu ba'i bgros byung res kyis mig chu dbang med 'ong ba zhig 'dug /ci yin ni ma shes/ pheb pa'ang
skyes mchog de gnyis bla slob bam/ rdo rje'i mched po zla med yin gshis/ 'di'ang sngon gnas rjes dran gyis rje nyid khyab bdag bka' 'gyur bar don gyis rtogs nus pa dang /
'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs kyi sbyar byang du rje bka' 'gyur ba nyid nas gter ston rig 'dzin chen po 'ja' tshon snying por ma 'ongs 'khrungs rtags kyi lung bstan zhus gnang
la/ skye ba phyi ma gtsang rta nag phyogs su sngags bon khyad par can gyi rigs su skyes nas bstan pa dang sems can la phan thogs 'ong tshul gnang ba'ang 'drar rung ba dang
/ zhes khengs bskyung gi gsung 'dis kyang khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen por bsnyon med du grub pas/ rje bka' 'gyur ba'i rnam thar rgyas pa ni gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga
pa chen pos mdzad pa de nyid las rtogs par bya zhing / gong du bshad pa ltar dge slong nam mkha'i snying po'i zlos gar rje bka'

'gyur ba yin pa ni rnam thar de nyid du gsal bar ma zad/ chos rgyal gter bdag gling pa'i rdor sems thugs thig gi kha byang lung bstan las/ gnubs ban nam mkha'i snying po ni:
rgyal lam bsod nams ming 'dzin paH sogs kyis gsal bar bstan cing / yang khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba dang / dpal sa skya'i 'jam mgon a mes zhabs gnyis thugs rgyud gcig pa ni/
gong du bshad pa'i bka' 'gyur ba'i rnam thar de nyid du/ me bya lo sa skyar pheb pa'i 'phros las/ gzhi thog tu zhabs drung rin po cher mkha' 'gro sun zlog dang 'brel ba'i
brtan bzhugs rgyas par phul nas/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa lnga'i bar du bzhugs pa'i bka' bzhes zhus par/ mkhan po rang bstan don la dgongs nas de tsam bzhugs na ni nga
rang de ga bgyid/ de min nged rang gnyis lhan du 'gro ba yin/ pheb pa'i gnas tshul rje bla ma 'bras spungs su pheb dus gsung 'phros gnang 'dug cing / sa phag hor zla dgu
pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la dam pa 'di dang / bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la bdag chen rin po ches me tog 'thor ba la dpag na bla ma rnam gnyis sprul gzhi gcig las bstan 'gro'i
ched du spro bsdu mdzad dgos par sems/ zhes gsungs pas na rnam 'dren dam pa de gnyis dbyer ma mchis shing/ rgyu mtshan de nyid kyi phyir 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi 'khrungs
rabs su/ byang sems rgya bod mkhas grub ji snyed gsung pa rnams khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po'i sku phreng du'ang 'gyur zhing / de nyid bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam
pa 'di nyid du sku'i skye ba bzhes pas gong du

bshad pa de dag las 'phros nas sku phreng kho na'i rnam thar kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod par sems so/ /'o na bdag cag gi ston pa dang 'phags mchog spyan ras gzigs gnyis
ni sangs rgyas zin pa dang / rab gsal dang bzang skyong gnyis ni rgyas 'gyur yin pa dang / 'phags mchog spyan ras gzigs rnal 'byor dbang phyug yin pa sogs mi 'gal lam snyam
na/ mi 'gal te/ spyir sa dang po'i byang 'phags rnams kyis kyang / zhing khams brgyar chos gsan pa dang / zhing khams brgyar chos ston pa sogs yon tan brgya phrag bcu
gnyis la dbang bsgyur na/ de bas lhag pa rnams la lta ci smos te/ sangs rgyas dang byang sems chen po rnams ni dbang bcu dang sprul bsgyur la mnga' brnyes pas gang 'dod
du skye ba len nus shing / de'ang gcig nyid mang por sprul ba dang / chung ngu chen por bsgyur ba sogs nus pas na/ sku'i skye sprul gnyis cig car du sprul nus pa la the tshom
ci zhig dgos te/ bla ma sa skya pa chen pos tshar khar khrid skyong ba/ sa skyar gsung ngag gsungs pa/ gung thang du mal gyi nye gnas mdzad pa/ 'gring mtshams su rab
gnas mdzad pa/ zang sdong du lam 'bras gsungs pa/ shab sgo lngar chos 'khor bskor ba ste/ sku'i bkod pa mi 'dra ba drug dus gcig la bstan cing / gzugs sku bsdu ba'i tshe'ang
/ bde ba can dang / po ta la sogs su gshegs pa'i bkod pa mi gcig pa lnga cig car ston par mdzad pa dang / de bzhin du rje btsun rtse mos kyang zhi

bar gshegs pa'i dus su bkod pa mi 'dra ba gnyis mdzad pa'i tshul yab sras gnyis po de'i rnam thar du gsal ba dang mtshungs shing / gzhan yang de 'dra'i rigs can mang du snang
bas so/ /gzhan yang bla ma sa skya pa chen po gzhon nu'i skabs/ grub pa'i dbang phyug gnang kha'u pas sku pang du bzhes nas/ 'di ni nges par spyan ras gzigs sam/ byang
chub sems dpa' sbyin pa'i dpal nyid yin la/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug nyid du'ang mi 'gal ba yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa 'dis ni slob dpon chen po nyid du'ang mi 'gal bar bstan
pa yin te/ slob dpon chen po ni 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs nyid yin zhing / de dang rnal 'byor dbang phyug mi 'gal bar gsungs pa'i phyir dang / sngar smos pa ltar rje nyid/
rje btsun chen pos rtse mor bstod pa las/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang byams mgon dbyer med pa'i/ /bla ma mchog dang dam pa khyod nyid la/ /khyad par 'ga' yang bdag gis yod
ma shes/ /zhes sogs dri ma med pa'i lung gis grub pa'i phyir ro/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dang por chos longs sprul gsum rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /bar du byang sems mkhas grub
bzang rim pa/ /tha mar khyab bdag bka' 'gyur mtshan can sogs/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma'i 'khrungs rabs yin/ /zhes so/ /de ltar bshad ma thag pa'i sprul pa'i sku'i bkod
pa ji snyed cig bstan pa de dag gis mdzad phrin bla na med pa'i rgyun slar yang spel nas snyigs dus kyi bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon mdzad par bzhed de/ ngur smrig gi bla gos
'chang ba'i rnam rol du bstan nas rgyal

bstan spyi dang / bye brag gi bdag por gyur pa'i bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid du skye ba'i cho 'phrul bstan pa'i tshul ni/ gang gi rnam thar gsol 'debs kun dga' ye
shes sgrol mas zhus ngor stsal ba las/ sngon goms dge legs smon lam 'bras bzang po/ /ma nyams lha yi rigs su yongs smin pa/ /skyon bral mtshan dpe'i dpal gyis mngon par
mdzes/ /mthong ba don ldan gzhon nu'i sku la 'dud/ /ces gsungs pa ltar rje 'di nyid gang du 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ de'ang skyabs mgon 'di nyid zhing khams gzhan du gshegs
nye'i skabs rmor du pheb dus gong gi zhabs 'bring snye thang 'phags bde ba blo gsal rab rgyas kyis da lam sku khams dwangs 'phral rmor 'dir thugs brel chung bar 'ong 'dug
gshis rnam thar rin po che zhal gsung ma zhig thugs rjes gzigs dgos tshul zhus par/ kho bo'i rnam thar kho na rkyang 'ded du bris kyang nying dgos ha cang mi 'dug pas/
nged rang gi bsam pa ltar na/ dang po rigs rus 'chad skabs su bod kyi mi rigs sogs byung tshul/ skyes pa'i skabs gza' skar gyi rnam gzhag sogs rgyas pa/ skye yul ngos 'dzin
skabs bod khams gling dgu dang stong sde bco brgyad sogs byung tshul/ rab tu byung skabs 'dul ba'i skor sogs kyi rnam gzhag rgyas pa/ dper na mi blo gros 'bring tsam zhig
gis rnam thar tshar gcig bklags pas phyi nang gi rig gnas gang ci'i don spyi char nges pa/ de'i khongs nas rnam thar yang thon pa zhig byung na snyam yang yi ges 'jigs
nas ma byung gsungs pas/ blo gsal rab rgyas kyis/ 'o na ci nas

kyang brtse gzigs sku drin che ba zhu shing / bka' bstan sogs kyi lung khungs len pa dang / yi ge'i zhabs 'degs zhu chog tshul zhus par/ ci'ang mi gsung zhes bshad pas/ rnam
'dren dam pa de nyid kyi thugs la shar ba bzhin lo rgyus zab cing rgya che ba zhig bdag lta bus 'dri ba rngo ma thogs kyang / thugs kyi dgongs pa khyad par can rdzogs pa'i
phyir dang / gang dag ma dad pa dag dad par bya ba'i phyir dang / dad pa dag kyang dad pa'i dngos po phyi phyir gong 'phel du 'gyur ba'i phyir dang / rang gzhan kun gyi
rgyud la ye shes gzigs pa'i byin rlabs khyad par can ci dgar 'jug pa sogs dgos pa dang nying dgos bsam gyis mi khyab pa nyid kyi phyir/ zab yangs yon tan rgya mtsho'i
brjod bya'i rang bzhin las/ rjod byed rang blos gang zin tsam zhig 'bri na/ sku 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ de'ang / tshul gsum gsal rgyan las/ de yi gnas ni stug po bkod pa ste/
/mi mjed 'jig rten khams sogs du ma zhig /nang du tshud pa me tog rgyan gyis brgyan/ /de 'dra du ma nang du tshud pa ni/ /rgya mtsho zhes bya longs sku'i phyag na gnas/
/zhes pa ltar/ ston pa rnam par snang mdzad gangs can mtsho'i phyag mthil gyi lhung bzed spos chus yongs su gang ba'i rgya mtsho chen po'i dbus su/ padma'i sdong po chen
po rgya khyon rab tu yangs pa skyes pa la/ me tog padma nyi shu rtsa lnga tho brtsegs su yod pa'i me tog re re'i steng du 'jig rten gyi khams re re yod par gsungs pa'i
/ padma bcu gnyis yar mar du brtsis pa'i dbus bcu gsum pa'i steng na gnas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams/ sprul pa'i sku ston pa shAkya'i rgyal po'i

gdul zhing mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams 'di la ri rab/ gling bzhi/ gling phran/ lcags ri dang bcas pa yod pa'i gling bzhi gling phran gzhan las khyad par du 'phags pa 'dzam
gling las kyi sa pa 'di la/ ri'i rgyal po gangs can/ brag gser gyi bya skyibs can/ mtsho chen po ma dros pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bas pa/ shing sA la'i rgyal po la sogs pa
yul gyi bkod pa ngo mtshar can du mas mdzes shing / ma dros pa'i 'gram du shing gi rgyal po 'dzam bu tri sha zhes bya ba la/ 'bras bu ro mchog brgya dang ldan pa rnams shin
tu smin par gyur pas/ chu nang du lhung ba na/ dzam zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ba las mtshon te/ 'dzam bu'i gling du btags pa 'di la grong khyer chen po lnga brgya/ ljongs
chen po bcu drug /yul phran stong / yul chen so gnyis/ gnas nyer bzhi/ dur khrod chen po brgyad/ mi rigs sum brgya drug cu/ skad rigs bdun brgya nyi shu sogs bsam gyis
mi khyab pa yod pa'i/ shar phyogs na rgya nag dang khri brtan/ rgya nag tu mkhyen rab kyi bdag po 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi pho brang ri bo rtse lnga/ lhor rgya gar dang kha
che/ rgya mtsho'i 'gram na 'phags mchog phyag na padma'i pho brang ri bo gru 'dzin/ nub tu stag sde dang gzig yan/ rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang po rnams dgyes rgur spyod
pa'i gnas mchog au Di ya na/ byang du khram dang ge sar/ chos rgyal rigs ldan rim par byon pa'i gnas shambha lar cha bsags kyi pho brang grong khyer bye ba dgu bcu dang bcas
pa yod pa'i yul gyi bye brag spur rgyal bod du grags pa gangs ri dpal dang ldan pas bskor ba'i ljongs/ 'phags

mchog spyan ras gzigs kyi gdul bya'i zhing du gyur pa ni/ padma drwa ba can gyi rgyud las/ sngon tshe 'das dus bskal ba ni/ /bye ba phrag brgya'i snga rol na/ /bde gshegs rdzogs
sangs rgyas kyi mtshan/ /tshe dpag med ces 'jig rten du/ /ston pa byung bar bdag gis mnos/ /de tshe phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis/ /bdag la dbang bskur lung bstan mdzad/
/phyis ni 'dren pa shAkya zhes/ /mi mjed 'jig rten khams 'khrungs tshe/ /mi yul las kyang khyad par du/ /yi dwags gling du skyes pa 'ga'/ /bstan la 'dud 'phel bya ba'i
phyir/ /mtshan mo mun nag sprin rum du/ /skad cig glog 'gyu ji lta bar/ /rig sngags 'chang ba gdong bcu gcig /yan lag stong dang ldan pa la/ /spyan ni chig stong sum
cu pa'i/ /tshe dang ldan pa'i sku 'byung 'gyur/ /zhes shAkya seng ge'i bstan pa la/ bod yul yi dwags kyi gling spyan ras gzigs phyag stong spyan stong gi gdul zhing du gsungs
pa ltar/ mkhas pa'i dbang po 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal bas/ thugs rje'i dbang pos byin brlabs gser gyi sa gzhi brdal ba gangs ri'i phreng mdzes khor yug can/ /nyes pa'i
gdung bral tshul khrims ma dros las 'ongs 'dus pa'i rgyun dag chad pa med par 'babs/ /bshad dang sgrub pa'i rin chen gyis gang mkhas pa'i rta gdong dag las chos kyi sgra
chen sgrogs/ /mtha' dag legs pa'i 'byung gnas gangs can 'di ni rgya mtsho che 'dra mkhas pas bsngags par 'os/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yon tan rin po che'i tshogs kyis mngon
par gang ba'i yul yi

dam gyi lha'i byin rlabs rgyud la zhugs pa'i mtshan ma gsal byed du byis pa dag gis kyang / oM ma Ni padme hU~M/ zhes gsungs mchog yi ge drug pa'i sgra rang byung du sgrogs
pa/ yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i ya gyal/ rgyal bstan rin po che'i srog gnas pas chos tshigs kyis phye ba'i yul dbus/ gangs can nam/ bod du grags pa 'di la/ stod na mnga' ris
skor gsum/ smad na mdo khams sgang gsum/ bar na dbus gtsang ru bzhi sogs yod pa las/ gtsang gi g.yas ru/ de la sngon gyi dus na bod dbus gtsang gi cha la/ stong sde bzhi
bcu/ stong bu chung bzhi dang bcas pa'i dbye ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ khyung po/ /spa tshab/ langs pa/ 'gos rnams la stong sde gnyis gnyis/ sle bya la stong bu chung gcig dang
bcas pa yod pa las/ sle bya'i stong sder gtogs pa/ rgya mtsho zhes bya ba o rgyan chen pos byin gyis brlabs pa'i sgrub gnas sog po 'dzur khung dang ha cang mi ring zhing
/ 'gro ba'i gdung sel rang byung khrus kyi rdzing bu dang 'dab 'byor ba/ mi rnams dpa' rtsal dang ldan pa/ g.yo sgyu med cing bzod bsran che la blo brtan pa/ gshong zhing
dang gam 'brog zung du spyod pas longs spyod che ba/ de lta bu'i yul gyi bye brag lo tsha zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid chen po 'di'i 'khrungs yul yin la/ khyab bdag rdo rje
'chang chen po 'di nyid mi'i zlos gar du bzhengs pa'i gdung rus ni/ bod snga rabs pa'i bshad srol bod yul ma sangs kyis bzung ba'i lo rgyus las bsnyad de bon gyi lugs ltar
'chad na/ rgyal rabs khug pa zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos las/ bod mi rgyud drug tu grol ba ni/ zhes sogs rgya cher bshad pa'i don/ bod mi

khri mtho zhes bya bar sras drug byung ba ni dbra 'bru ldang gsum sga dang bzhi/ nu bo dpa' rda gnyis dang drug byung ba la/ che rgyud gong nas ma shor ba/ /phu bo ldong gi
mi rgyud yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phu bo ldong las gyes pa la rus chen bco brgyad yod par grags te/ /rlangs kyi po ti bse ru las/ /che ba smug po chung ldong la/ /che drug
btsan drug rgyud pa byung / /nga che rus chen bco brgyad yod/ ces gsungs pa'i bco brgyad kyi dang po'i nang gses las brgyud pa mang du 'phel ba'i/ lcog rtse/ lcog ro/ 'bro/
khyung po/ zangs dkar/ 'a zhwa ste drug gis mnga' ris skor gsum bzung bar bshad pa'i 'a zhwa ste/ rgyal srid bon bzhin skyong ba'i rgyal po zhig yin pa la/ bod spyi la
dbang ba'i rgyal po gnya' khri btsan po'i mnga' 'bangs su gyur te/ rje dang gnyen bsres pas dpon zhang du song / bon gyi grub thob sha stag tu byung zhing / bla'i mchod
gnas su bkur ba'i che gnyen btsun gsum 'dzom pa'i rgyal po'i gdung dri ma med pa las rim gyis byung ba lags/ chos lugs ltar 'chad na/ 'jam dpal rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ nga
ni 'das nas lo brgya na/ /kha yi ljongs su mtsho bri nas/ /sA la'i nags ni 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bod yul 'di nyid dang po chus yongs su gang ba las rim
gyis bri ste sA la'i sman ljongs su gyur pa'i stod du glang po dang ri dwags/ bar na ri dwags dang spre'u/ smad na spre'u dang brag srin gyis bzung ste gnas pa las/ 'phags
mchog phyag na padmo dang rgyal yum phrin las lha mo'i thugs rje'i 'jug pa mchog tu zab pas/ spre'u dang brag srin mo 'dus pa las mi'i 'gro ba byung zhing / de dag las

rim bzhin rus chen bzhi'am/ mi'u gdung drug tu grags pa'i nang tshan lha rigs 'a zhwa'i rgyal po zhes/ rgyal brgyud gtsang ma zhig rim gyis bod rgyal po'i mnga' 'og tu gyur
cing / rje dang gnyen bsres pas dbon zhang du gyur/ rgya bod dbon zhang gnyis bsdum pa'i tshe nang rjer gyur pas dbon 'a zhwa rje zhes rdo ring gi yi ger gsal ba de'i gdung
rnam par dag pa las rim gyis byung ba lags/ yang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug zhabs kyi gsung las/ 'od gsal lhar babs khrel dang ngo tsha phyi thag
ldan pa nga / /ngo tsha ches pas dpon skya'i zla la ma chud pad gsung dang / /pha rjes snyogs phyir ngo tsha dam tshig phyi thag gang ring byed/ /legs par brtags na da lta'i
che che tshos 'gran pas do ba yang med/ /ngo ma shes na 'a zhA'i rgyal po kho yin pad gsungs dang / /ngo ma shes na gnas gsar stong dpon kho yin pad gsung dang / /zhes
'byung ba ltar/ 'od gsal lha las babs pa'i gtam rgyud ni/ de'ang sngon gyi dus na yul mnga' ris kyi ljongs na spyi la dbang ba'i rgyal po med par glang po che cang shes
rgyan gyis spras nas snar bum pa bzang po bcud kyis gang ba thogs te rgyal po 'tshol ba la 'bod par byed do/ /de'i tshe yul khams de nyid 'dul skyong gi dus la babs par
mkhyen nas lha'i bu mtshan dang ldan pa zhig mi khrom dmar nag 'khyil pa'i dbus su babs shing / de ma thag glang po cang shes kyis bum pa dbu thog tu bzhag cing rgyal por
dbang bskur/ mi'i grib kyis spyan gcig mi gsal bar gyur/ des na nam mkha' las babs shing / spyan gcig mi gsal bas/ mes po nam mkha' spyan gcig tu grags shing / de las rim
gyis 'phel ba yin zhes

pa'i lo rgyus kyang snang lags/ gang ltar khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan yan chad rnam thar snga ma rnams su gsal zhing / de'i sku mched la/ 'a zhwa nam mkha' don
grub dbang po dang / lcam gcig byung ba nam mkha' don grub dbang po ni yab mes kyi rnam thar kho na lhur mdzad de phyi dpa' mdzangs kyi spyod pas srid kyi 'dzin skyong la
mkhas pa/ nang du rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor la thugs gzhol bas grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po dang / lcam sring ma de'ang 'khor ba'i gnas tshul 'bar ba'i me 'obs ltar gzigs
te/ tshe 'di'i bde skyid snyan gsum mchil ma'i thal ba ltar bor nas gsang chen zab mo'i sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pa'i rang byung gi rnal 'byor ma chen mo zhig yod ces
gsungs la/ nam mkha' don grub dbang po'i sras su 'a zhwa mkhyen rab rnam rgyal dang / lcam sring ma mkhyen rab blo ldan gnyis 'khrungs par/ 'a zhwa mkhyen rab rnam rgyal
rang byams chen du chos sgor 'jug pa gnang / lcam sring ma'ang chos sgor 'jug bzhed la/ sde pa bkra shis rtse pa'i bdag mor nan gyis zhu ba mdzad par/ bkra shis chos sde'i
yon bdag gi rtsa bar song gshis zhal gyis bzhes kyang / slar bkra shis rtse pa blo 'gyur te bdag mo gzhan nas bsus pas/ 'jig rten lugs srol gyi bor rnams tshang ma bzhes
pa rnams la gtso bor brten nas bkra shis chos sder dkyil 'khor nyi shu rtsa gsum gyi sgrub mchod 'dzugs par mdzad/ lcam sring ma de nyid kyang dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes
te bkra shis chos sde'i bla brang rang du gtan chags shing / bzo'i rig byed la thugs rab phul du phyin pa'i phyag rjes kyang mang zhing / bi shwa karma'i

khengs pa 'phrog par nus pa sha stag mchis/ thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor la thugs 'grus shing / yab mes kyi srung ma rtsis mgon lha chen dpal 'bar 'khor bcas kyi bskang ba sogs chos
spyod kyi rigs kyang rtag 'grus su mdzad/ 'di la da lta zhabs drung mkhyen drung zhes ngag rgyun la snang ba mkhyen rab blo ldan zhes pa'i mtshan zur yin nam snyam/ de'ang
rig 'dzin yongs 'dus las/ chos kyi grwa 'byung dam tshig ma gtsang naH pho bdud 'khrugs pas nyer gcig gri ru 'chi: zhes pa'i lung bstan dus babs kyi sde pa bkra shis
rtse pa rdo rje 'chang khu dbon de dag la yid gnyis kyi 'khyogs la 'phyang ba'i spyod tshul ci rigs byung bar brten/ sde pa dngos grub rdo rje mtshon khar gums shing /
mi nor dpung bcas rtsa brlag gis ming tsam du gyur pa kun gyi mig sngar son pa 'di nyid lags/ gang ltar dbyings pa bsod nams chos 'phel nas/ rong byams chen gyi btsun pa
de slog pas rigs rgyud spel dgos tshul gnang ba dgongs pa nan zhus mdzad par/ sde srid nas bla ma'i dbu tshugs la ang / khyed rnams rigs rgyud gzhan dang ma 'dra bas rigs
rgyud de chad na mi 'ong bar 'dug bsam pa yin zhes gsungs shing / khrol cha ma gnang bar brten/ dbon mkhyen rab rnam rgyal la slar yang srid skyong gi thugs 'gan bzhes dgos
shar zhing / rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa lnga pa chen po'i zhabs 'bring du bzhugs/ gong du'ang mi snar lan 'ga' zhig pheb/ bka' 'bum rnams la bris zhus mdzad pas
mtshon zhabs 'gyur la mkho ba bcas/ zab rgyas kyi gdams pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / lha ldan du karma shag chen gyi sa ris 'dzin bdag mdzad pa sogs lugs gnyis ka'i sgo
nas bka'

drin chen pos bskyangs shing / lhag don thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid stsal bas nyams rtogs 'khrungs pa sogs kyi bsngags brjod dang bcas khyim pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa kho nar
nges shes rnyed pa'i thugs mthong mdzad/ rang gi mes po rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan dang / rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen
pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ zur khyab bdag chos dbyings rang grol/ zhwa lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rig 'dzin chen po kun bzang padma phrin
las/ bco brgyad chos rje mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub sogs grub mtha' ris su ma chad pa'i yongs 'dzin rnams las zab rgyas kyi gdams pa rgya cher gsan zhing
nyams bzhes la brtson par mdzad/ lan cig skyid smad phyogs nas po ta lar pheb skabs shig dpon g.yog rnams kyi thad du thog babs pa phaT sgra dang bcas sdigs mdzub kyis
bzlog par mdzad cing de'i gnas tshul rim gyis snyan du son pas gong zhabs rin po ches 'a zhwa thog rdugs ma zhes thugs gtsigs che/ lhag par zur kun mkhyen chos dbyings rang
grol la zhang bka' rgya'i skor yongs su rdzogs par gsan pa las brgyud de/ chos rgyal gter bdag gling pas gsan zhing / de las rgya cher 'phel ba deng sang gi bar du ma
nyams par bzhugs pas g.yu brag 'gro ba'i mgon po'i rjes su 'jug pa rnams dad pa'i nyi gzhon gyis bskyod pa'i lag pa'i kun da zum par rigs/ de ltar khyim pa'i rdo rje 'dzin
pa chen po de nyid kyi khab tu tshong 'dus dpon sa dang / lha ldan karma shag chen gyi dpon sa 'bal yag gnyis bzhes pa las/ dang po la/

sras nam mkha' bsod nams dbang rgyal dang / sras mo gcig bcas 'khrungs/ phyi ma la sras kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / zhabs drung nam mkha' don grub rgyal po/ sras
mo gcig bcas 'khrungs pa'i/ gcen nam mkha' bsod nams dbang rgyal ni dge slong nam mkha'i snying po'i sprul par grags/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs ngag dbang blo
bzang rgya mtsho'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa bzhes shing / slar bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i mtshan ngag dbang blo gsal mchog ldan du gsol/ gzhan yang gsang sngags gsar rnying
gi dge ba'i gshes gnyen du ma bsten cing / khyad par kun mkhyen lnga pa chen po dang / zhwa lu mkhan rin po che rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi bka' drin las/ gsung
ngag slob bshad lung phyag bzhes dang bcas pa/ dmar po skor gsum/ mkha' spyod skor gsum/ bstan srung skor phra zhib dang bcas pa sogs gsang chen kha'u brag rdzong pa'i
yab chos rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan zhing / bka' brgyad sogs gsang chen rnying ma'i chos skor yang rgya che ba gsan/ bsnyen sgrub yun ring mdzad pas nyams rtogs
kyi myu gu gong 'phel du 'khrungs/ bkra shis chos sde'i mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gi seng khrir zhabs sen bkod de/ gdul bya'i mos blo dang 'tshams pa'i chos kyi 'khor
lo bskor zhing / bkra shis chos sde'i bla ma lha khang la gsar bzo dang mtshungs pa'i zhig gso phun sum tshogs par mdzad/ skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen gzigs ngag dbang blo
bzang rgya mtshos chos srid kyi bka' drin mngon par lci bas bskyangs te/ gnas gsar dbon rin po che zhes bkur sti

bla na med pas gzengs bstod de slob bshad bstan pa'i srog gzung bar dgongs kyang / dus kyi skal bas mi ring bar nyang stod gnas gsar rgyal khang bla brang du ngo mtshar ba'i
ltas dang bcas te dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i thugs kar thim/ gcung kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan ni thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi rnam 'phrul du grags/
thugs mkhyen rab phul du phyin pas shes bya kun la mkhas shing / thugs rgyud zhi zhing dul/ rig 'dzin chen po padma phrin las dang / mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun
grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po sogs mkhas grub dam pa mang du bsten nas gsung ngag slob bshad/ mkha' spyod skor gsum/ dus kyi 'khor lo/ chos srung skor sogs chos
bka' bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan cing / thugs nyams su bzhes pas nyams rtogs tshad med par 'khrungs/ rig 'dzin chen po padma phrin las kyi drung du bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i
sdom pa bzhes/ gsang chen bstan pa'i 'byung gnas bkra shis chos kyi sde chen po'i mkhan por mnga' gsol/ bla ma lha khang gi shing rtsi dang / ldebs ris su lam 'bras dang
/ mgon po gnyis kyi bla brgyud/ chog mang sgrub mchod kyi dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo rnams dang / gzhan yang 'dod lha mang ba bcas bzhengs par mdzad cing / gcen ngag dbang
blo gsal mchog ldan gyi gdung rten gser sbyangs kyi pa tra 'od kor sogs kyis mdzes shing / dngul las grub pa'i rin po che du ma'i rgyan gyis phyug pa/ byang chub chen po'i
mchod rten bzo bkod phun sum tshogs pa/ 'dra sku rin po che dang bcas pa sgrub par mdzad

dngul gdung rin po che 'di'i gzungs gzhug la ston pa'i 'phel gdung 'khrul med dang / rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po'i sku chos tshang ma sogs gnas gsar pa'i nang rten thugs
gtsigs can du ma bzhugs/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la 'gran zla dang bral zhing gsang chen bstan pa'i srog shing chen por bzhugs pa las/ bstan pa rin po che'i gegs chag bzlog
tu med pas sa pho byi ba'i lo bkra shis chos kyi sde chen po'i gnas su zhag bdun gyi bar du thugs dam la bzhugs pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas
te mkha' spyod du gshegs/ rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po gdan drangs te/ sku gdung rin po che zhugs la 'bul ba dang / 'dra sku bzhengs pa sogs dgongs rdzogs rnams zhabs drung
nam mkha' don grub rgyal po dang / lcam sring ma rje btsun drung sogs nas bsgrub par mdzad/ lcam sring ma gcig gra nang khul sger sgang nas kyi srid 'dzin du byon/ rje
btsun ma kun dga' tshul khrims drung ni thugs mkhyen dpyod nam mkha' ltar yangs pa/ yab mes kyi bka' srung mchod pa sogs thugs dam la brtson pa snying stobs dang ldan
pas/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang blo gsal mchog ldan dag zhing du gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs rnams kyang phal cher 'di nyid kyis thugs 'gan bzhes te mdzad/ khyab bdag mgon po
bsod nams mchog ldan gyi thugs dam gzigs dpe rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che khyad 'phags byin can sogs grwa tshang du'ang sbyor 'jags rgya cher mdzad/ chos pa bzang por
rlom pa rnams kyang 'di'i drung duu bag zhum par 'gyur ba zhig yod snang / dgung lo'ang brgyad cu lhag par bzhugs so/ /de'ang gnas

gsar gyi zhal ngo rnams nas rtsis gnas gsar 'dzin bzhin gyi thog /bo dong / myu gu lung sogs su 'pho skyas dang / 'a zhwa mkhyen rab rnam rgyal la zhabs bzhugs kyi bzhugs 'tsher
lta bur lha ldan karma shag chen sa ris phran bu dang bcas pa gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen pos gsol ras su stsal yang / karma shag gi lcam des mdzad spyod mkhas
min la brten/ sde srid sangs rgyas rgya mtshos gzhung bzhes mdzad par/ slar yang yar klung zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis zhus ngor 'a zhwa
nam mkha' don grub sku na phra mo der 'phyang rgyas 'phreng smad rta drung gi sa zhig dang / yum dang lcam chung mar yar 'da' lding dpon smon mkhar pa'i sa cha gsol skal
du stsal zhing / gnas gsar sogs kyang phyir slog 'ong ba'i bka' bzhes mdzad mur bod sog 'dzings pas de don ma grub par/ rgyal bu nam mkha' don grub zhabs bzhugs thog
nas shong rgya mtsho'i 'ong sdud dang / yar klung ge ra'i sku mag sogs mdzad pa'i 'a zhwa nam mkha' don grub rgyal po'am/ zhabs drung o rgyan sgrol sgron du grags pa de ni
dpa' zhing brtul phod pa/ sgyu rtsal dang ldan ba/ rang bzhin bzang zhing mdzangs pa/ khrel ngo tsha dang gzhung phyi thag ring ba/ yi ge dang rtsis kyi rig byed la mngon
par byang chub pa/ ri mo la sogs pa bzo'i rig byed la'ang yun ring du sbyangs pa ltar mkhas pa/ lha dang bla ma dang grub pa'i mtha' la gus shing mchod pa dang / yon sbyor
ba la snying stobs kyi go cha brtan pa/ yi dam gyi bzlas brjod dang / yab mes kyi sku la mchod pa la brtson pa sogs rigs rgyud snga ma'i rjes su 'brang ba kho na'i spyod
tshul bzang po lhur bzhes

pa/ lugs gnyis kyi 'byor pas mngon par brgyan pa 'di ni bdag cag gi rnam par 'dren pa 'di'i yab yin lags/ cho 'brang ngam zhang rigs ni/ phyi dar bstan pa'i srol 'byed dam
pa glan ye shes 'bar dang / ye shes byang chub la sogs pa dang / gsang chen rdzogs pa chen po'i bstan pa'i srog 'dzin pa/ lha rje zur chung ba'i dngos slob/ glan shAkya bzang
po/ glan shAkya byang chub sogs dang / gzhan yang rgyal ba g.yung sten dang / glan bsod nams mgon po/ glan rtsod tsha nyi ma lcam sogs skyes chen dam pa du ma byung
ba'i gdung rus gsang chen rnying ma'i grub mtha' 'dzin pa'i sngags rgyud glan ljongs ldan ma'i brgyud pa dang / de las gyes pa khar kha 'phir byung gi brgyud pa sogs mang
du byung ba'i/ khar kha 'phir byung gi rgyud phun tshogs sgrol ma zhes g.yo sgyu med pa'i rang bzhin bzang ba/ bla ma dang chos la mos shing / las 'bras la zhib mor spyod
pa/ yo byad la mngon zhen chung bas mchod sbyin la brtson pa/ gzugs dang lang tshos spras pa/ bud med rin po che'i yon tan phal cher rdzogs pa de ni bdag nyid chen po 'di'i
yum yin cing / gong du bshad pa'i yab de nyid dgung lo nyer gcig gi thog gzhung zhabs rin po che'i shangs khul gyi yongs bzhes su pheb cing / de skabs rgyal yum 'di
nyid kyang dgung lo nyer gcig son pa ste/ de'ang yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che dang / bye brag rje btsun sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud bstan pa zab mo'i srog shing bdag chen
chos kyi rgyal po rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bltams pa nas bzung lo grangs nyis brgya re gcig pa rab nyi'i nang gi legs sbyar saM skr-i ta'i skad
du bhA nu tA ra/ stod

'grel las nyi sgrol byed/ tsi ni'i skad du gya shin/ dbang thang dang bstun pa'i shing pho spre'u'i lo/ /'byung ba sum ldan/ kha ral/ bkra shis kyi klung / pho brang gling
dgur yul lha'i me long gnas pa'i lo/ /bdag cag gi ston pa mnyam med shAkya'i rgyal pos mu stegs tshar bcad pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul du ma bstan pa'i dus bzang /
rta zla'i nang du yum gyi lhums su zhugs ma thag nas yum gyi sku'i zo mdog bzang zhing / thugs la sngar med pa'i dga' bde khyad par can 'khrungs pa dang / mnal lam bzang
po kho na byung tshod du 'dug kyang / de skabs su thugs 'dzin dang zin bris ma thub pas 'dir gsal bar bkod ma nus/ de ltar mngal gyi zla ba yongs su rdzogs nas/ lo de'i
nus ldan gyi dus/ rta bdun dbang po gzhu khyim du spyod pa'i skabs/ smal po zla ba ste/ sngon gyi dus 'jam dbyangs kyi rnam sprul slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo dang
/ chos rje khu dbon/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po dang thugs rgyud gcig pa'i 'jam mgon a mes zhabs sogs mkhas grub kyi skyes bu du mas zung 'jug gi go 'phang mngon
du mdzad de byin gyis brlabs pa'i dus chen rnams dang 'dab 'byor/ dmar phyogs rdzogs pa gnyis pa ste/ tshes nyer lnga/ dus 'khor ba'i dbyangs A: gsal byed pa/ 'byung ba
nam mkha'/ 'dod yon sgra/ dbyangs 'char rgyud las gsungs pa'i dbyangs au/ gsal byed Tha/ 'byung ba nam mkha'/ 'dod yon sgra/ dar gud smin pa/ res gza' nam mkha'i tog gam
bcu gnyis bdag po/ yang dag pa'i lam las drangs pas dar ba/

las skar bya ma'am me bzhi dang dgyes rgur rtse ba'i 'chi med grub pa'i sbyor ba'i dus/ sbyor chung stobs ldan/ sbyor ba 'phrod chen/ yid la dpal thob sbyor ba/ skal ba phun
tshogs/ byed pa biShti/ rten 'brel ming gzugs/ nyi ma me stag /spar kha li/ sme ba bdun dmar/ dus tshod tho rengs lcags stag /dus spar khen/ dus sme dgu smug /dus sbyor
byed pa'i gza' dkar po/ tarkal sdig khyim ste/ dgug pa'i las 'grub pa'i dus tshes bzang por padma 'dam las skyes kyang 'dam gyis ma gos pa bzhin du ngo mtshar ba'i ltas
du ma dang bcas te sku bltams ma thag rigs dang yul gyi lha mchod pa la sogs pa dga' ston rgya cher mdzad cing / mtshan bsod nams dpal 'byor du gsol lo/ /rnam 'dren dam pa
'di nyid kyi sku mched kyi gras ge re'i lcam la sras mo nor 'dzom rgyal mo dang / bsod nams 'phrod skyid/ de 'og tu lcam chung gnyis bcas byung ba las/ sngon ma gnyis rtsis
dpon nor 'dzin dbang po'i lcam mdzad/ de 'og gra sdum por byon kyang sku na phra mor gshegs/ de 'og yar lung bkra shis mthong smon du byon pa'ang gshegs nas/ da lta
sku mched kyi gras bsod nams 'phrod skyid bzhugs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ 'dzam gling yul dbus gangs can g.yas ru'i char/ /lha rigs 'a zhwa'i rgyal blon mkhas grub gdung
/ /glan gyi cho 'brang gis mdzes dge ltas bcas/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma'i 'khrungs tshul yin/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa la rgyal sras gzhon nu'i dus thos bsam gyi sgo nas
yab mes kyi chos la gsan sbyangs ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ rgyal tshab dam par mnga' gsol te mchog gi bla

ma dam pas snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa'i bdag por dgongs gtad ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i 'byung gnas bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pas thugs rgyud
yongs su gtams shing / lhag pa'i lha'i grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin pa'i tshul/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten pa kun gyi skyabs mgon dam par gyur nas yongs
rdzogs bstan pa'i rgyal srid la dbang bsgyur zhing / rgyal bstan ji ltar spel ba'i tshul/ bstan 'dzin gyi slob bu'i tshogs bgrang ba las 'das pa zhig bskrun te 'khor
ba ji srid bar phrin las kyi rgyun legs par spel ba'i tshul bshad pa dang lnga yod pa las/ dang po ni/ gang gi sku bstod grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtshos mdzad pa las/
sku mdzes pa mtshan dpe kun ldan zhing / gsung zab rgyas chos kyi dgaX' ston 'gyed/ thugs leXgs paX'i lhag bsam 'byungaX ba'i gnaXs/ rje gnas gsar chos rje zhes gsungs pa
ltar/ de ltar 'khrungs pa'i gzhon nu de ni sku blta bas chog mi shes pa/ dbu gdugs ltar zlum pa/ dpral ba'i dbyes che zhing shangs gzengs mtho ba sogs mtshan dpe rjes mthun
pas spras shing / kun spyod mtha' dag byis pa phal gyi ngang tshul las 'das pa/ legs sbyar gyi skad lta bu'i gsung mi go ba shin tu mang ba/ spyan nam mkha' la gzigs
nas yun ring bzhugs pa/ ljags kyi steng na yi ge a'i gzugs shin tu gsal bas khengs pa/ skabs 'gar 'bar 'bur tsam las mi gsal ba/ gsung bye ba tsam nas dbus skad shin tu
gsal ba lan kha yar gsung ba zhig yod ces yum mchog dbang mos gsungs/ dgung lo gsum bzhi tsam nas sngags

'chang gos dkar can shin tu bag dro ba zhig gis byin rlabs mdzad pa dran te/ su yin mi shes zhes rje nyid kyis gsungs/ dgung lo lnga pa kun 'dzin zhes pa sa pho byi ba'i lo/
/yul du 'brum yams shig byung bar rim gyis mched nas/ yum sras gnyis kas 'brum nad bzhes kyang shin tu yang bas yun mi ring bar dwangs/ yul pa'i 'brum yams kyang chad pas
zhabs drung chung ngu 'dis 'brum nad bzhes pas yul pa'i 'brum nad chad ces yul de'i rgan rabs rnams kyis smras par grags/ gzhan yang de lta'i skabs shig gzhon nu 'di'i
sku'i phyal yul mi bde ba zhig yod par yum sogs kyis dpal chen bos te/ dam can rdo rje legs pa khog zhugs kyi lung bstan zhus par/ gzhon nu de nga'i gam du khrid shog zer
ba dang / de bzhin mdzad pas sku phyal mtshon gyis dpral ba'i rma kha nas bsnyun gzhi thams cad chos skyong des za ba'i tshul byas te/ de nas slar yang na za' bsgron skabs
gsol phyu'i thu sne nang ma bltabs tshar ba dang / chos skyong de'i lag par thal ba bskus nas sbar rjes shin tu gsal ba zhig sku phyal gyi rma thad gsol phyu'i steng
du brgyabs/ de'i phyir thu sne phyi ma bltabs tshar ba dang sku rags bcings shing lung bstan mang du zhus te/ rma'i rjes mi mngon pa zhig byung zhes kho bo la sa skyar bka'
chos gnang skabs gsungs pa 'di ni bstan srung dam can rgya mtshos sku dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs te dngos brgyud kyi sgo nas zhabs tog phrin las gang dgos 'phral du bsgrubs
pa'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar can du snang zhing / sa pho byi ba'i lo 'jam mgon kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pas bkra shis chos sde'i
mkhan po

gnas gsar gyi dbon bzhugs chog pa zhig med stabs/ chos sde'i grwa slob bla zhen can rnams nas mgon 'di'i yab rgyal po la/ khyed rang la sras 'dra yod na yed tsho'i bla mar
spyan 'dren rgyu dang / de min khyed rang rab byung mdzad nas chos sde'i mkhan po mdzad dgos gsol zhing / de skabs su gzhung zhabs rin po che nas gnas gsar bar sras chung
zhig yod 'dra'ang sku na phra ba'i stabs kyis mkhan 'os su ma shar zhing / de bar la mkhan po'i 'os tho gyis gsungs par/ chos sde nas gzhan tshe'i bla ma nam mkhar 'phul
'gro ba zhig las/ gnas gsar ba'i sras rdor dril 'dzin shes tsam zhig nged tshor dga' bas/ gnas gsar ba rang bla mar zhus chog pa'i snyan sbron dang bcas dbu tshugs shin
tu che bar mdzad cing / yab rgyal por yang khyed kyi sras de gar bzhugs zhus par gtsang gi shongs phyogs na yod tshul gsungs pas rtsad chod de/ bkra shis chos sder chung
ngu nas spyan drangs pa yin zhes dngos su gsung las thos pa bzhin/ gsang chen slob bshad kyi chos grwa chen por bkra shis chos sde'i grwa dmangs bgres song rnams dang / zhabs
drung yab la sogs pa bka' bgros te/ skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid gdan 'dren pa'i sgo dod/ bkra shis chos sde'i grwa bgres mdo sngags rgya mtsho dang / ge ra'i zhabs phyi
don ldan gnyis kyis gtsang du bskyod de/ zhabs drung gzhon nu dbus su gdan 'dren mdzad rgyu'i rgyu mtshan zhus shing lam tsam dus bsgrigs te dbus su log /zhabs drung
sku na phra gshis re zhig par rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen por mkhan po gnang dgos tshul gyi zhu ba nan tan mdzad pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes te/ sa glang zla ba bcu gcig pa'i
tshes

bco lngar mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu blo gros nyid rang bstan gyi srog 'dzin pa'i thugs bskyed rma med pas bsam bzhin du byon pa rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid
'dus tshogs rgya mtshos bsnyen bkur dang bcas te zhabs zung seng ge'i khri la mngon par bkod/ ge ra chos mdzad bsod nams snang byed dang / ge ra'i gnyer pa phag skyag
sogs kyis gtsang nas yum sras gnyis gdan drangs te/ rim par nyang gzhung dang yar 'brog brgyud de/ 'gal ba zhes pa sa mo glang gi lo zla ba lnga pa'i nang du/ bkra shis dang
dge mtshan du mas mngon par spud pa'i gnas gsang chen zab mo'i chos sgra rgyun mi 'chad par sgrogs pa'i bkra shis chos kyi sde chen por zhabs sen gyi padmo rnam par bkod
pa na/ snyan brgyud bstan pa'i nyi mas phan bde'i pad tshal rnam par bzhad pa'i dge mtshan rmad du byung ba'i skya rengs cir yang shar bas nag phyogs bdud sde'i smag
rum mtha' dag ba mor nyi zer rnon pos bran pa'i chab rom ltar 'gyur ba'i sgo yangs por dod do/ /de skabs dbus nas gdan 'dren pa byung ba'i tshe/ zhabs drung gzhon nu'i thugs
la nged 'gro ba'i chos sde de ji lta bu zhig yod dam dgongs pa na/ ri nag po rtswa dang shing gis gang ba/ logs su chu bo chen po dal gyis 'babs pa/ gtsug lag khang dang
dge 'dun gyi gnas khang rnams bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa/ sngar gzigs myong myong 'dra ba'i bza' shing gi rigs du ma yod pa de rnams 'di lta bu zhig yin dgongs pa las/
gsung gis 'di ni 'di'o zhes skabs dbye bar mi nus pa zhig thugs la gsal bar byung bar/ rjes su gzigs tshe gong dkar chos sde yin par 'dug /ces dam pa mchog gi bka'

las thos pa ni/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyi yang srid du zhal gyis bzhes pa la the tshom mi mnga' 'o/ /nyang stong gnas gsar du pheb tshe skya ser thams cad
kyis gus pas 'dud cing bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstar/ lhag par rgan mo zhig gis phyag rten du sman rtse zhig phul ba na thugs dgyes pa'i tshul gyis bzhes nas phyag dbang mdzad
pas/ rgan mo dad pa'i shugs kyis drangs ba'i mchi ma lhung ba ni/ yang srid gong ma'i bag chags su mngon/ de nas re zhig bar khe gsum chos mdzad lung rigs rgya mtshos
'tsho skyong gi zhabs tog mdzad de bkra shis chos sde'i zur lcog tu gtan chags/ de tshe 'jam zhing yang ba'i na bza' dang / ro mchog phun sum tshogs pa'i bza' ba dang bca'
bas mchod cing / nyin re bzhin rin chen zangs kyi yol gor chab rgyun grang dro snyoms pas bkang ste/ zhabs drung gzhon nu'i sku lus legs par bkrus/ ras gsar pa'i steng
du bzhugs su gsol nas/ rtswi mar gsar pa bzhu ba'i khu bas sku lus yongs su khyab par byug pa la sogs pa sku'i sri zhu la mngon par brtson par mdzad/ ces thos shing / gnas
kyi slob dpon bsod nams snang byed dang / bsod nams rin chen gnyis nas yon tan thams cad kyi gzhi mo yi ge 'bri klog dang / chos spyod kyi rim pa sogs 'bul bar mdzad
pa'i tshe/ ji skad du/ chos kyi ma mo ma bslabs thugs su chud/ /ces pa ltar/ 'bri klog la sogs pa'ang brda bstan pa tsam gyis thugs su chud cing byang bar gyur te/ chos spyod
kyi rigs rnams kyang lan re zung re tsam gyis thugs la 'drongs pas dka' ba ci'ang med par mkhyen cing / lcags yos zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du/ 'phags yul paN grub dbang
po kun gyi

gtsug gi nor bu/ mdo rgyud spyi dang / khyad par yo ga'i srol 'byed chen po rgyal yum tshe sbyin dbang mos mngon sum du byin gyis brlabs pa'i grub pa'i gtsug rgyan dam pa slob
dpon kun dga' snying po de nyid kyi 'phags bod kun tu rnam par 'phrul pa du mas bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad cing / khyad par ljongs 'dir rgyal bstan spyi dang /
bye brag kha'u brag rdzong pa'i lugs bzang dri ma med pa de nyid gsal bar mdzad phyir bsam bzhin du sprul pa'i gar gyi rnam par rol pa/ rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs kyi padmo la gus pas btud cing / yang srid du mar bla slob tu gyur pa'i thugs kyi bag chags mngon par
sad pas sngar 'dris kyi mdza' bo phrad pa ltar bla slob thugs yid gcig tu 'dres shing / ston dang bstan pa gzhan nas mi 'tshol ba'i thugs kyi dgongs pa khyad par can 'khrungs
par gdon mi za la/ 'di skabs rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chos sder bzhugs zhag bco lnga tsam bzhugs kyang bka' chos gnang tshul rmor chen rnam thar na mi gsal/ de lo
grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan 'bul ba dang lhan du lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ de skabs pad dkar 'dzin pa ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho rgyal ba mdzad pas de'i drung du gtsug
phud 'bul bar mdzad/ mtshan ngag dbang sbyin pa zhes gsol/ de nas chos sder phyags pheb/ 'di skabs khe gsum chos mdzad lha ldan du dus las yol bas/ zhabs 'bring pa dge slong
blo gros ye shes kyis bgyis shing / de lo nas bkra shis chos sde bla brang gi phyag mdzod dang gnyer pa sgo bstun gyis bsnyen bkur la brtson par byas/ dge slong blo gros
ye shes kyang lung rtogs kyi yon tan

dang / phyag rdzas gnyis ka ha cang che ba med rung / bla ma gong ma'i byin rlabs rgyud la zhugs pas thugs dam chos spyod 'phel zhing / rje nyid la lhag par gus pa dang / sku'i
sri zhu la brtson par yod 'dug pas/ dus phyi'i kyang dge rgan blo gros ye shes zhes thugs gtsigs che bar mdzad pa ni/ byas pa shes shing byas pa gzo/ /zhes pa ltar/
byas pa drin gzo rgyal sras byang chub sems dpa'i ngang tshul bla na med pa'o/ /de nas bong bu zhes pa lcags mo yos kyi lo/ /gsang chen smra ba'i chos gra chen po bkra shis
chos sde'i gtsug lag khang du rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung du khyim pa'i rtags cha lugs rnams mchil ma'i thal ba bzhin du 'dor bar mdzad nas/ bstan pa rin
po che'i sgor pheb pa'i thog mar skyabs gsum 'dzin pa'i dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa yang dag par bzhes te mtshan kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas zhes stsal/ lo de'i mgo zla'i nang
du rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi spyan sngar tshar chen rdo rje 'chang rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa'i bzhed srol ltar dkar lha gsum gyi chos kyi sgo phye ste gsang chen kha'u
brag rdzong pa'i zab chos srung ba'i 'khor lo rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi khrid kyis mtshon pa'i zab chos rgya cher gsan/ gzhan yang gong du bshad
pa'i rnam thar zhal gsung ma de nyid las/ zlog med dad dang snying rje'i nor gyis phyug /thos bsam rtogs pa'i shes rab mi dman pas/ /sdom gsum rin thang bral ba'i rin chen
mchog /dri med rgyan gyi phreng bas mdzes la 'dud/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ dga' ba zhes pa chu 'brug dgung lo dgu pa'i steng du skyabs mgon rmor

chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi drung nas paN grub dbang po a bhA ya kA ra'i bzhed gzhung rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis/ grub pa'i dbang phyug darpan a tsArYa'i
bzhed srol kr-i ya sa muu nytse'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum dang bcas pa'i dbang rnams yongs su rdzogs pa/ dbu ma lugs dang / sems tsam lugs kyi sems
bskyed sogs/ zab chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan/ chu 'brug hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang du dbu btsugs te/ 'phags yul paN grub kun gyi gtsug rgyan/ grub dbang rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gi bzhed gzhung / bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa rnams kyi yab chos/ mdo rgyud thams cad kyi nying khu/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas
