pa'i dbang khrid/ lung man ngag dang bcas pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa'i phyag srol las ji ltar byung ba bzhin du rgyas par gsan
te/ paN chen klu sgrub rgya mtshos/ tshogs par bshad pa'i drang don za zi'i gtam/ /rnam par spangs nas slob bu mchog dag la/ /gces pa gdams pa nges don snying po'i bcud/
/zab mo'i slob bshad 'khyongs bar byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don mngon du gyur te/ chu sbrul gyi mjug dang shing rta'i lo mgo rnams la rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po
de nyid kyis mkhan slob sbrags ma dang / 'dul 'dzin blo gros ye shes dang / tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis zhabs phyi zhus te dgung grangs bcu gcig par tshig snga
ma dge tshul gyi sdom pas thugs kyi bum bzang yongs su gtams par mdzad cing / gzhan yang gsang ba 'dus pa'i smar

khrid/ gshed dmar skor zab cing thugs gtsigs che ba'i dbang khrid lung sogs shin tu mang bar gsan/ 'di skabs li'u thang gi khams btsun ngag dbang legs bshad zer ba zhig gis
gcod yul skor zhus pa'ang lhan cig tu gsan/ chos mtshams gung seng skabs sku rtsed kyi rnam pas/ bla brang steng na grwa gzhon 'ga' zhig la gcod khrid kyi dmigs pa 'phogs
pa'i tshul mdzad pa na tshig zur tsam yang ma nyams par byung bas/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gis gsan pas thugs lhag par mnyes/ byis pa rnams kyis byi'u dang byi ba sogs
bzung nas srog bslu zhus nas skur mnabs pa'i na bza' sogs kyang srog bslu'i yon du ster bar mdzad/ lan cig byis pa zhig gis ske rags slong mo zhus par/ zhabs drung gzhon
nu nyid kyi sku rags gser sked de gnang bar/ dge rgan gyis rtsad gcod zhus pas sngon du cang mi gsung zhing / rjes su slong mo bar ster dgos byung bas bya thabs ma rnyed
ces gsung ba sogs mdor na bdag bas gzhan gces kyi thugs bskyed rlabs po che de lta bu ni/ sbyor ba'i sngon du snying rje dang / /zhes sogs ltar/ gzhan rkyen la mi ltos par
rang chas su yod pas/ tha na khab skud tsam gyis mtshon pa'i dngos po che phra ci yin yang zhuu mkhan byung na de 'phral gnang / dge rgan sogs kyis rtsad gcod zhus na
lan ci'ang mi gsung ba sogs la 'di ltar gnang tshe mgo mi 'thon zhes zom po'i skur 'debs dang / skabs 'gar ha cang rgod drags pas/ 'di ni mtha' gnyis su 'gyur zhes kun gsal
yangs pa'i tha grur byis blo'i sbar tshod 'debs mkhan 'dra'ang byung bar grags pa ni shes bya lkog tu gyur pa dag gi khyad par gyi chos yang dag pa'o/

/gzhan yang gsang chen 'dus sde 'di nyid na bzhugs pa'i dbyangs rol gar sogs phyag len rnam par dag pa rnams/ chos mdzad gzhon du rgyal mtshan dang / bsod nams skal bzang las
dka' tshegs med par gsan cing / chos sder bzhugs pa'i 'chams kyi rigs ni gzigs yul du shar ba tsam gyis bde blag tu mkhyen no/ /skabs 'di dag tu srung mdud zhu ba kun
la phyag mdud dang / de la ljags mchil bran tsam gnang bas chu btags 'ur ba zhes drag tu 'khor ba de 'drar yang btags tsam nyid nas skad snyan par 'byin cing 'khor dal ba
sogs byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma mngon sum 'phral du mthong zhing / srung mdud kho nas 'gro phan kyang bsam gyis mi khyab/ deng sang ni gnod bya gnod byed kun la phan sems
bskyed de byas kyang phan gnod cher med pa 'dra zhig 'dug ces rjes sor bka' las thos/ shing lug lor rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang yongs su rdzogs pa bskyar chos su gsan zhing
/ gzhan yang rgyal yum rdo rje btsun mos grub chen nA ro ta pa chen po la dngos su gdams pa'i snyan brgyud gser chos zab mo rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i chos skor phra
zhib dang bcas pa/ dmar po skor gsum gyi skor dang / mgon pod kha skong dang / bka' gdams gzhung drug sogs lung gi rigs du ma dang / phyag drug mgon bka' bcu gsum gyi
rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang gi rigs shin tu mang ba gsan/ 'di skabs phrin las kyis 'gro don mdzad pa'i dus su ma babs pas/ na bza' skor dang 'tsho ba rang 'grigs tsam gyi
tshul bzhes stabs/ chos yon kyang gser dngul sogs kyi dngos po rin thang can ni 'bul ba gnang rgyu byung tshod du mi gda'/ 'on kyang bsngo rten 'bul

mkhan phran tshegs byung ba'i dngos po rnams kyi ras dang la tha sogs legs pa rnams phyogs gcig tu mdzad de/ rig 'dzin chen po kun bzang padma phrin las mjal skabs 'bul rgyu
yin zhes shin tu gces spras kyis sba bar mdzad/ de phyin gyis phyag rdzas tshang ma rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi phyag tu ci 'byor mdzad/ lan gcig rmor chen
rdo rje 'chang chen po rmor dgon du chibs bsgyur gnang skabs zhig zhabs drung sku na phra mo des/ kho bo rdo rje brag tu 'khrid grogs mdzod ces spyan chab kyis brnangs pa
ltar bshum pas/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ da lam zhabs drung gi na bza' yang ngan pa dang / nged tsho'i rta drel gyis kyang lcogs pa med pas/ slad mar na bza' legs par
bzos te gdan 'dren zhu zhes gnang bas dbugs phyung / rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po rdo rje brag tu pheb skabs rig 'dzin chen pos bkra shis chos sde'i zhabs drung chung ngu
de sku khams bde bar bzhugs sam/ zhes sogs thugs brtse'i sgo nas bka' 'dri mdzad tshe/ gong gi gnas tshul rnams zhu bar mdzad pas/ rig 'dzin chen po yang spyan chab yun
ring mdzad de/ zhabs drung de khyed kyis gdan 'dren zhus nas mi pheb pa zhes thugs mi mnyes pa'i rnam pa mdzad pa sogs ni/ mngon pa kun btus las/ dran pa gang zhe na 'dris
pa'i dngos po la sems kyis ma brjed pa'o/ /zhes pa ltar bla slob gnyis kar yang sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa zhes pa'i zag med kyi mngon shes de mnga' ba'i dge mtshan
yang dag pa'o snyam/ de skabs zhabs drung yab nas bzhes spro glang po che la nor bu bkal ba'i dbyibs can lo gsar

gyi legs 'bul gras su 'bul ba gnang bar zhabs drung gzhon nu thugs shin tu mnyes pas thugs gtsigs che bar mdzad pa/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gzims chung du bzhugs pa la steng
gi rgya mthongs nas gzigs 'bul mdzad de/ sku zhabs 'di la dges sam/ zhes zhu bar mdzad pas kho bo shin tu dga' gsungs pas/ de ltar na 'di 'bul zhes gsungs par/ des na
khyed rang la mi 'ong gsungs pas/ sku zhabs mnyes na nga la med kyang rung zhes/ de ma thag tu 'bul bar mdzad pas/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas kyang rab tu dgyes pa'i tshul
mdzad pas thugs blo shin tu bde bas deng sang brgya 'bul mdzad pa las kyang thugs tshim pa zhig byung ba/ dbang bzhi'i ngo sprod la/ gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa la/
/rten 'brel gnad du che bar bzhed/ /ces pa ltar/ rten 'brel gyi gnad la shin tu phan pa byung zhes phyis gsungs pa dang / rmor chen chos kyi rgyal pos kyang / rten 'brel
gyi gnad 'di col chung du snang yang 'bras bu che bas 'di la skur pa gdab tu mi rung bar gda' zhes yang yang gsungs par snang / me sprel lor grwa rigs blo ngan can rang 'dod
phugs su bcug pa sde dgon gyis zhabs 'debs dang / lar rgya zhes sogs ming snyan por btags te/ don du dam sel gyi sbyor ba rtsom mkhan re gnyis kyis thabs ngan g.yo 'phrul
sna tshogs la brten pa'i rkyen dbang las/ er khe dA'i tshing la mgo btags pa'i tsha bo rme ru a mchod zer bas/ bla brang tsha len byas te lo gcig tsam bzung bas lugs
gnyis ka nas phyi nang gi la rgyar phan pa lta ci/ kun spyod ngan pa kho nas kyang grwa tshang gi mig ltas la gnod tshab che bas sde dgon nyams gud du 'gro ba'i sgo dod
pa/ rig 'dzin chen po

kun bzang padma phrin las sogs/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i ring lugs dri ma med pa thugs dkyil du bcangs pa'i bla dpon gyi thugs kyis ma bzod pas rmor chen rdo rje 'chang
la/ da cha khyed kyis tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi bstan pa dang / sde dgon gyi la rgyar dgongs te dgon pa tshur len pa'i thabs gnang dgos tshul gsungs pa bzhin/ rmor
chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos kyang / de don kho na thugs la bcangs te/ rgyal po lha bzang la chos sde 'di nyid lo dus kyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod dang / cho ga phyag len
gang ci gzhan dang mi 'dra ba sogs kyi rgyu mtshan phra zhib zhu bar mdzad pas/ rgyal po'ang thugs nges pa 'drongs te/ dgon pa 'phral du rtsis sprod dgos tshul gyi bka' rgya
gnang zhing / de don bzhin gser 'phyang zhes pa me bya lor tsha bo rme ru a mchod zer ba'i lag nas rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gis rtsis bzhes mdzad de/ dgon gnas nyams
par sor chud kyang / mngon pa nas zang zing med pa'i tshor ba sdug bsngal du gsungs pa dang / bdag cag gi ston pa'i zhabs la seng ldeng gi tshal bu zug pa dang tshul mthun
par mi 'gyang bar dus 'gyur gyi dbang gis rmor chen rdo rje 'chang la 'o brgyal sna tshogs byung ba/ de nas grol te chos sder phebs skabs chibs su ser sbreng sogs dus gnas
dang bstun na legs pas mi dgos gsungs te chos sder pheb thog /tshogs mang nas sgrol dkar la brten pa'i zhabs brtan legs po zab rgyas dang / spyi sos rmor chen rje la
dus 'gyur skabs zhabs 'gyur dpe med zhus pa'i dge slong nam rgyal la drin gzo'i gos chen gyi snam sbyar zhig bstabs/ de nas ma 'gyangs par rmor chen rjes chos sde'i

gdan sa dgongs zhu mdzad de tshogs dbus su bstan pa spyi dang / bye brag tshar chen yab sras kyi bstan pa thams cad kyi thugs khur yang dag dgos pa'i zhal ta bzang pos nan
tan stsal te/ chos dang zang zing gi sbyin pas phan bde'i dpal la sbyar/ gong du bshad pa ltar gcod khrid de gsan skabs tsam la yin nam/ gang ltar yang / gzhon nu dus la
lar sa srib tsam nas chos sde'i ltag gi dur khrod der byon te gcod skor nyams bzhes mdzad cing / de na btsan gnas pa'i shing sdong gnyen po zhig yod pa de'i yal ga bcag ste
bzhugs gdan gyi 'og tu bcug nas 'tshubs 'gyur dang lhong zhig e 'ong snyam du dgongs kyang / ci'ang ma byung gsungs pa dang / slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas la
thugs dad shin tu che bas mtshan mo mnal la pheb khar rnam thar gsol 'debs chag med lta bur mdzad cing / bod yul nas srin yul du pheb tshul de gsungs pa'i tshe spyan chab
rang dbang med par byung zhing / thugs kyi khyer sor yang slob dpon chen po'i zhabs rjes su 'khril gyis pheb pa'i thugs snang dang bcas mnal mdzad pa kha shas byung gsungs
pa dang / gzims mal du mnal med pa'i skabs phal cher la'ang / thugs nyams la sku lus je che je cher song ste gzims chung gi nang khrigs gang nyams byed pa dang / thugs
snang de sad pa byung zhing / dgung grangs bco lnga tsam gyi bar la bar srid kyi snang ba de ma brjed pas/ skye srid tshor snang tur tur ba yang yang byung zhes gsungs
pa ni dgongs gzhi gzhan du gtad pa'i ldem po'i gsung kho na yin pa dpyod ldan dag gis gsung 'di nyid las 'khums shing / 'jam mgon a

mes zhabs sku gzhon nu gsung mkhyen tsam gyi thugs snang la/ yul phyogs kyi dbyibs kha'u'i chu tshan skor 'dra ba rgya gar gyi yul grong yin zer ba zhig 'dug pa/ de'i sgo nang
na yar 'byon dgongs nas cung zad byon pa na lce spyang 'dra ba'i sems can 'jigs su rung ba mjug ma ring la sbom po byas pa gnyis kyis pheb lam bgags nas ma btang ba'i
thugs snang shin tu gsal ba de la/ phyis gsung las/ kho bo rgya gar du skye ba len rgyu yin pa la ce spyang 'dra ba'i sems can mjug ma ring po byas pa gnyis kyis lam bgags
nas rgya gar phyogs la 'gro ma thub par log pa zhig dran gyin 'dug gsungs pa dang / cha 'dra bas skyes bu dam pa rnams thugs snang gcig pa'i ngo mtshar rtogs brjod kyi
gras dang / yang skabs shig tshas sder gnod pa'i gdug pa can zhig la ched gtad kyis zan gtor gru gsum chung ngu zhig bzhengs/ seng gdong ma'i ljags bzlas mdzad de dmigs
bya'i phyogs su 'phangs pas/ de'i dbyar byad ma de chus khyer nas tshe'i dus byas so/ /'di ni tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu'i tshe 'byung po zhig khyir brdzus nas mtho
'tshams pa na/ byis pa'i 'khor dang bcas gtor bzlog gi lad mo mdzad pas khyi de khrag skyugs nas shi ba dang chos mtshungs pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar du snang ngo
/ /'di dag gi don bsdu na/ skye 'gro'i rims srung gu rus byin gyis brlabs/ /srung mas las bsgrubs sngon gnas thugs la shar/ /gang gi gdan sar bslabs sbyangs tshegs med
mkhyen/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon gzhon nu'i rol rtsed yin/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa ni/ rnam thar gsol 'debs zhal gsung ma las/ tshe rabs

du mar dge ba'i bshes gnyen mchog /skyabs gnas kun 'dus rmor chen chos kyi rjes/ /gsung ngag chos kyi bang mdzod gnyer gtad pa'i/ /rgyal tshab sems dpa' mchog la snying nas
'dud/ /ces gsungs pa ltar rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid ni/ sku na phra'ang sku'i 'khrungs rabs mang por sbyangs pa'i 'bras bu 'gog tu med pa'i mthu las mkhyen pa'i cha shas
yongs su gang bas bstan pa'i khur chen 'degs par bzod pa'i stobs yongs su rdzogs pa dang / khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis kyang dgung lo bco
lnga'i steng du chos sde'i khri thog tu pheb pa dang dus kyang mtshungs pa sogs rgyu mtshan du mar gzigs te/ de'i phyi lo rnam 'phyang zhes pa sa khyi lor mkhan sa rtsis
sprod mdzad de/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling du chibs kyi kha lo bskyod/ de skabs skyabs mgon mchog gi zhabs drung du sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin
pa kun dga' dpal 'byor ba'i zhal snga nas kyis/ grwa rgan ne tso'i brtul zhugs la co 'dri ba re gnyis nas g.yo 'phrul du mas bslad pa'i dbang gis gnas tshul de rigs lags
na'ang / ji srid byang chub snying po'i bar gyi mgon dang gling du gyur pa ni rtsa ba'i bla ma nyid las gzhan du ma gyur pas/ thugs kyi 'dzin stangs gzhan du gzhol ba
sogs gtan nas med pa zhig dgos tshul zhu bar mdzad pas/ bka' las/ tshe 'di'i pha ma la log lta sogs ni ga la byed/ 'on kyang 'di phyi bar do gsum gyi skyid sdug legs nyes
thams cad skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po nyid las gzhan du re ba'i 'dun pa skad cig

kyang med ces gsungs pa bzhin/ don la'ang gnas pa kho na yin te/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mkhan sa rtsis sprod gnang nas/ rmor du chibs bsgyur skabs kyi rnam thar
las/ dbon rin po che ni bla g.yer mthil na byis pa chung ngu ltar bshums kyin skyel bar pheb byung zhes byung ba ltar ro/ /'di lo skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid dgung
lo bco lnga bzhes par rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye brag rje btsun brtse ba chen po'i ring lugs kyi nying khu/ gsang chen kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed srol/ tshar chen chos
kyi rgyal po yab sras kyi bstan pa 'di ni kho bo cag kho nas bzung ste dar zhing rgyas par byas la skal bzang gdul bya'i bung ba rnams/ snyan brgyud padmo'i ze'u 'bru
las 'ongs pa'i zab rgyas gdams pa'i sbrang rtsis myos par bya'o dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed rmad du byung bas nye bar drangs te/ gangs can ljongs kyi grub pa'i dbang phyug chen
po rnams kyi nang nas mchog tu gyur pa sangs rgyas gnyen ston de nyid phyi dar bstan pa'i srol 'byed chen po mnyam med dI paM kA ra'i sras kyi thu bo/ /'brom dang / khu
ston gnyis dag snang skyed par byed pa'i mtshams sbyor mkhan/ yon bdag shAkya mgon po zhes bya ba'i rgyud du sku 'khrungs shing / mkhas btsun bzang gsum mdzom pa'i snyan
grags spur rgyal bod kyi ljongs su mngon par gsal bas/ bod shing sgo can gyi rgyal po sne'u gdong gong ma'i ti shrI bkur zhing / mnyam med tshogs sde chen po bzhi'i ya
gyal/ tshags mig tshogs pa'i mkhan thog nyer gcig pa mthu stobs dang nus pa'i mnga' bdag /mtshungs

bral mkhan rin po che gzhon nu blo gros kyi bzhugs gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs sen gyi padmo mngon par bkod par/ spyi so/ bla brang / sbyin bdag sogs kyis zhal dkar/ legs
skyes/ bsnyen bkur yang phun sum tshogs par bsgrubs shing / gsang chen zab mo'i ring lugs 'jigs pa med pa gdong lnga'i dbyangs su sgrogs pa'i sngon 'gror/ rang gzhan gyi
dge tshogs chu bo'i rgyun rnams rnam mkhyen rgya mtshor 'jug pa'i thabs mchog bsngo ba'i rgyal po dpal gyi mgur las nye bar 'ongs pa'i legs bshad mya ngan med pa'i rol mos
phyogs kun rdzogs par mdzad pas gzur gnas kun gsang chen bstan pa'i srog shing gnas gsar pa yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa la mi phyed dad pa'i rang gzugs mngon par gsal
zhing lag pa'i padmo zum pa dang lhan cig bstod bsngags kyi me tog ci'ang 'thor bar byed ces thos so/ /gong smos ltar ljags sngags srung mdud kyis phan cha shin tu che
bas zhu mi mang du byung ba na/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid la gnyan lhog gdon zhud sogs la phan pa'i sngags shig zhu bar mdzad pas/ sku rtsed kyi rnam pas sa skya
legs bshad kyi 'grel par byung ba'i bram ze gtsug phud can gyi rdzun sngags/ oM sgrim skabs tshol/ kye ma re mtshar/ phyi nas sngon par 'ong / de nas khyed rang shes/ hu
hu hu swA hA/ zhes pa de ljags spod gnang bas/ 'di 'dra sngags min par 'dra zhu ba gnang bas/ zhal 'dzum pa tsam yang mi mdzad par sngags los yin gsungs/ phyag dpe'i khrod
nas legs bshad kyi 'grel pa shog 'khyar zh-ig ston par mdzad pas/ sku na phra stabs gong 'og la

thugs zhib ci'ang ma byung bar sngags de kho na'i thad la gzigs pas thugs yid ches te ljags bzlas mdzad pas nus pa shin tu che zhing / srung skud btags pa tsam gyis gdon gdug
pa can yang zhi nus par byung ba ni bla slob gnyis ka'i che bar mngon/ kun ldan zhes pa lcags byi lor dbyar smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling du phyags pheb ste/ rdo
rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi drung nas lung rjes gnang gi rigs shin tu mang bar gsan te/ slar bsti gnas dam pa nyid du chibs bskyod/ 'di lo srid zhi'i gtsug rgyan dam pa skyabs
mgon rgyal ba'i dbang po thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po blo bzang skal bzang rgya mtsho gser khrir pheb ste/ bod 'bangs thams cad la bde skyid kyi nyi ma shar ba'i
skabs su gyur pas/ thugs dges pa'i pad tshal ci'ang bzhad de/ khri 'bul rgya che spom mtho bstar ba gnang dgos dgongs kyang / gsog 'jog la brtson pa'i zhabs ring ba bzang
po med par ma zad/ de dag kyang brje len mang zhing / bla brang rtsis bzhes 'phral du'ang song ba bcas/ dngos po'i sgo nas gnang dkar bstan tsam byung 'dug pa/ zhabs 'bring
las byed rnams nas blos blangs na de tsam dgos don ci la srid kyang ji bzhin ma byung 'dug pa bcas/ 'on chos sdings su rgyal sras mchog sprul rin po che 'jigs med ye
shes grags par gnas tshul gnang bas khri 'bul gyi dngos po'i mthun rkyen rgya cher stsal zhing / chibs bsu'i chibs khal dang / zhabs 'bring ba sogs kyang chos sdings rang
nas thugs gra sgrig par mdzad de/ rgyal sras mchog gi sprul sku rin po che dang lhan cig tu stag rtse dngos

grub gling kha'i bar skyabs mgon rgyal ba'i dbang po thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po'i chibs bsur pheb ste lha ldan du mjal phyag sogs grub nas yar klung du phyags pheb/ 'di
lo bdag gi drin chen rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa yab rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched yum drung sku 'khor dang bcas pa gtso cher rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang bdun pa chen por mjal
phyag legs 'bul mdzad pa dang / dbus lho byang gi gnas rten rnams mjal bar pheb pa dang chab cig rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid kyis gdan sa yar klung bkra shis chos sder spyan
'dren mdzad de lugs zung dang 'brel ba'i phu dud bla med bka' drin bskyangs yod pa gor ma chag kyang / de skabs kyi zin bris zhib par ma rnyed/ 'on kyang gnas gsar 'jam
mgon gong ma'i thugs dam rten gur mgon 'jim sku chung ngu zhig dang / mgul du khyad mtshar sogs 'bul gnang la yab rje dam pa thugs gtsigs shin tu che bar mdzad/ 'phar
ba zhes pa lcags mo glang lor bkra shis chos sde'i 'dus pa'i tshogs dang bcas lhan cig lha ldan du pheb ste/ skyabs mgon rgyal ba'i dbang por sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i
tshe chog dang 'brel ba'i sgo nas zhabs brtan rten 'byung gi gsol 'debs mjal 'bul mdzad cing / rim bzhin smon dga' bsam gtan gling du pheb ste/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang
rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po de nyid zhabs pad brtan pa'i ched du rgyal yum tshe sbyin dbang mo'i thugs dam gnad nas bskul zhing / dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod sprin
dang chab cig par lung dang rig pa'i lam nas nye bar drangs pas/ zhabs pad brtan par bzhugs dgos pa'i gsol

'debs kyang mdzad par/ rje bla ma'ang thugs lhag par mnyes te/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i sgo 'phar rang 'grig tu gyur/ lo de'i zla ba lnga pa'i nang du dpal bsam yas
lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag chen po'i nye 'dab bu tshal gyi pho brang gong du/ mdo sngags rab 'byams smra ba'i bshes gnyen dam pa khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po sangs
rgyas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung nas/ rgyal pa'i bka' 'gyur ro cog gi lung rnam par dag pa gsal dag snyan gsum gyi sgo nas legs par gsan zhing / mdo mang gi lung
gsan mtshams su zhabs drung yab nas/ gnas gsar dang karma shag chen gnyis phyir slog gi zhu don rim par mdzad kyang / lhun sdings pa dang / bde chen rab brtan pa sogs kyis
rtsod pa byas pas ngal ba 'brel med du gyur pa thugs kyis ma bzod par lha ldan du pheb dgos byung zhing / mgron gnyer sbi chal chi ngag dbang blo bzang nas sne sbyor yang
dag gi /gun tshe dbang nor bus ched gnyer mdzad de lha ldan ru bzhi'i rgan po rnams la bdag khungs su yin rtsad gcod dang bcas/ rgya bod kyi mi sna rnams kyis bka' bgros
thog nas sa rigs bdag thob gang yin bdag 'dzin mdzad chog pa'i bka' shog stsal te/ bsam yas su phyir pheb/ sngar gyi chos 'phro rnams gsan/ slar yang ge ra'i sde pa rnam
rgyal nas gong sa skyabs mgon chen po gser khrir gegs med du pheb pa'i gtam snyan skyel pa'i mi snar gong du 'thon pa'i bdag rkyen du ger phyir slog zhus par/ skyabs
mgon dam pa 'di nyid nas lha sar pheb ste/ gun tshe dbang nor bus ched gnyer mdzad pa dang / sde

pa rnam rgyal nas sher sbyong ma nus par brten ger rang gnas byung zhing / de'ang rje 'di nyid dang po nas thos bsam sgom pa kho na'i thugs bskyed las sa ris dang sde dgon
gyi 'dzin skyong sogs la nan tar mi dgyes pa'i bla brang rang gis rigs 'dzin bzhin pa rnams kyang dka' tshegs chen pos gra tshang rang du sbyor 'jags gnang ba de bzhin yin
kyang / yab rje zhabs drung de nyid kyi sku drin bsab pa'i phyir zhu don snga phyi rnams kyang gnas gsar ba rang gi nang rten khyad can du ma'i phyag rten dang bcas nan
tan chen pos zhu bar mdzad cing / de steng nas tha na gsol zhing gcig tsam yang bdag gzung ma mdzad par/ sa ris yod do cog zhabs drung yab de nyid rang la rtsis sprod mdzad
pa yin no/ /dge byed ces pa chu pho stag /zhang zhung gi skad du zan yang ste/ lugs gsum mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por phyogs 'dus dang gnyug
mar gnas pa'i 'dus pa ches mang ba dang chab cig par/ skyabs gnas rgya mtsho'i snying po rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs drung nas gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad
thun mong ma yin pa dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / khrid/ lung dang bcas pa shin tu zab cing rgyas pa dang / rgyal yum mkha' sbyod dbang mo'i skor sogs chos bka' rgya
cher gsan/ grub mchog kha'u brag rdzong pa'i ring lugs gsang chen snyan brgyud zab mo'i tshogs spyi dang / bye brag gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi skor rnams bum
pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan cing / ma smin smin byed rgyu'i dbang gi skabs dbang stegs kyi dkyil 'khor rdul tshon gyis 'bri bar mdzad pa la/ skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid dngos
su bzhugs su

gsol te/ rgyal tshab kyi sras kyi thu bo mchog tu dbang bskur bas/ thams cad mkhyen pa klu'i zhabs kyis/ dbang lam lta khrid cha lag yongs su rdzogs/ /thun bzhi'i dbang dang
kha sbyor rlung la 'bad/ /'khor 'das dbyer med lam zab bla mar bshad/ /slob bshad snying la smin par byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes pa'i don mngon du gyur to/ /de dag gi don bsdu
na/ gzhon nu'i tshul 'dzin bsam yas yon tan bkra/ /shis pa'i chos sde'i khri chen la bzhugs pa'i/ /spyi dang bye brag bstan 'gro'i srog shing 'di/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon
gong ma'i rgyal tshab yin/ /zhes so/ /gsum pa ni/ de'ang / dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i sa bzhin du/ /yon tan kun gyi gzhi rten lags
par gsungs/ /zhes so thar gyi sdom pa bsrungs pas gnas skabs su mngon bar mtho ba'i srid pa rgyun mar thob cing / mthar thug sgrib gnyis bag chags dang bcas pa'i dgra tshogs
bcom par med thabs dang bral ba'i phyir/ sum brgya par/ nyon mongs dgra g.yul rgyal byed tshul khrims te/ /dge tshul brtul zhugs chu lon brtsigs pa dang / /'chi ba'i
mche ba 'byin par byed pa'i thabs/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub dpal nod dbang bskur yin/ /zhes dang / 'dul ba sman gyi gzhir/ dge slong dang tshul khrims goms par byas na ting
nge 'dzin yun ring du gnas par 'gyur ro/ /ting nge 'dzin goms par byas na shes rab yun ring du gnas par 'gyur ro/ /shes rab bgoms par byas na 'di lta ste/ 'dod chags dang
/ zhe sdang dang / gti mug las sems yang dag pa kho nar rnam par grol

bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes thub gsung brgyad khri bzhi stong rnams snying por dril na sde snod rin po che rnam pa gsum/ de'i nang nas mngon pa dang / mdo sdes bstan pa'i go chod kyang
/ ston pa'i go mi chod cing / 'dul ba gnyis ka yin pa'i phyir/ slob dpon chos kyi tshogs dpon gyis/ rgyal ba ston pa de yi dam chos dag /mdo dang chos mngon yin gsung
'dul ba ni/ /ston dang bstan bcos dngos yin de yi phyir/ /gnyis 'gyur phyag bya sangs rgyas khyod kyis bzhin/ /zhes gsungs la/ de lta bu'i khyad par 'phags pa'i sdom pa
de'ang rnam par ma dpyad pa'i som nyi'i rang bzhin zhig bzhes tshe rgyu 'bras mi 'chol bar chos nyid bcas na 'bras bu'ang de ltar 'byung ba las ma 'das pas nges shes 'drongs
ba zhig gal che ba/ bod yul gling dgu'i rgyal khams 'dir bstan pa snga dar la za hor rgyal rigs mkhan chen po dhi sa twas sad mi mi bdun sogs la bstan pa'i rtsa ba so
sor thar pa'i sdom rgyun 'dzugs par mdzad pa/ log smon nye bar bdo ste glang dar ma 'u dum btsan gyis bstan pa bsnubs pa'i tshe chu bo ri'i sgom grwa'i dmar g.yo gtsang
gsum gyis gsan pas gsang thabs kyis drel rgyab non pa'i 'dul dpe dang bcas mnga' ris nas byang lam brgyud mdo smad rma lung dan tig yang rdzong du bon gyi bu shes rab can
sngon las sad de rab tu byung bar bskul bar 'dul 'dzin gsum gyi steng rgya'i hwa shang ke 'bag gnyis kyis kha skong par mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i mtshan dgongs par
rab gsal du btags pas/ spa sar gnyis/ ja cog gnyis/ bzhad srags gnyis/ 'al snub gnyis/ zong tshur gnyis sogs mang dag sdom

bar bkod/ de skabs dbus gtsang du sdom pa 'bogs len dang 'chad nyan sogs kyi rgyun lo bdun cu tsam chad pa'i rjes dbus su mdo smad nas bstan pa cung zad tshugs pa mnga' bdag
tshal nas sogs kyis gsan pas cis kyang 'bad pas bstan pa spel bzhed de/ klu mes tshul shes/ 'bring ye ston/ sga tshul blo/ rag tshul 'byung / sum pa ye blo lngar mthun
rkyen dang bcas pa'i brdzang ba/ gtsang gi btsad po rnams kyis kyang thos nas lo ston tshong btsun/ mnga' ris pa gnyis/ bo dong pa ste dbus gtsang gi mi bcus bla chen por
bsnyen par rdzogs pa las mched pa ka bzhi/ gdung drug dang / lo tsho/ tshong tsho sogs mang du dar/ 'a zhwa ye g.yung gi chab gtor ma dang / 'bre'i der bsam gnyis kyi rgyun
kyang gtsang phyogs su mang po 'phel/ klu mes kyi slob ma gzus la bu chen bzhi byung ba'i/ phyi ma gsum dang / rgya 'dul dbang tshul gyis rgya cher spel bar snga phyi
bar tshar sogs shin tu mang / bstan pa phyi dar la lo chen rin bzang sogs snga rabs pa'i 'dul 'dzin sdom rgyun der brten pa dang / lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyi dus/ 'phags
yul shar phyogs kyi paN chen dharmA pA la'i slob ma pA la rnam gsum las kyang mang du 'phel ba stod 'dul bar grags/ ma pham pa'i rnam sprul khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i
dpal gyis dka' ba brgya phrag khyad du bsad nas kha che'i bsod snyoms pa paN chen shAkya shrI gangs can bsod nams gsog pa'i mgron du spyan drangs te chu shul srog ma dgon
par nyin gcig la sgrub grwa gsum dang mi gnyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i nang nas gro shul ba khed gad byang chub dpal dang / gtsang pa

rdo rje dpal gnyis mkhan bu'i gtso bor gyur te bod mun gling du 'dul bstan nyi ma ltar shar bas khyab cing khyad par sa paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ srid gsum 'gro ba'i
mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ shes bya kun mkhyen bu ston zhabs/ rgyal ba'i sras po thogs med bzang po dpal/ ngor chen kun
dga' bzang po sogs skyes chen dam pa de dag gis 'dul bstan gyi rgyal mtshan phyogs thams cad du 'dzugs par mdzad la/ bla chen sdom rgyun bka' gdams sogs phal mo ches phyag
len la 'debs par mdzad pa dag min gyi/ skur pa btab na chos spong gi sgrib par mi 'gyur ram snyam spros pa bskyungs mod/ gzhan du na bla chen pos bsnyen rdzogs mdzad dus
kha skong gi rgya ban gnyis sprul pa yin min the tshom pa'i sgros rnying dang chab pas sogs kyis kyang sbags ma sbags mngon shes kyis dpyod dka' zhing / 'dir ni de rnams
kyi skyon dris ma spags shing mchog tu gyur pa kha che'i paNDi ta chen po de nyid las gangs can mkhas pa'i dbang po sa skya paNDi ta chen pos sdom rgyun bzhes par mdzad
de spel ba'i rgyun bar skabs su cung zad nyag phra bar gyur pa na/ thams cad mkhyen pa mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos bstan pa'i rgyun la gcig tu dgongs pa'i sdom rgyun
bzhes 'dun yod skabs/ byang bdag nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes/ lu phu'i sgrub chen mkhyen yangs shig la sdom rgyun long gsungs pa'i zhal ta pheb nas/ de bzhin legs min
phyogs las rnam rgyal la bka' 'dri zhus pas/ rang re gnyis char byas chog gsungs nas/ mkhan po lu phu ba sangs rgyas 'od

zer gyis mdzad/ gzhan dge slong kha shas dang bcas blon po chu tshan khar gur gyi nang du bsnyen par rdzogs/ mdo rtsa las/ blangs pa la slar blangs pa med pa'i phyir ro zhes
gsungs pas/ sngar bzang bkras la dge slong gi sdom pa gsan pa de phul/ lcags thang pa la dge tshul dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa gsan pa de ma phul/ de'i tshe slob dpon dang gsang
ston 'os 'gyur zhig ma rnyed pas/ sangs rgyas 'od zer bas mkhan slob gnyis char mdzad/ gzhan dge slong gtsang ma gsum dang bcas bzhi'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan
slob cig car ba 'di la bu ston rin po ches/ mkhan slob gcig gis byed pa 'di bod gyi 'dul 'dzin rnams la ni snang / gzhung na bshad pa ni ma mthong gsungs pa de thugs mad/
'dul ba'i lung la bshad tshod yod kyang lag len med pa dang / lag len yod kyang bshad tshod med pa'i dmigs bsal mang bas de'i rnam dbye phye dgos/ yang kha cig dge slong
bzhis bsnyen rdzogs mi rung gsung pa ni/ tshig le las/ gal te bzhi ni las brjod mkhas/ /tshul khrims ldan par gyur na ni/ /bsnyen rdzogs ma smad gyur pa ste/ /lha yis
kyang ni phyag byar 'os/ /zhes pa 'di ma gzigs par zad/ /yang kha cig /bzhi'i steng du las rjod mkhan bsnan pas lnga tshang dgos zer nas 'bru skyog byed kyang / gal te bzhi
dang las rjod mkhan/ zer pa yod na bden mod/ gal te bzhi ni las brjod mkhas/ /zhes pas tshig nus la 'bru skyog de mi 'gro/ mdor na gsang ston yod na/ gsang ston bskor
ba'i las dgos/ bskor ba'i

las la lnga tshang dgos te/ bsko ba'i yul dge slong gcig /sko mkhan dge slong bzhi tshang dgos pa'i gnad kyis yin zhing / mdo rtsar/ skal pa dang ldan pa'i rang bzhin can la
bar chad ma dris par 'ong ngo / /zhes pa ltar gsang ston med na dge slong bzhis chog pa'i gnad ma go bar bab col ma mdzad cig /ces thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i
rnam thar gsung rtsom ma las tshig cung zad bsdus nas bkod pa yin la/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho nas brgyud pa'i sa paN gyi sdom rgyud khyad par can de dpal sa
skya'i chos grwa chen por ji ltar byung ba'i tshul ni/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi rnam thar phun tshogs bdud rtsi'i char rgyun las/ de nas sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen
pa chen po 'di nyid dgung gi 'jal byed lnga bcu rtsa bdun du pheb pa/ rnam rgyal zhes pa chu mo sbrul gyi lo gsar du shar ba na/ mdo khams nas a li chos rje grwa bu
slob mang po dang bcas/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma nyid dang / gdan sa chen po mjal bar 'byor/ lha khang chen mor mang ja brgyad tsam bskol zhing / ja dang ras la sogs pa'i gral
'gyed mang po btang / bdag nyid chen por ja gos dar la sogs pa'i 'bul nod rgya chen po sgrub cing shin tu gus par gyur/ rje btsun dam pa 'dis kyang chos dang zang zing
gi longs spyod lhug par stsal nas/ de dag gi re ba'i yol go yongs su khengs par gyur to/ /dgun thog der gtsang gram pa rgyang nas mkhas pa chen po mang thos blo gros rnam
rgyal gyi rje dbon rin po che mang thos grags pa rnam rgyal la gdan sa chen po 'dir 'jam pa'i dbyangs sa paNDi ta chen po nas brgyud pa'i bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom rgyun zhig
nges par dgos rgyur snang ba spel ba'i mkhan po'i 'os rigs

su khyed che bar 'dug pas/ bstan pa soms la myur bar spyon zhig ces pa'i bka'i spring yig gser gyi shing rtas legs par drangs te/ dpal sa skya'i dbu rtse snying ma'i dri gtsang
mchog tu chos kyi rje de nyid kyis mkhan po mdzad de/ dge 'dun grangs tshang bas cho ga rnam par dag pa'i sgo nas/ chos grwa lho byang gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang por/
kha che'i bsod snyoms pa chen po shAkya shrI bha dra nas/ 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub pa chen po 'jam mgon sa paNDi ta la legs par brgyud pa'i yongs su rdzogs pa
dge slong gi sdom pa yang dag par 'bogs pa'i mthun pa'i cha rkyen bzang po nye bar sbyar te/ dkar phyogs kyi lha klu sa gsum na gnas pa thams cad dga' ba'i zlos gar la
ngom pa med par rtser bcug go /zhes 'byung la/ sdom rgyun de nyid gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen po'i bzhed tshul ni/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug gi rnam thar
snying gi bdud rtsi las/ chu mo glang gi lor mkhan chen kun spangs pa chen po rin chen bsod nams mchog grub dpon slob rnams rnam 'dren dam pa 'di mjal bar pheb ste zhabs
brtan 'bul ba dang gong sa thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung rtsom gong ma yab sras kyi zhabs brtan/ 'jam dbyangs gdung brgyud myur 'byon gyi smon lam dang bcas pa de 'dus tshogs
su 'dzugs par mdzad cing / zab chos mang du gsan/ lhag par thub bstan lha chen gyi mkhan po byams pa bsod nams bkra shis dge 'dun grangs tshad dang bcas pa'i dbus su/
sa skya paNDi tas bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom rgyun bzhes te ma 'gyangs par rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po la phul ba'i rgyun de nyid deng sang rgya bod hor

gsum du khyab ste sa skya paNDi ta'i bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom rgyun rgya cher 'phel ba yin la/ zhes bshad pa ltar/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen pos bsregs bcad bdar ba'i
gser bzhin du legs par dpyad pas thugs nges 'drongs te dar rgyas su mdzad pa'i rgyun rnam par dag pa 'di nyid mchog tu gyur pas blang byar dgongs te/ legs sbyar skad
du shuu bha kri ta/ shar phyogs ma hA tsi nar zhin yin zhes 'bod cing / stod 'grel bod yul gyi skad du dge byed/ dbang thang dang bstun pa'i ming chu pho stag gi lo'i mnyam
med yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya'i dbang pos chos rgyal zla ba bzang por dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsa rgyud gsungs pa'i dus chen/ chu shel
dbang po nag pa'i dga' ma dang rtse ba'i gral tshes phun sum tshogs pa'i nyin/ bod yul gyi rdo rje gdan chen po dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang gi nye
'dabs su/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag /rig grol gyi yon tan du ma'i rgyan gyis nye bar mdzes pa/ bdag cag gi ston pa dang rnam dbyer ma mchis pa/ don
gyi slad du mtshan nas brjod na ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyis mkhan po/ mdo sngags rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son
zhing las kyi cho ga la mkhas pa khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis las kyi slob dpon/ nyes ltung dri ma'i chu 'dzin las grol ba'i sdom brtson
chen po tshul khrims rgya mtshos gsang ste ston pa/ dol chos 'khor gnas kyi slob dpon 'dul ba 'dzin pa kun dga' nor bus dus bsgo ba/ gnas brtan chen po phreng sgo gzhi
pa grwa

tshang gi slob dpon phun tshogs legs ldan gyis kha skong sogs mdzad de dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su/ tshigs gsum rim gyis nos te bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong
gi dngos po mngon du mdzad/ brje ba gnyis brjes pa'i mtshan brje ba'i skabs/ sngar gyi mtshan gyi steng du ngag dbang dang theg mchog dbang gi rgyal po zhes mtshan gsol
bar mdzad de/ rgyal bstan rin po che'i sgor zhugs la yongs su rdzogs pas ngur smin 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug gi rgyan bla na med par gyur to/ /dus de nyid nas bzung ste/
ltung ba sde lnga gnyen po'i khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu char gtogs dang bcas pa la spyan gyi 'bras bu ltar gces spras su mdzad de nyes pa'i dri ma phra mos kyang ma gos pa
lags so/ /de nas rang gi bsti gnas bkra shis dang dge ba'i mtshan ma du mas phyug pa gang der zhabs zung bkod de/ gsol 'debs zhal gsung ma las/ rim gnyis bsgom pa'i bsnyen
sgrub bzlas brjod sogs/ /dad mos spro bas nyin mtshan dbyer med par/ /rtag par gzhan gyi don la rab brtson pa/ /rgya chen sems bskyed 'gro ba'i mgon la 'dud/ /ces gsungs
pa ltar/ dpal kye rdo rje'i gzhi'i ljags bsnyen kha skong gi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa gnang skabs mkha' 'gros brda thabs dang yi ge sogs kyis rmi lam bzung ba'i grogs
yang yang byas gsung / ji ltar lags zhus pas/ nub cig chos sde'i rdo gcal du a ma skad lhang lhang 'dug par nyan pas rmi lam rmi lam zer yang bsam mno gtong dgos shig yod
snyam mam/ med lo ger snang ba las ngos zin pa ni ma byung / yang

nub gcig bud med cig gis labs kyang / mi go ba 'dug ces dpe shog cig gtad par bltas pas rmi lam gyi tshig kha yar 'dug pas rkyen byas rmi lam zin pa 'dra zhig byung zhes rjes
sor chos sder rje ngag la gsungs 'dug /'dis mtshon snga phyi rgyud sde gong 'og gi ljags bsnyen gyi rigs shin tu mang bar mdzad pa yin la/ 'di dag la brten nas rtags mtshan
ngo mtshar can mang du byung bar gdon mi za'ang / rjes 'jug rnams rtag par 'dzin pa'i 'ching rgyar tshud pa dang / lhag par rje nyid kyang yon tan sped pa la gtso bor
mdzad pas bsnyel tho zin bris 'dra'ang mi snang gshis rgya cher 'bri bar ma nus shing / sgra 'dzin gyi bu gar cung zad lhung ba rnams 'og tu 'bri bar 'gyur ba lags/ de'i
phyi lo rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas zan yangs mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du rdo rje phreng ba gnang skabs su dpon slob bcu skor dang bcas te rje bla
ma'i zhal dkyil mjal ba dang zhabs kyi padmo brtan par bzhugs su gsol ba'i rten 'brel bsgrigs par mdzad de/ sna tshogs dbyig ces pa shing sbrul lor gtsang du chibs kha bskyod/
gnas gsar brgyud de mkhas pa'i 'dun sa dpal zhwa lu gser khang khra mor phyags pheb/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub kyi ring lugs
la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i mkhas pa chen po kun spangs pa bla chen thugs rje brtson 'grus kyi drung nas/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi steng nas byis pa 'jug
pa'i dbang bdun/ gong ma/ gong chen/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ gdugs dkar mo can

lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang sogs rgya cher gsan/ rim bzhin 'og min gnyis pa dpal e wa~M chos ldan du gnas rten rnams la mchod 'bul smon lam mdzad/ 'di skabs gdan sa mkhan po mkhan
chen tshul khrims lhun grub yin 'dug cing mjal 'phrad dag snang sogs kyi nges sbyor ni byung tshod mi snang / rjes sor thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi bka' las/ chibs pa
dmar po ga zhur yod pa zhig bcibs nas byon song bas dag snang dang sems 'phreng po byung gsungs pa las zhal rgyas pa ni ma byung 'dug /de nas bod yul gyi rdo rje gdan chen
po dpal ldan sa skyar pheb ste/ bdag cag gi drin chen rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung nas/ dpal chen rdo rje gzhon nu'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang dang / lam dbang sogs chos bka'
mang bar gsan/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas kyang lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas bkur bzos phun sum tshogs par stsal/ rje 'di nyid kyi mtshan la/ 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug
rgyal mtshan rab brtan dpal bzang po zhes yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas stsal 'dug pa'ang 'di skabs lta bur yin nam snyam/ gdan sa chen po'i gnas rten khyad par can rnams la
mchod 'bul dang / spyi sgos kyi bstan pa dar ba'i smon lam mdzad de/ sgro mo lung du grub dbang dam pa de nyid dang zhal rgyas gnang ba'i tshul ni mkhas grub dam pa mang
thos mtshan can de nyid ni mngon par shes pa la thogs rdugs mi

mnga' bas/ sgro mo lung du pheb gong zhag kha shas nas/ ma chen dpal grub la/ rje'i gsung las/ deng sang 'o cag gi rtsar mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan pheb kyin yod 'dug pas
gzims gdan dmar po gsar pa zhig bcos gsungs pas/ de bzhin bcos/ pheb rgyu'i snga dror de ring gsol ja bzang ba zhig sbyor la ja thang zur du zhog cig gsungs pas/ ma chen
gyis ci mdzad zhus pa na/ kha sang nas 'phros byung ba'i mgron chen de de ring 'byon par yod gsungs nas/ gzims khang gi phyi nang kun la phyags dar mdzad/ zhabs phyi rnams
kyis su pheb 'ong ngam snyam yun ring bsgugs kyang / su'ang ma byung / nyi ma dgong khyog tsam la lung pa'i phu nas btsun pa bong khal ded pa kha shas byung bas mgron
'ong gsungs pa de ya gi lags sam zhus pas/ de ka yin/ pheb bsu gyis gsungs pa bzhin/ zhabs phyi rnams kyis pheb bsu dang bcas/ dpon slob kyi gzims chung min pa'i nang zur
pa zhig tu yid tsam bzhugs nas/ mjal phyag dang chos 'brel dgos tshul ma chen dpal grub la gsungs pas/ ma chen nas gong gi lo rgyus de zhus/ dum tsam zhig nas dpon slob
rang gis phrag par kha btags shig 'gel bar mdzad/ phyag na sba mkhar zhig bsnams nas gnas gsar rje dang mjal 'dzoms la pheb skabs thugs nyams 'ur pa lta bu'i gsung las/ shing
glang ma'i steng du bya khyung chen babs/ /khyed gnas gsar gyi dbon po khams chen de/ /nged sgom chen gyi gan du pheb pa ngo mtshar che/ /zhes sogs thugs shin tu spro
ba'i gsung gleng duu ma tsam

zhig gnang / de nas gnas gsar ba chen por ni gu'i chos skor yongs rdzogs dang / dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi dbang sogs rim bzhin stsal/ bzhugs ring gang por gsol zas sogs mthun
rkyen rnams gya nom par stsal bas rjes su'ang gsung las/ nga'i bla ma rmor chen rdo rje 'chang khams gsum dbang sdud de nyid kyi zhabs drung du 'dug pa las/ sgro lung pa
chen po sgom chen gyi bla ma'i drung du 'dug pa bza' btung mod pa byung zhes gsungs/ ni gu'i bka' khrid rnams stsal pa'i skabs nyin cig bzhugs g.yab na nyi sgrib kyi mthar
rdo bas mnan nas ljags lung gsan pa'i skabs su rlung drag pos rdo lag mgo tsam zhig dpon slob kyi sku mdun rang du shugs drag gis lhung byung bar chos zhu ba tshang ma
'jigs nas gsung shor/ dpon slob ni de ma thag sku drang por bsrang / spyan bar snang du hrig ger gzigs nas/ zhal nas a/ sgyu ma yin/ gsungs pa dang mnyam du yug cig lta
ba la 'byams song bas/ chos zhu ba gzhan tsho'i thugs la ci 'khrungs ni ma shes/ rje 'di nyid kyi thugs rgyud la sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin khyad par can zhig de dus
'khrungs par mngon te/ rje'i gsung las/ nged ni de skabs su sku mdun du chos gang zhus pa las de dus bogs che bar byung gsungs/ thon phyag gi skabs su gnas gsar rje'i mgul
la me long gi rgyab la rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i thun mong ba'i bsrung ba'i skabs kyi sku'i rnam 'gyur gyi ri mo yod pa zhig gsol/ phyag g.yas lcags kyi rdo rje
phyar ba'i stangs ka /g.yon

lcags phur thur du gnon pa'i phyag rgya mdzad du bcug nas/ dar cig de skad la bzhugs shig /khyed mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyi rnam sprul yin pas sgom chen gyi rten 'brel
zhig bsgrigs pa yin no gsungs/ brda don 'di la gnas gsar rje rang ci'ang mi gsung yang / kho bo'i bsam tshod la ni bsrung ba thun mong ba'i sku zhal nang bstan du yod pa
de gsung ngag tshogs slob gnyis ka'i bdag po mdzad pa'i brda dang / de'i phyi me long g.ya' yongs su dag par yod pa de rig gnas sogs shes bya thams cad me long gi gzugs
brnyan ltar mkhyen pa'i brda dang / de mgul du btags pa de chos kyi 'khor lo bsam gyis mi khyab par bskor ba'i brda dang / phyag g.yas lcags kyi rdo rje 'phyar ba de rdo
rje theg pa'i bstan pa'i srog shing sra brtan mdzad cing / thabs kyi phyogs su lhung ba'i bdud kyi bar chad thams cad la thugs bag mi tsha ba'i brda dang / g.yon lcags phur
thur du mnan pa de rdo rje phur pa'i chos skor gyis mtshon gsang chen rnying ma'i ring lugs kyi sgo nas snyigs dus kyi phung 'gong thams cad gnon pa dang / khyad par
nged rang nas rje btsun sa skya pa'i zab chos phur pa'i smad las drag po sgrol dbang gi thog ma de gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang la 'bul thub pa'i rten 'brel yin nam snyam zhing
/ rdo rje dang phur pa de rta mgrin lcags ral gyi dbang rdzas mdzad skabs lo rgyus 'di rnams gsung byung / sgro lung du bzhugs skabs phar yang dgongs bzhed bzhin dza bhir
rlung sbyor dang / mngar ris rig 'dzin chen po nas brgyud pa'i tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa 'bul bar mdzad cing / grub dbang de nyid kyis bskul ma mdzad pa bzhin/ de gnyis
kyi nyams len gyi yi ge gsar rtsom kyang mdzad de/ phyag na gang yod kyi dngos po thams cad phongs med du 'bul bar mdzad/ grub

dbang de nyid kyi'ang mgul khug nas gser gyi TaM ga gcig stsal te/ 'di nga la sa skya bdag chen gyis gnang ba yin/ khyed sku na gzhon pas gsan sbyong mthar phyin mdzad nas
bstan 'gror phan pa mdzad dgos zhes sogs zhal ta nan tan gnang bas bla ma yab sras 'bral mi phod pa ltar gyur/ thugs 'phreng bzhin du 'dar gzhung nas rim gyis brgyud de tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gdan sa 'dar grang mo che gsang sngags rdo rje'i pho brang gi shar tsam du pheb pa dang der yod dpon slob rnams kyis gnas gsar dbon rin po che
yin par ngo shes te mkhan slob grwa tshang bcas nas bla brang du gdan 'dren gzhis len dang / spyi khang grwa rigs rnams kyis mjal phyag sogs zhus te/ tshar chen rin po
che'i dus chen bla mchod chen mo la/ mchod 'bul mang ja rgyas par stsal/ 'du khang gseng g.yab steng bzhugs khrir gdan 'dren zhus te tshogs gzigs mdzad skabs/ gsung las/
tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gdan sa 'di mthong thos dran pa tsam gyis bla ma gong ma rnams nas dgon gnas 'di lta bur bstan 'gro spyi bye brag la phan bde rgya cher spel
'dug pas nged rang kyang skal pa bzang po byung gsungs nas shin tu dgyes/ zhag shas bzhugs par gnas gzigs mchod 'bul sogs mdzad cing / brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang gi gzims
spyil du gdan 'dren/ bsnyen bkur/ tshe dbang sogs bka' drin bskyangs/ de nas rmu gshongs/ mu gu lung / thub bstan dge 'phel/ cha lung rdo rje'i brag sogs la gnas gzigs
mchod 'bul mdzad pa'i pheb lam du brag rtsa

nang pas gdan 'dren/ 'bul ba/ zhabs tog rgyas pa dang bcas brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang gi yab de nyid kyi zhabs drung gnas gsar ba la phrin las 'gro don thogs pa med cing / sku
tshe thogs pa yod pas zhabs pad brtan ched tshe sgrub zab mo'i rim pa la thugs nan gnang dgos zhu zhing / spyan chab mang po bsil bas rkyen byas/ rje 'di nyid kyis kyang
spyan chab mang du mdzad pas sku rlung bzhes pa sogs mchod yon 'bral mi phod pa lta bu'i thugs snang shin tu dag pa byung / rmu gshongs la pheb lam du 'dar skyed gshongs
pas gdan 'dren zhus te 'bul ba zhabs tog dang / khong tsho'i gzhis steng shod tshang mar phyag nas mdzad de rmuu gshongs bla brang du bzhugs zhag gi gsung bskang / phrin
'chol/ 'dar grong mchod gzhis mjal zhu ba rnams la phyag dbang bcas mdzad/ de skabs rmu'i gnas brtan pa der/ bka' las/ mi khyod ni kun gzhi shin tu 'jam/ srung ma 'di ni
khyod la shin tu khros pa zhig 'dug pheb pa nas ma 'gyangs par kho bar rkyen ngan btud mar byung ba de sgrib bral ye shes spyan gyis gzigs par snang / sang nyin mu gu lung
dang / dge 'phel bcas la gnas gzigs/ mchod 'bul/ gsung bskang / mang ja sogs mdzad de/ dge 'phel du bzhugs/ sang snga bar kom 'dre brgyud de sgro mo lung du bzhugs zhag
dang / de gong sa skyar pheb skabs yum mchog bco brgyad ma sku drin can des slar rten 'brel gyi khyad sa skya nas dbus la pheb pa gnang dgos tshul gsungs pa bzhin/ slar
yang 'di phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur te lhun grub pho brang du

bzhugs/ 'di kha'i sde/ bstan pa/ gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i rkyen sel du gdugs dkar mdos chen gyi slob dpon rje 'di nyid kyis thugs 'gan bzhes shing / phyir 'phen pa'i zhabs
phyi bde chen gling ban tshang bsnyen song rags bsdus kyis zhus nas cho ga /phyag len/ zor 'chams sogs gzhan las phul du phyin pa bka' drin bskyangs pas/ yab rje rdo rje
'chang chen po dgyes pa'i rtser son zhing / gong dkar mkhas grub dam pa blo gros dbang phyug nyid btsun mo spel gyi rab gsal 'og ma na bzhugs skabs yin pas/ zor 'phen
pa'i sang der zhal 'dzom skabs/ gsung las/ kha seng gi mdos de sgra gcan gyi gdong rang la khel bas ya 'ud shin tu che bsam/ kho bos 'di nas bsrung dmigs nan tan bgyis yod
ces sogs thugs la bcar ba'i gsung sgros dang / de skabs sa skyar snga phyir bzhugs ring mgon po'i dbang chen lnga sogs gsung chos kyang ci rigs gsan/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang
gi bkas bskul te/ dpal sa skya'i mgon khang du mar sku khrus dang / gsung bskang / 'phrin 'chol gnang tshe/ gzhi thog mkhas btsun chen po'i thugs dam mgon khang tshom
bar du gsung bskang mdzad skabs thugs snang du mgon khang de la rgya mthongs zang thal phug ste mthil zhal gyi dbus lcags skyed zangs chen bcas btsugs nang sha btsos pa'i
rlangs pa skya bun bun 'gro ba zhig byung gsungs/ dbus la pheb khar yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi yum sku drin can bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mos na bza' dgun chas sogs 'bul
ba dang chab cig gang ci'i

gnas tshul zhu bar mdzad yod 'gro'ang / rgyus yod ma mchis shing / gang ltar yum de nyid kyi gsung dang mdzad pa 'di la dpag na kho bo mched rje 'di nyid la bcol dam mdzad
pa 'dra mo byung / de nas rim gyis dbus la chibs kha bsgyur/ gar gzhung du tsha phog gnang skabs a tsa ra dar ma gzi brjid can rked bar dgang gzar blugs gzar phyag tshad
can gzer ba zhig dang gsung sgros yun ring du mdzad de bag pheb pa ltar bzhugs pas/ des kho rang gi nyer spyad gang yod gzigs phul/ de gras la phreng ba rakSha phreng lung
dmar pos byas pa phreng rdog re re'i mtshams su rdo rje'i mdud pa btab pa zhig 'dug pas de dus ci'ang thugs snang ma byung / rjes su dgongs pas bgrang phreng gi rnam bshad
rnams nas de'i bshad pa nges sbyar byung bas rgyud dang / grub chen gyi gzhung bzang 'dzin pa zhig yin 'dra dgongs pa 'di'ang lkog gyur gyi gnas shig yin 'dra/ zil gnon
zhes pa me rta'i lo nang bkra shis chos sde'i 'du khang du tshogs pa sum brgya brgal ba la rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang gnang skabs phyag dpe klog tsam re dang / bshar sbyang
khyug tsam re gnang / phyag dpe 'gro min gyi skabs 'jam dpal la gsol 'debs nan tan gnang bas gsung bshad thogs med 'ong zhes gsungs/ sde srid dwa ching ba dur skabs
bstan srid jus rim du dus 'khor gyi sgrub pa 'dzugs dgos la grwa tshang nas dbang zhus pas zhal bzhes ma gnang / grwa pa rnams kyis dbu tshugs kho nas chos sde'i lam 'bras
lha khang du dus 'khor gyi thig btab ste sta gon gyi bca' bsgrigs nas/ sang dbang gnang zhig zhus pas/ de'i mtshan mo mtshams sbyor thugs rtog mdzad nas dbang chen thogs
med du stsal bas

dus 'khor la shin tu byang chub pa'i grwa rgan rnams kha skyengs par gyur/ de'i ston rmor chen rdo rje 'chang mjal bar pheb/ bka' chos ci rigs stsal zhing / rdo rje phreng
ba gnang ba la legs sor bla gos cha rog sogs stsal/ lo 'di'i mjug dang lug lo'i mgor bla brang rtser ljags bsnyen ci rigs mang bar gnang / dbyar smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan
gling du rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'i drung du zhabs thang la pheb skabs zhabs cung zad ngal nyams shar ba na/ lam bar du dzo ki zhig dang mjal bas de la zhabs ngal
nyams kyi brda mdzad pa na/ des zhabs ngar gyi nang nas bsnyun gzhi za ba'i tshul gyi rnam 'gyur bstan de gang yin gsung pa'i brda mdzad pa na/ des gshogs pa yod pa'i nyams
bstan pas thugs la khyung gi las tshogs rkang nad la phan pa zhig yin 'dra snyam pa 'khrungs shing / zhabs 'gros la'ang 'phral du bde nyams byung ba 'di ni sngon mkhan
chen gzhon nu blo gros zhabs cung zad 'dred par rdo zur gyis smas nas yun ring bsnyun tshul bzhes pa'i tshe/ thugs snang la dzo ki ras thod can byung bar zas skom gnang
/ rma bstan nas phan thabs kyis shig pa'i brda mdzad pas skra gseb nas sman bton nas byug pa/ dar gyis dkris/ dzo ki gar song cha med du gyur pa dang / dkris ma bkrol nas
gzigs par rmen pa tsam yang mi snang zhes gsungs pa dang 'dra bar mchis/ der zla ba drug tsam bzhugs te/ gsung ngag lam 'bras skor gyi chos bka' thun mong ma yin pa sogs
dbang lung shin tu mang bar gsan/ 'di skabs tsam la yin nam/ mdo smad sde bzhi dge bcu 'dzom pa'i yul

gru'i sa dbang chos rgyal chen po nas rje 'di nyid bstan 'gro'i don la yul phyogs der pheb dgos pa'i pho nya mngags pa bzhin 'byor/ de dang dus mtshungs tsam la/ 'dar grong
chen mkhan po gzhis rtse bas mkhan sa 'jog par mdzad nas grong chen pa rnams mkhan gsar 'os tho'i skabs gra dmangs kyis gleng rigs la brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang rang mkhan
po'i 'os yin kyang / da lta slob dpon gyi skabs dgon pa la phan pa 'di bzhin mkhan sa mdzad na ma byung dogs re zhig mkhan 'os gzhan zhig zhus/ slar slob dpon rin po che
'di nyid kyi sku drin bsab ched mkhan sar gdan 'dren thub pa zhig tshang mas byed zer ba'i gros mthun pas/ re zhig gi mkhan 'os la rje 'di nyid dang / thub bstan rnam rgyal
gyi mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang po gnyis byung ba bzhin/ grwa tshang nas rta nag tu bang mi zhu shog dang bcas gnas tshul zhus pa'i lan du/ thub bstan 'di grwa sa 'gangs
che bas ngos nas grong mo cher phan thogs pa zhig mi 'ong gsung bar/ bang mi spro thung de tshig pa zos nas log 'gro ba'i lam du/ bla ma grog ma gzigs yin 'dug /dgon
pa la bla ma mi 'byor ba rang mi 'ong ngam zer zhing song bar/ shul du thub bstan mkhan chen gyi gsung las/ lo shas grong chen mkhan po byed 'dod yod kyang bang mi la nyan
long med pas ma byung gsungs/ de nas rje 'di nyid mkhan por zhu ba'i yig rgya dang bcas rje drung skyid pa yab rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs drung du rdzong bda'
bzhin yar lam grub dbang sgro lung par mkhan sa su 'os gsung brtag zhus kyang ma gnang bar/ sa skyar 'byor tshe yab rje dam pa de nyid skyed lhas su sku

mtshams dang 'grigs/ mdzod du de skor 'phros pas/ lan du/ rta nag grwa sa che gshis grong chen par phan slebs med tshul dang / yar lung zhabs drung rin po che'ang sa khad 'gyangs
pa bcas ji 'dra/ 'ong ngam/ da rung grwa tshang gros thog nas 'os gzhan dgos tshul 'dra mo byung yang / rje drung skyid pas 'os tho 'di gnyis ma gtogs med pas gsung
brtags lan ma thon bar zhag grangs ji tsam bsgug dgos kyang de bzhin byed ces nan tan bgyis pas/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos brtag sgril mdzad pas bzang thon du rje
'di nyid byung ba'i gsung lan pheb pa dang bstun rje drung skyid pa grong mo cher 'phral du log ste/ grwa tshang nas dbus 'gro'i grabs yul gyi rje 'di nyid la zhu shog dang
/ gzhung zhabs rin po cher snyan sbron ched/ bka' blon lum pa ba/ lo tsA rje drung / g.yag rong zhabs drung rnams la zhu shog bcas grub nas/ 'di gar gang spyi'i gros
bsdur la byung skabs/ 'di nas dbus gtsang sa khad 'gyangs pas dgon pa'i yig rigs 'phral du 'gro ma thub tshe/ ngo tshab rgyal mtshan rin chen deng sang dbus phyogs la 'thon
nyer yod pas/ de dang chab cig legs 'dra zer ba bzhin 'dar grong ba'i shog rgya dang bcas thon/ ma 'gyangs par 'dar grong mchod gzhis la po ta la zhol gyi khral rigs 'ded
khra thon par gtan tshigs btsan dmigs spyan 'bebs kyis kyang go ma chod par rje drung 'brug chos 'phel lha sar thon pa dang 'di kha'i ngo tshab thug par mkhan skor thag
chod pa zhig ma byung bas/ da lam khyed rang phyin thog thag chod pa zhig dgos zer ba bzhin/ lo tsA rje drung brgyud gnas tshul zhus pas don smin gyi bka' shog mchod yon
rin po che gnyis char gyis stsal

nas re zhig gtsang la log /ma 'gyangs par bkra shis chos sder mchod yon gyi phyag dam dang bcas bang phyin ched mngags bzhin zhabs drung du 'byor yang / rje 'di nyid kyis dbus
gtsang sa khad 'gyangs pas mi 'ong gsungs nas zhu shog ma bzhes pas bang phyin des rmor chen rje'i zhabs drung du lhags te bka' khyab mgo 'dren zhus pa bzhin gsung shog
bang phyin gyi yi ge dang bcas grong chen gdan sa mdzad dgos nan tan stsal ba bzhin zhal gyis bzhes/ me lug hor zla drug pa'i tshes bco brgyad nas sa sprel hor zla lnga
pa'i nyer drug bar gangs ljongs bstan srid kyi gegs chag glo bur du langs pa lta bus gnam bskos dga' ldan pho brang pa'i bka' blon chen po rnams thugs ma mthun pas rkyen
byas dbus gtsang bde gzar langs/ nyes med skye 'gro du ma gums shing / spyi bye brag la phan nges pa'i gnas rten bstan 'dzin dge 'dun gyi sde kha shas la'ang nyams chag
byung ba bcas/ yang tig bod 'bangs bsod nams zad pa'i skal ngan de 'drar rlabs chen rgyal sras kyi spyod pas gtsang dbus gnyis char la gang phan mdzad pa'i dgongs gtad thun
mong min pa yod 'gro'ang / rmu rgod rnams re zhig gdul byar ma gyur pas chos sde nyid du gtan chags shing thugs gnyer thugs dam gyi rigs rnams rtag 'grus mdzad/ de skabs
rmor chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid mkhas grub 'gran zla dang bral bar bzhugs pas ris med che rgu phal cher gyi dbu blar gyur pa la dus ma bde ba de lta'i skabs gnas tshul
sna tshogs byung dogs bcas zhal slob spyi dang / khyad par rje 'di nyid kyis ched gtad zhabs drung

du bcar te/ dus gsum gyi gnas tshul gsol bar 'os pa rnams zhus pas/ rmor chen rjes rje 'di nyid sogs la gzhan ngal sel ba'i bslab ston tsam las gzhan ci 'ong ma gsungs/ de
nas ji skad du/ chos rnams thams cad rkyen bzhin du/ /'dun pa'i rtsa la rab tu gnas/ /gang gis smon lam ci btab pa/ /de 'dra'i 'bras bu 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar/ sngon gyi smon lam dus babs kyi dbang gis gtsang pa dpung bcas g.yul las rnam par rgyal te/ dpal mi'i dbang po bsod nams stobs rgyas de nyid gnam bskos dga' ldan pho
brang pa'i rgyal thabs kyi kha lo gyen du 'degs phyir zhabs pad gser gyi khri la bkod pa'i skabs lha sde mi sde tshang mas legs 'bul dgos pa bzhin dga' ldan khang gsar
du mjal phyag la pheb cing / legs 'bul sogs spyi 'gre ltar mdzad de yar klung du pheb/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang de'i dgongs gzhir/ srid gsum rnam 'dren rgyal dbang thams
cad gzigs pa chen po'i mdzad phrin mkha' khyab tu 'gyur ba dang / bod ljongs kyi skye rgu rnams bde legs su gyur na ci ma rung dgongs pa las/ phyogs phul rang rgyal gzhan
pham gyi thugs bskyed phra mo tsam yang mi mnga' bar mngon sum tshad grub dang / rdo rje 'chang gis rgyud sde rnams su mngon spyod kyi las bya ba'i yul du bshad cing / gang
la mngon spyod ma byas na rdo rje 'dzin pa la rtsa ltung bcu pa 'byung ba'i rkyen du 'gyur ba'i gdug pa can rnams la mngon spyod mdzad pa ma gtogs/ dgos med gya tshom
gyi rigs gtan mi mdzad pa ni/ spyir bstan pa rin po che'i sgor pheb pa'i bshes

gnyen dam pa yin par ma zad/ bye brag mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan mngon du gyur pa ni dus mtshungs kyi skye bo kun gyi spyod yul du gsal ba dang / de dus kyi zham ring
pa tshang mas nges shing gleng ba de bzhin lags kyang / lum pa ba dang sku nye mchod yon yin pa'i phul phyogs dang / phra ma mkhan 'ga' zhig gis dbyen bcos pa'i sku rkyen
la brten nas rdo rje 'chang de nyid la mi'i dbang po nas bla ma dgon gnas dang bcas par mdzad tshul de ltar shar ba'i lkog gyur mtha' dag rmor chen rje nyid kyis mngon
par shes pas dgongs pa bzhin bsti gnas nas pheb dgos dang g.yul rgyal lhun rtser sgor sgyil zhus par/ rgyal sras sprul pa'i sku rin po che ye shes grags pas nyid kyi sku
srog blos btang gis mi dbang chen por snyan zhu mdzad nas 'on chos sdings su gdan 'dren par mdzad de pheb lam yar klung brgyud de pheb par chos sde'i grwa bgres kha shas
kyis smon gro bkra shis sgang du mjal/ bkra shis chos sder gdan 'dren gyi zhu yig bang phyin ched rdzong gi lan du/ da lam pheb bskyod ma bde zhing myur mjal 'ong ba'i
gnas tshul stsal ba na/ rje 'dis bla brang steng nas spyan chab dang bcas phyag kho na mdzad pas steng grib bsnyun ro zhig yod pa de'ang 'phar ba lta bu byung gsungs/ sa
sprel dbyug zla'i nyer gsum la rmor chen rdo rje 'chang rgod tshang ri khrod du pheb nas ma 'gyangs par mjal phyag zhu bar pheb/ de'ang mdzod 'grel las/ byis pa lag mthil
'dra ba yis/ /'du byed sdug bsngal spu mi rtogs/ /'phags pa mig dang 'dra ba rnams/ /de yis rtag tu yid kyang 'byung / /zhes pa ltar/ skyes mchog spyi dang / khyad par rje
'di nyid ni phyi rkyen tsam lam ltos pa'i nges 'byung skyo shas drag po rgyun chags su bzhugs pa la bri gang

mi mnga' yang / tshur mthong dag gi snang ngor 'khrug long zi bun sna tshogs de dang / lhag par rmor chen rdo rje 'chang lta bu lhar bcas kun gyi bsod nams kyi zhing mchog
bla na med pa der/ sku nyid rang ngos nas tsandan dang stwe 'ur mtshungs pas 'o brgyal gyi rnam pa mi mnga' yang / gzhan dag bsod nams ma yin pa gsog pa la thugs yid lhag
par 'byung bas/ da ni ltag pa brag la gtad pa'i nye lam 'di la brten nas rgyal ba brag phug pa dang / dbang phyug bzhad pa rdo rje'i rnam thar 'khyongs nges pa zhig mdzad
snyam/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid kyi ljags lung zhu bar mdzad pas/ de sngar gsan grub nas yang bskyar ci mdzad gsungs par/ dus 'gyur 'di dag la dpag 'di la chig sgril
gyis 'di bzhin bgyid 'dod lags zhus pas/ de 'dra gtan nas mi legs/ de bas 'di gsan pa 'thad gsungs/ sngar ma gsan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad
pa'i rnam sras mchod chog gi ljags lung phyag dpe bcas stsal ba gsung chos dngos su gsan pa'i tha ma yin pas/ rjes sor bka' las/ tshul de longs spyod kyi rten 'brel
khyad par can la dgongs/ de'i rten 'brel mdzad pa yin snang bas/ deng sang dngos po'i sgo nas tshogs gsog dang / bstan don cung zad bgyid rgyu 'ong ba 'di de kho na'i thugs
rjer gda' gsungs/ de skabs kyang dga' skyo zung 'brel thugs dran mi gsos pa lta bu'i ngang nas skyabs mgon dam pa yab sras zhal rgyas gnang thub tsam byung / rmor chen
rdo rje 'chang de nyid gzhi nas sku khams mi dwangs pa'i khar rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po li'u

thang phyogs su chibs bsgyur gnang dgos tshul gsan pas rkyen byas te/ da rang dus skabs 'di 'dra la shi ba dga' gsungs nas/ sngar sku'i rnam pa grub chen birWa pa lta bu 'ber
mo'i tshul du yod pa las/ sku sha rnams kyang nyin khyad zhag khyad lta bus skam tshul bzhes te zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi tho rengs lam dus rgyas pa gcig
mthud/ gnyis mthud du mdzad rjes sku'i nang nas 'ur sgra dang bcas chos sdings rgod tshang ri khrod nas mkha' spyod chen por zang thal du gshegs/ phyag mdzod blo ldan nas
sku gdung zhugs 'bul sogs la skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid gdan drangs pa bzhin rgod tshang ri khrod du pheb ste/ rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi sku gdung rin po che zhugs la
'bul ba sogs zhabs tog rnams dpyis phyin par mdzad/ chos sdings kyi grwa bgres kha shas la rgyal yum mkha' spyod dbang mo'i byin rlabs sogs chos bka' mang tsam gnang ste
chos sder phyags pheb/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gshegs skabs dbus gtsang bde gzar gyi mjug dang gzhi nas bla brang du phyag 'byor chung ba sogs kyis dgongs rdzogs mchod
'bul ha cang gi rgya che ba zhig ma byung yang / gtso bor snyan brgyud bstan pa'i mnga' bdag tu bzhugs pa 'di zab dgongs yongs su rdzogs pa'i mchog dang / der ma zad thugs
dam rgyun 'phar gyi rigs thams cad kyang rje de nyid kyi dgongs rdzogs kho nar nges shing / yengs med brjed med bla ma spyi bor bsgom/ /zhes pa ltar dbang byin rlabs rjes
gnang rnams kyi so so'i ye shes dbab sngags rdzogs nas/ rab 'byams mdo sngags kun la mkhyen rab rgyas/ /zhes sogs

rmor chen rje'i gsol 'debs sha lo ka gcig gi mthar/ drin can bla ma'i zhabs kyis byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes chag med mdzad pa dang / dus phyis chos sde rmor dgon ma lag gsum du
zla rer bla mchod chag med dang / she'u grong du zla rer mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod/ bsam yas rab byung bar kye rdor dang / 'phags sder mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod rnams
'dzugs par mdzad pa sogs la rje de nyid thugs dgongs yongs su rdzogs par mngon te/ bka' las/ rnam dkar gyi bgyi ba mtha' dag rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs
thabs kho nar bsngos pas/ nub gcig rmi lam du/ dam pa de nyid 'khyags thog zhig la zhabs 'dred 'ong la khad lta bur pheb byung bas nged kyis rngul gzan 'khyags thog tu
bting ba'i steng la gdan 'dren zhus pas pheb bde zhing thugs mnyes pa'i tshul mdzad pa zhig byung bas/ gnyid sad nas dges tshor dpe med byung zhes rje ngag la gsung 'dug
pa 'di la dpag na/ nges don du rmor chen rje de nyid la skyon yon gyi rtog pa ci la mnga'/ drang don kun rdzob tsam du dus gsum du bla slob gnyis lhan cig tu 'brel zhing
/ rmor chen rje 'o brgyal gyi tshul bzhes na de la nges par rje 'di nyid kyis zhabs tog sri zhu yang dag par mdzad pa'i mtshan mar mngon no/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ sdom
gsum dpal 'dzin bzlas brjod pha rol son/ /gnas brtan mkhas grub mjal zhing zhal bcud gsol/ /skal ldan rjes bzung dam pa'i dgongs pa bsgrubs/ /gnas gsar mkhas btsun bzang
po'i rnam thar yin/ /zhes so/ / ! bzhi pa la thun mong ba spyir bstan pa

dang / mchog gi mdzad pa bye brag tu bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtshos/ ma 'gro kun sdug bsngal rgya mtsho las/ /phan bde dga'i grong du 'khrid
mdzad pa'i/ /skyabs legs pa'i 'byung gnas 'gro ba'i mgon/ /rje gnas gsar chos rje zhes gsungs pa ltar/ de'ang / zhi ba zhes pa sa bya lor slar yang mdo khams nas sde
dge sa skyong bstan pa tshe ring gis/ 'di khar sgrub mchod rgyas pa zhig 'dzugs rtsis la sa lugs kyi bla ma dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang lung / cho ga phyag len/ gar thig dbyangs
gsum gyi rgyun khungs gtsang yod nges shig cis kyang dgos tshul rgyal yab sku zhabs su zhu bar mdzad pa bzhin/ des kyang sa skyong mi dbang chen por snyan zhu mdzad
pa dang phyogs mtshungs su/ grub dbang dam pa sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'ang ched gtad kyis dbus su pheb ste nan tan zhu bar mdzad pas ha lam zhal gyis bzhes shing pheb lam
lam rgyus pa khams pa phyug rgyal zer ba zhig kyang 'jog par mdzad/ de lo bsam yas su chos skyong chen pos rab byung grwa tshang gi grwa pa lo nyi shu lon pa yan chad bsnyen
rdzogs sgrub dgos tshul gyi bka' lung stsal bar/ gra tshang nas dbu tshugs nan tan mdzad de rab byung gi grwa pa shin tu mang bar bsnyen rdzogs mdzad skabs/ khams pa
phyug rgyal sku mdun na yod skabs shig la grong chen bang phyin lung ru steng pa'i grwa pas gtsang du 'phral pheb dgos tshul zhus pa dang / khams pas khams la gdan 'dren
tshul smras pas de gnyis sku mdun du rtsod pa na/ grong chen bang phyin la thugs dgyes te khyod gdan sar zhen

chen po byung zhes gsung bar grags/ grwa tshang nas kyang legs so'i tshul du tshe dpag lha dgu la brten pa'i zhabs brtan dang maNDal 'bul ba'ang rgya che ba dang / sde pa kun
chos nas kyang khrom dbang gi sbyin bdag bgyis te bsnyen bkur zhing kar dril rtse lnga/ dbang rdzas nyer mkho/ na bza' sogs 'bul nod kyang gzabs rgyas bstar/ 'bras spungs
su rgyal sras rin po cher gser chos dmar po skor gsum sogs dbang bka' rjes gnang du ma 'bul bar mdzad de/ dga' ldan khang gsar du sa skyong mi dbang mjal phyag la pheb/
de skabs mi dbang chen po nas mdo khams su pheb dgos kyi bka' nan tan stsal te/ pheb lam du rdzong sgo so so nas gsol phog dang / rta 'ul/ dos khal sogs kyi lam yig bka'
shog sogs mdzad de/ de bar dgon gnas chos gzhis rnams la gang phan byed ces pa'i zhal bzang kyang stsal te mdo khams su pheb pa'i sgo dod/ rim bzhin bsam yas su pheb ste
grwa tshang gi 'dod pa ltar mdo sde mchod par bzhugs shing / gnas srung chos skyong chen po khog tu rlom par mchod gsol phrin bcol sogs mdzad cing / chos skyong nas kyang
'byung 'gyur gyi lung bstan yid ches pa mang du gsungs te skad cig kyang mi 'bral bar phrin las bsgrub par zhal gyis bzhes shing / lha rdzas dang sku srung lta bur ba
dan legs pa'ang stsal/ gong du bshad pa ltar 'dar grang gdan sa zhal gyis bzhes kyang bde gzar stabs gtsang du pheb ma thub gshis rim 'gyang du lus pas/ khams nas yar ma
phebs bar bla gzhis tshang ma grwa tshang spyi nas blangs pa'i 'ong 'babs rnams

kyis gtsug lag khang gi zhig gso dang / spyi rdzas gsar bzo byed dgos rnams gang 'grub byas pa'i slar 'di yin gyi zhus dag pher ba dang / sgrig lam kun spyod gang ci sngar
rgyun las nyams chag mi 'ong ba'i bkod khyab do khur dbu che las sne rnams nas theg pa khur len dgos tshul gyi bka' mchid mthar phyin stsal te bang phyin phyir slog mdzad/
yar klung du gsang chen 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis rje btsun yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgo nas zhabs zung srid mthar brtan pa'i thabs mchog snyan brgyud zab mo'i phyag len ji lta
bar maNDal 'bul nod rgya chen dang / sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po bsod nams snang byed kyi zhal snga nas kyis/ zhabs pad bskal brgyar brtan dgos pa'i shes byed mdo
rgyud kyi lung dang sbyar ba'i legs bshad kyi mchod sprin rgya cher spro bar mdzad/ chos sde nas phyag mdzod lhun grub kun dga'/ bla mchan dge slong kun dga' dpal 'byor/
mchod dpon dge slong kun dga' grags pa/ mgron gnyer 'tsho byed blo bzang tshul khrims sogs dang / bsam yas nas thugs sras phyag mdzod 'jam dpal rgya mtsho dang / ma chen
bzang po rgyal mtshan sogs dpon g.yog skya ser mang ba dang / de khul gyi lha sde mi sde kun gyis pheb skyel dang bcas te zla ba drug pa'i nang du mdo khams dge ba'i yul
gyi ris gsum gdul bya'i tshogs rnams smin grol la 'god pa'i thugs bskyed zla ba gsar pa la 'gran pa bzhin du chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te/ de nub rtses dong 'bras bu gling
du bzhugs/ de nas rim bzhin/ 'ol kha dang / rgya mda'/ star rdzong / sho pa mdo/ lho rong rdzong sogs nas gsol phog

dang star rdzong gi rdzong dpon bkra shis mthong smon pa dang / sho mdo nas 'phyong rgyas zhol khang pa gnyis kyis sna len zur gsos kyang rgyas par mdzad/ zhol khang gi sde
pa gshegs pa'i byang bzhu dang / rgya mda' khul du o rgyan bla ma'i sgrub gnas brag dkar lha chu'i gnas rten rnams la mchod 'bul smon lam mdzad de rim bzhin pheb/ spang
leb dgon du de'i bla ma rdo rje brag nas yin pa zhig 'dug pa des kyang ja zhus dang mjal kha mdzad/ tal dkar la rtser grub dbang dam pa sangs rgyas rgya mtsho dpon g.yog
nas pheb bsur pheb pa dang mjal/ zhal bsro sne len phun sum tshogs pa mdzad de lhan rgyas su chibs bskyod/ rje bla ma 'di dang sang mjal rgyu'i nub mo grub dbang dam pa de'i
mnal lam du/ thang chen po zhig gi dkyil na bla ma dpon g.yog mang po'i bzhugs sgar btab 'dug par/ bla ma de mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan yin/ da lta rang mjal dgos dgongs
pa gsal bar byung bas rje 'di nyid khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po'i yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad/ de nas rim bzhin dpal 'bar dgon nas gdan 'dren dang bsnyen bkur/
chab mdo nas mgron gnyer ngo ma mjal khar 'byor te dkar spro dang zur gsos kyang rgyas par phul/ lha thog gzhung du sde dge'i gnyer pa dar rgyas dpon g.yog nyi shu skor
chibs sngon po brtan brling 'dzoms pa gcig dang bcas pheb bsur 'byor/ ri mtha' rdzong nas dpon gu rus chibs bsu dang thab bsu ring thung sogs bkur sti phun sum tshogs pa
dang bcas te rdzong du gdan drangs shing bsnyen bkur 'bul nod kyang rgya cher bstar/ ye na rdzong du dpon dpal ldan gyis

kyang bsu ba bsnyen bkur sogs gong mtshungs bcas rim bzhin pho brang chen po lhun grub steng du phyags pheb/ mar lam gyi pheb lam lung pa gser gshong dang chu sogs yod pa zhig
tu gsol tshigs thon nas sku gseng la pheb ste dus 'khor gyi gar gyi stangs ka 'ga' zhig mdzad par/ de 'phral lung pa'i phu nas 'ongs pa lta bu'i ban gzugs hur spyod can
zhig byung bar khyed su yin gsungs pas/ nga mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor yin/ grub mtha' thams cad kyi gral mgor nga sdod pa yin/ khyed kyis da ci nas mdzad pa'i gar
de yang bskyar gnang zhu dang zer/ de bzhin mdzad pas khyed rang 'dir bzhugs shig /ngas nag guu ma zhig blang 'ong gi zer/ ci khyer 'ong ngam dgongs pa na/ chang phing
chung gang khur byung ba la ye nas ma gsol bas dbu tshugs kyis phyag mthil du thigs pa gcig gnyis blugs pa sogs lo rgyus ya mtshan can zhig nged rang la gsung byung bas/
de'i don rnal 'byor ni/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa'i/ /rnal 'byor de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs/ /zhes pa ltar gnyis med kyi don dang / grub mtha' thams cad kyi gral mgor
nga sdod pa yin zhes pas kyang rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po gnyis med dus kyi 'khor lo bstan pas/ mdo smad phyogs su de'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar mdzad bzhed la/ khro bo'i
dbang po rdo rje shugs sam/ khyung po rnal 'byor gyis nag gu ma ste ni gubta sbas tshul gyis ni gu ma/ shes rab ma da na yi chang / /zhes pa ltar shes rab bdud rtsi'i
rnam par bsgyur te zung 'jug gi rten 'brel bla na med pa bsgrigs par sems shing / 'di ni sngon

rje yongs 'dzin gyis e waM gyi 'du khang du rgyud 'bum gyi lung gnang skabs rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud kyi mgor grub thob sgog smyon pa chang dam chung gang dang khyi gu zhig
khyer nas dpon slob kun gyi phyag tu chang thigs re phul nas rgyud de'i lung rdzogs par nyan rjes gar song cha med zhig byung ba dang tshul mtshungs pas bsam gyis mi khyab
pa'i rnam thar ro/ /de nas thog mar 'di kha'i 'bul sdud bla ma'i khang par bzhugs/ de skabs sa skyong chos rgyal chen po de nyid dbyar 'dong la pheb par/ skyabs mgon
dam pa 'di nyid pheb pa'i gnas tshul gsan 'phral pho brang du chibs kha bsgyur te/ gza' tshes dus sbyor bzang por phan tshun gtong ba'i sgo brgya rnam par phye ba'i zang
zing gi tshogs dang gsung gsang gi nor bu re re las kyang legs par bshad pa'i 'dod rgu 'bum du 'dzag pa'i sngon rabs dam pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'i legs bshad kyi skyes bzang
po phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas te pho brang chen po dngul mda' steng du mchod yon mjal 'phrad thog mar mdzad pas sngar 'dris kyi mdza' bo 'phrad pa bzhin du dgyes pa
rab kyi rtser son pas gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi rten 'brel mtha' dag rang 'grigs pas/ rgya chen thugs bskyed kyi mthu las nye bar grub pa'i 'bras bu gzugs can bzhin du
gyur to/ /rje'i bka' las/ chos rgyal 'di rje btsun g.yu thog pa'i sprul pa yin zer ba 'dra mo'ang yod de/ zla ba bzhi pa'i nang mnga' zhabs kyi 'tsho byed mkhas pa rnams
bsdus pa'i mgor sa skyong rang yang byon nas sman sbyor phon shin tu che ba mdzad de/ sman sbyin gnang bsam gsungs/ mkhan chen bsod nams bzang po'i bka' las/

kun gyis 'di la bu rin po che dang bu tshang sogs zer bas/ 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud las/ chu bo gser ldan 'gram logs su/ /rgyal po gzhon nu'i ming can 'byung / /zhes pa de yin
'dug gsungs/ sa skyong chos kyi rgyal po dpon slob rnams la thog mar/ rje btsun ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes su gnang ba sngon du 'gro ba'i zab chos kyi rigs mang po dang
/ lhag par dpal dus kyi 'khor lo rwa 'bro gnyis kyi brgyud pa'i chu bo gnyis 'dres su gyur pa gangs can mkhas pa'i dbang po bu ston rin chen grub pa'i bzhed pa phyin ci
ma log pa'i mngon rtogs dang / dkyil chog nag 'gros bklags chog gi yi ge gnyis dpyad gsum rnam par dag pa dang / brgyud 'debs kha skong sogs gsar bsgrigs mdzad/ dgon chen
gyi grwa pa rnams la dpe cha blo 'dzin byed dgos kyi bka' khyab gnang bar/ zla ba gnyis lhag tsam la brgyud 'debs mngon dkyil dang bcas pa gcig bshur pher ba bdun cu lhag
pa byung ba rnams la gdangs dang gar thig rnams sbyong bdar mdzad/ 'di skabs so sor mang ja dang / dar 'gyed sogs gsol ras gya nom pa stsal bas/ thabs mkhas khyad par can
kho na las dbang chen dang she mong lta bu ye ma mdzad pas slob gnyer ba nyams cad dga' mgu yi rangs te/ bla ma dang sbyin bdag thams cad mdzad mkhan zhabs drung dbon
rin po che lta bu dkon zhes spro dga'i ca co ci'ang sgrogs shing / sa skyong chen pos kyang gar gos/ pang khebs/ rus rgyan/ skra zhwa/ rtse phran/ phur pa/ rnam bum sogs
nye bar mkho ba'i yo byad tshang ma rgyud dang mkhas pa'i dgongs pa bzhin lhag chad med par gsar bsgrigs mdzad/ sa skyong dpon blon dang / chog

grwa ba'i dge 'dun rnams la sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du thun mong byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/ gong ma/ gong chen/ bdag po chen po'i
dbang dang bcas pa tshigs gsum thob pa'i rnam gzhag dang bstun nas rgyas par mdzad de/ thun mong zhes pa lcags khyi lo 'o skol gyi rnam 'dren shAkya'i rgyal po des shrI
dha nya ka Ta kar/ rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po dpal dang po'i sangs rgyas dus 'khor stong phrag bcu gnyis pa gsungs pa'i dus chen nag ba zla ba'i gza' skar dus tshes bzang
por skyabs mgon mtshungs med dam pa 'di nyid longs spyod rdzogs sku'i chas kyis bklubs te gar dpon du pheb/ sa chog gi gar nyams dgu'i rol bas mngon par dpa' ba mthong
thos kyi skye bo rnams snang ba 'gyur nus pa dang / phur gdab/ sta gon/ sbyin sreg /mchod gar dang bcas sgrub mchod bdag 'jug phyag len phra mo tshun chad kyang ma 'phyugs
shing 'gad gtsang bar 'dzugs par mdzad/ sa skyong chen pos kyang 'dzugs ston dang rgyun gyi mang 'gyed sogs kyang phal gyi blor mi shong ba lta bu'i bsnyen bkur rgya che
la dngos gtsang bar bsgrubs par mdzad do/ /sa skyong chos rgyal chen po de nyid dbyar dbyar mthong dang / ston thog bsdu ba sogs la rdzong 'og nye skor rnams su pheb srol
yod par/ de skabs kyang 'bral med du pheb ste/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho sogs spyi bka' dang / zur bka'i dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang gi rigs rgyun du chag med lta bur 'bul
bar mdzad/ lo 'di'i ston mjug /sa skyong mchog nas 'bul ba snga phyir stsal ba rnams kyis mtshon dad ldan gyi dngos po rnams chud mi za ba'i phyir/

snyan brgyud kyi gdan sa bkra shis chos sder rgyun ja'i thebs su dmigs kyis bsal ba gser rkyang mgur zho brgya dang / gzhan ma sa skyong mi'i dbang po sogs la 'bul rgyu'i zhu
yig rten chas rnams dang / bzang ja sna tshogs 'khor drug brgya dang bdun cu/ wa lpags lnga bcu nga bdun/ gla 'khor bcu bdun skor/ rtsis rta mi the ba'i rta rkyang nyi
shu rtsa lnga/ mdzo bzhi bcu zhe bzhi/ dre'u bco lnga/ kha btags/ sman tshe/ ling zam sogs sna tshogs phon che ba bcas rtsis sprod gnang ste/ gser rkyang rgyun ja'i thebs
su sbyor rgyu ngo thog dang / dngos po byings kyi thog nas/ chog mang 'di dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod gzhan dang mi 'dra bar/ gtong sgo ba rnams khag sbyong che bar phan phyir
rab dngul srang brgya tsam/ tha na'ang dngul srang lnga bcu skor sbyor 'jags byed rgyu dang / de 'phros khams su dgos pa'i nyo cha phran bu ma gtogs/ de phyin rgyun ja'i
thog tu bsgril ba'i bka' bkod mthar phyin dang bcas phyag mdzod lhun grub kun dga' dbus su rdzong bda' mdzad par/ rgyun ja'i thog tu khyon bsdoms dngul srang brgya dang
/ chog mang thog tu srang bcu drug sbyor 'jags su stsal zhing / de mtshungs grong chen du'ang rdo rje slob dpon gtso bor smos/ las sne ba rnams kyis mtshon tshang mas
bstan pa snying khongs su bcangs pa'i mdzad bzang g.yel med dgos tshul gyi thugs dam rten bkras btags/ mang ja'i rgyur gser zho brgyad/ ko rtse bag gnyis/ chung ju bag gnyis
bcas kyang stsal/ phyag mdzod 'khor bcas phag lo'i ston mtshams su rje nyid kyi zhabs drung du 'byor bar/ rta gsum/ drel bcu gcig

/dngul srang bcu dgu/ na bza' cha tshang gnyis kyi rtsis snam bu dang ther ma sna tshogs bub sum cu skor/ gtsod do 'ga' zhig bcas phul/ skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid zang zing
gi rdzas la thugs zhen che ba ga la yin kyang sbyor 'jags gnang dgos rnams dgongs pa bzhin ma grub pas thugs 'khrugs par byung ba rjes su'ang yang yang gsung ngo / /khyi
lo'i mjug dang phag lo'i nang du phyag 'byor byung ba'i dngos po rnams mar dang mdzo mor bsgril bar gnang bar/ mar 'gar thar rgya ma'i khal brgya dang brgyad/ mdzo mo legs
nges brgyad/ gser srang gsum/ dngul rta rmig ma/ chibs chibs rol bcas pa/ dre'u gsum sogs phyag na gang yod spang dag gi tshul du gong sa thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen
por 'bul bar pheb lam gyi dka' tshegs khyad du bsad de zla ba dgu pa'i nang du hor gzhung brgyud 'gar thar du skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po blo bzang skal bzang
rgya mtsho'i zhabs drung du pheb pa na gong sa mchog dang sku 'khor tshang mas gnang skyes dang bdag rgyan phun sum tshogs par mdzad/ khri chen no mon han gyi drung nas/
thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i dag snang ma 'chi med rdo rje'i srog shing gi tshe dbang gsan/ slar yang dngul mda' lhun grub steng du chibs bskyod byi lo'i
nang du lhun grub steng gi ja mdzod du rgyal chen rnam thos sras kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rten rnams dang / phyi nang gsang ba rab 'bring mtha' ma sogs deng sang phyag len
du ji ltar mdzad pa ltar gyi rten 'dzugs kyi rim pa rnams gzabs rgyas su mdzad/ sa skyong dpon

slob nang skor rnams la rnam thos sras lnga phrag gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba rgyab brten gyi lung dang bcas/ zab pa'i mthar thug gser chos dmar po skor gsum gyi thun mong dang
/ thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs rjes gnang rnams dang / rje btsun rig byed dbang mo'i zab khrid snyan brgyud kyis brgyan pa/ de gsum ka'i be'u bum gyi lung dang bcas
pa rgyas shing gab sbas med pa lhug par stsal/ de skabs su phyi rol du ljongs rgyu bar pheb pa'i tshe a tsa ra zhig dang mjal ba na man ngag ci shes kyi gsung dang brda
mdzad pas/ des rgya dpe gang yod gzigs phul shing / khyad par shing shun zhig la sngags btab nas 'bab chur bskur tshe de 'dra tshar nyer lnga tsam la rgyal po dbang du sdud
thub pa'i man ngag yod zer ba lta bus rgya skad dang lag brda zhus 'dug pa ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su sems/ skabs 'dir gnam bskos gong ma bdag po chen po nas sde dge chos
rgyal de la gsol ras su mdzod dngul rta rmig ma nyi shu/ gos yug nyi shu sogs stsal ba/ de'i phud lta bur rta rmig ma gcig rjes gnang zhig gi skabs 'bul bar mdzad de/ rnam
sras kyi rten 'dzugs dang / dmar po skor gsum gyi chos skor sogs mdzad pa'i mthu las kho bo la rgyus med du gong ma chen po'i gsol ras 'di bzhin byung bas de'i phud yin
zhes zhu bar mdzad pas/ skyabs mgon dam pa des spyir rnam thos sras 'di nyid bsten sgrub mdzad pa'i lo paN skyes chen rnams la mthong chos kyi 'bras bu mngon gyur du ma
byung ba med cing / lhag par rang lugs kyi brgyud pa 'di la bco brgyad rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub des rnam thos

sras bran bzhin du bkol bar nus pa de nyid kyi gdams pa rnams rtsa ba'i bla ma rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po des yongs su rdzogs par gsan cing don rnams kyang thugs su chud/
dam pa de'i zhabs drung nas kho bos kyang dbang lung man ngag rnams ma tshang ba med par thob cing / phyag len rnams kyang khong du chud par bgyis pa dang / gtso bor
bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po nyid kyang sngon las bzang pos rjes su 'brel ba'i mthu las yid ches mos gus kyang mchog tu gyur pa sogs rgyu rkyen tshang bas byin rlabs kyi
nus mthu mi 'byung ba ga la yin/ 'on kyang da lam gyi 'di kho bo cag gi mthu las byung ba rang ji ltar lags rung / gzhi nas rten 'brel gyi la nye ni bzang po yin pa 'dug
ces zhu bar mdzad pas/ sde dge chos rgyal de nyid thugs shin tu dgyes par gyur to/ /gzhan yang pho brang bkra shis ltems su sa skyong mchod yon lhan rgyas la rnam thos
sras lnga phrag gsum gyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang / dmar po skor gsum gyi skor yongs rdzogs kyis mtshon pa'i zab chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'bul bar mdzad/ lo 'di nang
du sku gegs 'tshubs lhong lta bus rje nyid kyi yab rgyal po o sgron lags zhe dgu'i dgung keg thog dbus su zhi bar gshegs 'dug cing / de skabs rtsis mgon rgyun gtor gnang
bzhin par thugs dgongs su chos skor ji bzhin thob pa'i nges sbyar med pa'i gtor bsngo 'di'ang dgos pa chung dgongs/ mchod dpon par/ do nub nas bzung rtsis mgon gyi 'bul
gtor sogs bzo mi dgos pheb pa slar dus gnas brtsis bas/ yab rje gshegs

pa'i zla tshes kho nar 'dug ces gsung las thos pa yal yol tsam las ye shes kyi gzigs par chags thogs med pa'i brdar mngon/ chos kyi rgyal po bstan pa tshe ring de ni deng sang
gi dpon skya 'ga' zhig ltar bla ma dang zab chos khyad du bsad pa'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i chos la 'phrog thabs kyi rnam pa ye mi mdzad par yun ring po nas gsol ba 'debs
