pa dang / bla mas zhal gyis bzhes nas kyang dgongs pa dang sbyar ba'i tshul du zhu ba dang / phyag rten gyi dngos po tshun kyang mchog gi dngos grub sgrub byed dang /
gser chos kyi rigs la dngos po gser gyi mtshon pa'i rin thang can dang / thun mong gi rigs la las bzhi'i dgongs pa dang mthun pa'i kha dog dang dbyibs can gyi dngos po 'bul
bar mdzad pa sogs rten 'brel gyi gnad mkhyen cing rnam dbye phyed pas ston pa dang bstan pa la thugs gting nas dad pas gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi rten 'brel la ras
chod mi mdzad pa'i chos kyi rgyal po mtshan dang don du mthun pa zhig yod ces gsungs so/ /sde dge chos kyi rgyal po de'ang lugs gnyis gang la'ang thugs mkhyen dpyod mchog
tu yangs par ma zad/ 'khrul bral bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa la ston dang bstan pa gzhan nas mi 'tshol ba'i yid ches dang
/ lhag par skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di nyid gsang chen kha'u brag rdzong pa'i zab chos spyi dang / khyad par chos skyong che chung gi skor sogs dbang lung man
ngag dang bcas pa rang gzhan gyi grub mtha' spyi dang / bye brag bla chen dregs ldan dag gis spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i zab mo snyan brgyud kyi skor la gzhan

dring mi 'jog pa'i bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chen por thugs nges 'drongs pa'i yid ches bzlog tu med pa'i rgyu dang / sku gsung thugs gsum ngal dub khyad du bsad de dbus gtsang
chu ltar nyul bas yongs 'dzin du ma bsten cing / khyad par rdo rje 'chang rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'i zhabs pad yun ring du bsten par mdzad de chos skyong ba'i srung ma
che chung sogs zab chos rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan cing / bsnyen sgrub rnams kyang gang byung gis chog pa'i babs chol dang bshad yam tsam la thugs yid mi gtod
par/ brgyud ldan gyi man ngag bzhin du mthar phyin par mdzad pas rdo rje nag po chen po'i zhal mngon sum du gzigs shing / yab mes kyi sku dgra 'ga' zhig tshar bcad pa sogs
rtags mtshan mngon sum du ston par mdzad pa'i mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas kyis nye bar len pa'i rkyen mdzad par brten/ dpal
sa skya pa'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi rten gsum brgyud ldan gong ma'i bzhed pa ji bzhin bzhengs par dgongs te/ skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid la snyan gsan zhu bar
mdzad pa na dus la babs par mkhyen nas zhal gyis bzhes te thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i gzungs sngags sogs ring bsrel rnam bzhi/ rten gyi 'khor lo/ thugs rten gnam
lcags kyi rdo rje/ gsang rten gri lcags kyi gwa'u/ seng ldeng gi phur bu sogs nye bar dgos pa'i yo byad rnams kyang ma tshang bar med pa sta gon gyis ljags bsnyen kha gso
dang / bzo bo rnams la rgyu dbang / mgon po che chung gi rjes gnang sogs gnang / phrin bcol gyi bskang ba nan tan mdzad/

rgya bod kyi gnas chen du ma'i sa sna/ rdo sna/ rin po che dang / 'bru sna/ sman sna/ dam rdzas khyad can du ma bsres pa'i 'jim pa la byin gyis brlabs/ bzo bo rnams la sbyong
khrus/ las thams cad pa'i khro bor bskyed bstim gyi rgyun bsnyen dang / lag cha byin gyis brlabs pa sogs sngon du 'gro bas bag med ces pa chu glang lo'i nang du zla tshes
mtshan ldan la rus shing 'dzugs par mdzad de/ rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lcam dral lha brgyad/ dpal mgon bram gzugs/ beg tse lcam sring gsum/ nor skyong dur
khrod gyi bdag po yab yum/ 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje/ phur srung dkar bdud lcam dral/ ru 'dren sde bzhi rnams kyi lder sku khyad du 'phags par bsgrub pa'i bka' bkod
dang / sbyong ba bgegs skrod kyang yang yang mdzad cing / de dag gi gnas skabs su pho brang gi nye skor du mi bsad mang bas/ zhal bzhi pa'i rten rdo'i man ngag las/ mi gsod
myong ba/ bong thung / mdog nag can dgos pa'ang 'bad med du 'grub pa ni bstan srung chen po 'di nyid kyi cho 'phrul dang / nor skyong yab yum gyi sku brnyan bzhengs skabs
bzo bo dbu mdzad nor bu zer ba 'dred brdabs lta bu'i rkyen la brten brla rkang chag pa sogs 'tshubs lhong gi rnam pa che'ang gegs med du 'grub par thun mong dang thun
mong ma yin pa'i gzungs kyi rim pa zhabs 'og gi linggas mtha' brten pa rnams gong ma'i yi ge dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa'i gsung sgros
las ji ltar byung ba bzhin nan tan mdzad/ de'ang tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ drug ldan rten gyi tshogs rnams legs gshams te/ /rnam

gsum dmar chen gtor mas phur bur gtams/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ chos skyong ba'i srung ma'i dbang po rnams 'go zhing chags par byed pa'i thabs mchog sku gsung thugs dang / phyi
nang gsang gsum sogs kyi rten rnams tshang ba zhig dgos pa rten 'brel gyi che ba yin zhing / sa skyong chos kyi rgyal po dpon blon rnams kyang byas so ba'i mi chos tsam
gyis rjes su 'brang ba'i rgyu med kyi 'bras bu 'dod pa rnams dang mi 'dra bar/ dbang rnon chos rjes 'brang ba'i yid ches dang / gtong phod kyi snying stobs dang brtson
pa phul du byung bas ji ltar dgos pa'i yo byad rnams kyang phongs pa med par stsal zhing / rje bla ma rnam gnyis dang / bla mchan dge slong kun dga' dpal 'byor/ mchod dpon
dge slong kun dga' grags pa gnyis kyi zhabs 'degs bgyis te/ gsang ba'i rnga chung tsam ma gtogs rten yongs su rdzogs pa rgyu tshad tshang zhing phun sum tshogs pa rnams
la sgrub pa'ang nan tan mdzad/ rnam gsum gtor ma'i tshogs kyang gong ma'i yi ge dang man ngag las byung ba bzhin gtor sgrub dang bcas rgyas par mdzad/ de dag la sngags 'chang
mgul rgyan dang / rten gyi zhal bzhes thun mong ma yin pa sogs la brgyud pa'i man ngag gis brgyan pa'i rab tu gnas pa thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag bzhes 'khrul med du
mdzad pa sogs/ sa skyong chos kyi rgyal po de nyid bstan pa rin po che spyi sgos kyi yon bdag gzhan dang mi 'dra zhing / khyad par rje nyid la'ang mi phyed pa'i dad gdung
mnga' ba sogs rgyu du mas/ thugs ngal khyad du bsad de phyis kyi spyan ltos la phan nges shes pa mdzad pa yin no/ /'di lo yon

bdag chen po dpon blon gyi dgongs bzhed ltar bum gter mang du bsgrubs par mdzad de/ rdzong sgo khag la 'gyed par mdzad pas lo tog phun sum tshogs par byung bas/ dpon 'bangs
kun dga' mgu yi rang gi sa la 'god par mdzad/ de dag gi snga phyir chos rje bkra shis bzang po'i drung nas/ kye rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang / bde mchog nag po pa/ mkha'
'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang lung dang / kun rig gi dbang zhig kyang gsan pa/ bka' las/ de skabs gnas nyer gnyis so so'i ming re smos pa dang sngags rgya res gtugs pa spel mar
mdzad pa sogs shin tu yid ches pa byung gsung zhing / rje de nyid ni mkhan thog tu pheb min gyi khyad par las ngor gyi mkhan chen zhig dang mnyam zhes thugs dad shin tu
che bar gnang / mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub las sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad skor bcas
kyi dbang rnams gsan/ pho brang lhun grub steng duu sa skyong dpon blon dang bla ma khag rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i skal ldan gyi gdul bya ches mang ba la/ grub pa'i dbang
phyug chen po a bhA ya ka ra'i bzhed gzhung rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis/ darpan a tsArYa'i bzhed srol kr-i ya'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum ste
zhe lnga'i dbang rnams kyang rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyis rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyi drung nas phreng ba'i dbang tshar bcu gsan
pa'i phyag bzhes ltar rgyas par 'bul bar mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ sa bstan bdag po sa dbang sde dges mchod/ /dus 'khor la sogs

dus der chos char phab/ /chos srung rten btsugs chos srid gnyer gtad mdzad/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon rnam dkar phrin las yin/ /zhes so/ /de nas re zhig sa skyong chos kyi rgyal
po blon 'bangs dang bcas pa'i thugs dgongs de tsam gyis rdzogs par mdzad nas/ dbus ljongs chos kyi chol khas mngon par mtho ba'i phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bskyod pa'i sgo
dod/ 'di skabs bka' 'gyur rin po che'i mjug skyong phran tshegs ma grub par/ gsung rab grub nas zhu rgyur/ bslu yon ja 'khor drug brgya dang lnga bcu/ yar lam gyi khal
mdzo dgu sga bcas/ lag do'i za mgo bcas dang / glegs thag a lung la tshags kyi rgyu gser srang gang bcas 'jog pa gnang / sa skyong mchog nas rin thang can gyi dngos po brgya
phrag gsum lhag gi pheb rdzong 'bul skyes dang / dad ldan gyi grwa bu slob blon 'bangs dang bcas pas kyang pheb rdzong 'bul nod rgyas par bstar te/ mchod yon lhan rgyas
pho brang chen po lhun grub steng nas chibs bskyod de/ bkra shis ltems su phyags pheb nas kyang pheb rdzong du dngos po rnam par dag pa sum brgya lhag pa sogs 'bul bar
mdzad cing / sa skyong chen po de ni yang srid mang por yon gyi gnas dam pa rnams bsu ba dang skyel ba sogs la mngon par go mas pa'i shugs las/ rgyal thabs kyi snyems pa
yongs su btang ste/ rgyal blon 'bangs dang bcas pa rnams kyis sri zhu chen pos 'bri chu'i bar skyel thung mdzad/ sa skyong mchog nas slar yang yun ha cang mi ring ba nyid
du ljongs 'di'i skye rgu rnams kyi bsod nams kyi mgron du 'byon par mdzod cig ces zhu bar

mdzad pas/ yul dus kyi skal bar ma gyur na de bzhin du bya'o zhes zhal gyis 'ches nas bsrung ba dang shis pa brjod par mdzad de/ grub dbang mtshungs med dam pa sangs rgyas
rgya mtsho dang / zhabs 'bring du mngags pa'i tshong dpon sbe tshogs dang / sbe go gnyis dang bcas pa rnams kyis chu bo chen po rba rlabs kyi lteng ka g.yo ba mig gis kyang
blta bar mi bzod pa de las pha rol tu gshegs pa'i zhabs 'gyur yang dag pa'i skad cig la gdan 'dren zhus te/ byang lam nas rim bzhin 'phen yul nA lendrar pheb/ bco brgyad
nas chos rje rin po ches pheb bsu sne len yang dag dang / phar yang pheb skyes 'bul nod rgyas par mdzad/ rim bzhin gangs can 'dzin ma'i lte ba lha ldan 'phrul snang gi
'dabs su phyags pheb ste gzims khang lhun grub dpal khang zhes bya bar gtan chags/ jo shAka rnam pa gnyis sogs ngo mtshar rten mchog rnams la mchod 'bul dang / dpal mi'i
dbang po yab sras rnams la 'bul nod gya nom pa dang bcas te mjal phyag mdzad/ thugs dges pa'i gsung gis gzengs bstod dang / zang zing gi gnang skyes kyang stsal/ rgod dkar
la brgyud de bsam yas su pheb/ chos skyong chen por lha tshes sngon ma'i skabs mjal 'phrad mdzad rgyu'i snyan gsan dge slong bkra shis rab brtan nas zhus pas blang dor
sngon ma'i don ltar stag lor dge bshes dang ngos 'phrad skyong zhes gsungs pas shar rgyag yar klung du pheb/ 'dus pa'i tshogs la mang 'gyed gya nom pa dang / sngar phyag
mdzod lhun grub kun dga'i gdong du rgyun ja'i thebs su sbyor 'jags gnang rgyu dngul srang brgya'i steng du

srang nyis brgya dang drug cu gnang bar tshong rgyag rtsis kyi/ bang rin dngul srang sum cu/ sga cha 'grigs bcu phrag sogs tshong chas dang bcas pa sbyor 'jags gnang / rdo
rje'i chos srung rnams la gtang rag gi mchod gtor dang / zhabs drung yab gshegs pa'i gnas tshul khams su bzhugs skabs ma gsan pas/ de skabs yab kyi dgongs rdzogs su dmigs
yar 'phyong gnyis kyi dgon pa che phra mtha' dag dang / spus ri skor gyi chu lho byang gi sa dgon phal cher la mang ja/ sbyor sbrel bsngo rten/ gal che ba rnams la spyi
'gyed bcas dang / gnas chen rnams la mchod 'bul mdzad/ kun dga' zhes pa shing stag lo gsar tshes kyi dus ston kyang rgyas par gnang / grub dbang dam pa sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i
zhal snga nas dang / bla ma kun dga' rgya mtsho sogs bka' 'gyur gyi lung kho na don gnyer gyis byon pa rnams la gzims chung du rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che'i lung
yongs su rdzogs par mdzad/ chu stod zla nang yar 'brog brgyud gtsang du chibs bskyod/ gro bzhin bcu bzhi'i nyin 'dar grong chen dang khad nye chu gling na khar bzhugs
zhag thog nas jo tshed ja sngon 'gros la gnang ste/ sang nyin gro bzhin bco lngar tshar chen bla ma'i sku mchod thog gdan sar 'ong rgyu'i gra bsgrigs dgos tshul pheb pa
ltar/ brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang de nyid sogs 'dus tshogs tshang mas dang len zhus te/ grwa tshang gis ser sbreng / chibs bsu/ 'dar khul sbyin bdag rnams kyis kyang chibs bsu
dang bcas bco lnga'i snga dro gangs ri'i khrod kyi skad gnyis smra ba yongs kyi gtsug rgyan bla chen 'brog mi lo tsA ba la sogs

pas byin gyis brlabs shing / mkhas pa'i dbang po g.yag ston sangs rgyas dpal ba la sogs pa mkhas grub dam pa du ma'i bsti gnas su mdzad pa'i chos grwa chen po 'dar smad gnas
nang las mched pa 'dar stod chos 'khor yang rtser/ ma byon rnam 'dren gsum pa rgyal ba rab gsal de nyid gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bsam bzhin du skye ba'i cho 'phrul ston
par mdzad pa/ nges don bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bzhugs gdan seng khri la zhabs zung gser gyi 'khor
lo bkod de/ legs byas kyi sngon 'gror dge tshogs rnam mkhyen du bsngo ba'i tshul gyis gsung bshad rgyas shing mtha' chod par stsal/ gzhung sa mchog dang 'di kha nas kyang
bsko 'ja'/ khri 'gyed sogs dang / gzhan yang 'dus sde spyi sgos rnams dang / bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po 'dar nas sogs ser skya mchog dman rnams nas rang rang gi 'byor
tshogs ji snyed yod pa rnams legs skyes su bstar zhing / bla brang nas mang ja'i thog grwa pa lnga rer ja bag re/ dgon lag sgrub sde gnyis la'ang mang ja'i thog btsun ma
bcu rer ja bag re/ grong chen 'du khang du bla re che legs/ rgya sbub bkra shis 'brug sgra rnams stsal zhing / thog mar tshar chen rin po che'i rdo khri'i steng nas mdo
sde bskal bzang gi ljags lung dang / tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo/ mgon dkar phyag drug pa/ rnam sras rta bdag brgyad/ dur khrod bdag po rnams kyi rjes gnang stsal/ sang
nyin bzhugs khrir pheb rgyu'i nub mnal ltas su dung gi seng ge shin tu dkar ba zhig gi kha nas skyugs pa 'dra ba'i

de'i tho phyi kun tu khrag mang po 'thor pas chag chag btab pa ltar 'dug ces gsungs pa ni gsung rab dgongs 'grel snyan brgyud dang bcas pa smra ba'i seng ge chen po 'di nyid
kyis gnas 'dir zab chos thang mar brdal ba'i mtshan ltas yang dag par gor ma chag snyam zhing / bla chen 'brog mi'i mnal lam bka' rgya ma dang phyogs mtshungs tsam du'ang
go nus so/ /zla ba de'i mjug tu grong chen dus rim pa dpon slob dang chab cig 'di khar chibs kha bsgyur te yab rje mtshungs med dam pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin
chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal dkyil la longs su spyod pa'i legs skyes su gser srang gsum dang / rta drel sogs kyi dngos po spom stod pa dang
/ khyad du 'phags pa'i rten mchog rnam bzhi/ skyed lhas/ byas 'gyur sogs la mchod 'bul smon lam dang / chos dung rin po che gsung bskul sogs mdzad/ tshe dbang 'chi med dpal
ster/ 'byung po 'dul byed dang / mkha' 'gro lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / 'jam mgon bla ma'i zab mo sku'i dkyil 'khor du lam dus kyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub pa'i rgyun yang
dag par bzhes/ kom 'dre brgyud de mang mkhar thub bstan dge 'phel gyi gnas rten rnams la mchod 'bul dang / 'dus pa'i tshogs la mang 'gyed sogs phun sum tshogs par mdzad/
mar lam rmu mgon khang du mchod gsol phrin bcol mdzad cing / chos skyong gi sku mdun du gsol dpon lhun grub rab brtan sna khrag mang du gzegs te yun ring phro 'tshal
ba dam tshig gi nyes par sems/ 'dar bsam 'grub tu gdan 'dren dang

bsnyen bkur 'bul nod yang dag mdzad thog /khong tshor tshe dbang sogs 'dod chos kha yar stsal/ slar yang 'dar stod chos 'khor yang rtse nyid du gtan chags shing / brag rtsa
rdo rje 'chang sogs la/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal/ tshe dpag med dkar po/ sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrags/ zhal sgrub dus thun mong ba rnams dang / rgyal phur 'dzom nyin tshogs
bdag thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i sgrol dkar sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang / sbyin sreg /gong sa lnga pa chen po'i sgrol dkar la brten pa'i brtan
bzhugs kyi lung sogs zab chos mang du gsungs/ zla ba dgu pa'i nang du 'dar nas chibs bskyod cing ra sa brgyud de ngor gyi gnas gzigs dang / mchod 'bul/ mang ja sogs mdzad
cing spo 'bor sgong zhes par bzhugs/ de skabs e waM gyi gdan sa 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong yin zhing / shangs len bkur bzos yang dag par mdzad/ khyad par thams cad
mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum dbus su g.yar po 'bul ba gnang bar/ thugs shin tu dgyes pas de'i gnas tshul rjes sor yang yang yang gsungs/ thar rtse rdo
rje 'chang chen po dang yang zhal rgyas pas phu dud dang / bkur sti phan tshun 'gran pa ltar mdzad de/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos las brtsams pa'i gsung gsang legs bshad thar pa'i
snying po can yang ci dgar 'jo zhing / khyad par rje nyid nas grub dbang de nyid la lam dus skabs kyi dka' gnad cig la bka' 'dri zhus gnang la/ de skabs thugs tshom mer
lus pa 'dra zhig la/ sang nyin de'i lan rgyas

par zhu sam du gnang ba'i bstan bcos khyad par can yang yod/ 'di la rjes sor bka' las/ kho bos dri ba de min zhig la zhus pa de ni kho bo rang lta mtshems pa las bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang gi yi ger shin tu gsal bar 'dug /rje de nyid kyi dris lan de'ang legs bshad sngon med ngo mtshar can zhig byung 'dug gsungs/ zhwa lu sogs su re ba bzhed kyang
chos sde dang ri bo chos gling gnyis rtsod gzhi phran bu byung bar gdan 'dren gyi bang phyin 'byor ba gnas gsar du 'khyug tsam las/ gzhan ma shar rgyag yar klung du pheb/
thugs kyi dgongs gzhir 'jam mgon blo gsal mchog ldan sogs gong ma 'ga' zhig sku tshe mthar ma phyin pa dang / lhag par sgrub pa kho na la thugs gzhol ba'i da cha sde
dgon gyi 'dzin skyong yang chos kyi gegs rkyen lta bur ma zad/ chos sde rang la'ang phugs dge slebs che khyad mdzod par bka' bgros mdzad nas/ dpon g.yog gnyis nas thugs
thag bcad de mkhan sa slob dpon du phab/ bla gzhis grwa tshang du sbyar chog pa sogs kyis mi dbang chen por snyan sbron mdzad par/ gzhan mtho dman phal cher sa cha phar zhu
ba'i skabs su bla gzhis grwa tshang du sbyar chog pa zhu bar mdzad pa la mi dbang chen po'ang rjes su yi rang ste/ gzhan ma dgongs bzhed ltar los 'ong ste/ bkra shis chos
sde pa rang gi bya ba rlabs chen yin 'dug gzhis kho bos kyang blos dpyad mi nus pas/ jo shAg sku mdun du brtag sgril byas pa'i don bzhin 'ong tshul gsungs pa/ brtags
par yang babs pa bcas/ 'di lo ston steng nas bzung / bla gzhis gsar rnying gi sa ris bdag

thob shas bgos/ mo bran sogs tshang ma grwa tshang du 'bul sbyor gnang ba'i lo bstar cho 'phrul zla bar bka' 'gyur gsung sgrogs nyin gsum re dang / chog mang nyin bzhi re 'phar
ba dang / chos 'chad slob dpon gnyis la skal 'phar re dang / lo bstar phog 'phar khal bcu re bcas 'ong ba'i bka' khyab gnang / sde dge'i gnyer chen bstan pa bzang po
dang / drung yig tshe ring 'phel gnyis dbus gtsang du dge rtsa gtos chen bsgrub bar 'byor zhing / de skabs sde dge chos kyi rgyal po bstan pa tshe ring de nyid nas 'dir
mchod rten 'ga' zhig bzhengs 'dod la dri med rnam gnyis kyi dbang lung dang phyag len rnams dgos par sngon zhus bzhin skyabs mgon dam pa nyid mdo khams su cis kyang pheb
dgos tshul bka' shog gsung ngag dang bcas pa nan tan gnang ba 'byor/ tshong dpon 'bum skyabs gdong sngon nas bslu yon sogs phul tshar ba'i spar phud gras kyi bka' 'gyur rin
po che dngos gtsang ba 'byor bar mdzod pa ngo mas lha ldan nas gdan 'dren mdzad/ bzang gos kyi gdong dar/ glegs shing / glegs thag /kun dga' ra ba sogs gsar bzo rab gnas
dang bcas par mdzad de/ tshar gcig gsung sgrogs dang bcas bkra shis chos sder sbyor 'jags mdzad/ ston mjug lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ ra ba mthil du gtan chags/ rmor chen
chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi thugs sras dam pa mdo sngags rab 'byams smra ba 'phags sde mkhan chen ngag dbang blo gsal bstan 'dzin gyi drung nas/ tshad mas kun las btus
pa/ rnam 'grel/ rnam nges/ rig thig /gtan tshigs thigs pa/ 'grel rtag /rgyud

gzhan grub pa/ rtsod rigs / mngon pa kun las btus/ mdzod rtsa/ so thar gyi mdo/ mdo rtsa/ me thog phreng brgyud/ sum brgya pa/ de'i rang 'grel 'od ldan/ ka ri ka lnga bcu pa/
bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan/ mdo sde rgyan/ rgyud bla ma/ chos nyid rnam 'byed/ dbus mtha' rnam 'byed/ dbu ma rtsa ba shes rab/ rigs tshogs/ bstod tshogs/ gtam
tshogs/ dbu ma bzhi brgya pa/ 'jug pa/ spyod 'jug /byang sa/ bslab btus/ mdo kun las btus pa/ skyes rabs so bzhi pa/ bskal bzang gi sangs rgyas stong gi phyag 'tshal/
skyes rabs dpag bsam 'khri shing / phar phyin gyi 'grel pa don gsal/ tshad ma rigs gter/ sdom gsum rab dbye/ pha chos/ bu chos/ bka' gdams thor bu/ rin spungs skor gsum/
sum pa lo tsA ba'i blo sbyong gi nyams khrid/ klu dbang gi rgyal po lha lnga'i rjes gnang / gdugs dkar skor gyi yi ge mang po'i lung / dri med rnam pa gnyis kyi dbang lung
tshang ma/ rnam rgyal lha dgu'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ rdo rje nag po chen po gyi ljang lugs kyi chos skor tshang ma'i lung / lha mo dud sol ma'i rjes gnang dang lung tshang
ma/ gser chos seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i o rgyan bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang gsol 'debs le'u tshan sogs dang / gnubs
ston rig 'dzin chen po blo bzang don grub kyi drung nas/ byang gter thugs sgrub drag po rtsal gyi chos skor phal cher gong sa lnga pa'i gsan yig bzhin gyi lung / spu brag
bla chen legs pa

don 'grub las rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'i drung nas ma gsan pa'i 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi yi ge 'ga' zhig gi lung / bka' 'gyur ba rin chen dam chos las/ 'dul ba'i las chog
/rnam rgyal gser mdog sogs gong sa lnga pa'i bka' 'bum kha shas/ mi la bzhad pa rdo rje'i 'gur 'bum/ rnam thar sogs kyi lung dang snyan ngag gi phyag khrid sogs zhu bar
mdzad/ snga sor chos sder dgu mtha' gsan skabs slob dpon thugs yul dogs pas 'bul ma shes pa'i skyon gyis ma mkhyen par/ 'dir bka' 'gyur ba'i bka' las/ brtag zhu tshor dbyangs
'char gyi ri mo de gnang na khyad che 'ong pheb par/ de la dgu mtha' mi shes pa 'dug zhus pas/ de la dka' tshegs med ces/ gong du gcig 'phar bcur 'gyur te/ /zhes sogs
kyi rigs pas nas 'bru spungs nas brda ston tsam mdzad pas ri mor ma ltos par dgu mtha' yongs rdzogs tshegs med du mkhyen cing / phyis gzhan la phyag khrid gnang ba'i tshe'ang
blo la 'char bde zhing rtogs sla ba zhig byung ba ni/ skad cig gcig la chos rnams thugs su chud/ /ces pa der snang / snga lo nas snyan sbron grub pa bzhin 'di lo mkhan
sa slob dpon du phab pa dang bla gzhis chos gzhis tshang mar rgyab bsnon gyi gtan tshigs kyang zhu bar mdzad/ sde dge nas mi dbang chen por yang skyabs mgon 'di nyid
khams su pheb dgos kyi bka' khyab dang mgo 'dren rnams kyang brtse gzigs dgos tshul nan tan zhu bar mdzad pas/ mi dbang chen po nas kyang cis kyang mdo khams su pheb dgos
kyi bka' gnang

ba ltar mdo smad du pheb pa'i sgo dod de/ yar klung du pheb/ bkra shis chos kyi sder gsang chen 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis rje btsun yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgo nas zhabs pad brtan
par gsol ba 'debs pa'i cho ga rgyas par mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ mdo khams bder bkod dbus gtsang bsti gnas gshegs/ /rten gsum mchod cing 'dar grong gdan sar bzhugs/
/mdo sngags rigs gnas gsan zhing phan dgongs mdzad/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon thugs bskyed rmad byung yin/ /zhes so/ /de nas/ zla ba drug pa'i nyer dgu gza' tshes phun sum
tshogs pa'i nyin ser skya mchog dman mang pos mdun bdar te/ slar yang mdo smad phyogs kyi bstan 'gro'i don chen sgrub pa'i thugs bskyed rmad du byung bas chibs kyi kha
lo bsgyur ro/ /de nub sger par bzhugs/ rim bzhin bsam yas su bzhugs/ grub dbang bla ma kun dga' tshul khrims zhes rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gi zhal slob stan thog gcig tu
mkha' spyod ma'i ljags bsnyen la lo bco lnga bzhugs shing / me rlung gi nus stobs rgyas pa sogs nyams rtogs kyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab cing sku lus kyang smug 'ber rnal
'byor dbang phyug birWa pa lta bu zhig bzhugs pas de nyid mjal ba dang / gtsug lag khang yongs su rdzogs pa'i gnas gzigs dang mchod 'bul rgyas par mdzad/ tshes gnyis kyi
nub mo 'od gsal gyi ngang la shel brag gi rgyab ri dang mnyam pa'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po thang stong rgyal po'i sku shin tu che zhing brjid pa zhig zhal gzigs
shing / de'i sku'i cha thams cad la nu 'bur shin tu mang bar

'gro ba du mas nu ba bzhin rje de nyid kyis kyang sku g.yon gyi nu ma bzhos pas grub dbang de'i zhal nas/ khyed kyi sku tshe'i tshad lnga bcu nga bdun yin/ lam 'bras tshar
bdun gsungs shig dang bstan 'gro la phan thogs par 'gyur ro/ /zhes dang / rab byung gi bslab pa byang sgo sems bskyed gling gi gtso bo ma chags padma can la phul te rab tu
byung ba'i rtags rnams bor nas rnal 'byor spyod pa'i cha byad bzung na sku tshe mdzad phrin mtha' rgyas su 'gro tshul sogs dang / de ltar ma byung na lo gsum nas sku tshe'i
bar chad du 'gro tshul gyi lung bstan shin tu mang ba dang / ni guu ma'ang 'dir yod gsungs/ gzigs pas yum drung gi sku rgyan sogs ji lta ba gsal bar gzigs/ rje de nyid
kyi bka' las/ phyi nub bla ma mkha' 'gro yi/ /lung bstan yid ches du ma byung / /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ ni gu ma des kyang lung bstan shin tu mang bar mdzad dam snyam yang
/ skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid sba ba kho na lhur mdzad gshis bsnyel tho tsam yang mi snang zhing / zhal slob kyi gsung rgyun 'dra'ang ma thos/ de ltar lung bstan gyi don
ltar mdzad na sku 'di nyid kyi sku tshe sogs kyang mthar 'khyol dang / mdzad phrin gong 'phel du 'gyur bar ma zad/ sa lam gyi yon tan skad cig tsam gyis rdzogs pa sogs
dgos pa mchog tu che'ang / tshur mthong gi skye bo rnams ya ga dang sgro skur gyi yul dam pa la smad pa'i nyes pa chen po gsog par dgongs nas/ bdag bas gzhan gces kyi thugs
rlabs chen bskyed de rten 'brel gyi sna sel du snam sbyar dang lhung bzed byang sgo sems bskyed gling du 'bul ba dang / sku chos sogs rab byung

chas 'ga' zhig rab byung grwa tshang gi tshogs su spong thag dang / kha btags zhig rnal 'byor spyod pa'i dod du sku la dkri bar mdzad do/ /grub thob chen po'i lung bstan 'di
gnas gsar ba'i sku brgyud/ gangs ljongs bde thabs su yun ring gnas pa zhig byung na da dung mkhas grub kyi phreng ba zam ma chad par byon nas rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye
brag sa rnying gi bstan pa la shin tu khyad che bar 'ong yod 'dug kyang / spyi bye brag gi gdul bya'i bsod nams kyi skal ba der bas so/ /tshes gsum nyin gnas srung chos
skyong chen po khog tu rlom par mjal phrad mdzad par grub thob chen po'i lung bstan gyi dgongs pa ltar rten gzhi 'dul bar 'tshubs kyang / skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid kyi
thugs bskyed rlabs po che la chos skyong yang rjes su yi rang te/ rten gzhir 'tshubs kyang rten gsar los yod de/ /da lta'i lhag bsam rlabs chen skyong ba dang / /zhes sogs
kyi bsngags brjod dbugs dbyung dang / lha rdzas srid du ring ba dbu sdom dang bcas pa phul zhing blang dor gyi lung bstan mang po dang / gzhis byes kun tu mi 'bral bar
bka'i phrin las sgrub par zhal gyis 'ches/ rab byung grwa tshang gi mkhan slob 'dus tshogs dang bcas pas tshe dpag med lha dgu'i sgo nas zhabs brtan gyi gsung chog dang
'brel ba'i 'bul nod kyang gzabs rgyas mdzad/ de nas lha ldan du chos skyong gi lung bzhin jo shAka rnam gnyis sogs dang / 'bras spungs sngags khang / gnas chung lcog rnams
la mchod 'bul phrin bcol rnams dang / gong sa mchod yon gyi mjal

phyag sogs mdzad/ chos sde'i lam thog skor gyi bka' shog cig zhu bar gnang rgyur/ mi dbang nas sde dge bstan pa tshe ring dang nged gnyis ma mthong ba'i grogs po byas shing
/ nged pho lha tha'i ji'i bya ba la yin par 'dzin pa bstan pa tshe ring ma gtogs ma byung bas snying nye gshis bla ma khams nas pheb 'phral la yang bskyar pheb dgos u tshugs
zhus pas thugs mi mnyes pa byung med dam zhes gsungs par/ dam pa de nyid kyi kho bo la bsam rgyu bstan 'gro'i don las med gshis sde dgon 'di tsho nyams nyes kyi dogs
pa tsam las/ gzhan ma 'gro don phrin las skyong bar 'gro rgyur mi dga' ba ga la 'ong zhes zhu bar gnang bar/ dgon pa rnams nas gnas tshul rgyu mtshan byung phyin mgo 'dren
yang dag byed ces zhal gyis bzhes shing / da lam bka' shog kyang she bam rang 'bul gsungs nas gnang zhing / mjug tu 'ong mgo 'dren yang dag gnang 'dug /byang lam brgyud
de ra sgreng gi gnas gzigs sogs mdzad/ chos skyong gi lung du/ yang gcig mi mngon dbyings nas bya ra byas/ /bdun pa'i mjug dang brgyad pa'i mgo zhig la/ /lung pa chu gsum
'dzoms pa'i gnas gcig tu/ /nges par 'tshubs pas pe har rgyal po gsol/ /chu gsum 'dzoms pa'i ri yi shar phyogs su/ /shing nags 'tshubs cing 'dre ngan gnas pa'i sa/ /brag
ri bya rog 'dra ba lnga yod par/ /so so'i cod pan lo grangs btsugs na bzang / /zhes gsungs par/ shar chu kha zer ba der ri chu shing sogs ji lta ba bzhin 'dug par/ lung
pa'i phur ser ba chen po babs pas chu glo bur du rgyas te rab la pheb mi thub pa tsam byung bar/ gsol mchod rnams rgyas par mdzad pas brag ri'i rtser bya rog cig babs pas
skad drag po 'byin pa

dang chu 'phral du bri ste pheb rab shin tu bde/ chu 'gram du sde dge tshong dpon gyi lag do chu thig zer ba steng grib kyi rnam pas 'das pa sogs 'tshubs nyams che'ang skyabs
mgon rdo rje 'chang dpon g.yog tshang mar nyes skyon med par bde bar pheb pa bla ma chos srung gi che bar mngon/ khra bo thang du pheb bsu ba gnyer chen lha bu tshe ring
dpon g.yog chibs rkyang po shin tu bzang ba dang bcas par 'byor/ sku zhor du lha khang gsar pa'i rab gnas gnang dgos tshul gsungs/ de nas sde dge'i bka' bzhin 'bri chu
rgyud du dung mtha' dgon gyi lha khang gsar bzhengs la rab tu gnas pa rgyas par mdzad de/ sa skyong chen pos bsu ba'i bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas te lugs gnyis
kyi 'dun sa pho brang chen po dngul mda' lhun grub steng du phyags pheb/ de nyin rang chos rgyal chen po de nyid dang mjal phrad mdzad de/ rgyal yum rdo rje btsun mo'i snang
brnyan li ma khyad 'phags dang / zhal dkar/ khri rdo/ yul babs dang mthun pa'i snam ther sogs legs mjal 'bul nod rgyas par mdzad de/ chos rgyal de nyid thugs dgyes pa'i
rtser son no/ /sa skyong mchog nas kyang pheb lam du bde bar phebs pa'i legs 'bul rgyas shing spus dag par mdzad/ sde dge chos rgyal de nyid sngon gyi bag chags sad pa
lta bu'i rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa 'di'i bsnyen pas thugs 'phrogs te grwa tshang la cho ga grwa 'dzugs pa dang / sde dge nyid nas kyang bka' dbang
gsan pa'i sta gon gyi nub sa skyong chen po'i mnal lam du ma he 'dra ba'i sems can zhig gis rgyab tu

khyer nas 'dam rdzab mang po brgal te ne'u gseng me tog dang bcas pa'i gnas shig tu pheb pa'i mnal ltas kyis thugs dad cher g.yos te dbang brgya gsan bzhed bcas la de kha'i
snyan gsan gnang ba bzhin zhal gyis bzhes shing / bsam yas chos skyong chen pos/ 'bras spungs sngags khang mchod 'bul ngos kyis mdzod gsung ba 'jigs byed kyi 'gro don 'byung
bar dgongs pa yin snang ngo / /der zab chos nyer mkho kha shas dang / de nas 'jigs byed dbang brgya 'dzugs pa gnang ste/ 'di lo lnga bcu tsam rdzogs mtshams su/ sbrul
lo'i mgo nas bzung sa skyong chen pos tsandan dkar dmar las grub pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod rten brgyad dpangs tshad thog so phyed gnyis tsam shin tu spus gtsang ba
bzhengs par mdzad pa'i gzungs dang bzo bkod sogs dang bar rnams su dpon blon so so'i dgongs bzhed ltar chos bka' yang mang du 'bul bar mdzad/ bzo rnams phal cher grub nas
zla ba drug pa'i tshes bzhi la sa chog dang / bdun nas gzungs 'bul gyi dbu 'dzugs pa gnang ste/ dri med rnams gnyis kyi sgrub mchod shin tu rgyas pa dang / chos rgyal dpon
blon rnams la rigs gtad kyang mdzad cing / gzungs 'bul gyi rim pa rnams skyabs mgon mchog kho nas sku ngal dub khyad du bsad de 'bul tshul go rim ma 'khrugs shing phyag
'tshags dam pa sogs dang / rdor dkar sogs brgyud ldan gong ma'i phyag bzhes phra mo tshun chad kyang ma nyams par phyis kyi mig ltos la phan nges shes pa mdzad pas chos
kyi rgyal po de nyid ni dbang rnon chos rjes 'brang ba las cal sgrog gi brtul zhugs mi 'dzin pas byas

pa don ldan du song zhes thugs shin tu tshim par gyur to/ /ston mjug nas bzung 'jigs byed dbang brgya'i 'phros dang / tshe dpag dbang brgya sogs 'bul ba gnang / rta lo zla
ba gnyis pa'i nang du chos rgyal bstan pa tshe ring sku khams cung zad ltem par/ dmar chen gtor zlog sogs sku rim rgyun mi 'chad dang / sngon nas bzhengs gnang gi bde gshegs
mchod rten brgyad dang sku tshad mnyam zhing sku rgyu zhe mtshungs kyi rnam rgyal mchod rten gcig gsar bzhengs dang / 'di rnams la rab gnas skabs su chos rgyal de nyid
myur du zhi bar gshegs pa'i mi dge ba'i ltas su mi ngas sna tshogs shig byung 'dug kyang / gnas lugs bshad na skur ba'i rgyur mchis so/ /der dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi dbang
sogs 'bul ba gnang / lo de'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes gsum la sa skyong de nyid sku zhi bar gshegs pa'i thugs dam gsal 'debs/ sbyin sreg /zhe dgu 'dzin pa/ rus chog /sAtstsha
zhes bod skad dam pa'i gzugs te sA tsha dang tsha tsha sogs sgra nyams pa yin zhes mkhas pa rnams gsung / gang ltar tshwa chog /gdung khang / dngul gdung gi zhal bkod/
gzungs dang rab gnas rnams mdzad cing / chos rgyal de nyid kyi dgongs bzhed ltar lcags ra bsam 'grub rtse dang / rmad shod rdzong gsar dgon gnyis su so sor 'dus pa nyis
brgya brgal ba la rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang dang lung / phyag len gyi bslab sbyong sogs yang dag dang / dgon so sor grwa pa bdun cu skor
res rwa chen gyi mngon rtogs/ tshar chen

yab sras gnyis kyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs/ dkyil chog /lhan thabs dang bcas pa blo 'dzin gnang ba'i sgrub mchod tshar lugs kyi phyag len ji lta ba bzhin 'dzugs pa dang /
de bar bum 'dzin du pheb/ sgrub mchod 'dzugs nye'i skabs dgon chen nas rmad shod kyi bar la glang gi skad 'dra ba yang yang sgrogs pa kun gyis thos pa byung zhes rmad shod
bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho nas gleng / bsam yas chos skyong gi lung du/ mtha' bzhi'i yul du lug rta gang rigs su/ /nges par bsdu ba'i rten 'brel che na yang / /zhes sogs
gsungs pa'i lung gsal gyi zhabs brtan sku rim rnams bsgrubs zin kyang / sku nyen dogs che bar sbrul lo dang rta lo gnyis su'ang / tshe chog stong tshar drug tsam dang /
sgrol sher/ bsam pa lhun grub ma sogs khri phrag mang po/ chos srung la bskang ba sogs sku rim mang du mdzad/ lug lor lhun grub steng du mnga' zhabs la 'grims rgyu'i bum
gter mang po sgrub gnang la tshur mthong gi snang ngor sku 'khrugs lta bu'i sku ltem babs shin tu lci bar/ zhabs brtan sku rim du sde dge'i mnga' zhabs kyi dgon pa yongs
su rdzogs par so so'i lugs mthun gyi zhal 'don/ sgrol ma/ sher snying / bsam pa lhun grub ma sogs khri tshar mang po/ tshe chog stong rtsa gsum/ rnam rgyal stong rtsa/ ma
Ni dang siddhi dung phyur/ bka' 'gyur rin po che tshar gcig /brgyad stong pa brgya phrag tu nye ba/ gzhan yang chos srung gi bskang ba sogs la khyon ja rkyang du bsgrigs
na ja bag sum brgyar nye ba song zhing / zhabs brtan thog tu bka' 'gyur rin po che tshar

gcig dang / 'bum tshar gnyis/ sa skya bka' 'bum tshar gcig bcas spar 'debs zhu bar mdzad par ja 'khor drug brgya dang dgu bcu go dgu dgos par/ ja/ nas/ rta/ mdzo pho mo/ 'bri
g.yag sogs song 'dug cing / sman pa'ang sde dge'i thugs rjer phun sum tshogs pa dang / mdzod pa nas kyang phyag rdzas gang yod phongs med lta bu'i sku stobs la dpag pa'i
sku rim zhabs brtan rgya che gnad 'gror zhus shing / gtso cher skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid kyi thugs bskyed rmad du byung ba bcas sku khams kyang rim dwangs kyi
tshul bzhes/ drag po zhes pa lcags sprel lo dgung keg la'ang zhabs brtan du rnam rgyal ma/ tshe dpag med/ sgrol ma/ sher snying / bsam pa lhun grub ma/ le'u bdun ma/ ma
Ni/ siddhi/ chos srung gi bskang ba sogs shin tu rgya che ba dang / kaHthog gtsug lag khang gi zhig gso'i thebs su nas khal nyis brgya stsal/ sprel lor bkra shis ltems su
gdan drangs te dpon mor sras med par srid spel gyi thabs rim dang chos bka' shin tu mang ba stsal bas sras kyang 'khor zhing byin rlabs sogs la yun ring bzhugs/ de nas
'dzom thog rgyal po'i pho brang chen por yum sras rnams nas bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod rten brgyad dang / gur zhal lcam dral gyi mgon khang sogs rten gsum mang du bzhengs
gnang gi gzungs rab gnas sogs thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa rgyas pa dang / yum sras dpon blon rnams la dri med kyi dbang sogs zab chos kyang ci rigs stsal zhing / ngor
pa'i chos rje bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyi drung

nas/ rigs gsum spyi/ khros nag lha lnga/ gur rigs bsdus/ sambuTi/ mi 'khrugs pa dngos sta dang 'brel ba rnams kyi dbang dang / rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po dang / thams
cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i mgon po'i chos 'byung gi lung sogs gsan no/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ slar yang mdo
khams pheb tshe bla ma lhas/ /lung bstan srung mas las sgrub chos sku'i rten/ /bzhengs sogs ma lus gdul bya'i re ba bskang / /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bslu med thugs rje yin/
/zhes so/ /de nas mdo smad phyogs kyi gdul bya'i don rnams grub nas dbus su pheb par bzhed pa na/ sde dge bla chen phun tshogs bstan pas pheb rdzong dngos 'bul spom mtho
ba dang / gzhan yang zhal slob blon 'bangs dad ldan kun gyis so so'i 'byor bstun gyi dge tshogs spel phyir 'bul nod gzabs rgyas dang / sde dge'i sku tshab ched mngags dang
bcas te bya lo zla ba bdun pa'i nang du dbus gtsang phyogs su chibs kha bskyod de byang lam brgyud nas phyags pheb/ sgrub rgyud kyi gdan sa dpal ldan stag lung gi gnas
rten rnams la mchod 'bul smon lam mdzad/ nA lendra nas bco brgyad chos kyi rje dang khams tshan mi sna sogs kyis pheb bsu dang bcas te bco brgyad bla brang du pheb/ gzhis
len bsnyen bkur rgyas par mdzad de gdung brgyud rin po ches chos bka' gsan bzhed kyi snyan gsan 'bul ba gnang bar zhal gyis bzhes/ gnas gzigs rnams mdzad de lha ldan

du pheb cing / gong sa mchod yon gyi mjal phyag la dngos 'bul spom mtho ba dang / sde dge chos kyi rgyal po bstan pa tshe ring gi dgongs rdzogs su ched dmigs kyis jo bo'i sku
mdun du stong mchod dang / rtse shod ra mo che sogs su mchod 'bul dang gser chab sogs gzabs rgyas mdzad/ de skabs tsam la yin nam/ rje 'dis lha ldan du sku bsnyun tshul
bzhes skabs shig dga' ldan phun tshogs gling nas yin pa'i lcags zam pa blo bzang dpal grub ces grub dbang thang stong rgyal po'i rnam sprul du zhal gyis bzhes pa zhig yod
pa 'di lha sar pheb pa dang 'grigs pas/ rkyen sel la gdan 'dren zhu bar mdzad pas/ de 'phral chibs brgyugs kyis byon te spyan 'dren pa rjes su lus/ sku mdun du pheb ma
khad sku rgyab phred khug nas shing gi tshe bum bton te skog thag skog thag ces dbu thog tu 'bul bar mdzad pas bsnyun las grol zhing / sgrub thabs rin 'byung gsan pa'i snyan
sbron kyang bka' drin bskyangs/ sde ba spo ra ba ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs sogs la mkha' spyod ma'i chos skor ci rigs pa gnang ste mi ring bar yar klung du
chibs bsgyur/ rdo rje'i chos srung rnams la gtang rag dang / 'dus sde spyi la bzang gos kyi bla bre sogs kyi spyi 'bul dang / ja dngul mdzo sogs kyi 'gyed dang bcas pas pheb
skyes rgyas par stsal/ yar 'phyong gnyis kyi dgon khag tshang ma dang / yas mchog khul gyi sa dgon rnams bcas la mang ja/ sbyor sbrel/ bsngo rten/ sne gzhag sogs dang
/ grwa tshang che khag 'ga' zhig dang gal che ba rnams la rta sogs

kyi spyi 'gyed kyang gnang / klong nag bla ma kun dga' dpal 'byor sogs gsung ngag slob bshad zhu bar ched gtad 'byor pa'i khams 'grul ba kha shas dang / bkra shis chos sde'i
slob dpon gnyis sogs 'dus pa nyung shas la bla brang gzims chung du gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i zab chos mdo rgyud kun gyi snying po gsung ngag
rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa tshogs bshad dang / slob bshad gnyis las shin tu zab cing rgyas pa dpal kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bka' srol tshar lugs slob bshad thun
mong ma yin pa'i dbang / byin rlabs/ khrid/ lung yongs su rdzogs pa ste/ gsung ngag slob bshad gnang ba'i dang po dang / gzhan yang 'dod chos rigs shin tu mang bar stsal/
'di skabs snye thang 'phags sde'i mkhan por mchod dpon yar 'brog zhabs drung nas dgongs zhu mdzad par/ 'phags sde ba spyi sos skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid mkhan
por zhus chog pa'i dgongs skor phul ba'i phyir pheb tu/ khyed tsho'i bla ma gnas gsar dbon nas mdzad na sgrig lam kun spyod cho ga phyag len gang cir phan nges 'ong bar
'dug cing / 'di thog nas rgyu mtshan zhus 'thus pheb par/ 'phags sde'i gra bgres bstan pa rgyal mtshan nas yar klung du snyan 'bul zhu bar phyin te/ gang spyi'i gnas tshul
zhib tu gsol bar/ sde dgon gyi 'dzin skyong rigs 'di chos kyi 'gal rkyen du bsams nas bkra shis chos sde'ang mkhan sa slob dpon du phab pa sogs sgo du ma nas rnam g.yeng
mi 'byung ba'i thabs lhur len byas pa yin gshis/ dgon pa gzhan gyi 'dzin skyong rigs gtan

nas mi 'ong zhes zhal gyis ma bzhes/ de snga nas 'phyong rgyas 'du khang pa'i bca' yig gi thang ka dbus su 'phags mchog chos kyi rgyal po'i sku brnyan bris pa de'ang 'phyong
rgyas nas 'char ba phyag tu 'byor ba dang / grwa tshang gi zhu yig phyag tu phul ba dang dus mtshungs su dpyid 'brug gi thog ma bsgrags pas dgon zhol gyi mi rnams kyis
lha rgyal 'then pa sogs rten 'brel gyi mtshan ltas kyang legs shing / yang bskyar snyan zhu nan tan phul ba bcas zhal gyis 'ches pa ni/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog
dang / 'phags chen dpal ldan grags pa sogs nas bzung yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i nyi ma mkhan rin po che dbang phyug dpal bzang dang / mkhas grub dbang po ngag dbang chos
bzang la sogs pa'i bar du byon pa'i 'phags brgyud pad dkar phreng ba lta bu las brgyud de 'ongs pa'i phyi 'dul ba'i khrims kyis mngon par mdzes shing gzhi gsum gyi rnam
gzhag rnams kyang chad med du mdzad pas jo bo stan gcig pa'i brtul zhugs 'dzin pa/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo dang thugs rje chen po nam mkha'i rgyal po la yi dam gyi gtso bor
'dzin pas nang gsang sngags kyi rnal 'byor pa/ 'dod chung chog shes kyis dman cha lhur blangs te 'phags pa'i sde zhes mtshan don mthun pa'i ring lugs dbyar gyi chu gter
dang mtshungs pa de dus dbang gis sos kyi chab rom ltar 'gyur bar nye ba thugs kyis ma bzod par rgyal ba'i sras po dkon mchog 'bangs yab sras kyi chos kyi dbyings nas bskul
bar gdon mi za snyam mo/ /bsam yas rab byung dge slong dge legs bzang po dang / dge

'dun bsam 'grub gnyis nas sbyin bdag bgyis te/ rnga chen zhes pa chu khyi zla ba lnga pa'i nang nas dpal bsam yas dbu rtse'i bar khang g.yu zhal mthil du/ bco brgyad nas chos
kyi rje yab sras/ kha rag bod 'brug chos rje/ nyan po chos rje sku mched/ gling smad zhabs drung / gzhi pa dpon slob/ bkra shis chos sde'i dpon slob sogs phyogs 'dus dang
/ gnyug mar gnas pa mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa sogs 'dus pa sum brgya brgal ba la gsung ngag rin po che dbang lung khrid gsum shin tu rgyas pa ste/ tshar gnyis
pa dang / gzhan yang mkha' spyod ma dang rta mgrin yang gsang sogs 'dod chos kyang shin tu mang ba dang / ser skya stong phrag brgal ba la theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed/
gsung ngag tshar chos su ser skya shin tu mang bar 'chi med dpal ster gyi khrom dbang bcas stsal/ rab byung grwa tshang gi sbyin bdag sogs spyi sgos rnams kyis gtong ba'i
sgo brgya rnam par phye ba'i zang zing gi mchod sprin gzabs rgyas chad med du bstar/ de ltar chos srid kyi 'byor pa rdzogs ldan gyi rjes su snyegs pa la gnas srung chos
skyong chen po'ang rjes su yi rangs te/ dam ldan dge bshes kyis rdo rje gdan du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba legs shing / 'dre'ang yid spro zhes sogs kyis gzengs bstod dang
lha rdzas srid du ring ba phyag mtshan ba dan dang bcas pa phul zhing lus dang grib ma'i tshul du mi 'bral bar phrin las bsgrub par zhal gyis 'ches/ de nas lha ldan brgyud
de 'phags sder chibs bskyod/ gnyan mkhar nag gi 'brang la kha btags dri med cig phung nge 'dug par gzhis bdag gi mjal dar yin 'dug /

rten 'brel legs pa yin zhes gsungs/ dge 'dun 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis pheb bsu'i bkod pa zab rgyas dang bcas te/ 'bring ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi gnas gzhir bzung bas bka' gdams
pa'i dgon rnying la dus phyis thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun kun dga' snying po dpon slob kyis sgrub sde 'dzugs par mdzad pa'i gnas snye thang brag sna dgon du phyag na
padmo'i rnam rol 'phags chen dpal ldan grags pa'i khri la zhabs zung bkod de zab chos kyi sgo 'phar yangs por phye/ gzhung sa mchog nas bsko 'ja' khri 'gyed dang / gzhan
yang ser skya kun gyis rang rang gi 'byor tshogs mchis rgu lta bur mchod sprin du spros/ 'dus pa'i tshogs la dkar lha gsum gyis chos sgo phye ba'i kye rdor rgyu dbang / kun
rig gi dbang / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang / phyag drug pa'i gtor dbang sogs rjes gnang mang po dang / brag rdzong ma'i phyi khrid/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid/ gnyan
mgon dkar po tshe 'phel gyi khrid dang / lung gi rigs mang po/ ser skya shin tu mang bar khrom dbang sogs stsal te/ slar yang lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ se ra theg chen
gling gtor sgrub slob dpon yun ring du mdzad nas rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs yongs 'dzin du ma'i zhabs pad la gtugs shing / lhag par dpal rta mgrin la thugs dam gyi
gtso bor mdzad pas rta mgrin gyi grub thob tu grags pa de la rta mchog rol pa yang gsang gi rtsa dbang kun gzigs lnga pa chen po'i bka' 'bum khrod kyi yang gsang skor
phal che ba/ dge slong 'jam dbyangs grags

pa'i gsung skor rmor chen rje'i drung du ma gsan pa'i yig rnying thor bu dmag zor ma'i skor sogs dbang lung mang du gsan/ lha ldan du khams bod kyi dad ldan mang por gsung
chos kyang rgya cher stsal zhing / slar yang yar klung du pheb/ sde dge bsod nams mgon po dbus gtsang du dge sgrub la pheb pa yar klung du pheb cing / gzhis len rgyas par
mdzad/ khrag skyug ces pa chu phag zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu nas bzung / bkra shis chos sde'i bla ma lha khang du spo bo yar 'brog dgon gyi sprul sku lhun grub phun tshogs
dpon g.yog lnga/ 'bras gling rab 'byams pa mdo sngags chos 'phel/ tshag gur rab 'byams pa/ rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol sogs phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa'i 'dus
pa shin tu mang bar gsungs ngag rin po che dbang lung khrid sogs/ tshar gsum pa gzabs rgyas dang / mjug tu 'dod chos kyang shin tu mang bar stsal lo/ /de dag gi don bsdu
na/ sa dbang gnas skabs mthar thug phan bder bkod/ /bstan 'gro'i don phyir nyid kyi sku rim mdzad/ /dbus gshegs chos 'khor bskor zhing 'phags sde bzung / /gnas gsar 'jam
mgon rnam dkar mdzad phrin yin/ /zhes so/ /de nas lo 'di'i ston kho bos dbus kyi gnas rten rnams mjal bar phyin skabs nas bzung skyabs mchog yid bzhin nor bu 'di nyid
rnyed pa yin te/ de'ang kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rang lugs snyan brgyud bstan pa'i mnga' bdag yin pa dang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan 'jam mgon a
mes zhabs kyi dbu bla mdzad pa dang /

gnas gsar stong dpon sa skya pa'i sku nye yin pa sogs nged rang na phra bas ci'ang ha ma go /yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid nas gsung sgros kyi zur la yar klung dpon rin po
che zhes gnas tshul gsung skabs dgyes nyams mdzad pa dang / gzhan go thos sna tshogs la phyogs lhung gi gtam yang du ma go ba bcas/ yar klung dpon rin po che de bzang ngan
ci 'dra yin nam snyam pa las mtha' gcig tu nges pa'i bzang ngan med mur dbus la 'gro nye'i skabs thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha'i mtshan can de nyid kyis/ ma drung
dang mdzod pa bcas la yar lung zhabs drung sku rus sku yon sogs gang sa nas dbu blar bzhes thub pa zhig byung na pheb pa dang / rjes su phyag ris kyi'ang bskul ma gnang ba
bcas dbus 'gro'i skabs yar klung du de lugs kyi snyan sbron zhu rtsis yod 'dug pa ltar/ lo de'i mgo zla'i tshes nyi shur khra 'brug tu gnas zhag byas pa'i sang de thon
khar/ yar klung zhabs drung pheb bsur byon 'dug pas mjal phyag la bcar na zhes mgron gnyer gyis zer don bzhin de 'phral pheb tu bcug pas/ bla ma sku blta bas chog mi shes
shing / gsung 'jam zhing snyan pa/ mthong ba tsam gyis dad pa dbang med du 'gro ba zhig dang / thog mar mjal skabs/ gsung bgros yul tsam zhig las ma byung yang / rang nyid
kha blta phyogs kyi rten 'brel ma log par byang bltas su yod pa la rje 'di lho gzigs su thog mar 'jal/ rim gyis gtam snyan bzhugs khrir chos sde'i thab bsu 'dug pas/ de
thog tu chos rgyal 'phags pa'i lo rgyus sogs shin tu rgyas par gsungs/ yum bu bla mkhar gtsug lag

khang du ja gral skabs nged rang la sngon gyi lo rgyus las brtsams pa'i gsung gleng zhu rgyu med kyang / gtsug lag khang rten dang brten par bcas pa 'phral du snang ba la gang
shar de'i gnas tshul 'dra zhus pas/ rgyal rab chos 'byung lo rgyus chu babs su gsungs shing / zhal 'dzums mdangs dang bcas dges nyams 'dug pas/ sems la yab rje rdo rje
'chang dang / thar rtse rje/ brag rtsa chen po rnams rang nges shes rnyed pa'i bla ma yin kyang / da lta'i sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad spyod 'di la bltas na bla ma 'di de
bas lhag pa zhig med kyang mi zhan nges su 'dug snyam pa'i mos 'dun dang bcas pas yar klung du phyin/ ser sbreng dang bcas slebs 'phral 'du khang du dkar spro ja gral thog
grwa tshang gi 'phrad dar bstar/ bla brang gi sgo spe mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros kyi gzims chung du sdod yul snang tshad med pa'i bdag rkyen bka' drin stsal zhing /
de'i sang nyin sgrol dkar gyi gsung chog sgo nas ring 'tsho'i rten 'brel mdzad skabs ngos 'khor bcas la ston mo rgyas pa dang bcas sku gsung thugs rten/ dngul gyi maNDal/
dkar yol stegs bcas/ gding ba/ gos kyi bla bre/ yol 'khor/ gser srang / ja nag po 'khor drug /rta/ gos yug sogs yod pa'i dgu tshan brgyad/ gyon pa cha tshang / rgya sbub/
bzang ja 'khor drug /pags rigs drug sogs khyon sde grangs brgya dang lnga/ spyi so nas dgu tshan bdun tshan lnga re dang / lnga tshan bcas kyi mgor rta/ ther rgyu gtsang
gsum/ phrug gnyis/ dkar yol/ gzhan yang mdzod pa sogs la spyi sgos nas dngos po'i gnang sbyin

gzabs rgyas stsal zhing / maNDal gyi mthar yun 'tsho'i khas blangs dgos tshul gsungs dus/ bka' bstan thams cad thugs la bzhugs pa lta bu'i legs bshad bka' drin bskyangs byung
bas/ da cha bla ma 'di'i zhabs la gtugs nas gsung gi bdud rtsi myong chog pa zhig byung na ci ma rung snyam pa'i mos 'dun lhag par che bar yod skabs/ mdzod pa grwa tshang
ba rgyal mtshan rin chen gyis nged rang nas yab rdo rje 'chang sogs bla ma kha shas la chos thob tshul dang / da lta thos bsam byed mu yin pas rnam 'dren dam pa nyid
kyang dbu blar pheb dgos zhus shing / de'i rgyu mtshan thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi bka' pheb sogs zhus yod dam/ gang ltar kyang pheb lan du/ da lam chos 'brel zhig phul nas
'gyang min 'dod sbyar 'ong ba'i zhal bzhes pheb 'dug pas bka' chos song stsal rgyu'i do nub der dga' spro tshad med pa byung zhing / de'i sang nyer gsum la chos sde'i
lho phyogs kyi gtsug lag khang padma 'od du sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa stsal byung bar gsung bshad shin tu rgyas pas kye rdor rgyu dbang
mdor bsdus bskur ba'i yun tsam gyi tshod byung zhing / gong gi thugs rje dang rang gi dad pas byin rlabs kyang de 'phral zhugs pa lta bus ston dang bstan pa gzhan nas
mi 'tshol ba'i mos gus kyis tshim pa thob/ de skabs su'ang dkar spro dang / yang nged rang nas kyang rje 'di nyid dang bkra shis chos sde tshogs yongs la 'jam dbyangs dmar
ser gyi rjes gnang phul zhing / gong gi zhabs 'gyur ba mdzod pa 'jam dpal rgya mtsho nas dbang bzhi'i sbyin bdag gi mkho rgu'i yo byad gya nom

ba bstar/ chos sde'i gtsug lag khang dang / mgon khang / rnam sras lha khang sogs mchod mjal gyi skabs kyang 'bral med du pheb nas rten bshad mtha' dag zhib par stsal/ 'du
khang steng gi tshar chen rnam thar gyang ris de la bsam ngan gyis zhib 'jug byas pa min kyang / 'dar gdong 'khrugs pa'i zhing bkod kyi thad der 'di ci 'dra lags zhus pas/
'dir 'dar gdong 'khrugs nas phan tshun 'thab mo byed cing tshar chen rin po ches mchod g.yog la thog kha nas mi rkang bus gsungs pa dang ser ba babs shing / ma chen rdor
bkras kyis tshar chen la mthu dgos zhus pas zhal gyi ma bzhes par ngo nag thug ger bsdad pa sogs kyi zhing bkod yin 'dug gsungs/ de skabs su sems la rtog pa ni ci'ang med/
phyis su gnas tshul de 'dra ngan can gyis zhus pa min nam snyam pa'i dgongs pa tshom dogs 'gyod po byung yang / tshar chen rnam thar gyi ljags lung skabs sogs gang la
dpag kyang tshom gzhi ma byung 'dra/ chos sde nas 'ong skabs sri gcod 'bum par thab skyel skabs de skor tshong dpon dang ne tso'i lo rgyus sogs gnang zhing / mchod rten
de la bskor ba byas na sri las thar tshul gsungs/ bya sa lha khang du skyel mar pheb tshe de skor gyi rten bshad zhib par bka' drin bskyangs pa sogs skye ba dang tshe rabs
thams cad rjes su 'dzin pa'i sgo 'di nas dod de/ mig dmar zhes pa shing pho byi ba'i lo smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling du dge slong lhun grub mched kyis sbyin bdag
byas te/ rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol dang dpon slob dge 'dun gzhan phan sogs phyogs 'dus dang / gnyug mar gnas pa bcas la gsung ngag

rin po che'i dbang / byin rlabs/ rgyab brten lung bcas/ tshar bzhi pa rgyas pa dang / gzhan yang chos bka' rgya cher gnang ste/ 'phags sder chibs bskyod/ dge slong blo gsal
mkhyen rab/ dge slong blo bzang mkhas btsun/ grags pa bshes gnyen gsum gyis sbyin bdag bgyis te/ bco brgyad nas gdung brgyud rin po che/ bod 'brug chos rje/ rig 'dzin skal
bzang rnam grol sogs phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa bcas ches mang bar/ rgyal yum mkha' spyod dbang mo'i zab khrid mthong grol lde'u mig nang bzhin shin tu rgyas pa/
rgyab rten gyi lung sogs tshang ma/ 'bum dang brgyad stong pa sogs kyi ljags lung dang / gzhan yang 'dod chos mang du gnang zhing / rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po dang
/ mkhan chen ngag dbang blo gsal bstan 'dzin gnyis kyi sku mchod so sor mkha' spyod ma'i cho ga gsar 'dzugs kyi chag med 'ong ba'i thebs su dngul srang nyer drug sbyor
'jags gnang / gsar rnying gi rgyud sde'i phyag len man ngag rnams la rang byan tshud cing / khyad par gong zhabs lnga pa chen po'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rgyun kho na'i ched
du'ang dbu g.yor gnyis chu bzhin nyul te bla ma mang du bsten nas gsung 'bum phyi nang gsang gsum gyi lung rgyun bzhugs so cog gsan pa'i/ chos rje rin po che bkra shis pa'i
drung nas rnam rgyal grwa tshang gi 'don chog skor phal mo che/ rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po'i bka' 'bum phyi nang mang po/ gzhan yang phan cha'i skor shin tu mang ba
dang bcas pa gsan cing / slar bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs gsan pa'i snyan gsan 'bul ba gnang nas lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ rmor chen rdo

rje 'chang gi zhal slob grub dbang 'gyur med padma rgyal mtshan gyi drung nas/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus zhi drag seng gsum gyi dbang / tshe dbang / bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid/ gter
gzhung yongs rdzogs dang gsar rtsom gyi yi ge mang po'i lung / 'bri gung pas mdzad pa'i 'pho ba 'jags tshugs ma'i lung khrid/ rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po dang gter bdag
gling pa gnyis kyi gsung 'bum thor bu sogs kyi lung rnams gsan/ zhwa lu ba rin chen 'jam dpal chos mchog la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs rin chen snying po'i lung
gsan/ grub pa'i dbang po gnubs ston blo bzang don grub kyi drung nas/ byang gter tshe dbang lcags sdong ma'i dbang lung / rgya can tshe dpag med dwangs ma bcud 'dren gyi
dbang khrid lung sogs yongs su rdzogs pa dang / rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po dang rig 'dzin padma phrin las gnyis kyi gsung 'bum skor mang ba/ thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed
dang / hrIHdmar gshin rje 'dus pa'i yang snying / bla ma sku gsum gyi khrid lung yongs rdzogs sogs shin tu zab pa'i mnog chos mang du gsan te chos sder chibs bskyod/ zla
ba dgu pa'i nang du gtsang la pheb pa'i pheb lam du bkra shis lhun por paN chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por mjal phyag dang gnas gzigs mchod 'bul smon lam mdzad de
shab brgyud/ 'dar grong chen du pheb skabs bsu ba ser sbreng chibs bsu'i bkod pa rgyas par zhus/ rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che shog bu bzhi shog ma zhing khams che zhing
spar gsal chu skyon sogs med pa'i dngos gtsang dang / bzang gos kyi bla re che legs/ rgya sbub sogs 'bul sbyor

mdzad/ brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang blo gsal mtshan can gyi dbus 'dus tshogs rnams la ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi yig steng nas rnam rgyal lha dgu'i rjes gnang lung bcas
dang / de'i bstod pa ngor chen kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i 'dod gsol bcas gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi gzungs rtog pa dang bcas pa/ ngan 'gro yongs sbyong gtsug tor rnam rgyal
gyi lung stsal/ 'dus tshogs kyis sgrol dkar gyi cho ga dang 'brel ba'i zhabs brtan 'bul ba bsnyen bkur sogs gzabs te zhus/ de skabs brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang dang bla
brang du zhal rgyas mdzad skabs brag rtsa rjes gzhan ma rang gi blo la yod pa phal cher 'grub byung yang / 'dar shing mang gi 'du khang la nyams gso'i blo yod pa ma grub
pas rje 'di nyid la zhig gso bka' drin skyong dgos zhu bar mdzad pa'i lan duu da lam thub pa zhig ma byung / slar de bzhin 'grub par bgyi zhes zhal gyis bzhes/ grong chen
du pheb pa thos 'phral 'di nas gsol 'debs kyi zhu shog skyes bcas phul don bzhin chibs kha bsgyur te/ lo de'i zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyer gsum la sa skyar pheb skabs chibs
bsu ba sogs legs par bsgrigs te gnam gshis 'jam pa sogs dge mtshan dang bcas dpal sa skya'i gzhi thog bla brang gi gsang sngags pho brang du spyan drangs te bzhugs gdan
'jags/ pheb 'phral gsol ja gsol chas sogs phul zhing / dbang khang smin grol bde chen du mjal 'dzom zhus skabs tshur dngos po rgya spom che ba'i gsol ras stsal zhing /
phar gsol ja gsol ston thog nged rang nas pheb lam gnas tshul las brtsams pa'i gsung bgros yul tsam zhus shing /

gnas slob bzod pa bkra shis kyis rang bzhin gyi gleng mo sna tshogs zhus nas zhabs phyi rnams phyir gyes grub dang bstun dum tsam zhig bzhugs gdan 'jags thog /spyir kha'u pa'i
bla ma rnams mkhas grub gzhan dang ma 'dra zhing / khyad par rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po de nyid 'jam pa'i dbyangs dngos su bzhugs pa'i bka' drin gyis dpal sa skya'i
snyan brgyud zab chos rnams kyis mtshon chos bka' thob rgya ma chung tsam yod kyang / rang nyid skyes sbyangs kyi shes rab kyis dben pa sogs sgo du ma nas gdan sa chen po'i
dbu bla 'ong re med kyang / na nyin dbus su pheb skabs nas bzung bka' nan shin tu che ba bcas da lam sku mdun du bcar thog yab chos rnams 'bul thub re sogs shin tu skal
ba bzang ba zhig byung nas/ de skor 'di kha'i dgongs pa dang bstun rim bzhin zhus chog pa zhig dgos gsung bar/ nged rang nas thugs rje che zhus/ gnas slob kyis de'i lan
du/ mkhas pa snga mas sbyar ba yi/ /tshig don la ni byin rlabs yod/ /gsungs pa ltar sngon gyi bla ma gong ma'i phyag len ltar bka' drin bskyang bas des go chod par 'dug
/ces sogs bcos med kyi tshig hur thum rbad chod 'dra mo zhus song bas bzhad mo dang bcas pheb song / lo de'i smin drug zla ba'i nyer lnga nas bzung shing glang dbo zla ba'i
nyer lnga'i bar la gtso bor gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi dbang / byin rlabs/ lung / khrid bka' bcas/ tshar lnga pa dang / zhar byung du chos bsam gyis mi khyab
pa stsal pa rnams bsdams nas bkod na/ rjes gnang skor la tshe dpag med dkar po/ 'jam dkar gser gdugs dang ma ti lugs/ ye shes yon tan bzang po/ 'jam

dbyangs dmar ser/ smra seng / sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ spyan ras gzigs phyag bzhi par sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i chings/ bcu gcig zhal/ seng ge sgra/ spyan ras gzigs skyer

uu tswarya/ phyag rdor gtum po/ 'jigs byed dpa' gcig /gtsug tor rnam rgyal/ sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrags/ dbang gi sgrol ma dmar mo/ rdo rje rnam 'joms/ sme brtsegs sa
lugs/ khro mo sme brtsegs/ sme brtsegs jo lugs/ sangs rgyas klu dbang lha lnga/ sman bla mtho brtsegs/ rta mgrin grub rgyal/ skyer sgang / zla rgyal/ ye shes khyung khra/
sna tshogs yum/ rdo rje shugs/ sor 'brang dkar mo/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ dzam ser nag /seng gdong sngo dmar/ shangs lugs phyag drug sngo dkar/ dmag zor ma/ sher phyin dkar
mo/ nor rgyun ser mo/ dbyangs can dkar dmar/ gra dzam/ sa lugs dzam dmar/ dzam dkar lha lnga/ zhal dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ma yin pa/ khyung nag /seng ldeng nags sgrol/
phag dkar/ phyag rdor khang brtsegs/ zhang blon/ gnas brtan bcu drug /dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang ngor lugs thun mong ba/ rigs byed ma gsang sgrub lha lnga/ gza'
yum gtso 'khor/ dud sol phyi sgrub/ 'byung 'dul sems dpa' sum brtsegs/ tshogs bdag thun mong ma yin pa dang / khyad par mkha' spyod ma'i byin

rlabs/ bde mchog dkar po rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / gsung ngag dang rjes 'brel brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ slob ma rjes 'dzin/ kye rdor rgyu dbang /
lam dbang / rdo rje bdag med ma'i sindhU ra'i byin rlabs/ bir srung thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bla ma rin 'byung/ tshar gsum khug pa/ aShtA'i bzlas lung dang yig
brgya'i byin rlabs/ brda don gsal ba/ brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/ mgon rkyang rjes gnang rnams dang
/ gong du bshad pa'i rjes gnang / byin rlabs/ dbang de dag dang 'brel pa'i sgrub skor las tshogs thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge rnams kyi lung dang / bla ma
rgya bod kyi lo rgyus/ lam 'bras kyi chos 'byung kha shas/ gong ma lnga nas bzung mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi bar dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang nas bzung rmor
chen chos kyi rgyal po'i bar gyi bla brgyud khag che ba rnams kyi rnam thar/ pod ser/ pod dmar/ pod nag /de dag gi dgongs don thun mong ma yin pa kha'u brag rdzong pa'i
ring lugs kyi yi ge bdag chen rdo rje 'chang dang / tshar chen yab sras rjes 'brangs dang bcas pas mdzad pa'i lung rgyun dgos gal che nges rnams dang / ljags bshad kyi skabs
su gsung ngag chos 'byung khog phub/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar/ bla ma bsten thabs dang dam tshig rnam bshad/ phyi nang gi bskyed rim gyi bshad pa sogs zab cing gting
dpag dka' ba'i tshogs kyis nye bar brgyan te snang gsum rgyud gsum sogs kyi zab khrid

shin tu mtha' chod pa/ lus sbyong nyi shu pa dang / phrin las so gnyis sogs 'khrul 'khor gyi phyag khrid bcas/ mdor na phyag len phra mo tshun chad kyang ma nyams pa bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang sogs mkhas grub gong ma de dag mngon sum du byon pa lta bu'i sgo nas bka' drin chen pos rjes su bzung ba'i tshe/ snang gsum gyi skabs der ri klung thams
cad kha bas dung mdog tu btang ba sogs tshar lugs bla ma gong ma kha shas kyi rnam thar na bstan pa dkar 'byams su 'gro ba'i ltas yin gsungs pa de mngon du gyur pa lta
bu'i dge mtshan dang bcas pa ste/ 'di dag zhib tu rtogs par 'dod na kho bo'i thob yig ltar ro/ /de skabs gsung ngag zhu mir nged rang mched gnyis/ rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku
mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mchod dpon/ gsol dpon/ rje de nyid kyi zhabs phyi gsum/ rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku'i zhabs phyi gnyis rnams snang gsum skabs yod cing
/ de dus drung yig kun sangs nas snang gsum gyi bka' khrid nged tshor gnang ba ste grol 'phral gsang sngags pho brang duu zhus 'dug pas nyin rang po dang nam phyed yol bar
gsung chos kho nar 'gor/ de nas mnal cung zad re mdzad de tho rengs snga mo nas thugs dam nyams bzhes rnams bka' drin bskyangs pas sku shin tu ngal ba de sems kyis ma bzod
par sems bskyed chen mo nas bzung drung yig kun dga' sangs rgyas kyang lhan cig la yod cing / thog mtha' bar gsum du gser dngul gos dar sogs zang zing gi 'bul ba dang
dkar spro phran bu/ grol nyin tshogs kyi yo byad rgyas pa bcas zhus

khul dang / shing glang rgyal zla'i lo gsar nyin gong rjes gnang gi gras su bshad pa'i gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i rjes gnang de stsal zhing dga' ston gyi tshogs
su'ang spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur thog mkhan rin po che kun dga' zla 'od kyis lo gsar gsung bshad de shin tu 'jebs pa zhig yod pas de skabs nas bzung thugs mnyes/ lo de'i

dam pa 'di dang rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku gnyis char byon byung bas shin tu 'tsher snang shar/ dbo zla ba'i tshes drug la gong byin rlabs kyi gras su bshad pa'i rnam 'joms
bir lugs kyi byin rlabs de sogs stsal/ bdun nas bzung chu stod zla ba nyis brtsegs kyi phyi ma'i tshes lnga'i bar la bka' 'gyur rin po che'i ljags lung stsal bar/ gong

bzung bka' 'gyur rin po che chig sgril bka' drin bskyangs te myang 'das chen mo'i ljags lung skabs ljags dbugs 'tshangs/ mgul 'khril/ spyan chab chu bo'i rgyun bzhin mdzad

'gyur ljags lung bshol nas lhan du pheb ste der skyabs mgon 'di nyid kyis bsang chab klu/ lha mo'i gtor bsngo sogs bzhugs sgar de thog nas stsal zhing / gnas gzigs snyan shal
'bul gnang dang / gsol ston sogs zhus/ brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang zhing khams gzhan du gshegs nye'i skabs zhu shog ched mngags kyi snying por bdag ni dus tha 'dir thug song
bas sku zhabs nas dgon gogs 'di la brtse bas dgongs dgos tshul 'bul bar mdzad de/ drug pa nyis brtsegs kyi snga ma'i tshes bdun la mya ngan las 'das/ phyi ma'i tshes

bka' 'gyur rin po che yongs rdzogs thugs 'khur chen po'i sgo nas sku ngal dub khyad du bsad de ljags lung bka' drin bskyangs pa bcas kyi chos yon du dmigs/ dbang khang smin

po bas spyan drangs te zhag bzhugs kyi tshe dbang sogs gnang / nas khal brgya tsam 'bul mi byung ba dgon pa de rang du sbyor 'jags mdzad/ ri bo che nas mar lam chu tshugs mdo/
ar po/ ngang la/ zha lung / sa dmar mngon dga' rnams su rim bzhin zhag sa mdzad/ mngon dgar sgro lung pa chen po'i dus chen la TaM bco lnga sbyor 'jags dang / khyung
nag rjes gnang yig lung bcas stsal/ de'i sang sne gzhir kun dga' rab rgyas/ mgon blo grong chen spyi sa rnams pheb bsur 'byor/ yangs gru'i dar thon zhing shing glang rgyal
zla'i mjug grong chen du pheb ste thugs brel gyi 'phros 'ga' zhig mdzad nas/ 'dar bsam 'grub pas gdan 'dren zhus pa bzhin zhal ngo rnams la tshe bka' dang gzhis la phyag
nas/ dus rim pa grong chen grwa slob rnams dang chab cig rje nyid kyis tshogs dbur mdzad de gtor zlog /gtor spod/ thug gso zungs gso rnams sngar srol bzhin dang / me stag
lo gsar rta zla'i tshes gcig dga' ston bzhugs gral la mchod yon gdan 'dzom zhing grong chen pa rnams kyis dung rgya gling sgrogs pa sogs dgyes ston rgyas par mdzad/ mar
lam rmur pheb nas skya ser mang por tshe bka' stsal te grong chen du pheb/ rdzong rams par tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i kye rdor bskyed rim rnam bshad dang / chos rgya mtshor
mdo mang / lam 'bras pod ser sogs kyi lung gnang / gter bdag gling pa chen po gar dbang 'gyur med rdo rje'i zhal slob sbas pa'i sangs rgyas 'gyur med kun bzang klong
grol spyan drangs te pheb nyin o rgyan smin grol gling gi chos spyod ljags lung dang / lo zla de'i tshes bcu nas

'dod 'jo'i bum bzang gi dbang lung / rdor sems thugs thig /snying thig /btags grol/ rgyud drug /gter gsar/ drag dmar rnams kyi dbang lung khrid sogs chos skor yongs rdzogs
dang / gcod dbang nam mkha' sgo 'byed/ thugs rje chen po bde gshegs kun 'dus yab bka'/ yum bka'/ bka' srung bcas dang rig 'dzin thugs thig /gshin rje dregs 'joms rnams kyi
dbang lung phal cher/ phur pa'i rnam bshad 'grel chen 'bum nag /dzam dmar gsang sgrub/ gter chen 'gyur med rdo rje'i rnam thar sogs shin tu mang bar gsan no/ /de skabs
sngags srung ma bka' shin tu dog pa'i 'phros shig la/ rje 'di'i gsung las/ nga chung ngu'i dus ne thang zhig na dud 'gro 'dra dang bcas yod bsam par lha mo dmar mo kha TwAM
'phyar zhing thod pa thugs kar bzung ba'i khebs dar dmar zhig 'dug pa de rlung gis bskyod pas dmar lhab lhab byed pa zhig mthong yang ngo ma shes/ rjes su bsams pas e
ka dza tI 'di yin par 'dug gsung zhing / grub dbang nas kyang 'di'i rjes gnang rje 'di nyid dang mchod dpon ma gtog gzhan gang la ma gnang / de dus bkra bzang rig 'dzin kun
bzang ye shes mang mkhar gnas gsar nas rje nyid 'di mjal bar byon par mkha' 'gro snying thig gi khrid yig ga nor bu lugs su bsdebs pa de'i lung gsan/ bkra bzang pa'i gsan
yig la thugs rtog mdzad pas phur pa'i skor zhig gsan rgyu snang gsung skabs shig 'dar pas spyan dras te/ der bzhugs dus gsung las/ sngar grong chen slob dpon lags de
nyid kyis nged la shing mang 'du khang

gogs po zhig gso ma grub song bas de bzhin dgos pa yod kyi nan tan gnang ba de ma grub pas/ blo kha rdzogs pa zhig ma byung pheb par/ rje drung skyid pas bla brang sogs phog
thog nas 'dar khal brgya/ pad kha nyi shu phul nas zhabs bskul zhus pa bzhin khyed rang sang nyin grong chen du song la rdor 'thags gyis gsung zhing / bsam grub kyis thugs
brel chod ma thag pheb lam rkyang ste shing mang du pheb/ der zhag shas bzhugs thog gsung chos ci rigs gnang zhing 'du khang zhig gso'i zhal bkod stsal/ de nas grwa bu
dgon gsar la pheb/ der bzhugs ring kyang bka' chos ci rigs stsal/ grub chen rnam rgyal bstan skyong gis grub dbang thang stong rgyal po'i sku zhig dang ka pA la bdud rtsis
gang ba zhig 'gur ma dang bcas te phul bar 'gur lan gnang / de gang nas sku khams cung zad bsnyel tshul bzhes pa zhig yod par/ gsung las/ da nga drag 'gro ba nga rang
gis khag theg /khams su 'gro tshe'ang lam bar du bro 'tshal skabs chu dkyil pha wang zhig gi steng na grub thob rin po che'i sku pad bral la khad pa zhig 'dug pa blangs
pa nas bzung je bder song zhing sku de sde dger 'jog dgos byung gsung ste/ ka pA la'i bdud rtsi de nas thig gcig zhal du bzhes/ gzhan der yod kun la 'gyed pa gnang / de skor
gyi thugs brel rnams chod par gnang ste grong chen du pheb/ rje nyid kyi gsol dpon 'jam dbyangs mchog grub dang gnyer pa mgon blo gnyis kyis do dam dang / rkyen sel du
rdzong ri rab 'byams pas 'phags chen pod bzhi klog pa/ grong chen rdor slob sbyin pa bzang po nas ldebs bris rnying

pa rnams la argha'i cho ga bcas gogs po de bshig tshar ba dang / 'gram 'ding khar zhabs phyi bsod nams dpal 'bar dang rje drung skyid par dar gos kyi sna mang po mjug tu stsal
ba bzhin brtan khyad rtsig 'gram gting ring du brus par lci ba dang ril ma mang po bsgrigs pa'i bang rim ltar chags 'dug pa gnas 'dir shing mang po 'dug pas dgon pa'i
ming shing mang yin no zhes byang sems zla rgyal gyis gsung zhes rgan rabs kun zer ba der snang / ar zug gi las grwa rgyun ring tsam 'gor zhing / grub bstun phyag nas mdor
bsdus gnang skabs/ gsung las/ mkhan chen rin chen 'jam dpal gyi 'du khang de nged kyis 'di bzhin du btang gsung zhing dgyes/ rtsi tshon gyi zhabs 'gyur sogs rje drung
skyid pas kyang zhus shing / grong chen lha rigs pa 'chi med la tshon rtsi skor bka' pheb par tshon rnams rje skyid kyis khas blangs byung yang rje drung ru ngar ba dang
a Ni tsho mthu mo 'dug pa bcas ldebs bris 'ong mdog ma kha gsung yang / ldebs bris skor dgongs bzhed ji lta ba bzhin 'grub/ shing mang sgrub sde la tshes bcu/ sgrub skor
rnam gsum/ smyung gnas skor sogs bka' chos kha shas stsal/ gong du bshad pa'i lcags zam pa de rag rdzong zam par nyams bzo mdzad skabs de yin nam snyam ste/ gang ltar skyabs
mgon dam pa 'di nyid dang mjal ba'i gsung sgros la bla ma des sa skya pa dang ri bo che pas nga la ma nyan pas gdung brgyud dkon po 'ong gsung ba de 'ong 'dra mo byung
zhing / bla ma de rang la zhal slob btsun ma kha shas yod pa'ang 'u cag gnyis khyad med pas shing mang dgon gsar du sbyor cig gsungs

nas/ de ltar mdzad pa'i bgros shig kyang snang / zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis bla ma de'i mdzad spyod la khrel ba'i rnam pa byas pas/ rje 'di nyid kyi gsung las/ rang res lung
chung re'ang chos la 'jug mi thub/ khong gis rgyal khams chos la 'jug thub gsungs nas thugs dad lhag par che mur grong chen du rje 'di nyid mjal bar pheb/ lcags zam pas
rje 'di nyid kyis sngar nas bsgrubs gnang gi tshe bum de bzhes nas tshe dbang phul ba'i zhor la grwa rigs sbyin bdag mang pos kyang thob/ deng sang dbus gtsang na nged rang
gnyis las 'gro don che ba med/ rten bzhengs phon chen 'di 'dra la gsol mar thogs 'ong bas sang len mi thong gsungs nas mar gyi 'bul ba'ang mdzad/ sngar brag rtsa rdo
rje 'chang de nyid kyi sku thog la grong chen sgo 'phyor gyi byang shar na nang stong zhig yod pa der rnam sras lha khang gnang dgos zhes 'dus spyi nas zhus pas/ de'i bka'
babs nga la med/ zhabs drung dbon rin po cher zhus gsungs pa bzhin/ rgyu mtshan phul ba ltar tshul khrims bkra shis kyis 'jim bzo dang / grong chen sbyin pa/ rdzong ri
rab 'byams pa gnyis kyis gzungs gzhug spar 'debs sbrel mthud/ dri bzang byug sgril sogs bgyis te rnam sras kyi sku mi tshad ma de'i gzungs tshang ma phyag bstar dang / phyag
nas gtor 'dzugs sogs bcas mdzad de deng sang yang zhal dkyil la rdul mi chags pa sogs byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba de'i dbu thog tu bla re sogs mchod chas kyis spras
pa bzhugs/ 'di skabs grub chen la bka' chos gsan pa'i

sngar dgong srod gung gseng rnams la zangs bstan spor ba'i grwa pa kha shas la lha brgyad/ khro bcu'i rjes gnang lung bcas dang / bskang ba'i lung / 'og min chos sde'i dbu
byed 'gyur med kyi 'dod zhus mngon dga' dbu byed chos dar/ rdzong rams pa sogs kha shas la ngag dbang chos grags kyi yig cha'i steng nas mkha' spyod ma'i khrid dang / be'u
bum gyi lung / nor skyong rjes gnang dang / be'u bum gyi lung bcas gnang / mngon dga' dbu byed nas lung zhig phul 'dug kyang gang yin ma nges so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/
'dar stod gdan sa ri bo che sogs su/ /chos 'khor bskor zhing zab chos du ma gsan/ /nyams gso gsar bzhengs dge rgyun sbyor 'jags sogs/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon thugs bskyed
rten 'brel yin/ /zhes so/ /de nas nag zla'i nang du 'di phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur bar 'dar grong pheb skyel gyi sar bsod nams dpal 'bar brgyud grong chen sbyin pa dang rdzong
rams pa gnyis la zur chos stsol ba'i bka' stsal pa/ gzhan yang de skabs grub dbang dam pa sgro mo lung pa chen po mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel gyi zhal slob btsun
ma bcu skor zhig la dgon pa'i rten gso med cing ri khrod ma pher bas khyim du sdod pa de thugs kyis ma bzod par dgon gsar gnang ba'i thugs bzhed kyis yar lam sa yul gzigs
rtog bka' drin bskyangs/ 'dir pheb skabs thab bsu/ chibs bsu/ bzhugs yul mjal 'dzom gong dang 'dra bar zhus shing / lo der bka' chos stsal ba rnams la/ zla tshes bgrang
chags kyi zin bris bkod thub pa zhig ma byung yang / pheb 'phral

nas bzung / thar rtse paN chen gyi yig steng nas sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ lung skor la brgya rgyam gyi rgya gzhung / 'dul ba'i las chog bu ston gyis mdzad
pa/ so thar brgyud 'debs gong sa lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa/ grang chen bco brgyad/ der ma 'dus pa tshad ma sde bdun/ 'dul ba me tog phreng rgyud sum brgya pa/ 'od ldan/
ka ri ka /dbu ma rigs tshogs/ bstod tshogs/ gtam tshogs/ bka' gdams gzhung drug /dpag bsam 'khri shing / sher phyin 'grel pa don gsal/ mdo kun btus/ jo bo'i chos 'byung
brgya rtsa/ blo sbyong brgya rtsa/ bka' gdams thor bu/ blo sbyong gsung sgros ma legs bshad kun 'dus/ gong sa lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa'i sman bla'i mdo chog yid bzhin
dbang rgyal/ tsandra go ma'i gdugs dkar zlog zor/ de'i dkyil chog shAkya dpal/ de'i lhan thabs mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ bka' 'gyur ba'i gdugs dkar mdos/ rmor chen gdugs dkar
byad grol/ zhwa lu mkhan chen gyi gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i dkyil chog /thugs sras lo tsA ba'i gzungs grwa lnga'i dkyil chog /de'i lhan thabs bco brgyad 'jam dbyangs
chos rje/ rnam sras be'u bum rje de nyid kyi gsan yig nang bzhin/ jo bos 'brom la gnang ba'i sgrol mdos/ ri khrod ma'i bum chog 'phags pa dang sdong ra ba/ gung ru'i gzhan
phan mtha' yas kyi zur 'debs/ kun rig bstod pa'i phyag chen zin bris/ zin bris mun sel sgron me/ zin bris bsdus pa rnams kyi lung / rwa tshar thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag
len ltar 'jigs

byed bcu gsum ma'i dbang sngon 'gro'i rwa khrid dang / rnal 'byor rim bzhi'i khrid smin rgyas dang / dkar chag gis zin pa dang ma zin pa'i rwa pod yongs rdzogs kyi lung rje
nyid kyi gsan yig nang bzhin/ 'chi bdag dpa' gcig dang bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang / rta mgrin yang gsang gi dbang chen/ tshe dbang / bka' gtad/ be'u bum lung bcas/ yang bde
mchog skor la/ nag po gzhung drug /mkhyen rab rje'i rim bzhi'i khrid yig /nag po lhan thabs dang / zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sangs dpal gyis mdzad pa she lo'i sbyang gzhi sbyong
byed sbyor tshul/ nam dpal gyi lo hi'i mngon rtogs gsal byed dang / nag po mngon rtogs nag 'gros/ dril bu sgrub dkyil/ lo hi'i rdzogs rim mkhyen rab rjes mdzad pa/ bzang
dpal gyi nag po bskyed rim rnam bshad rnams dang / dpyid thig gi yi ge /glo bo mkhan chen gyi bsnyen thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ sa lo'i rdzogs rim 'khor lo gnyis
pa/ a mes zhabs kyi chos 'byung dang / lo nag dril gsum gyi bskyed rim rnam bshad/ bsnyen thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum nag po sgrub dkyil/ ngag chos kyi lo nag dril gsum
khrid kyi khog dbub/ bsnyen thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ nag po bskyed rim rnam bshad gnyis/ dril bu byin rlabs dang khrid yig rnams kyi lung / tshe dbang sngon 'gro'i
grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe khrid/ dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang dang be'u bum gyi lung / a pa ra tsi ta/ rnam sras drag sgrub/
mgon po phyag bzhi lha mang / stag zhon lha mang / rdo rje rab brtan

ma/ tshe ring mched lnga rnams kyi rjes gnang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sngon 'gro'i khrid rim rgyas pa'i sa bcad mthong grol lde mig gnang bzhin gyi khar chos nyid dngos
bstan gy-i byin rlabs dang dbu ma che ba'i khrid/ indra dang maitri'i byin rlabs/ phag mo de gsum gyi be'u bum rmor chen dkar chag nang bzhin gyi lung / rig byed ma thun
mong ma yin pa dang / dmar chung skor gsum/ tshogs bdag chags rdor dang / phyag bzhi rnams kyi rjes gnang / dkar chag gis zin pa dang ma zin pa'i dmar po skor gsum gyi
be'u bum gyi lung / thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid tshem bu lugs/ tshar chen gyi de'i brgyud 'debs/ mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig /sgrub thabs dang bsnyen thabs bsam yas sa phug
bla ma kun dga' tshul khrims kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang / mgon po'i be'u bum yang skong rmor chen dkar chag nang bzhin dang / gyi ljang
/ dud sol gnyis kyi be'u bum dkar chag gis zin pa dang ma zin pa'i lung / dud sol rjes gnang / nan chags ma/ zhal bzhi'i gsang sgrub rjes gnang sngon 'gro'i gsang khrid
dang / dkar chag gis zin pa dang ma zin pa'i zhal pod kyi lung / beg tse 'khor mang gi rjes gnang dang / beg pod kyi lung / khro phu brgya rtsa las yig sna nyis brgya
re gnyis tsam dang / khrid brgya'i lo rgyus/ brgyud 'debs/ spyi sdom/ spyi ching / sngon 'gro thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa/ dngos gzhi khrid brgya brgyad kyi lung
/ sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs dang / de'i yi ge g.yag pa/ mkhyen brtse/ ngag dbang chos grags/ a mes zhabs rnams kyis

mdzad pa/ bu ston chos 'byung / g.ya' bzang pa'i gza' bcos/ rong ston gyis yum la gnang ba'i 'pho dmigs dang / rtsa ba'i yi ge /gsal byed bco brgyad chen mos mdzad pa rnams
kyi lung / kun mkhyen rin po che bsod nams seng ge'i bka' 'bum sngags pod gsum/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyi bka' 'bum pod gcig ma/ kha reg sgom chung pa'i ang yig
bdun cu pa/ tshar chen bka' 'bum thor bu'i lung la bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ de bstod bla ma rgyang 'bod/ gsung 'gur skal bzang bzhad pa'i rdo rje'i glu/ lta sgom spyod 'bras/
chu mgo gangs dkar ma/ yongs rdzogs don ldan/ rang sems gsal 'debs/ snying gi skyo bsangs/ kye ho mi zad smin byed dbang bzhi rnams dang / dkon mchog lhun grub/ rab 'byams
rin rgyal/ bya btang dbang po rnams la mdzad pa'i chab shog /gong sa lnga pa chen po'i bka' 'bum thor bu la dmar po skor gsum dang chos skyong che chung gi man ngag dang
'khor lo'i gsal byed/ lam rim khrid yig 'jam dpal zhal lung / nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i brgyud 'debs dang / khrid kyi sa bcad mthong grol lde'u mig /rmor chen rdorje 'chang
gi bka' 'bum thor bu'i lung thob kyang / slar yongs rdzogs thob khongs su 'thus/ ngor chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi bka' 'bum pod phyed dang bzhi'i lung / a mes zhabs
kyi sa skya'i gdung rabs chen mo dang / yo ga chos 'byung / tshe dpag lha dgu'i sgrub dkyil/ seng ge sgra'i cho ga /chab klu rnams dang / paN chen nam dbang gi gzhan phan
mtha' yas kyi tshig don gtan 'bebs la chos dbang gis zin bris

mdzad pa dpag bsam ljon pa/ cha gsum rnam bshad rnams kyi lung / thugs sgrub rnam gsum gyi tshes bcu'i chog bsgrig dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa/ 'ja' tshon snying po'i
gter ma dkon mchog spyi 'dus dang / tshe sgrub lcags kyi ri bo'i dbang lung / byad 'grol gnubs lugs/ tA ra nA tha'i sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa brgya nyer lnga'i lung / gzhan
yang kha 'bar ma dkar mo'i 'chi bslu sogs man ngag kha 'thor gsar rnying la grags pa kha shas kyi lung bcas stsal zhing / de lta'i skabs dbo zla'i nang tsam du da lta'i
gzhi dgon mkhan chen bsod nams dpal bzang 'di nyid grwa rkyang gi skabs yin pas/ 'dir drung yig kun sangs drung nas gsan sbyong mdzad bzhed kyis pheb pa dang 'grigs te/
rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid dang zhal mjal zhing gsung 'phros mdzad pas/ bde mchog dang yo ga'i skor sogs yig rgyun shin tu dkon pa kha shas kyi dbang lung gsan dang gsan
rgyu 'dug pa bcas de skor gyi phyag dpe bzhes par mus phyogs su 'phral rdzong mdzad de tshur 'byor 'phral nag zla'i nyer gsum nas bzung mus chen dang / rdzong ri dpon
slob/ grong cen sbyin pa gsum la/ mgon chen skor gyi rjes gnang phal cher dang / brag rdzong ma phyi nang gsang gsum gyi khrid dang / lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i gsang
khrid/ me 'bar snyan brgyud kha skong / yang skong / gyi ljang pod/ mgon po'i chos 'byung bcas kyi ljags lung stsal zhing / de dag gi gseng dbar rnams su rje btsun ma
kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma'i zhabs drung nas/ gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun

sa skya pa rnams kyi yab chos yang phur gyi rdzogs rim zab mo bsam gtan gling pa'i a ti'i skor gyi lung yongs su rdzogs pa dang / phur pa rtsa dum sa skya paN chen gyi 'gyur/
sgrub thabs bklags pas don grub/ sgrub thabs don grub snying po/ yang snying lhan skyes gsal ba/ dkyil chog rtogs par sla ba rnams dang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan
gyi bka' 'bum yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / bde mchog lo hi pa'i smad lngar grags pa'i nang tshan mngon par rtogs pa/ shes rab bsrung ba'i chos bzhi'i nang tshan mngon
'grel/ phyi rol mchod pa/ lag mchod bcas kyi lung gsan/ mkhas pa'i dbang po kun dga' sangs rgyas kyi drung nas sgra mdo pA Ni pa 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i lung dang / ri mo'i
phyag khrid gsan te/ kun dga' sangs rgyas des sgra mdo pA Ni la tshegs med i ki a tsa la yang na'o zhes pa 'di shes nas grol ba yin/ zhes zhus pa tsam gyis thogs med du
dgongs te/ lung gsan pa dang / ri mo mdzad pa dus mnyam du grub/ 'di ni sngon kha che paN chen la 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta chen pos bdag cag bod la/ sngo ma yin pa las
log pa'i sngo tsam bya ba zhig 'dod lags na/ de ci ltar lags zhus pas/ sngon po don la yod tsam tsam mang po de nga la cha med gsungs pas/ tshad ma'i gnad thams cad der
go zhes bshad pa dang mtshungs so/ /skyi ston padma phrin las nas brgyud pa'i 'pho ba 'jag tshugs ma'i lung khrid kyang gsan/ mus chen bsod nams dpal bzang las/ bde mchog
lU nag dril gsum gyi dbang dang / gong du nged rang la stsal ba'i sa skya pa'i gdung rabs chen mo dang /

bde mchog dang / yo ga'i skor mus phyogs kyi mkhas grub rnams kyis mdzad pa de dag gi lung rnams gsan/ yang de skabs ma drung zhabs 'bam gyis shin tu bsnyun pas 'byon mi thub
pa de 'khyogs la bteg nas gzims chung dang nye skor gyi mgon khang du tshe dbang bla ma zhi khro zhus skabs/ da lam mi skyon gsungs nas/ tshe dbang brgya tshar gnad smin
