stsal zhing / gsung sgros kyi zur la zas min gyi 'phros shig byung bas/ 'di 'dra bla ma sa skya pa chen po nas bzung sa skya'i gdung rabs rnams la shin tu lan chags par
yod pas khyed rang sku mched rnams 'di zlos shig gsungs nas/ 'jigs byed nag po'i dug sngags chig brgyud ma de de 'phral lag khrid mdzad de gnang / rjes su de'i man ngag
te ra wa la'i khyad chos de'i ljags lung yang stsal bas de kho na'i byin rlabs kyis yin nam/ gzhan nged rang la'ang sngon las lta bus 'di 'dra myong dgos pa'i mtshan ma
zhig yod kyang sngar phan ci'ang ma skyon pa ni 'di kho na'i thugs rjer mngon no/ /yang sa ga zla ba'i nang tsam la nged rang la dbang bka' gsan bzhed kyi bka' pheb byung
bar/ rang nyid ni dpal sa skya'i gdung du skyes pa'i rigs rus che ba tsam las/ skyes sbyangs kyi yon tan sogs gang sa nas mkhas grub dam pa 'di tsam gyi dbu blar 'pher ba'i
re med kyang / bla ma lnga bcu pa las/ bla ma mnyes byed gang yin bya/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin dgongs par gtad tshe rang yang de bzhin skal ba bzang snyam pa'i spobs pa
bskyed de/ chos bka' phran bu phul bar/ rdo rje phur pa'i stod las/ yang dag lha dgu/ kye rdor rgyu lam/

bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ a ra pa tsa na lha lnga rnams kyi dbang / gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum nas bde mchog /phur pa/ mi g.yo ba/ don zhags/ seng ge sgra/ sgrol ma rnams kyi
yig skor dang / sa chen gyi bstod pa tshangs dbang ma/ lam 'bras brgyud 'debs/ rigs gsum spyi dkyil/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs tshigs bcad/ yang de'i sgrub thabs dkyil
chog /'jam bstod brgyud gsum 'khor lo/ gtor chen lo rgyus dang / cho ga gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rtog pa'i Tikka dang sa bcad/ bum gter gzhug tshul/ mtshan brjod 'don thabs/
phyag chen gces bsdus rnams dang / dpal sa skya'i chos spyod rab gsal/ bskang ba'i skor/ chos rje bla ma'i phur pa'i sgrub thabs 'bring po don grub snying po dang /
dkyil chog rtogs sla/ sa lo'i dkar cha bzhi dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg /phur pa'i brgyud 'debs/ bla mchod rgyas pa'i gzhung rkyang / bsnyen sgrub gsal byed/
sngags 'chang chen po'i gtor ma brgya rtsa dang / tshe dpag lha dgu'i nyams len snyan brgyud ma/ dkon mchog dpal ldan gyi dpal mo lugs kyi smyung gnas/ sgar chen gyi bstan
pa gso chog /a mes zhabs kyi rdo rje dril bu/ bgrang phreng / dgang blugs/ bum pa rnams kyi rnam bshad phrin las kun khyab dang / bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrub tshul bla ma gong
ma'i gsung rab mang po phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho/ mangga'i mtshan can gyi chag med bzhi/ mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub thabs/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ srung
'khor brag rdzong ma/

bstan pa gso chog /sgrol ma maNDal bzhi'i cho ga rnams/ nged rang nas brtsams pa'i yab rje'i gsol 'debs nyi gzhon gsar pa'i thig phreng / yang dag brgyud 'debs/ sgrub thabs/
beg tse'i brgyud 'debs/ gur lcam dral dang zhal gyi bstod pa/ rje de nyid la phul ba'i zhabs brtan rnams kyi lung / ri khrod ma'i bum chog bkru byab bsrung gsum/ smad las
drag po sgrol dbang / yangs pa'i grong khyer/ ri khrod ma'i gzungs/ de'i phyugs srung / 'od zer can ma'i gzungs/ tshe mdo/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ bkra shis brtsegs pa/ phyogs
bcu mun sel rnams kyi lung phul zhing / de gras phur pa'i stod las phur sgrub skabs dang / smad las brgyad pa'i nyer lnga/ gong ma'i gsung rab sogs lung de rnams dgu
pa'i tshes gnyis nas zhag shas kyi bar/ ri khrod ma'i bum chog dang / mdo mang gras kyi lung rnams pheb nyer phul zhing / lcam dral zhal bcas kyi bstod pa gsar brtsams de
tha skar zla nang brtsams phral phul bar thugs shin tu dgyes nyams kyis mgul khug nas bal TaM rnying ma zhig gzhan lag ma brgyud par stsal ba de 'di kha'i rnam sras kyi
sku zhig gi gzungs la phul snyam/ tha skar zla nang der rgyan mchog ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams mthu stobs dbang phyug gis dus 'dir chos 'chad kyi thog mar 'jam dbyangs
dmar ser gyi rjes gnang phul zhing / de'i dbyar der nged rang gi che zhe kun dga' bsod nams bstan pa'i nyi mas mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / kun dga'

bstan pa'i sgron mes drag dmar nyang lugs kyi dbang phul/ 'di lo snron zla'i nang gzims phug sprul sku rin po che blo bzang bstan 'dzin mgon po las tA ra nA thas mdzad pa'i
ni gu'i khrid yig zab don thang mar brdal ba dang / grub dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyi rnam thar zhal gsung ma dang / de'i kha skong grwa thang mkhan chen kun dga' mkhyen
brtse phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i lung dang / yang tha skar zla nang tsam la thub bstan lha khang chen mo'i mkhan rin po che byams pa kun dga' zla 'od las/ de nyid
kyis mdzad pa'i yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar yid bzhin nor bu'i ljags lung gsan zhing / sngar nas thugs nang shin tu dag gshis dpon slob gyes khar phan tshun gnyis
char nas mnyam phyag dang / gcig gis gcig la 'chang bar mdzad de spyan chab dang bcas gsung sgros thugs smon gyi rigs dum tsam zhig gnang song ba ni/ de'i phyi lo mkhan
chen de nyid zhing gzhan du pheb pa'i 'byung 'gyur yang dag par mkhyen par mngon no/ /gong du bshad pa ltar dgon gsar gnang ba'i spom gta' 'dzugs mi sa skya guu ra ba dang
/ sa chog la rdzong rams pa byams pa phrin las pa sa skya nas ched rdzong gi bka' bkod du/ khyed rang ma gir kye rdor dus 'khor gang rung gi sa chog gam/ yang na/ gser
mdog sa yi lha mo ni/ /zhes sogs gang 'os byas chog cing / klu sman ril thum 'di grog po lho byang gi chu mig der chug /chab klu/ chab gsum/ bsil gtor gang drag gyis/ gdan
sa nas zhus pa'i bum gter 'di rtsig rmang du tshud gsungs pa bzhin rdzong rams pas de bzhin dang / khyad par klu sman bcug pa'i chu mig byang

ma de na sngar pha waM gi steng nas chu thigs byed pa las rgyun 'babs med kyang / ril bu bcug pa'i sang nas bzung chu gang 'dod byung / de skabs kyi ril bu de nas nyung ngu
zhig rdzong rams pas 'tshags mdzad de/ slar rdzong ri'i phu'i chu mig gnyis su bcug pas sngar bsags rdzing dang chu sne bzhi nas 'dren pa de ma dgos par/ da lta zhag rdzing
gi chu shin tu mod par byung ngo / /las 'go 'jam dbyangs mchog grub kyis bgyis te/ der 'du khang rung khang sogs mdzad/ btsun ma rnying pa rnams dang / rin chen chos
sgron sogs gsar du skra phud phul ba bcas bcu drug tsam gyis kyang so so'i grong khang brtsigs shing / dgon pa'i ming bkra shis chos sding zhes rang byung du chags/ mgo zla'i
tshes mgor 'di nas chibs kha bsgyur te dgon gsar bkra shis chos sding gi bzhugs khrir pheb skabs/ gsung las/ 'di gsar 'debs yin kyang gnas rnying 'dra ba zhig byung
gsungs te dges/ der bzhugs zhag gnyis gnang zhing phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa kha shas la tshe dbang bla ma zhi khro dang / dgon sar mang ja gral 'gyed stsal/ de lo
dgun chos zhag bco lnga bla brang nas gnang zhing lo bstar dgun chos zhag bco lnga re 'ongs pa dang / grub dbang dam pa sgro mo lung pa mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel gyi
snang brnyan gsar bzhengs mdzad cing / sku mchod du bla ma'i rnal 'byor zla ba byung ngo cog gtong rgyu bcas kyi thebs kyang stsal/ dgon pa de dmag zor ma la gnyer gtad
mdzad pas legs nyes stang 'dzin 'phral du byung bas na/ dgon gsar gyi lha mo zhes snyan grags che'o/ /de nas grong chen du

phebs/ yang grub dbang kun bzang klong grol gdan drangs/ a ti zab don snying po dang / mkha' 'gro snying thig sogs kyi smin khrid gsan/ rgyab rten lung la/ snying thig chos
tshan bdun cu rtsa bzhi/ rdzogs chen rgyud ma bu bcu bdun/ g.yu thog snying thig gi dbang / me dbang mtha' brten dang bcas pa/ mchog dbang / don dbang / tshe dbang / sman
gyi lha mo'i rjes gnang sogs/ gza' rgod dug gi spu gri'i be'u bum/ gter chen 'gyur med rdo rje'i gsang ba'i rnam thar sogs mang du gsan no/ /'di skabs mus chen nas/ dud
sol ma'i rjes gnang zhig gsol ba btab pas/ nam 'ong gi bka' gsal ma byung bar gsang ba'i mgon khang na mus chen/ rdzong rams pa gnyis yod par/ skabs shig srod yol tsam la
rdzong rams pa thugs dam grol nas gzims/ mus chen gyis ma grol bar mnal dang 'dres mur shin tu bzhad bro ba'i nyams mdzad pas/ rdzong rams pas thugs dam gyi mur bzhad bro
rgyu ci 'dug zhus par/ a 'jigs pa la/ gtor sgam gyi rgyab de na bud med 'jigs su rung ba ral pa rting par sleb cing / mig hrig hrig /so tham tham/ spar ba deng deng byed
pa zhig 'dug gsungs nas/ thugs dam grol te gzims tshar ba dang / dum tsam zhig nas sku mdun du 'bod mi gnang ba bzhin bcar bas dud sol ma'i rjes gnang gnang ba grol mtshams/
gsol ja'i skabs/ rje 'di nyid kyi gsung las/ mdang nga'i rmi lam du mdun 'di khar bud med gos hrul po gsum bsgrigs nas nga la kha khrig khrig mig hrig hrig byed cing
/ cung mi mnyes pa lta bu

zhig byung gsungs pas/ rdzong rams pa'i thugs la/ bzang ngan ci ltar yang bla slob dam pa 'di gnyis la ni gzigs snang gcig pa de 'dra byung 'dug /mgrin bzang gzig lpags gyon
pa khyod gnyis snang gi sbang dri 'tshub be ga le sku bzhugs gnang zhig snyam pa byung gsung / khong gnyis la dud sol dang beg pod kyi lung beg tse lcam dral dang lha mang
gnyis kyi rjes gnang rnams stsal/ yang de sngon tsam la mus chen la bka' gnang ste sgrub chen ting 'dzin chos rgyal drung nas ma gcig thang stong snyan brgyud lugs mus
chen gyis gsan pa de phul skabs/ gsung las/ kha seng dbyar rmi lam du ma gcig gi sku gcig mjal byung ba chos 'di thob pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug gsungs so/ /rab byung zhes
pa me yos lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du lha ldan karma shag gi lcam sring ma bro shin tu 'tshal bas myur mgyogs chibs bskyod dgos tshul gyi gnas tshul 'byor don ltar dbus
su pheb/ byin rlabs gegs sel du yun ring bzhugs pas nye zho las grol/ de skabs bar seng rnams la sde pa sbor ba sogs lha ldan gyi sbyin bdag kha shas la chos bka' ci rigs
gnang zhing / lhag par sog yul ha la shan gyi bla dpon tho yon dar rgyas nas sngon gyi las 'phro sad pa lta bus rje 'di la bzlog med kyi mos pa thob ste/ dmar po skor gsum/
rnam sras skor sogs chos skal shin tu mang ba nos shing thugs yid gcig 'dres su gyur pas/ tho yon chos rjes rang yul du rje 'di nyid dus 'khor 'dzugs pa sogs la pheb
dgos kyi snyan gsan phul bar/ sku rtsed kyi rnam pas/ nga sog yul du 'gro ba la de na la phug med 'gro bas mi 'ong gsungs pa na/ de

'dra spang gi ldebs la gang mnos su skye ba yin zhes sogs rnam pa du ma'i sgo nas gdan 'dren re zhus 'dug kyang / re zhig gdul bya'i zhing du ma gyur/ de nas yar klung du chibs
bskyod/ 'brug lo bco brgyad gdung rin po che dang / bod 'brug chos rje sogs nyung shas la gcad rgya'i thog nas nang khrid ma gtogs mgon po che ba'i skor yongs su rdzogs
pa/ mkha' spyod ma'i khrid/ dbu ma che ba/ lung yongs rdzogs/ gser chos skor tshang ma/ rnam sras rin chen bco lnga'i rjes gnang lung bcas pa/ gzhan yang dbang rjes gnang
zur bka' shin tu mang ba sogs lo 'khor la nye ba tsam gsung chos chig sgril mdzad/ de skabs mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs grub nas/ gdung rin po che'i zhal dkyil chus
bkrus kyang / dbu dpral gyi sindhUr ma nyams par zhag shas gsal por gnas pa ni bla slob gnyis ka'i grub rtags dang / sgra mdo kA la pa'i sa ris phyag khrid mdzad pas thogs
med du mkhyen pa sogs la thugs lhag par mnyes shing / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad do/ /sa sbrul lor phal cher gcad rgya
kho nar bzhugs pa'i thugs dam gyi rim pa la nan tan mdzad de she'u grong du pheb zhor rmor du pheb cing / grwa pa rnams la mang 'gyed dang / rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gi
sku mchod du zla ba byung ngo cog la bla ma mchod pa gtong rgyu'i thebs su dngul srang nyi shu rtsa drug /mdzod pas zhal 'debs srang do bcas dang / rmor gyi dgon lag /rab
brtan dgon gsar dang / bsam gtan gling bcas par rdo rje 'chang gi sku mchod thebs kyang rgyas par stsal/ rta lo she'u grong gsang sngags gling

du nang pa shag gi chos mdzad kyis sbyin bdag bgyis nas phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa shin tu mang bar mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs khrid lung yongs su rdzogs pa dang /
gzhan yang 'dod chos mang bar stsal zhing / rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'i dgongs rdzogs su rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i tshes bcu'i cho ga zla rer chag med 'ong ba'i
thebs su dngul srang sum cu so dgu dang zho drug sbyor 'jags mdzad/ rim bzhin bsam gtan chos gling dang 'phags sder yang zab chos rgya cher stsal te lha ldan du phyags pheb/
lcags rta lcags lug gnyis su chu lho byang gi dgon bzhi bcu skor la mang ja sbyor sbrel dang / gal chen rnams la 'gyed kyang stsal/ lug lor gong zhabs lha mi'i rnam
'dren dam pa rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por bla ma grwa tshang thun mong gi zhabs brtan 'bul ba gnang ba dang chab cig dpal phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po'i
dbang bskur gnang ba'ang gsan no/ /bco brgyad nas gdung brgyud rin po che dang / bod 'brug chos rje zhi ba lha sprul pa'i sku sogs dang / sde pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin
phun tshogs/ sde pa lha dbang nor bu sogs la zab chos ni gu chos drug /gshed dmar gyi dbang / khrid/ lung yongs rdzogs sogs chos bka' rgya cher gnang / 'phan yul du bco
brgyad la gdan 'dren gnang ba bzhin pheb/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang lung bcas dang / gzhan yang zab chos mang bar stsal/ dpal ldan rtse dang nyan po sogs su'ang
chibs bskyod/ slar yang lha ldan brgyud 'on chos sdings su rgyal sras mchog gi

sprul sku rin po che'i mjal phyag la pheb/ chos sdings grwa bgres mang por mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sogs zab chos mang bar stsal lo/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ sgrub pa'i sde
btab bla med chos 'khor bskor/ /skal ldan rjes bzung zab chos bdud rtsi gsol/ /dgon gnas gnyer gtad dbus ljongs 'gro phan mdzad/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon phan bde'i bum bzang
yin/ /zhes so/ /anggir zhes pa chu sprel zla ba dang po'i nang du gtsang la chims bskyod de yar lam bo dong / dga' ldan phun tshogs gling / chos lung / byang rtse/ brag
hram sogs la gnas gzigs mchod 'bul thugs smon mdzad de/ gtsang gzhung brgyud nas pheb par shag mtshal nas grong chen pas chibs bsu zhus te/ de'i lan brgyud rim gyis gram
pa rgyang gi gtsug lag khang rnams mjal bar pheb ste/ da lta'i grong chen dbu byed 'dis gnas bshad pa zhus te/ rgyal ba rigs lnga bzhugs pa'i lha khang zhig la 'di la
chos rgyal lha khang zer zhus pas/ 'o 'di na chos rgyal srong btsan sgom po bzhugs 'dug gsung / sngar phan lha khang de'i ming don 'phrod pa zhig med pa la de phyin kun gyis
nges shes rnyed/ yon po lung dang rgyang 'bum mo che sogs la gnas gzigs mchod 'bul thugs smon mdzad de/ de nub mtsho sor bzhugs/ nag zla'i tshes gcig la grong chen du
pheb skabs ser phreng sogs sngar bzhin zhabs tog zhus te/ zhag gnyis sku ngal bso ba lta bur bzhugs par/ grwa tshang nas rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i zhabs brtan
'bul chog

phan bde'i 'od dkar bzhin phul te/ grwa tshang la tshe dbang dang / dbu byed 'di par gur gyi dmar chen gtor zlog /ru mtshon dang phyi rten 'dzugs pa'i yi ge brgyud 'debs dang
/ bla ma'i sku bstod kha shas kyi ljags lung stsal/ skabs 'dir dgon dmar nub nas grub dbang kun bzang 'brug rgyal byon te/ mtshan brjod kyi ljags lung zhus par/ do nub
phyis pas mi 'ong gsung ba na/ bla ma 'dis khyed rang ni chos nyid mngon du gyur pa yongs grags kyi bla chen zhig yin 'dug /chos thams cad ni chos nyid las 'da' ba med/
nged rang yang chos nyid cha tsam rtogs shing / don de la 'khu 'phrigs med pas/ thog mtha' bar gsum gyi lung gis 'thus zhus pas/ khyed kyi lta ba'i rbad khams de kha yin
mdog rnams kyang da lta'i lag len rtsings spyod de 'dra brgyud pa 'di'i phyag bzhes la med par ma zad/ lag len dogs phyogs nas byed pa zhig bstan pa rin po che'i rgyan du
che ba yin pas/ lung song 'bul gsungs nas gnang / bla ma 'di la 'brel thogs rnams log 'tshor skad cig kyang mi 'gro zhing / thugs dam bzang ba'i tshad thub pa zhig 'dug
gsungs nas thugs gtsigs shin tu che/ yang dgon dmar shar byams pa dpal ldan yang sku mdun du 'byor te/ nged cha lugs 'di bzhin byas pas gzugs por khyad che ba zhig byung
tshul zhus shing / bka' 'grel zhig gnang 'dra'ang gang yin ma nges/ zla nang der grong chen las tshan 'pho len dang / tshes bcu drug la las tshan rnying pa rnams kyi gsol
ston thog /da lta'i 'dar grong mkhan

chen ngag dbang shes rab 'di la thog ma'i 'byor phyag stsal ba ni/ slad kyi gnas tshul sgrig med du gzigs par snang / bcu dgu'i nyin mang mkhar chab tshan la chibs bsgyur/
gter ston bdud 'dul gling pa'i dngos slob byang chub zer ba zhig dang mjal bas/ gter ston de'i gter chos mang du thob 'dug gsungs/ yang de skabs zla dkyil la dpag tshad lnga
bcu yod par gsungs pa 'char tshul la dpag /dbugs kyi 'gro 'ong dang bstun nas brtsi tshul ltar brtsis pas/ cung ma 'grigs par rang nyid nad can du song bas yin nam gsungs/
yar mar gyi pheb lam gnyis kar bsam grub rtser gdan 'dren zhus te zhag gnyis bzhugs/ grong chen du pheb nas zhag shas bzhugs shing / sa ga'i tshes mgor 'dir phebs bsu
sogs sngar bzhin zhus te pheb/ de skabs nged rang spun lha chen phun tshogs gling dbang khang na/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi sku rim la/ mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor zlog
cig sgrub skabs su yod pas/ de'i seng dbar zhig la mjal 'phrad zhus/ zhag shas sku ngal mdzad par sgo rum nang so sogs kha shas su rnam 'joms khrus gsol dang / gsung bskang
gnang / da lta'i 'dar grong mkhan chen 'di nyid gzhon nu nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi bag chags sad pa lta bus rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye brag sa ngor gyi bstan pa
la thugs dad phul du byung ba bcas/ mkhas grub dam pa du ma bsten mu las rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid la'ang mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob ste/ 'di gar yang gsung chos kyi gras
su tshud pa zhig dgos tshul dang / rje 'di nyid la'ang de bzhin

sngar nas gsol 'debs mdzad yod 'dug pas/ nyer len mtshams sbyor yang dag zhus te chu sprel dang / chu bya lo'i bka' chos phal cher gyi slob gras su yod pa ltar/ zla ba de'i
tshes bcu gsum nas bzung / rtse chen lha khang du bka' chos btsugs par ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma/ bco brgyad byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyis mdzad
pa'i rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i gson sbyong / mchod rten bzhengs tshul dang / srog shing 'dzugs chog mkhyen brtse 'od zer dri med kyi dkyil chog dang / de'i kha skong / gtsug
tor dri med kyi dkyil chog /dri med rnam gnyis kyi gzungs chog /'chi bslu mthong ba don grub rnams mkhan chen zhwa lu pas mdzad pa/ thugs sras lo tsA ba'i gtsug tor dri
med kyi tsha chog /srog shing 'dzugs chog gsal byed rmor chen gsung la kha rag chos rje blo bzang don grub kyi zin bris/ rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i dmag zor ma'i las gsum
rnam bzhag /gu ge paN chen gyi bde mchog bor zhal mngon dkyil chos rje bla ma'i thugs rje chen po'i smar khrid che chung / bu ston rin po ches mdzad skor la/ chos spyod
rnam mkhyen bde lam/ dus 'khor rgyud bshad/ rin chen gces pa'i lde'u mig /sgrub thabs rin chen snying po/ /cho ga dngos grub myur stsol/ gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel/ gsang ba'i
sgo 'byed/ bde mchog rgyud kyi spyi don rnams dang / mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang gis mdzad skor la/ 'jigs byed 'khrul 'khor rnam bshad/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ de'i
bu yig lnga/

rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags bzang gis mdzad skor la/ dus 'khor sgrub thabs/ bdag 'jug gnyis kyi lung dang / a mes zhabs kyis mdzad skor la/ kun rig sgrub dkyil gzhan phan lhun
grub/ de'i snyen thabs sbyin sreg dang bcas pa ma nor don gsal/ tshe dpag lha dgu'i sgrub dkyil 'chi med dpal ster/ sngags 'chang chen po'i tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang chog
'chi med lam bzang / dkon mchog lhun 'grub kyi tshe dpag lha dgu'i brgyud 'debs/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang skal bzang rgya mtsho'i bde mchog tshogs mchod snying po rab
dgyes/ 'jigs byed chos skor 'bri gung dpal 'dzin be'u bum/ sngags rams pa dge 'dun bkra shis dang spyid shod pa bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho'i yig steng nas phyag drug mgon po'i
bka' bcu gsum dang / mgon po snying zhugs kyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i rtsa brgyud bla mar gsol 'debs dang / dus min 'chi zlog /'od zer can ma'i sgrub
thabs/ bsam yas bka' 'gyur ba buddha'i mtshan gyi kun rig dpa' gcig sgrub thabs/ ngag dbang chos grags kyi lho sgo'i lhan thabs/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyi 'jigs byed
brgyud 'debs/ rmor chen rje'i bka' 'bum phal cher/ rje nyid kyi gsung 'bum gras nas rgyud bzhi'i brgyud 'debs/ yang rje rdo rje 'chang dang grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho
gnyis kyi gsol 'debs/ rje nyid kyi rnam thar gsol 'debs dang / zhabs brtan gsol 'debs tsho lnga/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ khyung khra nag rnams kyi sgrub thabs/ tshA dkyil
'bring

po'i thig rtsa/ dus 'khor brgyud 'debs/ sgrub dkyil rnams dang / gzhan yang rdo rings kun spang chen po'i gsol 'debs mtha' yas ma sogs kha shas/ g.ya' bzang pa/ bya khyung
pa/ snye mo ru'i gdung sogs kyis mdzad pa'i steng gdon gso ba'i man ngag shin tu mang ba/ de gras a mes zhabs dang / rigs 'dzin phrin las lhun grub kyi nyi ma mdung gang
gi man ngag /a tsar dmar po'i ser srung skor/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po'i gsung la nyag re rin grags kyis zin bris mdzad pa'i srog shing 'dzugs chog /dus 'khor rgyas pa'i
sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs yon tan rab rgyas/ de'i ngag 'don mdor bsdus/ dus 'khor sa chog gi ngag 'don/ dus 'khor zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sdug bsngal zhi byed dang / sgra pA
Ni'i mdo 'grel bcas rgya gar nub phyogs kyi paNDi ta go kuu la nA tha dang / 'dar lo ngag dbang phun tshogs gnyis kyis bsgyur bshad lung rgyun sogs shin tu dkon cing zab
pa'i lung mang po dang / mkhas grub shangs pa do ku ba'i gser chos la/ 'jug sgo yon tan kun 'byung / chos drug so so'i bka' sogs byin rlabs kyi rigs dang / bla ma brgyud
pa'i rnam thar nas bzung / be'u bum bzhugs che nges kyi lung / grub dbang thang stong rgyal po'i khrid yig la gzabs bshad du mas brgyan pa'i khrid bka' smin rgyas/ 'chi
med 'khrul 'khor gyi lag len rags rim sogs/ shangs chos ni gu'i skor la'ang 'di bas lhag pa med snyam pa'i nges pa can dang / ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i
sgrub dkyil la/ kha'u brag

rdzong pa'i bla ma gong ma'i phyag len gyis brgyan pa'i chag lugs/ gshin rje'i gshed dmar po lha lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du sta gon dang / dngos gzhi gnyis kyi sgo
nas smin byed dang / 'od gsal 'char ba'i byin rlabs grol byed spros med kyi khrid/ chos 'byung khog dbub/ bskyed rim gyi bshad pa sogs legs bshad ganggA'i chu rgyun zab
cing rgya che ba'i sgo nas rjes su bzung ba dang / rjes 'brel 'di skor rgya bod kyi yig sna kha shas kyi ljags lung dang bcas pa stsal/ 'di skabs zhi dgon mkhan chen bsod
nams dpal bzang dang / rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol kyang chag med yod/ de skabs ngos la gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dbang rgyun dgos gsungs pa bzhin de gong nas dpe
'dzin grub pas phul chog ma yod kyang / glo bur du cham pa zhig gis rkyen byas 'bul stabs bde min gyi skabs/ rje'i gsung las/ da lam dbang rgyun de rten 'brel gyi gnad
cig gis cung zad ma 'grigs pas mi zhu zhing / 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po dang / sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon bcas kyi rnam thar lung dgos
gsungs pa ltar 'jam dbyangs sku mched kyi rnam thar a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa dang / dus zhabs pas mdzad pa'i a mes zhabs kyi rnam thar/ mangga'i mtshan can gyis mdzad
pa'i bsod nams dbang phyug gi rnam thar/ nam bsam pas brtsams pa'i kun dga' bkra shis kyi rnam thar rnams kyi lung phul/ chu stod zla mjug tsam la 'di nas chibs kha bsgyur
te dbyar grong chen du pheb/ tshar chen gyi dus

mchod chen mo'i tshogs dbur yang pheb cing / de skabs mnal ltas su yol ba zhig gi nang na kye rdo rje'i sku skye mched shin tu gsal ba zhig yod pa gzigs gsungs pa ni cho ga
rnam par dag cing / ting 'dzin las su rung ba'i gzigs snang du mngon/ grol nyin char smug shin tu che bar la cha'i sbal gzugs la brten pa'i char gcod zhig gnang bas nam
mkha' kun char smug gis 'thibs bzhin du/ de thad kyi nam mkha' dwangs shing 'od gsal bas kun gyis ngo mtshar du 'dzin pa byung zhing / gtor zlog nyin dpa' dam shubs ldan
legs pa zhig bsngo rten 'bul mi byung bar/ rten 'brel gyi la nyer shin tu bzang / mi mthun pa'i g.yul las rnam par rgyal bar 'dug gsungs/ sku mchod grol 'phral rje nyid dang
/ grwa tshang / mus chen/ da lta'i 'dar grong mkhan 'di dang bcas 'dar gyi gla tshal du chab bdug la nyin gsum tsam pheb skabs tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi 'gur 'bum
gyi ljags lung gnang bzhed yod par phyag dpe thugs stabs ma bde bas gnang ma thub kyang / dpon slob tshang ma thugs spro ba'i tshad thub pa zhig byung zhing / gsung bag pheb
la byin che ba du ma zhig slob snang yod 'dra'ang ji bzhin ma nges/ gso rig rgyud bzhi'i lung gnang skabs bco brgyad gdung rin po che de nyid ltem babs lci bas gsung
brtag zhu mi byung bar/ bka' las/ da lam blo tshab nyams kyis brtag pa ji bzhin byed thub pa dka' bas blo la gang shar zhig zhu bas zla ba 'di kha'i tshes bcu bzhi tshun
la skyon ma byung na sku rim 'di rnams mdzod gsung ba stsal yang / rjes sor

tshes de'i sngon la mya ngan las 'das zin 'dug pa 'das pa'i dus la ma thogs ma chags pa'i ye shes kyi gzigs pa 'jug pa/ zhes nyan rang dang ma 'dres pa'i sangs rgyas spyi'i
khyad chos der snang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i bka' 'bum gyi lung / grub chen lcags zam pa'i rnam thar 'gyur med bde chen gyis mdzad pa de ljags lung sang gnang rgyu'i
nub rje ngag gi rmi lam du rtogs ldan ral pa sngo bun ne ba/ sha rtsi dmar nyams che ba zhig mnyam gzhag sogs lus gnad dang ldan pas rje ngag la mig zur gyis bltas pas
bag chags 'di rang grol rang yin zer ba zhig rmis pas/ nangs snga mus chen dang gsung gleng byung 'phral bla brang du 'bod mi gnang bas dbang khang steng gur g.yab cig
gi nang na bzhugs nas gsung 'phros su/ khyed dpon slob la mdang dgong grub thob chen po'i mnal ltas bzhin e byung pheb par/ mus chen nas de'i lo rgyus zhu ba gnang ba'ang
gong dang 'dra zhing / gzhan yang dur khrod bdag po dang / rnam sras ser chen gnyis kyi rjes gnang / khrid brgya'i zhen pa bzhi bral dang / sum pa lo tsA ba'i blo sbyong
gnyis la gsung bshad dang nyams khrid/ gzhan rnams kyi lung yongs rdzogs/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi dbang lung khrid rnams yongs rdzogs stsal/ yang 'og min chos sde pa ngag
dbang nor bu grong chen slob dpon sbyin pa dang dbu rnying / da lta'i dbu byed sogs nyung shas la sgrol dkar/ 'jam nag rnam 'joms/ seng gdong sngo dmar/ zhal dkar po tshe
'phel rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / de rnams kyi las

tshogs yig lung kha shas stsal zhing / de dag dang dus mtshungs dge 'phel lha bzo ba kun dga' rgya mtsho 'dar smad lha khang du sgrol ljang gi sku skya bzo'i bka' bkod stsal
ba bzhin zhus/ khrums zla'i bco lnga la snye thang 'phags sde ba kun dga' smin grol/ byams pa dpal ldan/ grong chen dbu byed blo gsal chos 'dzin rnams la bsnyen rdzogs
gnang / tha skar zla nang ding rir chibs bskyod de bsam grub tu bzhugs zhag dang / de nas rim gyis brgya tsho la brgyud pheb lam rnams su shel spe lding dpon/ 'ga' ra ba
sogs nas kyang tshe bka' zhu ba dang zhabs tog rgya cher sgrub cing / rim gyis glang 'khor du pheb ste/ zhi byed bstan pa'i bdag po glang skor gdan sa pa'i gdung brgyud du
'khrungs shing / gzhon nu'i dus su byang ngam ring du mtshan nyid kyi skor la gsan sbyong mdzad/ de nas rang gi khu bo bla chen 'chi med blo gros bstan pa sogs yongs 'dzin
du ma bsten nas/ mdo sngags kyi chos tshul spyi dang / bye brag zhi byed brgyud pa phyi ma'i skor la gsan bsam dang sgrub pa mthar phyin mdzad pas blo sbyong lam lnga'i
dka' thub kyi srang las brgal zhing gzhan snang zil gyis gnon pa sogs sku che ba'i yon tan du ma dang ldan pa des/ snga thog ding ri khul du zhi byed kyi chos 'di dar
thub pa zhig mi 'ong 'dra bas/ gter chen 'gyur med rdo rje'i zhabs nas rnying lugs chos bka' du ma gsan nas/ gang la gang 'dul gyis 'gro don byed snyam smin grol gling du
byon te/ bka' chos ci rigs gsan nas rang yul du log rgyu'i thon phyag skabs/ gter chen chos kyi rgyal

pos glang skor gdan sa pa zhes 'bod pa gnang nas/ khyed rang rje dam pa sangs rgyas nas brgyud pa'i zhi byed bstan pa'i bdag po yin pas/ de kho na dar zhing rgyas pa'i thugs
bsam che bskyed dgos so gsungs pa bzhin/ lugs 'di la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad cing / 'chi med kyi rig 'dzin brnyes pas dgung lo dgu bcur nye bar bzhugs pa'i grub pa'i
dbang phyug chen po 'chi med gzhon nu blo gros kyi drung nas/ zhi byed brgyud pa phyi ma'i skor las/ blo sbyong gi rtsa ba'i byin rlabs A li kA la'i brda dbang chen mo/ yi
dam 'khor lo bde mchog /phag mo zhal gnyis ma lha dgu/ phag mo dmar chung khros nag /bdud rtsi bum pa/ gtum mo che chung bzhi dang bcas pa'i dbang / thugs dam bde gshegs
bcu gnyis kyi rjes gnang / zhing skyong kun tu ri ka'i rjes gnang dang / ye shes kyi mgon po a gho ra'i rje gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ spar bu nag po'i rjes
gnang / zhi byed blo sbyong lam lnga'i khrid/ gso rig pa gcer mthong gi khrid gnyis/ A li kA li gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa chu klung chen po'i rgyud/ mngon dkyil
dbang rjes gnang sogs kyi yig skor tshang ma/ dam pa bla mchod/ rten 'brel khang 'jug sogs rten 'brel skor/ mgon po'i skor sogs skyabs mgon dam pa nyid nas gsan/ rje 'di
ding rir sang pheb rgyu'i nub mo bla ma'i mnal ltas su/ ding ri bla brang gi bzhugs khri'i steng du bud med shin tu yid du 'ong ba blta bas chog mi shes pa zhig gis mar me
chen po spar bas yul khams spyi dang / lhag par shar phyogs su gsal bar snang ba rmi

bas/ zhi byed 'di dbus su dar ba zhig ci nas kyang 'ong 'dra bas sku zhabs dang chos mdzad lags dpon g.yog gnyis nas rem mdzod ces gsungs zhes bka' las thos so/ /mgon po'i
rjes gnang skabs mgon khang nas btso rgyugs pa ding ri ba kun gyis mthong ba'i cho 'phrul che bar byung 'dug /der chibs drel sogs kyis ha cang yun ring bzhugs ma thub pa
dang / bla ma'ang sku na smin ches pas 'phar lung du gsan dgos bcas lung ltos che ba rnams gsan par rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol 'jog par mdzad/ gnya' nang sogs su gnas
gzigs la pheb bzhed che'ang kha ba che gshis pheb ma thub/ mar lam ri bo che pas lcags chu mor gdan 'dren gnang ste/ gdung brgyud rje btsun ma mched sogs la brgyad stong
pa'i lung dang tshe dbang sogs gnang / slar yang grong chen du pheb/ zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyer lnga nas grong chen pa'i dge 'dun 'ga' zhig dang / zangs ldan pa'i grwa rigs/
bsam chos pa/ shar chen pa/ mngon dga' ba/ spo ra ba/ phug chen pa/ khro phu'i sgrub chen 'og min chos sde'i dbu byed 'gyur med/ rdzong rams pa bcas dang / da lta'i
grong chen mkhan po ngag dbang shes rab bcas par/ mkha' spyod ma skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid lung shin tu rgyas pa/ 'di skabs snga chos la kye
rdor rgyu dbang ma thob pa'i bla brang rdzong pa'i dbu byed la sogs pa kha shas la thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid tshems bu lugs gnang / khrid rnams grol mtshams zangs bstan
pa'i grwa

rigs shin tu mang bar nyin gcig la kun rig gi dbang cha gsum dang / rdzong rams pas gsol ba btab ngor/ gtsug lag khang du seng ldeng nags sgrol gyi chings sngon 'gros jo lugs
sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang nyin gcig la tshar ba dang / 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal lha lnga/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub/ spyan ras gzigs gtso rkyang phyag bzhi pa rnams
kyi rjes gnang / rgyal sras bka' 'bum gras nas smyung gnas kyi skor dang / rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i smyung gnas/ sa los mdzad pa'i mi 'khrugs pa dang / kun rig gnyis kyi
brgyud 'debs kyi lung / thugs rje chen po'i sgo nas mig gsal byed nyang ston grub pa'i gter ma sogs/ gzhan yang yig cha du ma'i lung stsal lo/ /dgung keg rkyen sel la zangs
bstan grwa rigs kha shas kyis sgrol ma 'bum ther 'don pa'i dam bca' phul/ rje ngag /shangs dga' ldan chos 'khor gyi grwa pa/ ri bo che mkhan chen gyi zhal gras/ khro
phu'i sgrub chen gsum la chos chung brgya rtsa/ rgyal sras bka' 'bum sogs kyi ljags lung kyang stsal/ dgun der rdzong rams pa sogs byang rigs kha shas kyi tshogs 'khor dang
bcas sku zhabs su bcar dus tshe rta sogs kyi dbang stsal/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bco lnga nas bzung dza lung rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos lha btsun kun bzang rnam rgyal
gyi dag snang rig 'dzin srog sgrub kyi chos skor pusti gnyis/ pad gling phyag rdor dregs 'dul/ shar gter zhi khro nges don snying po/ /shar gter dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi
chos skor rnams phul/ chu bya lo

gsar tsam la/ chos zhu ba byings po gyes shing / rje ngag nas phyag dpe kha cig gi zhus dag zhu mur 'grel pa dur seng steng nas kA la pa'i mtshams sbyor ri mo bka' drin stsal/
rje nyid nas lam 'bras lha khang gi dpe rnying 'ga' zhig la rdul sprug dang sbrags gzigs rtog gnang bas rkyen byas thog mar mgul cham dang / rjes sor glo tshad lta bur
ltem bab lci bar/ nged la smad 'di rang 'phrod pa 'ong yod ces glo gnyan gcig shos shig rje ngag la bka' stsal gyis sbyar ba phul zhing / phyag mdzod nas mang 'dar khul
gyi dgon gnas tshang mar mang ja/ grong chen du'ang mang ja kha shas thog pho rta spus legs kyi rta 'gyed/ bskang gso snyan shal 'bul ba sogs zhabs brtan ji snyed bsgrubs
rjes/ bka' las/ mdang dgong rmi lam du rgya dpon 'ga' zung dges nyams kyis dpa' dar dgos zer bar kha 'thags btags pa rmis pa bcas da rang skyon mi 'ong ba 'dra pheb pa
nas bzung sku khams jai bder song mtshams/ 'dar bsam grub tu sman thang yum/ bsam grub dgon gsar nas dge slong gnyis bcas par mkha' spyod ma'i bshar khrid byin rlabs bcas
stsal zhing / yum nas mkha' spyod ma'i bsnyen pa'i tshad cho ga dang sbyin sreg nag 'gros ma gnyis gsar bsgrig zhus pa bzhin mdzad/ slar yang khrid zhu ba sogs zhal ngo
tshang ma dang / rmu brag shod ri khrod nas rje ngag /da lta'i grong chen dbu mdzad bcas 'byor pas tshe bka' rgyas par stsal zhing / 'og gi mnal ltas lung bstan kyang 'di
skabs gnang ba yin zhing / gang ltar

zla ba bzhi pa nang mang mkhar chab la chibs bskyod/ slar yang bsam grub tu yum sras la chos bka' ci rigs gnang zhing / dza lung dpon slob nas snyan brgyud dza bhir gyi lung
dang / rlung zas kyi spungs khrid zhag gsum tsam la rdzogs par gsan nas grong chen du pheb/ zla ba lnga pa'i nang grwa phu dgon gsar du pheb/ grwa phu gzhis gnyer sger
dang / sgrub sde/ mi ser mang tsam bcas par tshe dbang / sgrub sde/ grong chen dbu mdzad/ rdzong rams pa bcas par byang gter thugs sgrub drag po rtsal gyi byin rlabs thugs
dbang / de'i las byang / thugs rje chen po 'gro ba kun sgrol gyi las byang / gsol 'debs le'u bdun ma/ gter bdag mchod phreng sogs yig lung tshang ma dang / rta mgrin gsang
sgrub kyi rjes gnang / gter chen bla mas mdzad pa'i gu ru padma'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs char 'bebs/ gzhan yang ljags lung gi rigs mang ba dang / tshogs 'khor
gzabs rgyas bcas stsal/ de nas shing mang dgon la pheb/ rta mgrin ma gtogs dbang lung tshang ma gong bzhin stsal nas 'dar smad du pheb skabs/ da lta'i grong chen dbu byed
'dis rnam 'joms kyi khrus bsgrubs nas gtsug lag khang la khrus gsol dang / rje nyid pheb 'phral sku khrus 'bul ba sogs byas/ phyag mdzod 'jam dpal dang chos mdzad rnam
grol/ gsol dpon mchog grub bcas nas rje nyid der pheb/ gdong du sgrol ma'i rtsi gsol rnams grub ste pheb bsur byung ba dang smad lkog pa'i chibs bsu ba rnams kyang der 'byor/
shing mang ba'i pheb skyel ba dang bcas pheb lam

gyi grong khyer dang smad lkog pa rnams nas dar 'phyar bsang dud dang bcas pheb/ zhag shas bzhugs thog sgrol mar phyag nas dang / phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa'i skye
bo stong phrag brgal ba la bla ma zhi khro'i tshe dbang rgyas par stsal zhing / de rnams kyis zang zing gi mchod sprin bteg /der yod drag gras rnams nas so so'i khyim du
gdan 'dren zhus/ 'dar khang gsar pas gos ling gi snam sbyar dmar po zhig phul ba'ang jo bo'i sku la 'bul bar gnang zhing / kha shas la phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi ljags lung
sogs chos bka' ci rigs stsal/ sgrol ma'i sku la dpon g.yog tshang mas snyan dar phul bar mdzad/ gsol tshigs skabs da lta'i grong chen dbu byed 'di rdor dkar du yod pas
chos mdzad rnam grol nas khyod la 'di skad 'dri ste/ sha zos pa dang ma zos pa la phan yon dang nyes pa ci 'dra yod ces byung ba na/ rje nyid nas theg pa che las sha rnams
bkag /zos na ngan 'gro'i rgyu ru gsungs/ /bya ba min nam/ zhes gsungs nas bzhad mo mdzad/ yang snga dro zhig grong chen dbu byed 'di la khyung lung ma'i gtor ma zhig bzos/
na nyin nas gzhi bdag phyir spos pa 'di khyung lung ma rang du 'dug pas gtor bsngo byed pa yin gsungs pa ni 'od gsal gyi ngang du gzigs par mngon/ de skor gyi thugs brel
rnams chod bstun grong chen du pheb nas lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad de/ 'di khar chu stod zla ba'i bdun brgyad gang rigs shig
gi nyin shar nas thar rtse rdo rje 'chang

dang / nub nas rje 'di nyid pheb pa nyin gcig la shar bas/ 'dren mchog gnyis ka'i drung pheb bsu sogs sngar rgyun bzhin bsgrigs te rig 'dzin pho brang gi gzims chung 'og mar
thar rtse rje dang / steng du rje 'di nyid kyi bzhugs yul bsgrigs par mjal 'dzom zhus skabs/ gsung las/ thar rtse grub dbang chen po'i bzhugs yul 'og na yod pa 'di bzhin
zhe 'tshor bas lhun grub pho brang du spo dgos gsungs pa bzhin/ sngon gyi nang gogs bzhugs mi spro bar yod kyang / bla bre yol ba/ sngags 'chang chen po'i thugs dam rten
sngags thang gras gcig zhal phye ba sogs kyis mdzes par bgyis te/ de kha'i nang shar nub gnyis su dpon g.yog tshang ma bzhugs gdan 'jags/ nged rang gi nu bo rgyan mchog
gcong chen der chu stod tshes bcu'i nyin zhal dkar bas sbyong btang bar shar phyogs dam sel can zhig slebs pas rkyen byas rlung gi rnam pas lnga'i lam po cher chas pa na/
skyabs mgon mtshungs med 'di gnyis kyi srung 'khor dang ljags gul gyi dud pas 'chi bdag gi lam nas slog tsam byung yang / shin tu nyams nyes su gyur pa'i skabs rnam 'dren
dam pa 'di nyid kyi tshe dbang brgya tshar stsal ba'i sang de nas cung zad drag ngo bltas/ de nas phun tshogs gling dbang khang du nged rang mched sogs la rgyud gsang
ba snying po'i sems nyid ngal bso rtsa 'grel/ ngal bso skor gsum gyi spyi bshad legs bshad rgya mtsho/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i bka' 'bum tshang ma/ mkhyen brtse'i zhal
gyi gtor chen/ sngags

'chang shAkya dpal gyi gdugs dkar dkyil chog /de'i lhan thabs zhwa lu mkhan chen/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi gsung skor la/ gsung ngag khog phub/ snang rgyud legs
bshad/ sems bskyed chen mo/ slob ma rjes 'dzin/ aShtA'i bzlas lung / dam tshig gi rnam bshad/ phyi nang bskyed rim gyi bshad pa/ tshar gsum khug pa'i yi ge /lam dbang mtha'
dpyod zur 'debs/ bdag med ma'i byin rlabs/ lam zab bla ma rin 'byung / brda don gsal ba/ lam sbas bshad/ brda chig brgyud dang / sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas
gdab/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ mgon rkyang rjes gnang rnams kyi yi ge dang / bka' 'gyur ba'i gdugs dkar mdos chen/ gong sa lnga pa chen po'i gnas brtan mchod chog dang sgrol
mdos/ a mes zhabs kyi kye rdor bsnyen thabs/ mgon po'i chos 'byung / gsung ngag chos 'byung tshigs bcad ma/ bstan pa'i rdo rje'i gsung ngag khrid yig /gter bdag gling pa'i
gsang ba'i rnam thar gnyis dang / mya ngan 'das byung gi skor bcas de rnams kyi lung stsal/ nged rang mched sogs kyis phur sgrub sngon 'gro'i phrin 'chol sogs brel ba
dang / rnam 'dren dam pa zung zhal dgyes legs par mdzad de/ bdag mor legs skyes gsol ras stsal/ phur sgrub chen mo'i skabs rje 'di nyid nas thar rtse grub dbang mchog la
stag zhon dang trag shad kyi rjes gnang gsol 'debs mdzad pa bzhin/ thar rtse rjes trag shad rjes gnang tshar gnyis gnang grub mtshams spyan

'gribs 'phar bas/ stag zhon gyi rjes gnang de rten 'brel ma 'grigs gsungs nas stsal ma thub/ gzhan yang 'di skabs lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i legs bshad kha shas yod 'gro'ang
ji bzhin ma dran/ khrums zla'i nyer gsum nas bzung phun tshogs gling gi dbang khang du dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor yongs su rdzogs par stsal
bar/ phyi khrid sngon 'gro mgon po khro bcu dang / gsang khrid sngon 'gro gur lha dgu/ ba ri mgon rkyang / lcam dral lha gsum lha brgyad thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin
pa/ bcu gnyis ma thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa/ ber nag zangs gri can/ pu tra'i zur bka'/ gcer bu zangs gri can/ bran bdud thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes
gnang rnams dang me 'bar snyan brgyud/ kha skong rnams kyi lung / brag rdzong ma phyi nang gsang gsum dang gsang khrid thun mong ma yin pa bcas kha'u brag rdzong pa'i
bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung rgyun phra mo tshun chad kyang ma nyams shing / chos skyong 'di'i man ngag khog phub kyi legs bshad shin tu rgyas shing mtha' chod par stsal/
'di skabs thar rtse rdo rje 'chang la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs kyang 'bul ba gnang / gzhan yang lo de'i dbyug zla'i nang gzhi thog dbang khang smin grol du gter chen
chos kyi rgyal po gter bdag gling pa'i zab gter gras nas tshe sgrub yang snying kun 'dus kyi lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang / tshe 'khor bcud len/ rgyun khyer las byang
/ dbang chog /tshe khrid/ brtan bzhugs/ bsnyen yig /bstan srung mchod phreng rnams

kyi lung dang / yang de gras gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang zhus nyin sa g.yos shin tu che ba zhig byung bas dregs pa'i srog gtad zhu ma nus pa rten 'brel shin tu 'khyugs rkyen
du song zhing / 'di'i chos skor/ lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs/ las byang / phrin las/ kha skong / dbang chog /lha srin dam 'dogs/ mnan sreg 'phang gsum dang / bsrung bzlog gsad
gsum gyi man ngag /rgyal 'gong gnad 'bebs/ las tshogs bdun pa/ gter srung bdud btsan klu gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ las bum sgrub chog /bsnyen yig /brgyud 'debs/ rgyun khyer/
las byang / gtor ma'i las rim/ me'i las sbyor/ hom yig /de'i ngag 'don/ gnad 'bebs/ gsal byed/ bka' bsgo/ gter bdag gtor chog /mtshams sbyor le'u tshan/ ser srung sogs gter
gzhung ngo ma dang / gsal byed rnams kyi lung / rdor sems thugs sgrub ras bris dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur gnang nas/ lung gi skor la/ zab gter kha byang / rtsa ba'i chos
sna bcu gcig /khrid yig rab gsal snang ba sogs/ de skor gsal byed kyi yi ge kha shas bcas kyi lung / gsang sngags gsar rnying gi yi dam chos srung mang po'i rjes gnang
dkon pa rnams gter bdag gling pa chen pos phyogs gcig tu bsdus par mdzad pa 'dod 'jo'i bum bzang gi dbang lung tshang ma'ang stsal zhing bka' rgya ma'i rnam gzhag sogs phyag
len phra mo tshun chad kyang ma 'chol bar mdzad/ yang byang gter byin rlabs thugs rje'i dbang sngon du

'gro bas thugs sgrub chos skor pod chung gnyis tsam gyi lung dang / dri med rnam gnyis kyi dbang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du stsal/ yang gnyan mgon yid bzhin nor bu stobs
'phrog dbang po'i chos skor stsal ba la/ sgrub dus thun mong ba/ bsnyen dus/ gdong brnyan can/ dkar po tshe 'phel/ thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa/ ser po rgyas byed/
dmar po dbang sdud/ nag po dgra bgegs sgrol ba/ gshin rje ltar sgrub pa/ khyung zhal can rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang / sgrub dus thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang
skabs rang bsrung bka' rgya can gnang ba/ de'ang chos mdzad skal bzang rnam grol gyis shin tu dngos gtsang 'bri bar mdzad de/ rje 'di nyid kyi sgrub pa gnang bas byin
rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba kho bo mched kyi bsod nams bgo skal du thob cing / bram ze mngags gtad kyi rjes gnang dang / ha la nag po'i be'u bum 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi dkar
chag nang bzhin gyi lung kyang kho bo mched ma gtogs gzhan la ma stsal/ 'di gras bri yig thun mong ma yin pa rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis a mes zhabs la'ang
ma gnang ba zhig 'dug pa de/ shing glang lor dpal sa skyar pheb skabs thob/ 'di skabs klu ldings mkhan rin po che rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan stod phyogs dgon lag
rnams su 'byon pa dang mnyam du 'di khar yang pheb par/ stong ra ba'i yi ge'i steng nas bcu gcig zhal lha lnga'i rjes gnang phul ba gnang zhing / dag snang dang 'bul nod
phan tshun 'gran pa bzhin mdzad/ lo 'di'i smin drug zla nang ngos nas pu

tra dang / las gshin rigs gsum gyi rjes gnang rje nyid dang / zhabs phyi tshang mar sgra mi snyan gyi tshe dpag med kyi tshe dbang rnams phul te/ lo 'dir 'dar nas dbus phyogs
la pheb rgyu bcas pheb phyag sngar rgyun bzhin dang / zla ba de kha'i nyer lnga'i snga dror pheb khar dbang khang smin grol bde chen du nged rang mched dang / ma drung
/ sring mo bcas nas mjal kha zhus thog /ma drung de nyid kyis gdung shugs chen po'i sgo nas phyag 'tshal ba dang bcas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don du rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan dang dgung mnyam bzhugs pa sogs zhabs pad yun du brtan pa'i thugs dgongs g.yel med gnang dgos zhu ba mdzad song bar/ phyag dbang dbu thug dang bcas yum
drung rang de bas kyang lhag pa/ nga grub chen thang stong rgyal po dang dgung mnyam byas nas sdod chog ces sogs gzhan ngo srung zhing brtse bas mi bskyungs pa'i zhal bzhes
bzang po dang bcas dgyes nyams 'dzum zhal gyis spras te pheb song bas/ nged rang la sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i sems la 'phreng nyams shin tu che ba zhig byung ba bcas chibs
rags nam mthong bar la 'chi med rdo rje'i gur khang rab gsal nas bltas pa ni dus 'dir dpal sa skyar sku dngos mtha' ma pheb pa'i snga ltas so/ /anggi ra dpal gdong lo
la gtsang phyogs pheb/ /gnas rten mkhas grub gzigs shing zhal bcud gsol/ /gdul bya'i 'phro bskyangs ris med grub mtha' gsos/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon
yin/ /zhes so/ /'di nas chibs skyel thab skyel bcas dang / pheb lam gyi

grogs sbyin bdag rnams nas kyang so so'i mkhos bstun gyi bsnyen bkur dang bkra shis chos lding lta bur zhag sa gnang nas grong chen du pheb bam snyam zhing / gang ltar/ der
grwa tshang nas zhabs brtan gsol 'debs rgyas pa dang / 'dus tshogs sbyin bdag sogs la tshe dbang smin rgyas stsal/ bla brang steng gi ru mtshon rnying pa rnams gsar bzo
bka' drin bskyangs pa sogs chos srid kyi mdzad phrin kha shas bstar yod 'gro'ang de skabs kyi zin bris zhib par ma rnyed/ de nas lha sar sde pa spo ra yab shin tu bro 'tshal
bar brten chibs bsgyur gnad dgos kyi gsol 'debs zhu shog rta bshad kyi thog nas 'byor par de bzhin bka' drin bskyangs te/ mgon khang chen mo/ gsang ba'i mgon khang /
rmu mgon khang bcas su bskang phrin pa brgyad grwa re bka' bkod gnang / rgyal zla'i tshes bcu bzhi la grong chen nas chibs kha bsgyur te la mo sgang du de kha'i dgon ma lag
sbyin bdag bcas nas pheb skyel zhus par/ 'dus tshogs kyi dbus su bzhengs nas lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i bslab bya zhib gsed mthar phyin gyi bka' bkod nan tan stsal te
chibs kha bsgyur/ khog rdzing du grong chen pas thab skyel zhus/ gzhis chen du bzhugs zhag gnang / song nyin gro bo la brgyud de pheb nas grong chen pa'i chibs skyel ba rnams
la gsol ras dang bcas slog pa gnang / de nas pheb lam la zhag grangs ji tsam 'gor dang / bstan 'gro'i don kha shas bka' drin bskyangs yod 'gro'ang zin bris shig ma rnyed/
gang ltar/ 'di skabs rten 'brel mi shis pa kha shas byung snang ba gtsang pheb tha ma'i la nyer mngon/

mar lam gzhis rtser bzhugs zhag gsum bzhugs pa'i bkra shis lhun por rtse shod tshang mas mjal phyag zhu ba gnang zhing / rje ngag la bka' bsgo gzabs rgyas dang / mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i bde mchog nag po pa'i sgrub thabs kyi ljags lung stsal nas phyir pheb/ snye thang brag sna 'phags sde'i gtsang khang sa mug gis zos che
bar zhig gso dang / de zhor 'du khang ma mor yang spen bad gtong rtsios 'dug par thebs su dngul srang bco lnga/ bzang ja 'khor drug /nas khal sum cu/ pho rta legs pa rnams
stsal/ gang spy-i'i bka' slob rnams rgyas pa mdzad de/ lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ gong zhabs lha mi'i rnam 'dren dam pa thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog gi mjal phyag skabs
gong nas dpon rin po ches dbus gtsang kun tu ris med kyi chos sbyin rgya cher mdzad pa bka' drin che zhes dgyes zhal lhug par bstan/ snga lo chu sprel sa bstan spyi dang
/ bye brag kha'u brag rdzong pa'i sgos chag lta bus bco brgyad gdung rin po che mkhyen brtse nus gsum gang sa nas 'gran zla dang bral ba de zhabs pad ma brtan gshis dgongs
rdzogs su dmigs pa'i bco brgyad bla brang nas gsung ngag lam 'bras shig brtse gzigs dgos tshul gyi snyan gsan gnang ba bzhin zhal gyis bzhes shing yar klung du chibs
bsgyur/ chog mang gi tshogs dbu sogs la pheb/ dngos po zhes pa shing khyi zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du 'phen yul du pheb nas bco brgyad kyi tshogs khang du bco brgyad bla brang
gi zhal ngo rnams dang / bod 'brug chos rje/ skyed tshal gong nas chos rje gnyis/ thub bstan ra ba smad kyi bla ma rab 'byams smra ba kun dga' shes rab/

rnam rab dwags po grwa tshang gi bla ma las thog pa/ nyan po chos rje sku mched/ sde pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs sogs dang / gzhan yang phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar
gnas pa nyis brgya brgal ba la gsung ngag rin po che snga chos phyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa rgyas par stsal/ yang tshar bdun pa dus 'dir gsung ngag rin po che'i chos 'khor
bskor ba'i tha ma'o/ /der chos zhu ba byings la cham yams lta bu zhig byung bas rim gyis mched de skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid la'ang mgul cham bzhes par chos thun rnams
sngar mus bzhin chag med dang / cung zad bsdus pa tsam yang ma gnang ba'i sku 'khrugs dang / gzhi nas nyams grib lta bu'i rkyen gyis sku shin tu ltem pa byung bar stag
rtse em chi bsod nams dngos grub 'bod par gnang ba'i 'phrod gzhes dang / zhabs brtan sku rim yang rgya cher gnang ba bcas sku khams dwangs skyed yod tsam byung ba 'phen yul
na lendra nas chibs bsgyur bas/ de nub rang nas cung zad dwangs bskyed yod pa lta bu dang / de nas bzung rim dwangs su gyur/ lha ldan du 'phrod gzhes dang bcas zhag shas
bzhugs thog /snye thang brgyud de yar klung du pheb pa'i lo mjug dang / phag lo'i nang phal cher gcad rgya kho nar bzhugs mur/ ngor bla ma tshe mtshams bsam gtan phun
tshogs dang / 'dar grong mkhan chen ngag dbang shes rab la nA ro mkha' spyod dang / rtsa dbuu ma che ba'i khrid dang / thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum
sogs stsal zhing / zhi ba lha sprul pa'i skur yang grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe khrid sogs stsal/ gzhan

rim gnyis zab mo'i thugs dam kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad/ 'di lo bkra shis chos sde'i gtsang khang gi sku rten rnams la zhig gsos/ zhal gser sogs phun sum tshogs par mdzad cing
/ rten gtso thub pa'i dbang por snam sbyar dang sku pang / nye ba'i sras brgyad la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ khro bo gnyis la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ stag sham/ rten
gtso'i dbu thog tu bla bre/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan bcas kyi 'dra sku rnams la sku pang
dbu zhwa/ mkhan chen gyi dbu thog tu dbu gdugs bcas dang / thub dbang gi phyag gi lhung bzed khebs su gos khra bsgrigs kyi rten khebs/ snyan shal nang mdzod/ nye sras khro
bo bcas la so sor snyan shal bsod btags rnying ma gnyis re ste khyon nyi shu rnams 'bul sbyor mdzad pa'i/ na bza'i rgyur bzang gos sna tshogs kha nyis brgya dang bdun
cu don gnyis tsam nang sha dang bcas pa stsal/ shing phag ston mjug nas bzung ngos mched 'khor bcas kyis gtso cher gong sa rgyal dbang mchog la mjal phyag zhu ba dang /
dbus lho byang gi gnas rten dge 'dun gyi sde bcas mjal bar phyin skabs/ lha sa/ bsam yas sogs su bka' shog rim par pheb ste rnam 'dren dam pa gong gi gdan sa ga la bar yang
bcar dgos tshul pheb don bzhin/ rim gyis khra 'brug tu slebs pa'i sang nyin de yar klung mdo'i gtam snyan bzhugs khri'i drung rje 'di nyid slob tshogs dang bcas pa pheb
'dug pas de 'phral rta babs te mjal dar phul/

bzhugs khri'i ja gral gyi thog dbus lho byang gi gnas tshul las brtsams pa'i gsung gleng zhus pa thugs shin tu dgyes nyams che zhing / rje 'di nyid dpon g.yog rags bsdus bcas
der du ma tsam zhig bzhugs/ ngos 'khor bcas dang / phyag mdzod 'jam dpal bkra shis mthong smon pa'i sde pa bgres pa sogs kyis yum bu bla mkhar mchod mjal grub nas/ rje
dpon g.yog dang lhan cig bkra shis chos sder pheb skabs ser sbreng gi ljags bkod shin tu rgyas pa dang / sleb 'phral gsol ja dang dkar spro/ sku zhabs nas ngos 'khor bcas
la zur chas su/ rtse ja sbag gcig /shan ja sbag gnyis/ mar khal dgu/ rtsam zhib rtsings sdom khal nyer gnyis/ lug khog bzhi/ tshag sha stod gshags/ 'bras ltang gcig /chag
chu ldur sdom khal nyer bdun dang / chos sde nas rtse ja sbag gcig /shan ja sbag gnyis/ mar ltang gcig /rtsam zhib rtsings sdom khal bzhi bcu/ lug khog bzhi/ tshag sha
bzhi 'degs gcig /chag chu ldur sdom khal nyer lnga rnams stsal ba sogs gya nom gyi gsol ras de dag la longs spyod bzhin par zhag lnga bsdad thog ston mo dang / ngos mched
la chos sde'i ring 'tsho'i bden tshig gnang skabs dgu tshan lnga/ bdun tshan bzhi/ lnga tshan gcig /mdzod dar me long ma gnyis/ snam dkar bubs lnga/ gos kha bcu bcas stsal
te yun du 'tsho ba'i khas len dgos tshul sogs kyi gsung bshad zhib rgyas dang bcas rjes su bzung / phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa rnams la dbang bzhi btegs par mdzad
nas kho bos grub rgyal ma'i khrom dbang bgyis

skabs bla brang gzims chung nas ngos mched la nang mdzod me long ma re/ sku gsung thugs rten tshar gnyis bcas phyag bdar du stsal zhing / nged rang la dngul gyi maNDal/ gser
srang gang / bzang gos kyi bla re rgya bzo ma/ gos ling gi yol ba/ rgya phying dmar po'i stan/ stod 'gag /sham thabs/ 'gan sbyar/ lhwam rnams dang / rgyan mchog la'ang
de mtshungs la sham thabs kyi rgyur ther rgyu gtsang bubs zung / lhan du dgu tshan bcu gsum gy-i mgor brjod bsdoms/ dngul srang brgya/ gos yug drug/ ja 'khor drug gnyis/
rgun ltang gnyis/ shing 'bras ltang gcig /pho rta gnyis/ dre'u gcig /kha btags rtags brgyad ma dgu rnams dang / mdzod par nang mdzod me long ma/ dgu tshan gsum gyi mgo brjod/
stod 'gag /lhwam/ gos yug /ja 'khor drug gcig /zla bo drag gras la dgu tshan gnyis dang / dngul srang bcu/ ja 'khor drug /ban tshang par/ dgu tshan/ ja 'khor gsum/ bying
la ja 'khor drug /dgu tshan bcas zang zing gi sbyin pa bla na med pa'i bka' drin stsal/ bkra shis chog mang skabs mdzad pa'i gar dang 'chams sogs bka' drin bskyangs/
nged rang mched la 'gol mjal yang yang gnang zhing / gtsug lag khang mgon khang bcas par mchod mjal/ grwa tshang la bsnyen bkur bcas zhus shing / khyad par mgon khang chen
mor ngos mched kyis zla mjug dus gtor mchod gtor gzabs bsham bcas bgyis te/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med kyis rjes su 'dzin pa dang / snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa dar ba'i phrin
'chol zhus

nged rang gi gsar brtsams rmor chen gsol 'debs/ gong sa rin po che blo bzang skal bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs brtan/ dkar bdud bstod pa/ rtsi dmar drag bskul/ zhal gyi mnga' gsol
rnams kyi lung phran phul zhing / rkyen sel du grub thob tshe dbang zhus thog dngos 'bul brda mtshon tsam phul zhing / dus 'dir bka' 'brel gyi rjes ma yin/ gter ston
chen po kun bzang bde chen rgyal por nged rang nas lung bstan kha shas zhus pa'i gras la/ bsam yas chos skyong sku pheb min gyi skor kyang yod pas de lta'i tshig ris shig
la/ 'di la lha mi gnyis kas bskang bshags bya/ zhes gsungs 'dug pa lhas mi la bskang bshags ji ltar byed ces nyams ldan gyi gsung dang bcas bzhad/ chos sde nas thon nyer
gang spyi'i bslab bya zhib rgyas stsal zhing / sri gcod 'bum par thab skyel bka' drin bskyangs te sku gsung thugs dgyes pa'i rnam rol du bzhugs drung nas thon cing / slar
yang myur mjal kha btags kyi g.yab mo sogs bka' drin bskyangs pa bcas tshe 'dir dngos mjal gyi tha ma yin kyang / yang srid rin po che sogs myur du mjal ba'am/ yang na
skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du rjes su 'dzin pa'i rten 'brel phun sum tshogs par 'grigs so/ /de skabs she'u grong gsang sngags gling gi zhal bdag zhus par zhal bzhes
ma byung yang / nan bskyed zhus pas slar zhal gyis bzhes/ gzhan yang me byi'i lo mgo der lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i mdzad phrin kha shas yod 'gro'ang zin thor ma gsal/ chog
mang gi tshogs dbur pheb cing / zla ba lnga pa'i nang lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ gong zhabs lha mi'i rnam 'dren

chen por zhabs brtan gyi tshul du 'bul skyes rgyas par mdzad/ de'ang rgyal ba'i lung gis zin cing rtsod bral gyi mkhas grub chen po zhang 'gro ba'i mgon po'i chos skor 'di
rnams gter chen chos kyi rgyal po dang / zur chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam par sprul pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams gnyis kyi thugs rje'i bdag rkyen la brten rgyun ma chad
par lus pa rnams gso ba'i dgongs bzhed kyis tshal nas sum ldan rig pa 'dzin pa ngag dbang padma dang / dge slong 'gyur med chos 'phel gnyis gdan 'dren mdzad de/ rig 'dzin
bla ma'i drung nas/ zhang gi bka' rgya'i skor las/ rgyu lam gyi dbang / tshom bu zhe bdun ma'i dbang / rnam thar lha sa ma dang / bsam yas ma gnyis kyi dbang / phyag bzhi
pa'i rjes gnang rnams dang / rgyab rten lung gi skor la/ kha reg pa 'dul ba 'od dang / gtsang ston rnal 'byor/ lo zhig rnams kyi lugs srol tha dad pa la rgyas 'bring
bsdus gsum du grags pa'i skor yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gzhan yang nyang gi phag mo khros nag gi dbang dang / lung phal che ba sogs gsan par mdzad/ dge slong 'gyur med chos
'phel gyi drung nas bka' 'bum pod bzhi'i lung tshal pa kun dga' rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dkar chag nang bzhin gsan/ rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang kun gzigs lnga pa chen po'i gsung
'bum skor rnams yongs su rdzogs pa zhig gsan bzhed kyi rtsad gcod mdzad par/ grwa tshang rnying pa'i grwa gras sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa dge slong blo bzang bsod nams
de nyid kyis bla ma mang po'i zhabs la gtugs te yongs rdzogs gsan cing brgyud khungs dag pa bcas yod

pa'i khungs gsan pas gdan 'dren mdzad de/ bka' 'bum phyi nang skor yig sna brgyad cu brgal ba'i lung gsan/ lho byang chu bzhin nyul nas dam pa'i chos ris su ma chad pa'i zab
don gyi bdud rtsi 'tshol ba la rgyal sras rtag tu ngu'i mched zlar gyur pa bka' 'gyur ba bka' chen thabs mkhas rgya mtsho'i drung nas/ chos sde chen po gsum gyi chos spyod
skal bzang mgrin rgyan tshang ma/ rje rin po che'i sngags rim chen mo/ lam rim sogs mang du gsan/ phar yang mngon rtogs rgyan/ 'grel pa don gsal/ byang sa/ mdzod rtsa/
blo sbyong dpal yes ma/ po to ba'i chig lab ring mo sogs mang du stsal/ rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang po padma bde chen gyi drung nas/ khyab bdag bla ma mi bskyod dkon mchog
lhun grub kyi rnam thar gyi lung sogs gsan/ skal ldan mang por dbang lung khrid shin tu mang bar stsal zhing / 'phags sder chibs bsgyur/ sa skya'i chos spyod rab gsal gyi
lung sogs nyer mkho shin tu mang bar stsal/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyang mang du mdzad de/ bsam gtan chos gling brgyud shel grong gsang sngags gling du 'dus pa'i tshogs
kyis ser sbreng rgyas pa dang / gzhan yang ser skya kun gyis pheb bsu dang bcas te phyags pheb/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad rgyal phur 'grub sbyor gyi nyin she'u
grong gsang sngags gling gi khri la pheb/ ser skya kun gyis legs 'bul phun sum tshogs par bstang zhing / khri ston gyi mang 'gyed sogs kyang gzabs rgyas dang / sgrol ma
nyer gcig g-i rjes gnang / brgyad stong pa'i ljags lung sogs chos bka' mang bar stsal/

snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma lcang skya thams cad mkhyen pa'i bla sman se kun pa dar han em gyi dpon g.yog ched gtad byung bar g.yu thog snying thig gi dbang lung yongs su
rdzogs par stsal/ gcad rgya thung tsam mdzad de/ me glang lor zla ba dang po'i mjug tu smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling du chibs bskyod/ de'ang rmor dgon gyi bla ma ra
ba smad sku rten pa 'das rjes gra pa rnams kyi 'dod mos dang / lhag par rmor chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi thugs sras kyi mchog snyan brgyud bstan pa rin po che'i mnga'
bdag tu gyur pa bcas gong sa nas 'os babs su dgongs pa'i 'gan bzhes dgos tshul gyi zhu shog phul bas rmor chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi gdan sa zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes
gsum gza' tshes bzang ba'i nyin mkhas pa'i dbang po kun mkhyen grags 'byor shes rab nas nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'i bar gyi gong
ma na rim gyi bzhugs stegs seng khri'i spo la zhabs sen gyi zla dbang gsar pa bkod pas dge legs kyi kunda yongs su bzhad pa la rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po'ang chos kyi dbyings
nas mngon par dgyes pa'i shis brjod kyi me tog 'thor bar mdzad dam snyam/ 'di nas bsko 'ja' khri 'gyed sogs dang / gzhan yang sde ba spo ra ba sogs yon bdag ser skya
rnams nas kyang legs 'bul rgyas par mdzad/ de'ang dge 'dun rnams dang dgon lag phan tshun bcas la khri ston gyi mang 'gyed/ sku gsung thugs rten rnams la mchod pa/ gser
chab/ dkar me rgyun 'dzugs sogs dang / phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa rnams la 'dod chos kyang ci rigs stsal/ de nas

'phreng 'og dga' ldan gling du gdan drangs/ der yang zab chos ci rigs dang / mdzod du rje btsun rig byed ma'i gtor 'dzugs sogs mdzad de/ bsam yas brgyud chos sder chibs bskyod/
chog mang gi tshogs dbur pheb cing zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du sku gcad rgya'i thog nas dam rdzas bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa gnang / zla ba lnga pa nas rig 'dzin chen po
tshe dbang bkra shis pa'i drung nas/ gter chen sangs rgyas gling pa'i gter chos bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa'i dbang lung yongs su rdzogs pa/ gter ston 'ja' tshon snying po'i
gter chos dkon mchog spyi 'dus/ zhi khro/ rta nag /tshe sgrub/ ma ning sogs kyi dbang lung phal che ba/ hU~M nag snying thig /'ja' tshon pa'i chos spyod/ ma Ni bka' 'bum
bsdus pa sogs kyi lung / gzhan yang / bka' 'dus las rtsa ba gsum gyi dbang / de'i tshe dbang / chos srung rnams kyi gtor dbang bka' gtad/ rgyab rten gyi lung bcas dang
/ rta mchog rol pa nA ga rakSha'i dbang rgyab rten gyi lung dang bcas pa sogs gsan no/ /me byi lo'i ston mjug tsam nas bzung 'di khar sger chag mtha' dag langs pa lta bus/
nged rang gi nu bo de kye rdor gzhi bsnyen la bsdad mur srog rlung sogs nad babs lci mos me glang chu stod tshes bzhi'i bar je lod du bzung skabs/ gsung brtag dang gang
ci'i gnas tshul gsol ba rnams la bka' slob zhib rgyas su pheb don ltar bsgrubs kyang / dus der myong skal lta bus bya ba thabs zad du gyur skabs ljags bsngo skyabs 'jug
'phral du zhus tshe/ de skabs kyi gter ston lung dang bstun gang ci'i mtshams la sems bso yang

dag bka' drin bskyangs shing / ma 'gyangs par nged rang la dpal sa skya'i chos srid 'dzin skyong gi bka' slob bod yul che grwa phal cher gyis mdzad pa dang / khyad par rnams
'dren dam pa 'di nyid dang 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gnyis nas blo rmongs bdag cag la zhib gsed kyi bka' stsal te/ yang tig dpal sa skya'i gong ma rdo rje 'chang
dang zhal mi gnyis pa de dag gi thugs kyi dgongs pa ji lta ba bzhin 'grub pa zhig byung na ci ma rung dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed kho nas rang gzhan bstan 'gro yongs la dge
ba'i bslab bya yang dag par stsal ba'i bka' shog rin po che da lta lag yod 'di rnams dpyod ldan gyis mthong tshe dad 'dod yid ches kyi mos pa dbang med du skye bar 'gyur
ro/ /de nas sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa blo bzang bsod nams de nyid kyi drung nas rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa lnga pa chen po'i bka' 'bum 'phro rnams gsan bzhed dang /
lhag par bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi mgon du gyur pa lcang skya mchog sprul rin po che'i mjal phyag sogs la lha ldan du chibs bsgyur zhing pheb lam du bsam yas su rab byung
grwa tshang gis gdan drangs te cho ga dang 'brel ba'i zhabs brtan 'bul nod rgyas par zhus/ khrom dbang dang mang 'gyed kyang stsal/ rdo rje 'dzin pa blo bzang bsod nams
drung de nyid la sger gzhung du ma'i rim gro mang po mdzad dgos mur bro 'tshal ba je lod kyi mthar gshegs pas bka' chos gsan pa'i gegs su gyur/ lcang skya mchog sprul rin
po che'i mjal phyag kyang che rgu gzhan gyis mjal phyag rnams grub mtshams su gnang bzhed la

mgron gnyer rab rgyas zer ba tshur rtsad dpyod la gtong ba gnang gshes 'phral du pheb pas shin du dges shing / gsung rab spyi dang / khyad par gsang sngags las brtsams pa'i
gsung gleng yun ring bar mdzad cing / lha ldan du bzhugs ring yang yang sku mdun du pheb dgos tshul gyi bka' gnang zhing pheb skyes kyi gsol ras kyang rgyas par stsal/ 'di
lo karma shag tu lcam sring ma shin tu bro 'tshal bar gegs sel du yun ring bzhugs gdan 'jags shing / sku tsha drung dang / sde pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ zhabs
'bring pa dge slong ngag dbang 'jam dbyangs gsum dang / blo gsal rab rgyas bcas la/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i khrid thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa yongs su rdzogs
pa/ khro bcu dang lha brgyad sogs kyi rjes gnang / lung gi skor sogs dang / rje btsun rig byed dbang mo'i rjes gnang byin rlabs dang / khrid nyer mkho'i lung sogs dang
/ mkha' spyod ma'i khrid dang lung sogs kyang stsal/ sde pa grong stod dang / bon grong sbo ra ba yab sras sogs la thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs kyi dbang lung khrid yongs
rdzogs sogs stsal/ nA lendra pa sogs kyi bsnyen rdzogs kyang mang du mdzad/ lcang lo can gyi gur dang lcam sogs la gter gsar gur drag gi dbang sogs kha shas dang / grub
thob brgyad cu'i thang sku phun sum tshogs gsar bzhengs la rab gnas mdzad/ mkhan po blo bzang dpal 'bar dang / em ji theg mchog gling pa sogs la g.yu thog snying thig
gi dbang lung tshang ma dang / em ji gnyis la rgyud bzhi'i lung yang gnang / gzhan yang sde pa nang pa

nub pa dang / me tog ldum ra sogs kyis mtshon yon bdag rnams la'ang so so'i 'dod chos ci rigs par stsal/ gter ston chen po kun bzang bde chen rgyal po'i drung nas rtsa gsum
bka' 'dus kyi rgyud kyi lung gsan/ bco brgyad nas chos rje sku gzhon pa bsnyen rdzogs mdzad pa'i mtshan ngag dbang kun dga' mkhyen rab sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
du 'dogs par mdzad cing / kye rdor rgyu dbang lam dbang sogs chos bka' kha shas stsal/ rgyal tshab thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku bcar slob dpon pa dang / mkhan po blo bzang
dpal 'bar sogs la/ mgon po khro bcu dang lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / slob dpon pa la rnam rgyal gra tshang gi 'don chog nas gur zhal/ beg tse gsum gyi gtor bsngo/ bstod
bskul/ bskang bshags/ tshogs 'khor bcas kyi lung rnams dang / zur mchog gi sprul sku phrin las blo ldan rgya mtsho sogs nyung shas la snying thig thig le gsang skor gyi dbang
lung rnams stsal/ gzhan yang sku gzugs sku 'khrugs kyis zin gshis thugs blos ma 'khyud pa lta bus chos bka' stobs che ba'i rigs gnang ma thub kyang / dbang rjes gnang
sogs gcad rgya lta bur bzhugs na ma gtogs gseng dbang cung zad tsam yang mi 'byung ba lags/ de nas chos sdings nas zhi byed kyi dpe rnams g.yar zhu gnang ste/ rig 'dzin
skal bzang rnam grol gyi drung nas sngar ding rir gsan ma thub pa'i zhi byed kyi lung rnams 'bul bzhes kyi dbu tshugs/ sngar nas bka' 'gyur bslur ma gnang skabs kyi kha
lhag gi ja dang / gzhan yang rta mdzo sogs dngos po gang yod phul ba'i

gzigs dpe gnang rgyur bstan 'gyur rin po che tshar gcig zhu rgyu'i sde dger snyan gsan dang / yang bskyar zhu yig gnang ba bcas bstan 'gyur rin po che spus gtsang ba/ glegs
shing / glegs thag /chab mgo dang bcas pa 'di lo'i ston gnyer chen don grub kyi gdong nas 'byor pa bzhin yar klung du gdan 'dren mdzad/ dgun thog 'phags sder bzhugs gdan
'jags te/ rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol gyi zhi byed lung 'phros dang / rgya can ma'i lung rnams phul/ sku gcad rgya zla gcig tsam mdzad/ phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas
pa rnams la 'dod chos mang bar stsal/ rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol/ sde pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs dang / 'tsho byed bsod nams dngos grub/ phyogs 'dus dang
sku drung du 'khod pa bcas 'ga' zhig la zhi byed lam lnga'i dbang sogs 'dod chos mang bar stsal/ 'phags sde gnyer tshang la ar po byas par legs skyes kyi gsol ras rgyas
pa dang / snye thang 'or sgrol ma'i sku mdun du 'phags sde grwa dmangs nas sgrol bstod 'bum ther 'gro nges shig grangs gsog gnang / 'phags sde tshogs yongs nas bla brang
la zhig gso byed rgyur dngul srang bco lnga/ ja 'khor drug /pho rta bzang ba/ gyon pa sna tshogs bcu skor bcas stsal/ gter ston chen po 'dzam gling rdo rje nas brgyud pa'i
gza' bdud kyi skor ma lus pa bum pa gang byo'i tshul du bzhugs shing / drang srong bran du 'khol ba'i grub dbang dam pa blo bzang gar gyi dbang po'i drung nas/ gong gnon
gtum po ras chung lugs gtso rkyang gi rjes gnang /

las 'brel rtsal nas brgyud pa sogs/ brgyud pa'i chu bo du ma 'dres pa'i gza' dbang / las 'brel rtsal gyi gza' pod nas nyer mkho mang po/ /g.ya' bzang ba'i nyi ma mdung gang
ma'i skor/ kun bzang rtse pa zi ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad skor/ gling ras bla mchod nA ro gsang spyod kyi yi ge gnyis bcas kyi lung rnams gsan no/ /de nas 'bru
mang zhes pa sa stag lo'i zla ba gnyis pa'i nang bsam gtan chos gling brgyud she'u grong du pheb/ dge 'dun rnams la gsung chos ci rigs gnang mur/ rgyal tshab rin po che'i
sku'i rkyen sel du byad 'grol 'bul bar pheb dgos kyi bka' lung stsal ba bzhin lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ byad 'grol lan kha shas dang / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang
/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i bshar khrid/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi khrid yig gi lung sogs 'bul ba gnang ste/ slar yang she'u grong dang rmo ra sogs brgyud chos
sder phyags pheb/ chog mang gi tshogs dbur pheb cing sa chog gi gar dang rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg sogs kyang sngar 'khyud bzhin mdzad de/ sa ga dang snron zlar sku gcad rgya'i
ngos nas thugs dam dang / nyin gung rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol gyi drung nas/ skyabs mgon rgyal ba'i dbang po gong zhabs lnga pa chen po'i rnam thar gsang ba rgya
can gyi skor gyi dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang yongs su rdzogs pa/ bu yig skor phal cher gyi lung rnams gsan/ 'di lo bya sa lha khang gi gtsang khang dbus mar zhig gso/ zhal
gser/ tshon rtsi/ gser shog bcas

rgyas pa dang / gtso bo rnam snang la stod g.yogs/ sku pang / sangs rgyas kyi sku brnyan che chung gsum la snam sbyar/ birWa pa'i sku brnyan la sgom thag rgya bzo ma/ nye sras
rnams la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ khro bo gnyis la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ stag sham bcas dang / snyan shal rnam snang la nang mdzod gnyis/ mar me mdzad dang byams
pa gnyis la nang mdzod re/ thub dbang dang birWa pa gnyis la bsod btags re/ nye sras brgyad khro bo gnyis bcas la bsod btags rnying ma gnyis re rnams 'bul sbyor mdzad pa'i
na bza'i rgyur bzang gos sna tshogs kha nyis brgya dang drug cu skor/ gos ling kha nyi shu skor nang sha bcas dang / mchod 'bul dang rab tu gnas pa'ang rgyas par mdzad
do/ /lcang skya mchog sprul rin po cher shar phyogs su pheb tshul gyi bka' shog stsal gshis lha ldan du chibs bskyod/ sku zhabs lcang skya rin po che dang / phyag mdzod
dza sags bla ma gnyis kar pheb rdzong gi 'bul nod dang bcas/ ris su ma chad pa'i grub pa'i mtha' thams cad gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi legs tshogs stsol ba la khyad par
med gshis/ gangs ljongs kyi chos lugs kun rang rang gi gna' bo'i lugs srol las g.yo med 'jam chags su gnas chog pa sogs kyi khur bzhes brtse gzigs dgos pa dang / bod 'bangs
kyi 'gro ba rnams kyang brtse bas mi 'dor ba sogs kyi gangs can bstan 'gro kho na'i don du dgongs pa'i zhu ba rgyas par mdzad pa la rjes su yi rang gis thugs lhag par
dgyes pas/ de ltar bgyis par zhal gyis bzhes/ 'di lo sde dge nas dus 'khor slob

dpon bla ma phrin las dpon g.yog la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo dang / mgon po che chung sogs chos bka' shin tu mang ba dgos tshul gyi zhu shog 'bul nod rgya chen dang bcas pa 'byor
zhing / sku khams ha cang dwangs rgyu med gshis/ nged rang la sne sbyor gyi bka' shog bcas rdzong bdar gnang ba bzhin ston gzhug dang dgun mgor rdo rje 'jigs byed/ dmar
po skor gsum/ rnam sras skor/ chos skyong thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa gzhan gyi skor/ grwa lnga/ gdugs dkar gyi dbang sogs/ mdor na dbang lung rjes gnang rnams
kho rang tsho'i 'dod pa bzhin bgyis nas/ sku drung du brdzongs don bzhin 'byor te/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du dus 'khor bla ma phrin las dpon g.yog la bong kha'i mkhan
chen skal bzang mchog grub/ bod 'brug chos rje/ sde pa spo ra ba yab sras/ rig 'dzin rnams sras rgyal po/ zhabs 'bring pa dge slong ngag dbang 'jam dbyangs sogs/ chos sde'i
grwa pa kha shas bcas la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang slob ma rjes gzung nas bdag po chen po'i bar rgyas par dang / rdo rje shugs dang / sna tshogs yum gnyis kyi rjes
gnang / bsdus rgyud kyi lung / gzhan yang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil/ mchod phreng dang / bstod pa/ smon lam/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /rgyud sde'i
sgo 'byed rnams dang / rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs ku sA li pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang gis mdzad pa/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin
sreg /sgrol

mdos dang / gdugs dkar mdos skor/ byad dgrol gser gyi lde'u mig gi yig sna drug tsam/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i yig cha skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid kyi ljags bsgrigs ma/ brgyud 'debs/
mngon dkyil rnams kyi lung sogs shin tu mang bar stsal/ rgya tshab chen por byad 'grol kha shas dang / gsung bskang ba tshogs yongs bcas la mgon po lha brgyad ma/ zhal
dkar po tshe 'phel/ puu tra gnod sbyin lcam sring lha mang bcas kyi rjes gnang dang / gong zhabs rin po che lnga pa'i ljags bsgrigs kyi gtor bsngo/ bskang bshags/ bstod
bskul/ tshogs 'khor bcas kyi lung rnams dang / bod skyong brtan ma bcu gnyis/ dri za'i rgyal po lha chen 'bar ba rtsal/ btsan rgod ya ba rkya bdun bcas kyi srog gtad rnams
'bul bar mdzad/ gzhan yang rgyal tshab thams cad mkhyen ba sku 'khor nyung shas la 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang / khro bo'i rgyal po rta mchog rol pa yang gsang
gi rtsa dbang / tshe dbang bka' sdod gying lnga/ gza' gdong gi bka' gtad/ yig skor nyer mkho 'ga' zhig gi lung bcas 'bul bar gnang / gur mgon/ zhal/ lha mo/ beg tse sogs
kyi 'cham sku gsar bzheng gnang bar bla rdo srog 'khor gzhugs pa dang / thun mong ba'i ru mtshon bca' ba dang sgrub pa sogs nan tan mdzad/ bod 'brug chos rje/ sde pa spo
ra ba yab/ dbu mdzad rnam sras rgyal po sogs la/ bi ma snying thig dang / zab mo yang tig gi dbang spros bcas/ spros med/ shin tu spros med sogs rdzogs pa dang / bi ma snying
thig gi lung

sogs stsal/ gzhan yang mkhan chen blo bzang dpal 'bar dang / rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol/ sde pa spo ra ba sogs la/ ma gcig gsang spyod snyan brgyud kyi mkha' 'gro sde lnga'i
dbang sogs spyod skor gyi dbang lung mang po/ mang ra mkhan zur la dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi yi ge du ma'i lung gnang zhing / tshur yang chos rje gling pa'i phyag
rdor seng sgrog gi rjes gnang / drang srong gi bka' gtad dang / yig skor gyi lung sogs gsan/ nub khang gsar du rnam thos sras kyi phyi nang gsang ba rab 'bring tha ma'i
rten 'dzugs rnams rgyas par mdzad cing sgrub pa sogs nan tan gnang / zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du/ sde ba zhol khang nas kyis stag rtse rgya rar lha khang gsar bzhengs gnang
ba'i rab gnas la gdan 'dren gnang ba bzhin stag rtser pheb/ gnas rten rnams la dpal kye rdo rje'i sgo nas rab tu gnas pa rgyas par mdzad/ sde pa dpon g.yog rnams la mkha'
spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / rta mgrin gyi rjes gnang sogs chos bka' mang ba dang / yul mi dang bcas par khrom dbang zhig kyang mdzad/ grub pa'i khyu mchog dpal dam pa
sangs rgyas kyi thugs kyi sprul pa dbus smyon kun dga' bzang pos skal ldan 'gro ba 'bum phrag du ma 'khor ba las bsgral ba'i gnas mchog dpal gyi rtsi dmar du gnas gzigs la
pheb/ kha TwAM bkra shis 'od 'bar sogs nang rten rnams dang / sku gsung thugs rten rnams la mchod 'bul snyan shal gzabs rgyas dang / grub thob chen po'i dpon brgyud bla
ma dbon zhang gnyis dang / btsun

ma rnams la mang 'gyed dang / der 'dus ser skya rnams la chos 'brel du thugs rje chen po'i sgom lung sngon 'gro'i chos bshad dang bcas pa shin tu rgyas par stsal bas/ phal
cher gyi mig mchi mas gang zhing dad gus kyi ba spu ldang ba dang / grub thob chen po dngos byon pa lta bu'i dga' spro rgya cher thob par gyur te/ slar yang lha ldan du chibs
bskyod/ grub pa'i dbang po me long rdo rje de nyid slar yang gter ston chen po bde chen gling pa'i dbon brgyud du 'khrungs shing / sgrub pa snying por mdzad pas rtsa
gsum rgyal ba'i tshogs kyis dngos nyams su zhal bstan zhing gsung gi dbugs dbyung ste zab mo'i gter la rang dbang du gyur cing / rgyal dbang padma'i lung gis mngon par gzengs
bstod pa'i gter ston chen po gar dbang las rab rtsal gyi drung nas/ yang rdzong gi gter byon thugs sgrub kyi skor yongs su rdzogs pa/ dag snang bla sgrub kyi sko tshe
sgrub kyi skor/ rig 'dzin chen po thugs mchog rdo rje rtsal gyi gter byon gtum po nA ga rakSha'i skor/ gzhan yang padma khrag 'thung gi skor sogs mang du gsan/ pha bong
kha mkhan po sogs la/ mkha' spyod ma'i skor yongs rdzogs/ chos nyid dngos bstan gyi byin rlabs khrid lung dang bcas pa/ indra dang mai tri gnyis kyi dbang lung / dur bdag
gi rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa/ thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs kyi zhi drag gi dbang / khrid lung yongs su rdzogs pa sogs zab chos rgya cher stsal/ de ltar phyogs de'i
gdul bya rnams re zhig de tsam du dgongs nas snye thang du chibs bskyod/ bod 'brug chos rje

sogs bsnyen rdzogs rab byung mang du mdzad/ chos rje la mtshan mkhyen rab ngag dbang blo gsal phun tshogs su 'dogs par mdzad/ der yang mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / lam
'bras thob pa rnams la lam dbang sogs chos bka' mang ba dang / btsun chung chung ngu rnams la'ang rab byung dang / lus bsgyur ma tshar ba rnams la'ang skyabs sdom tshun
thugs khur chen pos mdzad pa sogs lugs gnyis kyi dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pas ci dgar tshim par mdzad/ zla ba lnga pa'i mgon po sgrub mchod du bzhugs par zhus kyang zhal
gyis ma bzhes par nyer gsum la 'phags sde nas chibs bskyod/ rim bzhin bsam gtan chos gling dang she'u grong rnams su chibs bsgyur/ she'u grong du'ang dge 'dun rnams la
tshe dbang sogs stsal te zhag kha yar bzhugs dgos tshul gyi gsol 'debs nan tan zhus rung zhal gyis ma bzhes bar bzhugs zhag gsum mdzad nas rmor dgon du pheb ste phyogs nas
ched gtad 'byor pa 'ga' zhig la gsung chos ci rigs stsal/ de'ang snga lo rnams nas lha ldan du bzhugs ring gi bsngo rten gyi gos zan sogs phal che ba 'phags sde/ she'u
grong rmor dgon ma lag bcas la so sor nyin bzhi lnga la nyung mtha' byas pa'i zhabs brtan du ched dmigs kyi sgrol ma 'don pa'i yon du 'gro bar gnang gin yod pa ltar/ 'di
lo'ang dgon so sor nyin bzhi lnga tsam re'i sgrol 'don gyi mang ja bzhes thug dang / gsol ba yon sogs gzabs rgyas dang / rmor dgon du'ang sgrub mchod 'dzugs pa dang rmor
chen rdo rje 'chang gi sku mchod thog

mang 'gyed/ 'dra sku rin po che sogs la gser chab/ snyan shal/ dkar me rgyun 'dzugs sogs kyang sngar rgyun bzhin mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ spyi bye'i bstan 'gro'i don
slad dbus ljongs khag /yang yang gshegs shing zab don gsan spel dang / /bsdu dngos phyin drug gang 'dul der ston mdzad/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon ngo mtshar rab 'byams yin/
/zhes so// ! gnyis pa mchog gi mdzad pa byed brag tu bshad pa la/ rang don thos bsam bsgoms pas thugs rgyud ji ltar sbyangs tshul dang / gzhan don 'chad rtsod rtsom pas
thub bstan ji ltar spel ba'i tshul gnyis/ dang po la zab mo'i nyams bzhes ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul dang / de la brten nas grub pa'i mtshan ma ji ltar brnyes pa'i tshul gnyis
las/ dang po ni/ mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen zhabs kyis/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ /bsgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /zhes dang / mgon po byams pas/ gal te thos pa
tsam gyis don mthong 'gyur na sgom pa don med 'gyur/ /gal te ma thos par yang bsgom 'jug 'gyur na bstan pa don med 'gyur/ /zhes dang / 'jam mgon bla ma sa skya paNDi ta chen
pos/ mkhas pa rnams kyis legs bshad rnams/ /shin tu legs par go bzhin du/ /de don nyams su mi len na/ /bstan bcos shes kyang ci zhig bya/ /zhes bstan pa rin po che'i
sgor zhugs pa dag gis thos bsam sgom gsum zung 'brel gyi tshul du thos don nyams su bstar dgos par gsung zhing / de'i tshul yang sems dpa' chen pos/ nyams su len pa'i chos

la/ /glo snying brang gsum gtod cig /'di phyi bar do gsum du/ /'di yis bslu ba med pas/ /ma nor lam la 'bungs shig /ces gsungs pa'i don rnams bdag cag gi skyabs mgon mtshungs
pa med pa nyid kyis thugs kyi klong du sim par mdzad nas/ thos pa de dag thams cad kyang / /ming rkyang tsam du ma bzhag go /zhes pa ltar/ mkhas grub kyi bla ma 'ba' zhig
bsten nas thos pa mdzad pa yin te/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ yul dbus gtsang khams gsum chu bzhin nyul/ /chos dbang lung gdams pa'i bang mdzod 'dzin/ /nga phyogs 'dzin
a 'thas mi che bas/ /bod gangs can sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin pa/ /mtshan mi 'dra sa rnying kar 'brug dang / /dge ldan zhes 'khrul med bstan 'dzin kun/ /dad mos pas mjal zhing
zab chos zhus/ /nga chos dad che yang rtog dpyod can/ /chos 'khrul zad khungs thub 'bad pas nyan/ /nor snyan grags kyi rjes su nga mi 'brang / /zhes 'byung ba ltar mkhas
grub du ma zhig bsten par mdzad pa yin te/ gang gi rnam thar gsol 'debs tshigs bcad ma las/ mtshungs med mkhas grub bla ma bcu phrag gsum/ /lnga phrag dag gi zhabs pad
nyer bsten nas/ /smin grol bshad sgrub gdams pa'i bdud rtsi'i bcud/ /ngoms med gsol ba chos kyi rgya mtshor 'dud/ /ces gsung pa ltar rnam thar tshigs bcad ma 'di ljags rtsom
gyi tshe'ang mkhas grub dam pa 'di tsam zhig bsten par mdzad zin la/ phyis nas de bas kyang ches mang ba zhig bsten par mdzad pa rnams rtogs sla ba'i phyir 'dir phyogs

gcig tu brjod na/ dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi spyi gzugs snyigs ma'i dus 'dir rje btsun sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag ris med grub mtha'i
chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun mi 'chad par bskor ba'i ston pa bla na med pa rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ /gang
gi thugs sras 'phags sde mkhan chen ngag dbang blo gsal bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho/ bsam yas bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ grub dbang bla ma kun dga' tshul khrims/
khams ston grub pa'i dbang phyug sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ 'khor lo sdom pa chos 'khor gnas kyi slob dpon kun dga' bsam gtan/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed la grub pa'i mtshan
ma brnyes pa bkra shis chos sde'i slob dpon bsod nams snang byed/ grub dbang 'gyur med padma rgyal mtshan/ nges don zab mo'i dpal 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol/ rtogs pa'i
mnga' bdag puu hrang bla ma legs pa don grub/ rta mgrin grub brnyes gtor sgrub slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa/ gsar rnying gdams pa'i mdzod 'dzin mang ra ba mkhan po blo
bzang dge 'dun/ mkhas btsun dam pa gangs can mkhan po ngag dbang rab brtan/ mkhyen yangs 'phags sde ba bstan pa rgyal mtshan/ dgon gsar slob dpon mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin
bzang po/ /'tsho byed ngag dbang don grub ste rmor chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras bcu drug /gzhan yang rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid ni yang srid rin po che sngon ma du ma dang
/ da lta'i sku thog bcas la rtsa ba'i grub mtha' rje btsun sa skya pa'i lugs

'di gtso bor thugs nyams su bstar bas na/ de dang rjes 'brel gyi dbang du btang ste/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ /rje btsun mkha' spyod dbang mo kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma/ grub dbang sgro lung pa chen po mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel/ bla mchan dkon mchog rgyal
po/ /gong dkar chos rje blo gros dbang phyug /ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gdan sa pa chen po mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang
