nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong / chos rje bkra shis bzang po/ /bla ma nam mkha' dpal bzang / bla ma kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ chos rje bstan 'dzin phun
tshogs/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bur gtogs tsam za nyal 'chag gi rnal 'byor pa zog rdzun mkhan kun dga' blo gros/ lhag bsam can mthu stobs dbang phyug /che zhe bsod nams bstan
pa'i nyi ma/ mchog gsum phrin las dbang mo/ /rab byung mkhan po bzod pa 'od zer/ dpon yig pa kun dga' sangs rgyas/ zhe dgon mkhan chen bsod nams dpal bzang / /gzims phug
sprul pa'i sku blo bzang bstan 'dzin mgon po/ /gzims khang 'og sprul pa'i sku sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin/ /bod 'brug chos rje mkhyen rab blo gsal phun tshogs te/ 'khon rigs
'dzin pa 'gran bral gnyis dang / tha shal bzhi/ rjes 'brang mkhas grub bcu drug /srid gsum lha ma'i gtsug rgyan rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang blo bzang skal bzang rgya mtsho/
khri chen no mon han ngag dbang mchog ldan/ rgyal sras

mchog gi sprul sku blo bzang 'jigs med ye shes grags pa/ zhi ba lha sprul pa'i sku 'phags ba dge legs rgyal mtshan/ 'bras spungs bka' 'gyur ba rin chen dam chos/ bka' 'gyur
ba thabs mkhas rgya mtsho ste mnyam med ri bo dge ldan pa'i bstan 'dzin dam pa drug /rig 'dzin grub pa'i khyu mchog kun bzang klong grol/ thugs sras mchog sprul mchog grub
dpal 'bar/ kaHthog rig 'dzin chen mo tshe dbang nor bu/ sa smad dpal yul bla ma padma nor bu/ zur mchog sprul phrin las blo ldan rgya mtsho/ glan ston theg mchog 'od gsal
rang grol/ gter chen bla ma gar dbang las rab rtsal/ gter chen kun bzang bde chen rgyal po/ /rig 'dzin tshe dbang bkra shis/ snub ston blo bzang don grub/ sngags 'chang
rin chen bkra shis/ rdo rje 'dzin pa blo bzang bsod nams/ grub dbang padma bde chen/ grub mchog rnam sras rgyal po ste gsang chen rnying ma gtso bor gsan pa'i mkhas grub
bcu bzhi/ mtshur phu'i bla chen tre bo gong ma/ si tu chos rje karma chos kyi 'byung gnas/ 'brug pa thams cad mkhyen pa bka' brgyud phrin las shing rta/ ri bo che'i mkhan
chen blo bzang stobs ldan dpal 'byor/ grub rigs ngag dbang yongs grags/ lcags zam pa blo bzang dpal grub/ glang 'khor gdan sa pa 'chi med gzhon nu blo gros/ grub dbang
ngag dbang padma/ dge slong 'gyur med chos 'phel/ zhwa lu bla chen thugs rje brtson 'grus/ zhwa lu ba rin chen 'jam dpal chos mchog /zangs bstan spo ra dbu chen chos grags
bzang po/ /grub mchog blo bzang gar dbang / 'tsho byed chen po bzhi ste ris med

grub mtha' sna tshogs skor gsan pa'i bla ma bcu bzhi bcas sdom bdun cu don gnyis/ gzhan yang cho ga phyag len dogs gcod mdzad pa/ rig gnas skor gsan ba dang dogs gcod mdzad
pa sogs/ mdor na mkhas grub kyi yongs 'dzin bsten pa'i rnam thar kyang tshong dpon gyi bu khye'u nor bzang dang / mkhas grub khyung po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa sogs kyi rtogs
brjod las 'byung ba kho na ltar ro/ /de dag gi zhal gyi bum bzang las gdams pa'i bcud ngoms par gsol ba/ yang gong gi de nyid las/ so thar byang sems rig 'dzin gsang
sngags kyi/ /smin grol zab dang rgya che'i chu 'dzin dbang / /gcig 'dus sgra brgya sgrogs pa las thon pa'i/ /mthu stobs drag po'i rtsal 'chang khyed la 'dud/ /ces gsungs
pa ltar/ de dag nyams bzhes kyi phreng ba bstar bar mdzad pa'i tshul yang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i nyams len thams cad bsdu na sdom pa gsum gyi nyams len du 'du zhing
/ de'ang bla ma mtshan nyid dang ldan pa rnams nas/ theg pa chen po lugs gnyis kyi cho ga dang / gsang chen bla na med pa gtso bor gyur pa'i rgyud sde chen po bzhi dang
'brel ba'i cho ga rnam par dag pa las nod par mdzad pa las/ so so'i rtsa ba dang yan lag gi bslab bya phra zhing phra ba tshun chad tshul bzhin du bsrung sdom mdzad pa la
gus sbyor shin tu che ba'i stobs kyis yul dus gnas skabs thams cad du bstan pa'i mig rgyan la phan pa'i kun spyod kho na mdzad pa'i sgo nas bskyed rdzogs zung 'jug gi ting
nge 'dzin las nam yang g.yo ba med bzhin du/ rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs las zab pa dang rgya che ba'i dam pa'i

chos ji snyed cig yod pa thams cad lus pa med pa lta bur gsan pa de dag thos blo tsam ma yin par/ bsam byung gi rig pas tshul bzhin du dpyod de dka' ba'i gnas phra mo tshun
chod la sgro 'dogs chod par mdzad pas 'chad sgo gang mdzad kyang thogs med kyi spobs pa mchog tu gyur cing / rdo rje theg pa gtso bor gyur pa'i lam dri ma med pa rnams rgyun
gyi nyams bzhes khrigs chags su mdzad pa dang / chos mthun gyi mdzad spyod gzhan yang ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul 'dir mtshon pa tsam zhig brjod na/ thog mar tho rangs
nyams bzhes kyi gtso bo lhag pa'i lha gang yin de'i ldang ba'i rnal 'byor gyis bzhengs nas/ tshe sgrub zab mo'i rim pa dang / gsung gtor/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i thugs dam
chag med bzhi/ gur zhal dmar po skor gsum sogs gsang sngags gsar rnying dang 'brel ba'i zhi khro rab 'byams kyi dkyil 'khor du ma zhig gi nyams bzhes dang / lha bsang /
gtor bsngo/ bskang ba sogs bstan 'gro'i ched lugs zung dang 'brel ba'i mdzad phrin thugs g.yeng chung skabs nyin mtshan 'khyongs pa lta bur mdzad kyang rkang grangs ji lta
ba bzhin dngos su gsungs pa dang / zin thor thebs pa mi snang / dper mtshon na kho bos phyag rdor utsArYa sogs kyi sngags la zhu dag zhus par/ 'di sogs las sgrub kyi sngags
du ma zhig rgyun par bzlas brjod byed pa yin gsung ba la dpag na bsgom bzlas kyi rim pa du ma thugs nyams su bzhes tshod du 'dug cing / de dag kyang ming rkyang tsam
ma yin par thugs dam gzhi'i bsnyen pa dang / rgyun bsnyen sogs/ mdor na bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi rigs phal cher sla

chos su ma song bar sngon 'gro rnams thugs rgyud la skye nges dang / bskyed rim la gsal snang thob cing / rdzogs rim bde stong zung 'jug gi lta ba'i yang rtser pheb pa zhig
ste/ gsung las/ nga chung ngu'i skabs bskyed rim la rtsal sbyong ba'i tshe mi 'ga' re dang 'phros gtam lab kyang / de'i mig gi rgya mo'i nang du kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
rten dang brten par bcas pa gsal e thebs lta zhing sgom pa yin gsungs pa la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam thar yod par sems shing / /gnyis pa ni gong gi de nyid
las/ dag pa'i rmi lam nyams kyi snang ba la/ /bla ma yid dam chos srung nor lha yi/ /gsang gsum rnam 'phrul ngo mtshar ji snyed pas/ /byin rlabs mtshan ma brnyes pa khyod
la 'dud/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ zhal gzigs lung bstan gyi rigs dang grub pa'i rtags mtshan la sogs pa dpag tu med pa zhig byung bar gor ma chag kyang sba ba kho nar mdzad
gshis gsal bar mi gsung la/ gal te gsungs kyang mnal lam gyi zol dang / dngos su byung ba ltar gsungs pa zur tsam las mi gsung ba bsnyel tho 'dra'ang mi snang bas/ rgyas
par 'bri rngo ma thogs shing / rang gzhan gyis mthong thos cung zad byung ba rnams bkod na/ dgung grangs gsum tsam bzhes pa'i dus rnal 'byor pa sngags dkar lcang lo'i tshul
can shin tu bag dro ba zhig gis gzims khang du byon nas byin rlabs mdzad pa dran te/ rjes su yum sogs kyis ma nges par 'dug gsungs pa dag snang zhig yin nam snyam/ sku
na phra mo'i skabs ljags kyi steng du a yig gsal por yod pa sogs gong gi gseb tshags sna

tshogs su ci rigs bkod pa rnams dang / gzhan yang dgung lo dgu tsam gyi tshe sku rtsed kyi tshul du zan ril chung ngu bdun la phyag mtheb kyi rjes su a yig gsal bar byung ba
phyis su'ang 'ga' zhig gi dad rten du yod par grags/ chos sde'i bla brang rtser sgrol dkar gyi ljags bsnyen gnang ba'i tshe grub thob chen po byon nas/ rgyal ba tshe dpag
med dang rnam par rgyal/ zhes sogs kyi zhabs brtan tshigs bcad gsungs pa dang / skabs shig mnal ltas su grub thob chen po gzi brjid dang ldan pa zhig gi sku mdun du rin
po che'i snod bzang po'i nang du snying rlon pa dkyil gshags pa zhig gzigs byung gsungs pa gzhan stong lta ba'i gnas lugs ston pa'i brdar sems shing / gzhan stong la thugs
gtsigs kyang shin tu che/ lha sa'i dga' mo 'phrang du grub thob chen po byon nas lcags zam gsar rnying gso 'dzugs mang du mdzad pa'i las dpon sde pa spo ra ba byung ba'i
mnal ltas shar ba bzhin sngar nas gsung sgros yod pa ltar/ dus phyis lcags zam pa grub dbang blo bzang dpal grub kyis dbus gtsang du lcags zam du ma spel zhing / lhag
par dga' mo 'phrang du lcags 'dzugs kyi mgo ba spo ra bar babs pas/ sde pa de rje bla ma gnyis kar mi phyed pa'i thugs dad dang / khyad par lcags zam pa der skye bo phal
gyis skur 'debs byed kyang sde pa spo ra ba brgyud bcas ni grub thob chen po dngos kyi dad 'dun mdzad/ yang skabs shig mnal lam du mkha' spyod ma'i bris thang zhig gi steng
gi cha la bla ma brgyud pa dang bcas pa bzhugs shing rje btsun ma'i sku las 'od zer du ma 'phros pa'i rtse la 'phags yul grub chen brgyad cu 'od kor gyi rnam par ltar
bzhugs

pa so so'i drung na rnal 'byor ma rgyan cha lugs sku mdog phyag mtshan mi 'dra ba re re bzhugs pa'i rdo rje dril bu par nan tan gyis gzigs pas zhabs pus g.yas kyi thad tsam
na da lta bris skur 'ong ba'i rnam pa ji lta ba mkha' spyod ma dmar mos 'khyud pa zhig dang / de'i nye skor der mkha' spyod du gshegs pa'i bkod pa 'dug pas thugs rje chen
po'i sku zhig kyang yod dgongs nas gzigs pas de'ang gsal bar byung gsung / 'og yul ljongs kyi rnam pa dang / bla ma brgyud pa rnams bzhugs pa'i bar snang shin tu khad 'gyangs
pa sngo seng nge ba zhig 'dug par da rang lam 'di la brten nas mkha' spyod du gshegs pa zhig mi 'ong ba 'dra dgongs thugs khral mdzad bzhin pa'i ngang de khar yul
ljongs kyi re rtse zhig nas sprin skya thol gyis byung ba bla ma rnams bzhugs pa'i sprin dang 'dres song ba zhig byung bas da dung rang re'i rjes 'jug lam 'di la brten nas
mkha' spyod du gshegs pa'ang 'ga' re 'ong ba 'dra gsungs/ gzhan yang rgyal yum rdo rje btsun mo'i gzigs snang ni dngos nyams du mar yang yang 'ong bar nges te/ bka' las/
gsung chos sogs kyis thugs g.yeng gi stabs mkha' spyod ma'i ljags bzlas cung zad g.yel bar gyur na de ma khad rnam 'gyur du mas bskul ba zhig 'ong gin 'dug pas 'di'i bzlas
sgom cung zad kyang g.yel mi thub pa 'dug gsung / yar 'brog sgang du rdo rje btsun mo dngos su byon pa sku 'khor zhig sku mdun du 'ong ba'i rkyen gyis yal bar gyur pa'i
lo rgyus kyang gnang / dpal 'khor lo bde mchog kyang dzo ki sogs rnam 'gyur du mar sprul nas mnal lam

dang thugs nyams su gzigs gsungs/ lung bstan yang mang po zhig yod tshod gda' ste gsal bar ma shes/ chos sder bzhugs skabs shig nam mkha'i khams kun me tog padma'i sdong po
mang pos khengs shing / de re re'i steng na sman bla sogs sangs rgyas sprul sku'i rnam pa can du ma zhal gzigs gsungs/ 'khrungs rabs kyi phreng ba rnams kyang mnal lam du
byung ba'i zol mdzad pa sogs ni khengs bskyungs kho na yin par sems te/ gtan tshigs du ma mthong ba'i phyir/ kha'ur pheb res kyi dpal mgon bram gzugs dkar po zhig gar dgu'i
nyams dang bcas te gzigs gsungs/ rje 'di nyid spyir gsung chos zhu ba byung na thugs dgyes bzhin du lhug par gnang mod/ gsang chen kha'u brag rdzong pa'i man ngag spyi
dang / bye brag gnyan mgon gyi skor la dam dog shin tu che bar mdzad de/ 'di'i rjes gnang zhu ba phal cher la dkar po tshe 'phel kho na mdzad la/ de nas kyang nan tan
chen pos btud na bsnyen dus sogs rim gyis gdams ngag gi sarga ma log par gsungs pas zhag bdun tsam la chos skor yongs rdzogs 'dod pa'i ham can rnams la 'bul ba sogs ji tsam
yod kyang thugs brel lta bur bsnyad 'dogs kyis mi gsung bas/ 'di'i chos skor yongs rdzogs thob pa kho bo cag sogs gnyis gsum tsam las med par sems/ seng ge sgra'i ngag
srung 'grol gyi sgom zlas la nan tan mdzad pas ljags kyi mtha' yongs rdzogs la ljags gsar pa khab sbom tsam zhig mthud ma'i tshul du 'phel ba dang / chos sder rdo rje 'jigs
byed kyi sgrub mchod cho ga grwar pheb pa'i nub/ mnal lam du gtsug lag khang zhig na mkhan

chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya can sku yom yom bzhugs shing / de'i dbu na 'jigs byed rigs lnga'i sku thog tshad tsam bzhugs pa zhig gsal ba dang
/ yang skabs shig thugs snang dang mnal ltas ci ltar yang / gcen thang lha ri rol po'i 'dabs su kye rdo rje'i chos skor zab gter du bzhugs pa zhig mkhyen pa dang / yang
skabs shig mnal ltas su chu brag 'thabs pa'i gnas shig nas ngang pas bse sgom tsa ka li'i ba gam lta bu phul ba zhig byung gsungs pa dang / kho bo la gsung chos thog mar
gnang rgyu'i nub mo/ nged rang gi yab rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis rje nyid la sbyong khrus rgyas par stsal ba mnal ltas su shar ba dang / dus rgyun du chos srung rnams la
bka' bsgo phrin bcol sogs bla ma gong ma'i gsung ngar po de dag gsungs pa'i tshe/ rje nyid yi dam du gsal ba'i dbu gtsug gi rigs bdag des gsungs pa'i thugs mos gnang ba
bzhin/ skabs shig chos sder pu tra'i bskang ba las bzhi lhun grub kyi gnad bskul de la gong gi spyan dmigs de mdzad pas tshogs gsham na mon pa'i gzugs byang 'brog gi zhwa
mo gyon pa zhig 'chams stabs byed pa gzigs pa dang / sa skyar bzhugs skabs mnal ltas su/ lha khang mthil na ngos 'khor bcas phur pa'i 'chams sbyong byed cing 'dug pa la/
khrom rnams kyis sngags 'chang chen po pheb byung zer zhing 'ur shog byed mur sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' rin chen sku 'khor rags bsdus dang bcas pa zhig pheb
ste/ kho bo'i khri'u shing de la 'khyil mdzad nas baiDUrYa'i zhal dkar zhig tu gsol zho gsol ba dang sku bgres nyams kyi dbu skra dang zhal rgyan skya

bun ne bzhugs 'dug pa la rje nyid kyis phyag dang phyag dbang zhu bar mdzad nas thugs la 'dar gdong 'khrugs pa'i skabs de snyan gsan phab na tshar chen rin po che la bslab
don ci gnang dgongs mur mnal ltas gzhan zhig la 'byams song gsung ba dang / gzhon nu'i skabs rmor chen rje la rjes gnang zhig gsan tshe dur khrod bdag po sku mdog ljang gu
yab kyi phyag mtshan mda' gzhu rgyab nas 'gengs pa zhig byung gsung pa dang / yang skabs shig mnal ltas su rnga yab gling phran dpal ri padma 'od du pheb pa na/ lcags ri
chen po zhig gi nang na srin po thams cad bcug pa'i sgo de bye la khad 'dug pa dang / sgo drung na grub dbang thang stong rgyal po grod pa chus bkang ba zhig dbur bzhag
nas bzhugs pa la sgo nang nas srin po mdog ser po mche ba gtsigs pa zhig rje nyid kyi sku mdun du rgyang mchongs pa na grub dbang des dbu thog gi grod pa 'phang song bas
srin po sngar shul du log pa zhig byung gsungs pa dang / dbu bla kha reg chos rje blo bzang don grub gshegs nas ma 'gyangs par tho rengs shig mnal dang 'od gsal 'dres mur
bla ma de nyid sku mdun gyi nam mkhar lus gnad kyis bzhugs te/ spyan bar snang la nag hrig ger gzigs pa zhig shar bas/ lta ba la gzhan las bogs thon pa zhig byung gsung
ba dang / yang brag rdzong ma'i khrid gsan skabs shig sngon 'gro rdor sems sgom bzlas la nan tan mdzad pas sku smad kyi cha la bsnyun zug dum tsam byung mur sku'i gsang
ba nas srog chags gdug pa can zhig gzugs dmar po che chung mi gzugs tshad ldan gyi mthe'u chung ma'i mgo tsam zhig thon

pa dang bsnyun las grol zhes gsungs pas/ lam de skabs kyi dngos rtags shin tu gsal ba dang / sa skyar sngon pheb skabs zhal gyi gsang khrid gnang dus spyan ltas su dril lce
zhig gi ldebs la sprin bun long gi dbus na kye rdor gyi sku chung ngu zhig dang / de'i 'og na zhal bram gzugs yod pa zhig shar gsungs pa dang / kho bos mgon po drug cu pa'i
zor 'dzin thog mar bgyis skabs man ngag nas 'byung ba bzhin gri gug gsar bzo bgyis te yar klung du phyag nas la bskur ba'i phyir pheb tu/ rtags ngo mtshar can byung gsungs
pa bzhin rjes su dngos mjal skabs ci byung lags zhus pas/ de nub rmi ltas su sgyogs rdo'i 'khrul 'khor nam mkha'i mthong la reg pa zhig bcas par shar gsungs pa dang
/ rjes su zhal gyi rjes gnang yongs rdzogs stsal skabs kyang gzigs snang ngo mtshar can re gnyis byung song yang / re zhig chos skyong bka' gnyan pas 'dri bar ma nus shing
/ yang grong chen mkhan po ngag dbang shes rab nas gsung ngag slob bshad ma thob tshul zhus par nged kyi lam 'bras tshar bdun song / da rang byed thub par dka' gsungs
pa'ang de kho nar song ba dang / khong la sdeb sbyor gyi phyag khrid gnang ba'i tshe pra stAr 'god tshul de la thugs cung zad the tshom gyis 'god mi mkhyen pa ltar byung
ba'i song zhog mjal skabs/ bka' las/ da nangs gung seng skabs prastA ra 'god ma shes pa blo ma bde bas gung seng rnams bdud rtsir dmigs pas yi dwags sogs la bsngo bzhin pa'i
tshe prastA ra prastA ra zhes pa zhig byung nas lhang lhang 'dug par prastA ra 'god tshul rnams rnam pa

gsal por shar byung zhes 'god tshul thogs med du stsal zhing ljang rtsom sha lo ka gcig kyang mdzad pa'i kha yig zhal byang du/ rgyun ldan mkhas pa'i dmigs bu dang / bral ba'i
lo rgan gzu lum pa/ /srang 'khyams spar tshod stes dbang gis/ /rnyed 'di gter mdzod lde'u mig 'dra/ /zhes stsal zhing / yang skabs shig bde mchog gi bzlas sgom bgyid
dgos pa'i bskul ma 'di yang yang 'byung ba zhig brda ste/ kha sang nas kyang khams phrug cig gis rgya mthongs kha 'dir bde mchog gi rtsa sngags dag gsal 'don pa zhig byung
gsung / yang mdang nub rmi ltas su rnal 'byor ma'i thang sku phyag g.yon gyi mthil na 'od kyi gru gu zhig snang ba las 'od zer 'phros pa'i sne la brgyud pa'i bla ma re
re bzhugs pa rnams la'ang rnal 'byor ma re res 'khyud par snang bas rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang gi skuu la ched kyis bltas dus rnal 'byor ma skra zings pa mdze mo'i rnam pa lta
bu zhig gis 'khyud 'dug gsung / yang skabs shig ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi sku thang ri mo shin tu legs pa zhig bkram 'dug par zhal khebs kyis bkab byung bar rtse gdong
sprul pa'i sku 'dra ba zhig gis zhal khebs nam mkhar 'phang song ba de 'dra lan gnyis gsum byas pa zhig byung gsung / yang yar rgyas bla ma bsam gtan phun tshogs la da
rang nged kyi rmi lam du/ sngon gyi chos rgyal rnams kyi cha byad can gyi mi zhig gis gtam sna tshogs zer ba 'dra zhig byung bas/ khyed rang mkha' spyod ma sngar lugs bzhin
gyi steng du spyan ras gzigs la yi dam du byas na legs pa 'dra gsungs/ yang 'dar grong chen du mus chen dang mkhan chen zhal dkar ba gnyis la rwa khrid gnang

skabs/ gsung las/ khyed gnyis kyi bka' drin gyis mdang dgong nged kyi rmi lam du rdo rje 'jigs byed dkar po zhal phyag yongs su rdzogs pa shin tu gsal ba zhig byung gsung yang
/ grong chen du spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa'i rjes gnang gnang skabs 'dir zhal gzigs kyi brgyud pa bar ma chad pa yin/ nged kyis kyang zhal mthong gsungs par/
lan zhu ba med pas yud tsam nas lha sa bsam yas sogs kyi thugs rje chen po'i sku rnams mjal ba yin pas zhal mthong ba de kha yin mod/ gsungs pa'ang dgongs pa can gyi gsung
du sems/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong dbus phyogs gnas gzigs la pheb skabs/ bka' las/ da lam ni mjal ma thub/ da'ang yar klung du pheb pa dang mjal ba mi 'ong gsungs
pa'ang de kha bzhin byung / yang nA lendra'i 'bul sdud bla ma dge 'phel zhes par khyod nged kyi 'bul sdud du 'gro dgos/ de'ang 'brug lo tshun la ma 'khor na don med gsungs/
bdag gis 'gro thub pa'ang mi 'ong ste/ 'bul sdud kyis ci mdzad zhus pas/ 'jam dpal 'di la zla bo yang dag med pa bcas dngul gdung gi rgyu byed snyam pa yin gsungs pa
sogs kyang ma 'ongs pa mngon sum du gzigs pa'i gsung dang 'di ni sngon rje bod mkhar ba zhing brje kha ma'i skabs/ gsung las/ nged rang gi lo'ang rgan rabs song / ci 'dra
'ong yang 'things dka'/ dang po spyan snga rin po ches 'bul sdud rdzong ba gnang bas/ rjes su dgongs rdzogs kyi rten bzhengs la shin tu phan pa zhig byung / nged rang la
yin min byung tshe rten bzhengs bzhin ma byas na'ang da lta

sbyin bdag yag po yod pa nas cung zad ngo tsha/ nga rang la rten bzhengs byung ma byung la khyad med de/ khyod rnams la byed dka' 'ong ba 'dra/ de'i tshe na zhabs drung thams
cad mkhyen pa bzhugs thog la btang na legs pa 'ong gsungs shing / 'bul sdud thon khar bka' bkod du khyi lo'i nang du slebs par gyis/ tha ma'ang phag lo'i nang du ma slebs
na stabs med pas/ de dus ma slebs na rgyu'ang dgos dus phan thogs pa zhig mi 'ong ba dang / khyod rang yang mtha' khob tu rgyun ring na sdug pa las med gsungs pa dang
gcig par mngon/ yang mkhan chen zhal dkar bas 'dar bsam 'grub tu mjal bar byon skabs/ bka' las/ khyed tshar lugs 'di la bag chags shin tu bzang ba zhig snang / mdang nged
kyi rmi lam du thang yangs po zhig la rgyal ba rdo ring pa'i sku 'bri ba zhig byung ba/ de ring rang re 'phrad pa la brtag par 'dug gsungs pa bzhin ma 'gyangs par tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gdan sa zung gi mkhan por gyur te/ kha'u brag rdzong pa'i ring lugs 'di la phan zhing phan par 'gyur ba'i mtshan ma shin tu gsal ba sogs grub pa
chen po'i sa la bzhugs pa'i ltas dang gsung sgros mang bar mchis kyang 'dir zin pa de tsam mo/ /ched du gtad pa'i mngon spyod kyi rigs cher mi mdzad kyang rdo rje'i chos
skyong rnams bskul ba la ma ltog par phrin las sgrub par mdzad de chos sde'i bstan dgra kha re dang / gzhan 'byor phun tshogs la mi bzod pa'i skye bo ser skya 'ga' zhig
la rtags mtshan byung ba'i lo rgyus mang yang zhib par 'chad pa skabs su ma 'brel/ gzhan yang gtsang dbus khams gsum du skye 'gro

rgyal gdon gyis nyen pa du ma'i don yang bsam gyis mi khyab par mdzad mod/ zhi ba byang chub kyi thugs kho na'i sgo nas gtor ma sbyin zhing bka' bsgo sbyong ba sogs mdzad pas/
de dag zhi zhing slar mi 'byung ba yin la/ drag spyod sogs ye mi mdzad/ char dbab gcad sogs thun mong gi las tshogs rnams kyang thogs med du 'grub cing / sku na gzhon
nu'i dus rdzas sngags kyi sbyor ba sogs mdzad pa'i tshe char ji ltar dkon yang char 'bebs rdzas skyel bar char rdung ma byung ba mi srid pa lta bu dang / dus phyis kyang
char dkon pa'i tshe sbyong khrus dang cha gsum gtor ma re mdzad pa'i nyin gsum tsam na char shin tu che ba 'babs pa mngon sum du mthong bas dam pa 'di nyid gang du bzhugs
pa'i phyogs su char chu phun sum tshogs par 'byung ba yin la/ /! yang zhabs gras em chi shes rab rgya mtsho sogs kha shas la sman gyi lha mo'i rjes gnang gnang skabs gla
rtsi lta bu'i dri bsung kun gyis tshor ba byung ba ni/ sman dpyad kyi sgo nas 'gro don rgya cher mdzad pas sku dang grib ma ltar 'grogs pa'i ltas sam snyam pa dang / lhag
par thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed kyi sgo nas gtsang dbus kun tu sman pas bor ba'i nyam thag du mar gsal byed kyi dga' ston stsal bas sman pa rnams kyang ya mtshan gyi
dpal la bkod/ phyi ltar byang chub kyi thugs 'byongs pa dang / nang ltar gdams pa'i zab gnad gzhan dang mi 'dra bas dregs ldan du mas zhabs la 'dud pa/ legs skyes 'bul ba/
bka' bzhin sgrub par dam bca' ba sogs dang / yul phyogs gang du bzhugs kyang gzhi bdag gis

mthun rkyen sgrub pa sogs ngo mtshar zhing rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar pa du ma snang ngo / /de dag gi don bsdu na/ thos bsam sgom gsum mthar phyin bstan pa'i bdag /byams
dang thugs rje'i gter chen sems dpa' che/ /nyams dang rtogs pa'i rtser son grub pa'i dbang / /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bstan pa'i mdzad pa yin/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa gzhan don
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas thub bstan ji ltar spel ba'i tshul ni/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gsol 'debs las/ 'chad blo gsal mkhas kun yid rab
'phrog /gsung dgongs 'grel 'bel mchid dga' ba skyed/ /rtsom legs pa'i dgos don 'byung ba'i gnas/ /rje gnas gsar chos rje/ /zhes pa ltar/ bdag cag rnams kyi mtshungs pa
med pa'i skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid kyis bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum la brtson pa rab kyi pha mthar son te/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang mkhyen rtse nus pa'i yon
tan phun sum tshogs pa la rang dbang 'byor pas mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che ches cher rgyas par mdzad pa ste/ de'ang
'chad pa nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis blo gsal blo gros kyi pad tshal rgyas par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis yongs 'dzin du ma'i zhal bum las 'ongs pa'i chos
tshul zab mo'i bdud rtsi rnams brtson pa gnyis kyi snyim pas yang yang gsol zhing blo gros ro 'dzin gyis dges par myangs pas lung rtogs yon tan gyi bcud kyis rdo rje gsum
gyi sku brtas par gyur te/ mdo sngags gnyis kyis bsdus pa'i lam srol

yongs su rdzogs pa du ma zhig brgyud pa'i phreng ba zam ma chad pa las 'ongs pa/ 'khrul pa'i dri ma bral ba rje btsun sa skya pa'i gong ma lnga sogs mkhas grub kyi skyes bu
du mas thugs nyams su bstar zhing / 'chad nyan gyi gtan la phab pa'i rgyun dri ma med pa'i dbang bka'/ bshad bka'/ lung bka'/ khrid bka'/ man ngag gi bka' la sogs pa zab
cing rgya che ba'i tshul mtha' yas pas phyogs dang ris su ma bcad pa'i snod ldan gyi gdul bya blo gsal zhing don du gnyer ba'i dad 'dun can gzhal du med pa mchog dman 'bring
gsum so so'i khams dang / mos pa dang / bag la nyal mkhyen pa'i sgo nas smin cing grol ba'i lam la 'god par mdzad pa'ang / gong du rim pa ltar bshad pa de rnams yin
la/ de lta bu'i chos tshul de dag gang 'chad kyang / thos bsam gyis sgro 'dogs legs par bcad cing / bsgom pas thugs nyams su myong ba'i sgo nas stsol ba kho na dang / 'chad
tshul yang / blo chen rnams la zab rgya che/ /blo chung bzung bde go sla ba/ /de las ldog na mkhas rmongs kyi/ /slob ma dga' ba skyed mi nus/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ mdo
sngags gang 'chad kyang gdul bya rang rang gi khams dang / bsam pa dang / bag la nyal gyi rim pa dang mthun par ston par mdzad cing / khyad par gsang sngags zab mo'i chos
tshul rnams ni/ nyams su blang ba'i mtha'/ nyams su myong ba'i mtha'/ byin gyis brlab pa'i mtha'/ grub pa'i mtha' ste/ mtha' bzhi'i bdag nyid can dang / dbang gi chu bo
ma nub pa/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa/ gdams

ngag gi sarga ma log pa/ mos gus kyi bsam pa tshim pa ste snyan brgyud bzhi sogs kyi sgo nas go rim ma 'chol bar dkri bar mdzad la/ thugs kyi lhag bsam kyang / dbyig gnyen
gyis/ chos sbyin nyon mongs can min pas/ /mdo sogs ji bzhin yang dag ston/ /zhes dang / bslab btus las/ chos kyi sbyin pa zang zing med/ /bsod nams 'phel ba'i rgyu yin no/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar rnyed pa dang grags pa bsgrub pa'i kun slong rnams rgyang ring du spangs te bstan pa dang sems can gyi don kho na la dgongs nas/ sku ngal dub kyi tshogs
khyad du gsod pa mdzad pa ni sku 'khor ba sogs mtshan dpe'i snang ba mngon du gyur pa'i skye bo kun gyis shes pa ltar ro/ /de mthun gsang sngags kyi zab chos bka' nub
pa rnams la thugs kyi phongs sems chen po dang / chad du nye ba dag kyang rgyun chad dogs mi bzod pa lta bu mdzad cing / zhal nas kyang chos 'di dang 'di'i bka' nub pa
de phongs po rang yin 'dug /da dung dbang dang rgyud bshad sogs rgya che ba'i rigs rnams rgyun ma nyams tsam byung na snyam spel gang thub byed bsams kyang / dus dbang gis
rgyun ring ma byung dogs pa ka 'ong gin snang bcas yang yang gsung ba thos la/ de ltar mdo rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa'i zab chos gang 'chad kyang sla bcos dang / mi 'os
pa'i ris 'gre/ rung mthun dang / rang bzo sogs kyi dri ma mtha' dag dang bral ba/ rang rang la skabs su babs pa'i thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa sbyar 'os pa rnams
ma lus shing / mi 'os pa cung zad kyang ma lhag par chos de dang de'i brgyud pa'i rtsa ba ni 'di nas brgyud/ rten gzhi rgyud

'di yin/ rgya gzhung dang bod gzhung 'di snyed cig mchis pas de rnams babs bsgrigs nas bla mas kyang bshad/ slob mas kyang don gnyer chen po'i sgo nas mnyan te chos kyi babs
go bar byas na 'chad nyan rnal ma zhig 'ong ba yin gsungs shing / gzhan la dbang khrid sogs mdzad pa'i tshe rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi gsung bshad chu 'babs ltar dang
/ dmigs pa'i gnad phra mo tshun chad kyang ma chad pa/ gong 'og ma 'dres shing / ma 'chol ba/ gsal zhing rtogs sla yid la 'jebs pa/ bka' khrid lta bu'i skabs kyang / dang
po sa bcad las je rgyas su 'gro ba ma gtogs/ sa gzhung mi mtshungs pa'i hol khongs sogs mi 'byung bar ma zad/ rang lugs gang yin rgyas shing mtha' chod par gsungs pa las/
gzhan lugs la zur mi za zhing / grub mtha' so so'i nyer mchod sgrig tshul gyi bar ma 'dres par mdzad pa sogs/ mdor na kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bla ma gong ma rnams kyi rnam
thar ji lta ba bzhin mchis shing / khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba'i rtogs brjod las/ sku che ba'i yon tan brjod skabs su gsungs pa rnams skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid la yongs
su rdzogs par mnga' ba yin pas/ bdag sogs gdul bya rnams chos zhu bar bcar ba'i tshe yid dga' yal le/ shes pa spro sing nge ba'i ngang nas chos thun yun ring po ji tsam
mdzad kyang dub pa'i rnam pa cung zad kyang med cing / nged rang lta bu blo rmongs kyi rigs rnams mig phye ba ltar 'gyur ba sogs gzhan du lo brgyar sbyangs pa byas pa las/
rje'i drung du chos thun gcig nyan pa don che'o/ /rtsod pa rdo rje'i

shugs kyis log rtog gi brag ri bsnyil tshul yang / rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid ni 'jam pa'i dbyangs dngos su mchis shing / sku phreng du mar paNDi ta'i sku skye brgyud mar bzhes
pas skyes stobs kyi thugs gsal kho nas sku phreng 'dir rigs gzhung la sbyong ba gtan ma mdzad kyang / gzhung lugs du ma'i 'gal 'grel gcod pa la mkhyen rab klong du gyur
mod/ 'on kyang snyigs ma'i rang mdangs ches cher bdo ba'i skabs 'dir gdul bya'i mos ngo dang mthun par rtsod yig dang zur za'i rigs la nan tar mi dgyes shing spros pa
mi mdzad kyang / don la ni de dag kyang phul du phyin pa zhig ste/ dper mtshon na sku na phra mo'i skabs ngor pa dge slong sangs rgyas lhun grub bam/ 'dan ma rab 'byams par
grags pa'i yon tan dang rang snang can de rje bsod nams snang byed drung du byon par de gshegs pas sku zhabs nas mkha' spyod ma'i bka' khrid gnang skabs/ dge slong nas
khrid 'di'i brgyud par bco brgyad rje dang / rmor chen gnyis bzhugs pa legs sam zer bar/ de kha yin gnang bar/ a kha zer/ ci yin gsung pas/ khong dpon slob phrin las ches
pas yun bsrings te bsgom long byung med 'gro bas nyams khrid gsha' mar i 'gro zer bar/ rje'i gsung gis/ de ltar na/ sa paNDi ta dang 'phags pa rin po che'i tshod khong
gnyis kyi phrin las byis pa'i rtsed mo dang 'dra bas 'phags pa khu dbon nas brgyud pa'i khrid la khyod log rtog de ltar mdzad dam/ gsungs pas/ shin tu mad zer mchi ma 'don
bzhin du phyag mang po 'tshal ba sogs kyis mtshon/ mkhas pa su zhig zhabs drung du 'ong ba rnams

kyis dka' gnad kyi don la dogs gcod gang zhus pa rnams la mtha' chod cing don 'grel ba'i gsung gis the tshom dang / log rtog gi dri ma bsal te/ nges pa'i don la sbyor bar mdzad
pa ni dpyod ldan gzur gnas kun la mngon du gyur pa yin la/ gsum pa rtsom pa nyin mor byed pa'i 'od phreng gis bstan pa'i pad tshal rgyas par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ tshig
rgyan gyi bstan bcos me long las/ snyan ngag dam pa'i rgyan 'di ni/ /bskal pa'i bar du gnas par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ rtsom pa po tshad ldan gyis bskrun pa'i bstan
bcos rnams ni/ ma 'ongs pa ji srid bstan pa gnas kyi bar de srid du rgyun ma nyams par gnas pas bstan pa yun ring du mi nub pa'i rgyu dang / mkhas pas yang dag sbyar
ba yi/ /ngag ni ngag gi 'dod 'jor bshad/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ bla ma rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi yon tan brjod pa dang / rgyal ba'i bka' dri ma med pa
dag gi dgongs don gsal ba'i phyir dgos sogs chos lnga ldan las brtsams te 'phags yul gyi gnas lnga rig ba'i paNDi ta chen po rnams la grags pa ltar sdeb sbyor gyi gtsug
lag dang mthun par brtsams nas/ rtsom pa kho na la brten nas lhag pa'i lha zhal ston pa dang / chos kyi gnas lugs mngon sum du mthong ba la sogs pa rang don phun sum tshogs
pa 'grub cing / don du gnyer ba gzhan dag yul mchog la ma dad pa dad pa dang / dad pa rnams phyir zhing 'phel bar 'gyur ba dang / mdo rgyud bstan bcos dang bcas pa'i
dgongs don bde blag tu rtogs nas gzhan la'ang tshul bzhin

du ston nus pa'i spobs pa dge ba sogs gzhan don 'bad med du 'byung ba'i 'dod 'jor yang bshad cing / yang sdom gsum rab dbye las/ mkhas rnams dga' ba'i sdeb sbyor ni/ /blun
po rnams kyis go dka' bas/ /tshigs gi sbyor ba spangs nas kyang / /kun gyis go bar bya phyir bshad/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ sgra dang / sdeb sbyor dang / snyan ngag dang / ming
gi mngon brjod/ tshig gi rgyan la sogs pa rnams ni rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas pa'i skye bo dag gi 'jug ngogs yin kyang / de las gzhan don gnyer blo dman pa dag la phan
pa'i rngo mi thogs pas mkhas blun thun mong ba'i blo gros kyis dpyad byar 'os pa'i chos ni snyigs ma'i dus 'dir phan yon gyi sgo nas gzhan las khyad par du 'phags par
'khums la/ de ltar na bstan pa rin po che rgyun ring du chags pa'i slad dang / don gnyer yongs la phan pa'i thugs bskyed zla med pas nye bar drangs te legs par gsungs pa'i
bstan bcos tshig don 'brel chags shing kun gyi blo yul du 'jebs par 'char ba'i rtsom pa ni thub pa'i bstan pa 'dzin pa'i rgyu tshogs bla na med pa ste/ de lta bus phan
'bras phul du byung ba thams cad kyang bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di'i rmad du byung ba'i thugs bskyed dang / dri ma med pa'i mkhyen rab zung 'jug gi chu gter chen pos
nye bar bskrun pa'i legs bshad phan bde padmo'i gnyen du gyur pa 'di dag la gnas pa gzhir bcas kyang / sngon gyi yi ge rnying pa rnams 'phel rgyas la dgongs/ gsung rtsom
gyi rigs kyang cher ma mdzad cing / mdzad pa rnams kyang gab dkrugs dang 'don mi bde ba sogs bsal bar mdzad cing /

ngo bo rgyas su 'gro ba las mdor bsdu gang thub byas pa la mi dgyes shing / so so'i blo dang mthun par bka' rtsom mdzad pa rnams smos pa 'di/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i brgyud
'debs bu'i kha skong bcas/ tshe dbang bla ma zhi khro dang / gso rig rgyud bzhi'i lung gi brgyud 'debs/ gsung ngag dang / 'jigs byed dbang brgyud lugs gsum/ smar khrid tshems
bu lugs/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ gur zhal rnams kyi brgyud 'debs tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i kha skong / sgrol ma'i gsol 'debs/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gi mchog sprul myur
pheb dang / yab rje rdo rje 'chang ratna'i mtshan can/ bco brgyad gdung khyab bdag mtshan can/ ngor chen bkra shis lhun grub/ bsam yas sa phug chos rje kun dga' tshul
khrims/ khams ston sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ bla ma lcags zam pa rnams kyi gsol 'debs dang / rje nyid kyi 'khrungs rabs dang / rnam thar gsol 'debs/ sku bstod brtan bzhugs
bcas sum cu rtsa grangs tsam/ yang chos rgyal yab sras/ zhwa dmar sprul sku/ ngos mched/ ma bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo rnams la gsungs pa'i bden tshig /bla ma yi dam chos
srung thams cad kyi bris 'bur 'dod gsol dang / mchod rdzas zhal byang sogs sdom nyi shu brgal tsam/ yi ge'i ma mo la spel ba'i 'gur ma gsum/ sor 'brang bsnyen thabs/ khyung
khra'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ khyung nag /sgrol dkar/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ dbyangs can dmar mo'i gsang sgrub/ sme brtsegs dud ka /bgegs mthar byed rnams kyi sgrub thabs/ dza
bhir dang /

mnga' ris rig 'dzin chen po nas brgyud pa'i tshe sgrub/ rig byed ma'i byin rlabs kyi gsal byed/ dus 'khor sgrub dkyil/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /de'i dkyil 'khor tshon tho/ dri
med sA chog gi thig rtsa/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs tshigs bcad lhug /dkyil chog /sbyin sreg /mtshams tho bskyed chog dang / cha gsum nag 'gros/ rdzogs
chen snying thig /khrid kyi zin bris/ rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i bstod pa dang / gtor mdos zung 'brel/ sngags drug phyag drug gi zin bris/ rnam sras gtor bsngo/
gtor bskul 'og min bde chen ma'i kha skong zangs gri skor gsum dang / sku lngar tshigs bcad/ rdo rje shugs ldan/ me sna lha btsan/ she'u grong gzhis bdag /she'u grong
rgyal po rnams kyi gsol kha/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po nas brgyud pa'i 'pho ba/ gong sa mchod yon la zhabs brtan 'bul skabs zhal bzhes zhu ba'i legs bshad/ sgra mdo pA
Na'i cho ga'i bsdus don gsung rtsom 'phro can sogs te de dag kyang brjod bya'i don rgya che zhing / rjod byed kyi tshig brling ba/ 'gal 'brel gyi rnam dbye phyed pa/ mkhas
blun kun gyi rnar snyan zhing gzung bde ba sogs/ gsung gi gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pas 'doms par mdzad pa kho na ste bsdebs legs rtsom pa'i phreng bas kyang bstan
'gro yongs la phan bde'i dpal ster bar mdzad pa zhig go /de ltar sku tshe ril por bstan pa'i rtsa lag 'chad nyan la rtag 'grus su bka' drin bskyangs pas spyi bye brag gi
bstan 'gror phan bde spel ba'i byed po bstan 'dzin gyi skyes chen duu ma dang / gsung gi gsang ba

'dzin pa'i zhal slob nam mkha'i skar tshogs lta bu mchis pa de dag re re nas 'bri ba ga la langs/ 'on kyang gdul bya rnams kyi dad pa'i gsos su rags rim tsam smos na/ 'dzam
gling bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rgyal tshab 'khrul pa'i dri ma zad par spangs shing mtha' dbus bstan 'gro'i nyer 'tsho bla na med pa de
mo rin po che ngag dbang 'jam dpal bde legs rgya mtsho/ bdag cag gi drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha'i mtshan
can/ ris med 'gro ba'i 'dren pa 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong / e waM mkhas pa'i dbang po 'jam dbyangs chos kyi bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes/ zab don nor bu'i bang mdzod
brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang blo gsal bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shar chen chos kyi rje rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ kho bo cag mched/
gzhon nu nyid nas mkhas grub kyi rnam thar bdag gir bzhes pas rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi thugs sras gces spras su mdzad cing bsngags pa'i me tog yang yang 'thor bar mdzad
pa bco brgyad gdung rin po che dga' chen khyab bdag snying po/ lce rigs mkhas grub dam pa'i rgyud las byon pa bco brgyad bla brang gi da lta'i zhal ngo gnyis/ grub dbang
thang stong rgyal po'i gdung 'dzin gcung ri bo che pa sku mched/ blo bzang stobs ldan dpal 'byor dang / ngag dbang yang grags/ mthu stobs dbang phyug khams ston sangs
rgyas rgya mtsho sogs mdo khams khul gyi bla ma mkhas grub du ma dang / kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyi gdan sa pa bod

'brug chos rje mkhyen rab ngag dbang blo gsal phun tshogs dang / chos grwa chen po nA lendra'i bla ma slob dpon du ma/ paNDi ta shAkya mchog ldan gyi rgyal tshab rtse gdong
sprul pa'i sku mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhas dbang dam pa gzims phug sprul pa'i sku blo bzang bstan 'dzin mgon po/ nyams rtogs klong gyur gzhi dgon mkhan chen
bsod nams dpal bzang / 'dar grong mkhan chen mkhyen pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang shes rab/ nyams rtogs nus pa mthar phyin bla ma dam pa rnams la mos gus kho nas grol ba rig
'dzin skal bzang rnam grol/ sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin zhing sa lam gyi rtogs pa mngon du gyur pa rdzong ri rab 'byams pa byams pa kun dga' phrin las skal bzang bstan
'dzin/ gling smad zhabs drung phun tshogs bkra shis sogs gsang phu ne'u thog dang 'bras yul skyed tshal gyi bla ma slob dpon du ma/ snyan brgyud zab mo'i mdzod 'dzin rdo
rje 'dzin pa bsod nams snang byed dang / bsod nams rin chen/ kun dga' dpal 'byor sogs bkra shis chos sde'i slob dpon du ma/ rab byung mkhan po bzod pa 'od zer/ bka' 'gyur
ba chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa phug grub dbang kun dga' tshul khrims/ dge slong bsam gtan rgyal mtshan/ nA ro'i rnam sprul 'brug pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ paNDi
ta karma chos kyi 'byung gnas/ rgyal sras mchog gi sprul sku blo bzang 'jigs med/ zhi lha sprul pa'i sku 'phags pa dge legs rgyal mtshan/ rngog gi gdung 'dzin nyan po khu
dbon/ zur sprul pa'i sku phrin las blo ldan rgya mtsho/ se bo sprul sku lhun grub phun tshogs/ gangs can mkhan rin po che

ngag dbang rab brtan/ 'phyong rgyas ri bo bde chen gyi mkhan chen bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho/ pha bong kha'i mkhan chen skal bzang mchog grub/ mang ra mkhan chen blo bzang dpal
'bar/ kong po zho kha bla ma zla ba bzang po/ sgrub rnying slob dpon lhun grub rgyal po/ nyang stod pa brtse chen bla ma byams pa shes rab/ skyed tshal 'og bla ma rong pa
skyid gshongs chos rje/ 'bras gling bla ma mdo sngags chos 'phel/ bka' chen thabs mkhas rgya mtsho/ gshegs khar zab don mngon du gyur pa zhwa lu dbu byed kun spangs/ grub
mtha' ris med la mos shing lhag par rje 'di nyid la mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang ldan pa sog yul ha la shan gyi bla dpon zung 'brel tho yon dar rgyas sogs byang rigs bla
dpon mang po/ rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye brag sa ngor bstan pa'i sbyin bdag sa skyong rgyal po'i rigs su 'khrungs shing / chos rgyal mtshan don dang mthun pa bstan pa tshe
ring yab sras blon 'bangs du ma/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bstan pa'i sbyin bdag 'dar pa yab sras/ bka' blon paNDi ta mdo mkhar zhabs drung tshe ring dbang rgyal/
rim gnyis zab mor rtag 'grus spo ra ba ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ rje nyid kyi brtse ba chen po nas lhag par skyong zhing rnam dpyod blo gros gsal ba nam mkha'
rin chen/ sgo gsum 'dun pa chig sgril gyi bla ma dam pa'i zhabs tog la gcig tu 'grus pa 'jam dpal rgya mtsho sogs rje nyid kyi zhabs gras blo gros dang ldan pa du ma
ste/ mdor na rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid dang bla slob sogs 'brel ba'i skyes chen dam pa rnams dang / gsung gi gsang ba 'dzin pa'i bstan

'dzin mkhas grub du ma/ bshad sgrub kyi sgo nas rgyal ba'i ring lugs spel ba'i dge 'dun gyi sde/ bstan pa'i sbyin bdag rgyal blon sogs skal ldan gyi gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab
pa bskrun par mdzad pa'i rigs can de rnams las/ rab dang phul du gyur pa rnams kyis ni snyigs dus su bstan 'gro spyi dang bye brag la dgos 'dod kyi char ci'ang 'bebs
shing / de las zhan pa rnams kyis la las rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang mthun pa'i 'chad nyan dang / la las sgom sgrub/ yang mthar gyur pa rnams kyang dge ba'i bag chags bzang
pos dus 'das te/ mdor na rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid mthong thos dran reg tsam gyis kyang mngon mtho dang nges legs la bkod pa'i rnam par thar pa'ang bsam gyis mi khyab
bo/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ mdo rgyud man ngag rig gnas 'chad la mkhas/ /lung rig 'gal 'brel rtsod dang legs bshad brtsams/ /ris med grub mtha'i bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho
bskrun/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon mkhas pa'i mdzad pa yin/ /zhes so// ! spyi don gsum pa mthar gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan cing / dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa
dang phrin las kyi rgyun ji ltar spel tshul la/ gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdus tshul dang / dgongs rdzogs spel tshul gnyis las/ dang po ni/ bdag cag lha dang bcas pa'i
'gro ba yongs kyi skyabs mgon dam pa 'di nyid dgung grangs nga bdun du pheb pa lcags pho 'brug lo yan chad du bstan 'gro'i don rlabs po che mdzad pa rnams la thugs dgyes
shing / snyigs dus bstan 'gro spyi bye brag gi nyams

chag gso dka' ba rnams la cung zad nges par 'byung ba dang / zhing 'di'i sku dngos kyis gdul bya re zhig de tsam gyis rdzogs nas/ zhing khams rgya che ba gzhan gyi don mdzad
par dus la babs pa na de lta'i snang tshul ston par bzhed de/ de'ang 'di lo sku dkyil sngar las lhag par dwangs shing / chos 'chad sogs la thugs spro ba ltar mdzad/ spyan
cung zad mi gsal ba'i rnam pas phyag dpe yi ge phra ba rnams mi gzigs pa la/ thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed kyi gdams pas gzhan la phan pa dga' mo byung ste/ kho bo rang
la cher ma phan par 'dug /mig gis dpe cha ma mthong na de khas rtsal rdzogs pa yin/ da rang tshe ring bar dga' rgyu med ces sogs thugs nges 'byung gi rnam pa kho nar mdzad/
myos ldan zhes pa sa yos lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang phyag mdzod 'jam dpal rgya mtsho shin tu bro 'tshal skabs gsung 'phros kyi lhongs su/ da lam sku zhabs zhabs pad
brtan ring shi'ang mi 'gyod tshul zhus par/ skyag re la/ a khyod de 'dra byas pas mi 'ong / gnas gsar ba gdung gis 'dzin yang da cha gdung ni med/ nga shi na skye ba rtsad
gcod 'dra'ang byed dgos gsungs / tshe dbang stong rtsa zhig nan tan chen pos mdzad pas bro 'tshal ba las myur du grol/ skabs gseng gsung gi lhongs su snyan brgyud kyi
bstan pa nyag phra tshul gsungs shing / da ni skye ba 'dra byung yang gsang sngags gsar rnying gi zab chos 'di rnams zhu sa'ang dkon po 'ong ba 'dra zhes dang / thar rtse
rdo rje 'chang de nyid sa lugs kyi bstan 'dzin 'gran med/ ha cang gi sku nar son pa

zhig min kyang shing khyi lor zhing gzhan du gshegs pa dang / ngor chen dpal ldan chos skyong slar yang mdo khams su pheb ste bstan 'gro'i don chen mdzad bzhed de'ang sa yos
lor bar chad du song ba dang / 'khon rigs 'dzin pa nged rang gi nu bo rgyan mchog de me glang lor tshe mthar ma phyin zhing / de dag gi sngon du bco brgyad gdung rin po
che mkhas grub dam pa myur du 'byung nye de'ang glo bur du gshegs shing / sa skya pa'i gdung nyag phra ba sogs rang lugs la shin tu ya nga ba'i skabs de dag gsungs pa dang
chab cig /da ni rang re sa skya pa'i re bar kho bo kho na las med tshul sogs thugs ngal gyi rnam pa dpag med mdzad/ de lta'i skabs/ lha ldan du gsung chos kyi snyan gsan
phul ba zhal gyis bzhes pa rnams kyang phal cher rdzogs par mdzad/ sde pa sku tshar yang nyin par gzhung zhabs kyi thugs brel stabs gnang ma thub kyang / nub mo zab chos
kyi rigs kyang stsal/ bod phrug chos rje sogs 'dus pa nyung shas la bi ma snying thig gi dbang lung rnams stsal skabs/ nub cig 'od gsal gyi ngang du 'ja' tshon kha dog
lnga ldan zhig nam mkha'i dbyings nas sku mdun bar thal ler zug cing / de la cher gyis gzigs pas thugs bde stong gi ngang du cham gyis song ba zhig byung gsungs/ lha ldan
du thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs kyi sku gsum snying po'i don khrid gnang skabs/ kho bo'i rmi lam du stag rtse rgya ra yin snyam pa'i khang pa dang lha khang nged rang
gi khri sogs ji lta ba bzhin 'dug par nged rang khang pa'i phyir 'khod kyang rtsig pa sogs la sgrib g.yogs med par zang thal gyis mthong zhing /

khri'i steng na yod snyam par de la ched du bltas pas thugs rje chen po zhal bcu gcig pa'i sku shin tu gsal ba thog tshad ma zhig bzhugs par mthong zhing / de kha la nub phyogs
nas 'ja' kha dog lnga pa zhig thal gyis byung ste khri'i steng du zug pa dang dran med du song ba lta bu'i ngang du cung zad lus pa dang gnyid sad pa zhig byung gsungs/
zhabs phyi rnams kyis ci yin nam zhus pas/ khrid bshad pa 'di'i bag chags yin nam gsungs/ blo gsal rab rgyas kyis gsung ngag ma thob pa la yi mug skyes tshul zhus pa'i
lan du/ sngon 'phags pa rin po che'i skabs su lam 'bras mdzo 'gros mar grags pa byung ba'i lo rgyus kyang yod pas dga' mo thob 'gro zhes gsungs na'ang / 'di lo lan cig
gsung las/ da rang lam 'bras shig mi byed pa 'dra gsungs pas zhabs phyi rnams kyi blor sku'i ltem babs sku 'khrugs lta bur song ba de khar dgongs pa yin nam bsam pa ma gtogs
zhabs pad mi brtan pa'i dogs pa ma shar/ da lo bsam yas mdo sde mchod pa'i skabs nged rang nas zhu yig phul khongs su/ rwa tshar thun mong ma yin pa'i 'jigs byed bcu
gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil la dogs zhu phul ba'i bka' lan dang chab cig /'di nas g.yar phul 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi bka' 'bum pod bcas stsal ba ni dus 'dir bka'
shog pheb pa'i tha ma yin no/ /'phags sder bzhugs skabs snga dro nub phyogs su 'ja' zug pa dang / spyir 'di lo char dkon kyang 'phags sder bzhugs ring char che ba dang /
lhag par chibs bsgyur gnang skabs skyi chu glo bur du rgyas

shing chu thon ma khad drag char shin tu che ba sogs kyi 'tshubs lhong dang / rmor dgon du chibs bsgyur gnang res kyi bye la'i rtse nas dgon par ma phebs bar bya rog gnyis
zan slong ba'i tshul gyis 'ongs pa'ang 'di lo ma byung bas/ bka' las/ da lo rmor pa'i pheb bsu'ang ma byung gsungs/ lha ldan du bzhugs skabs shig kyang 'di lo bya rog 'di
'gyang du song ba zhig 'dug ces gsungs/ rmor dgon du pheb 'phral tsam la sbus ri'i ri rgyud thal mar ngur ba dang me 'bar gyi rnam pa yang yang brgyugs shing rmor gyi rgyab
rir 'ja' btud mar zug pa/ bkra shis chos sder dpal mgon zhal gyi gtor chen 'gyel ba/ mgon khang gi ka ba khrag 'dzag ma'i thad nas lcam gnyis chag pa/ phyi rten gyi mgon
khyi smyo zhing shi ba/ yar klung khul du srod la nam langs pa lta bu'i snang ba shar ba/ yul khams byings la'ang than pa che zhing zla 'dzin nyi 'dzin mang ba/ dpal
sa skya'i lam 'bras lha khang theg chen pho brang gi ga ya dha ra'i bum chu'i snod gas nas chu zegs stobs che zhing kha shin tu dma' ba sogs mi dge ba'i mtshan ma mtha' dag
spungs pa ltar gyur kyang / sku khams ni sngar las lhag par dwangs shing / zhal mdangs sogs kyang shin tu legs pa bcas ltos bcas tshang mar dogs gnad tsam yang ma shar/
tshes bdun tsam nas sngar gyi smug po'i bsnyun gzhi de cung zad 'phar ba'i rnam pa byung yang bsnyung gsol ma zhus par gsang ba kho na mdzad cing / rgyun du'ang bsnyun
gzhi de ltar 'byung ba'ang rgyu rkyen nges pa can la mi ltos shing / dwangs bskyed kyang 'phrod gzhes sogs la cher mi

ltos pa sogs phal pa'i blo yul las 'das pa zhig 'ong 'dug pa de kha yin khul gyi rmor em ji lhun grub dar rgyas nas gsol sman 'bul ba sogs sngar rgyun bzhin byas 'dug kyang
/ dwangs bskyed cher ma byung bar/ stag rtse em ji 'phral 'bod gnang ba'i 'phrod gzhes rnams kyang 'dod pa bzhin dang bzhes mdzad/ chos sde sogs dgon pa phan tshun rnams
su zhabs brtan sku rim bsgrub rgyu 'phral rdzong dang / rmor rang du'ang sgrol 'don dang bskang ba 'dzugs pa sogs mdzad/ tshes bcu'i nyin rdo rje phreng ba'i lugs kyi sa
thig bskor bar thur 'dzugs kyi phyogs 'tshol mdzad de 'di nas brtsis pa'i phyogs kyang lugs 'di ltar yin 'dug ces brda sprod dang / rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol/ zhabs
'bring pa dge slong ngag dbang 'jam dbyangs/ blo gsal rab rgyas bcas la chos rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i lam sbas bshad kyi lung stsal ba gsung chos kyi tha ma yin/ tshes
bcu gcig bcu gnyis sogs su spyan nam mkha' la gzigs nas gsung gleng ci'ang mi mdzad par yun ring bzhugs pa lan mang por mdzad/ tshes bcu bzhi'i nub mo nas bsnyun gyi rnam
pa ci'ang med cing nyin par mnal gyi rnam pa yod tsam byung / tshes bcu drug nyin gzims chung 'di tshad pa che gshis nang shar mar spos shig gsungs pa bzhin sku chas rnams
rags tsam bsdus nas der bzhugs gdan 'jags/ de'i nyin zhal mdangs cung ngan par zhabs 'bring pa sbyin pa rgya mtshos phyag dbang zhus skabs mchi ma bton par/ zhal 'dzum
mdangs dang bcas mchi ma 'don mi dgos/

dga' mo 'ong 'gro zhes sems bso mdzad/ de'i mjug tsam du phyag mdzod 'jam dpal nas kyang de ring sku khams cung zad zhan pa ltar snang bas bdag sogs mgon med rnams la brtse
bar dgongs te zhabs pad brtan par bzhugs dgos zhes mchi ma 'don zhing zhus par/ zhal 'dzum dang bcas te/ de 'dra'i skyag re chung ba byed mi dgos/ grub thob gong ma'i gsung
las/ nga 'chi bas mi 'jigs skye bas 'jigs/ /skye ba las kyi rjes su 'brangs/ /zhes gsungs pas/ spyir 'chi ba 'di skye 'phags kun gyi lam po che yin pas 'jigs rgyu med/
'chi ba gcig pos mi chog skye ba len dgos/ /de la rang dbang thob pa zhig med na 'jigs pa yin mod/ 'on kyang kho bo cag lta bu dam pa gong ma khyad par can de rnams kyi
rigs su skyes/ bla ma mtshan nyid dang ldan pa du mas rjes su bzung / bsam pa rnyed nas da bar chos kyi bya ba ma gtogs mi dge ba'i las ni ma bgyis/ mi lus mi 'thob pa'i
don med/ skye ba 'dra 'ong shas che bas rtsad chod/ dpe cha dbang rdzas rnams ma bor bar gyis/ bu chung dang khyed rang gnyis gcig la gcig dgos pa 'ong bas sngar lugs bzhin
du mthun pa gyis zhes sogs bka' slob rgyas par stsal/ lar sku tsha nam mkha' rin chen 'di la dus rgyun du bu chung zhes 'bod par mdzad cing / 'di nga'i yab rgyal po de'i
skye ba 'khrul med yin/ chos sgor zhugs na bla ma nga rang las kyang lhag pa zhig 'ong tshod dang / yang na khyim so zhig zin pa legs 'dra'ang / sde pa nor 'dzin dbang
pos thugs snang ci'ang mi snang zhes yang yang bka' pheb pa'ang

ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i gsung kho nar nges/ phyag 'dzod gzims chung phyir thon pa dang / blo gsal rab rgyas la mdangs rmi lam du cung ri bo che ba'i grwa rigs du mas snga phyi
bar gsum gyi lugs gnyis kyi gtam du ma gleng ba zhig byung gsungs bar/ de ci lags zhus pas/ ci yin mi shes zhes sba bar mdzad/ de nas btags grol dang mgul gab rnams phud
nas dbu thog tu thogs gsungs pa bzhin dbu thog tu btags/ thugs ka'i thad der ltos dang zhes gsungs par sku 'ching bkrol nas bltas pas sngar dang mi 'dra ba ni gang yang
mi 'dug /rjes su byas tshe dbyar dus su song ba dang thugs dam la bzhugs gshis sgul skyod ma thub dogs na bza' srab pa dang sku 'ching 'grol ched du sems zhes gleng /
de nas nyi ma nub par nye ba na dgong thun gyi mkha' spyod dbang mo'i thugs dam nan tan stsal/ blo gsal rab rgyas kyis ljags bzlas ha cang mang na sku rlung skye shas kha
zhus pas/ de kha byed gsung / de nas bzhugs gdan srab mo zhig gi steng du na bza' sku 'gags sku g.yogs rkyang pa dang bcas/ dgung lo nga bdun bzhes pa lcags 'brug zla ba
drug pa'i tshes bcu drug gi srod 'khor snga cha tsam nas zhal shar du gzigs/ sku drang por bsrang / zhabs skyil krung / phyag mnyam gzhag gi ngang nas/ rgyal yum rdo rje
btsun mo'i nye lam la brten nas kun rdzob gzugs sku'i bkod pa don dam chos sku'i dbyings su snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas phyag mdzod 'jam dpal gyis sngon nas zhal bzhes
bzang po stsal ba'i don bzhin spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / bye brag rje

btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che/ yang sgos tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa rin po che rnams kyi ched dang / bdag cag mgon med nyam thag rnams
kyi don du yang srid gsal dwangs myur du 'byon dgos zhes sogs kyi gsol 'debs dang / rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol nas kyang gong bzhin gsol ba btab pas thugs dam du bzhugs
zin pa las slar yang cer gyis gzigs pa ni de ltar bgyi'o zhes zhal gyis bzhes par nges so/ /'dir smras pa/ mi mjed 'gro la rjes chags shAkya'i rgyal/ /bsil ldan gdul
bya'i skyabs gcig pad dkar 'chang / /mkhas grub du mar rnam rol gnas gsar rje/ /mgon khyod snying nas dran no brtse bas dgongs/ /rigs rus cho 'brang ldan pa mtshan dpe'i
sku/ /zhing dul 'dzum mdzes dri zhim ngur smrig g.yo/ /deng dus mngon sum spyod yul ma gyur na/ /kyi hud rdo rje'i sku de gang du gshegs/ /shes bya'i gnas kun 'doms pa dpal
gyi mgur/ /'jam zhing snyan pa'i dbyangs kyis blang dor ston/ /deng dus cha tsam thos par ma gyur na/ /kyi hud thar 'dod lam mkhan su yis byed/ /mkha' khyab rgyal ba
kun dang ro gcig thugs/ /lnga bdo'i 'gro la thugs rje'i gter 'chang ba/ /deng dus gzhan du g.yel ba'i tshul ston na/ /kyi hud gdul bya khrel bar ma gyur grang / /skye rgu'i
phan bde'i rgyal bstan dar ba'i gzhi/ /thub pa'i rgyal tshab bstan 'dzin la rag na/ /gangs khrod mkhas grub du ma gzhan du gshegs/ /yang dag bstan pa'i rgyun 'di ci 'drar
'gyur/ /khyad par rdo rje 'chang dngos sa skya pa'i/ /yang zab bstan pa'i nying khu kha'u pa'i/ /slob

bshad chos kyi 'byung gnas gzhan du gshegs/ /bdag sogs rjes 'jug skal bzang zad 'dir skyo/ /mgon khyod gang 'dul 'gro ba'i don mdzad phyir/ /ris med dam pa'i zhal gyi bcud
gsol zhing / /sku gsung thugs rten smin grol nyer mkho'i chas/ /da lta grangs med so sor skyo ba 'phel/ /mnga' ris dbus gtsang khams sogs grangs med 'gror/ /'dzum zhal snyan
gsung brtse ba'i thugs 'chang ba/ /da ni yongs rdzogs dor nas gzhan du gshegs/ /dag pa'i zhing na 'gro don 'phel gyur te/ /sngon tshe 'khrul zad grags pa rgyal mtshan
la/ /bde ba can du spyan 'dren bkod pa'i tshe/ /ma dag zhing la rjes brtse'i gsung byon yang / /mgon khyod thugs kyi 'dzin gtong 'gyur ram ci/ /'on kyang 'di lta'i gnas
skabs mi zad pa/ /rnam 'dren dam pa'i skyon du mi 'tshal gyi/ /thog med 'khor bar las nyon khur ldan pa/ /skal dman bdag sogs rnams kyi skyon du mchis/ /gang gi brtse chen
gsung las 'di skad du/ /'khor 'das chos kun sems kyi cho 'phrul te/ /zung 'jug brjod bral don gyi bla ma zhes/ /legs par gdams 'di kho na ngal bsor thob/ /des na deng nas
byang chub ma thob bar/ /dus gsum dge tshogs mchod sprin rgya mtshor 'bul/ /nam yang 'du 'bral med par rjes bzung nas/ /gdod ma'i mgon po'i 'dzum zhal myur mthong shog
/de nub zla khyim dang 'brel ba'i 'ja' sprin phra mo mang pos khengs shing / de nas bzung nyin kun nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa dang / mtshan kun char rgyun chen pos sa gzhi brlan
par byas so/ /de nas

zhabs phyi rnams nas sku gdung rin po che bzhugs pa'i gnas dang nye skor kun tu du chom sogs kyi sgra med pa dang / sku mdun du mchod tshogs rgyas par bstar ba'i bkod pa bgyis
te/ de 'phral rgyal tshab rin po cher thugs dam gsal 'debs zhu rten/ jo shAkya rnam pa gnyis la brgya mchod snyan shal/ dgon phan tshun gyi zhabs brtan bsgrub rgyu kun
rig sogs su bsgyur ba/ bkra shis chos sde nas mchod 'bul ba 'bod pa sogs bgyis te/ thugs dam ma grol bar sku gdung rin po che'i sku mdun du rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol
nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang 'brel ba'i mchod 'bul la brtson par mdzad/ de'i tshe zhal dkyil sngar las lhag par dwangs shing / dkar mdangs che ba/ spyan zim
bur bzhugs pa lta bu/ zhal gyi mchu sgros sogs cung zad tsam yang ma nyams par bzhugs pa las/ tshes bcu dgu'i tho rengs 'ur sgra shin tu che ba dang bcas dri bsung phun
sum tshogs pas gzims khang gi nang gang ba sogs ya mtshan gyi ltas du ma dang chab cig sku gdung rin po che nas byang sems dkar dmar 'dres pa shangs bug g.yon nas mtho gang
tsam babs shing dbu cung zad dud nyams dang bcas thugs dam grol ba na/ sku gdung rin po che la ga bur sogs dri bzang gi chus sku khrus gsol zhing / dri bzang pos sbags
pa'i lha rdzas kyi na bzas mngon par bklubs te/ gnam sa bar gsum gyi rgyan phun sum tshogs shing / mchod tshogs rgya mtsho'i dbus su longs spyod rdzogs sku'i cha byad kyis
bzhugs su gsol/ de nyin chos sde'i grwa pa rnams kyang slebs 'phral nas bzung rim bzhin rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid dgyes mdzad

rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bor bzhengs pa la mchod pa'i phyir sta gon dngos gzhi bdag 'jug len pa bcas bsgrubs/ 'du khang du rmor pa dang 'phags sde tshogs yongs bcas kyis
kun rig sgrub mchod dang / bla ma mchod pa sogs bgyis/ phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa'i tshogs la gdung mjal kyang btang / tshes nyer gnyis mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus
khyad par can la tsandan dang a ka ru sogs dri bzang gi ljon shing phung por spungs pa'i dbus su bla ma kye rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du gsal btab ste mchod tshogs
rgya mtshor bcas pa'i dbus su zhugs la zhen pa na/ thog mar sku gdung rin po che gdan 'dren pa'i skabs char zim bu sa sbangs pa tsam me tog gi tshul du babs shing / cho ga
tshugs pa dang zhugs phul ba'i tshe sprin rnams dwangs pa'i nam mkha' g.ya' dang bral ba'i ngos su 'ja' tshon kha dog sna lnga'i gur dang / rtsibs kyi rnam pa dang / g.yung
drung dang / dga' 'khyil/ chos 'byung sogs dang / mchod pa'i rnam pa lta bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa cho ga ma rdzogs bar du rgyun mi 'chad par byung zhing / cho ga rdzogs
pa'i shis brjod kyi tshe char zim bu sngar ltar babs so/ /nyer lnga'i nyin gdung khang zhal phye ba na/ gdung rus la ba~M yig mang po dang / hU~M yig dang / dga' 'khyil
sogs shin tu gsal bar byon shing bu slob rnams la dad rten du bskur ba 'ga' zhig la lha sku'ang ci rigs byon zhes gleng zhing / blo gsal rab rgyas la rdo rje 'chang de
nyid zhal bzhugs skabs stsal ba'i tshems shig yod par de snga ring bsrel phra mo las med kyang zhing khams

brjes nas ring bsrel mang po dang / ba~M yig li khri'i mdangs ldan zhig kyang byon zhes gleng / gdung sol dang spur thal rnams la sAtstsha btab ste bzhugs gnas khang bu brtsegs
pa'i mchod rten ring bsrel gyi snying po can mtshan nyid dang ldan pa zhig smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling du bzhengs shing / rab tu gnas pa'ang grub par bgyis so/
/de dag gi don bsdu na/ zhing 'dir bstan 'gro'i don mang lhun grub nas/ /rtag mtha' sel zhing gzhan don dgongs pa'i tshe/ /ngo mtshar bcas gshegs mchog sprul zhal bzhes
mdzad/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma'i gshegs tshul yin/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa ni/ bshad ma thag pa de rnams dang / gzhan yang 'di lo nged rang nas rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid
kyi sku drin gsob pa'i ched dang / 'di kha'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud bcas kyi rim gror dmigs/ snron zla'i zla mjug tsam nas bzung rwa tshar thun mong ma yin pa'i lugs
ltar dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod brgya tshar grangs gsog ste chu stod zla mjug bar la ci 'grub bgyid skabs yin pas/ de dang dus mtshungs
zhing khams brjes 'dug pas na dgongs rdzogs kyi rnam pa 'dra mo byung 'dug cing / de nas ma 'gyangs par gro bzhin phur sgrub kyi skabs 'di kha'i shar phyogs brag chung gi
ri'i bye ma la bzang ngan brtag dpyad byed srol yod pa ltar/ sngon du chu sprel gro bzhin tshes gsum gyi tho rangs de thad nas ri brag duu ma tsam zhig pas rkyen byas/
chu bya sa ga'i bar ri bkra ngan pa kho nar yod cing / khyad par rmor dgon nas mchod dpon

'jam dbyangs mchog grub 'di khar ched rdzong byas pa bzhin lo de'i gro bzhin tshes bcu skor la 'byor nyin rgan rabs kyis dran ma myong ba'i ri ltas shin tu ngan pa zhig 'dug
pas sems blong blong po'i mu nas phur sgrub grol bstun beg tse'i chos skor sgrig skabs su da lta'i gnas tshul ngan pa thos pas 'di yin med pa'i gzi thom me ba zhig byung
zhing / de'i sang snga bar 'jam dbyangs mchog grub dang ngos phrad bgyis skabs phyag mdzod 'jam dpal gyi yi ge dang bcas sku gsung thugs rten/ na bza' nyer spyad/ zang
zing dngos po rgya spom mtho bar bstar zhing / thugs dam gsal 'debs dang / yang srid rin po che myur pheb kyi gsol 'debs/ gzhan yang gang spyi'i bslab bya dgos tshul 'dug
pa bzhin rang ngos nas gang shes 'jam dbyangs mchog grub la gleng zhing lan 'debs kyi khongs su'ang 'thus pa dang chab cig dgongs rdzogs zhal 'debs kyi rim pa bskur zhing
/ de 'phral nged rang nas dgung zhag sgrub mchod tshul du mkha' spyod ma'i dkyil chog chag med dang / ngo mtshar rten bzhis thog drangs gtsug lag khang rnams su 'di kha
dang rje de nyid kyi zhabs phyi rnams nas bskur ba'i sna lnga'i brgya mchod/ 'dus sder mang ja/ tshes bcu drug tshes mchod nyin chos sde lho nas kun rig sgrub mchod dang
/ byang nas mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod/ /'dar grong du dus rim pa rnams 'di lo snga bar bos te kye rdor sgrub mchod zhag bdun bcas 'phral sgrub bgyis shing / gzhan yang
dbus phyogs su zhabs phyi rnams nas dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa ji ltar bgyis pa rnam bsdoms su bkod pa la/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen

gzigs chen po/ nged rang dang 'di kha'i rje btsun ma rnams/ rgyal tshab rin po che/ rdo rje brag dang smin grol gling / karma pa yab sras sogs bla chen dang sprul sku'i rigs
du ma/ chos sde khag gi bla ma slob dpon mang po/ skyabs mgon dam pa de nyid nas chos 'brel tsam gsan pas mtha' brten pa'i bla ma zhal bzhugs so cog dang / zhal slob bgres
song mang po/ ri khrod kyi sgom chen pa sogs la thugs dam gsal 'debs rten phul ba dang / mang skol rjes 'brang gi bsngo rten bcas par li sku dang gser sku/ sna tshogs
ngo bcu bdun/ sku thang legs nges lnga/ dril bu theg chen dang sder dril bsdoms bcu drug /bka' gdams gdung rten bcu gnyis/ phyag ting gras ting shag spus legs gsum/ gser
srang lnga bcas dang / de phyin dngul thog tu bsdoms pa dngul srang stong dang lnga brgya/ srang gsum/ zho gang / skar lnga/ gong sa rdo rje 'chang skal bzang rgya mtsho'i
mchod sdong sa gsum rgyan gcig dang / lha sa/ bsam yas/ khra 'brug /sa skya sogs su mchod 'bul snyan shal song ba bsdoms dngul srang lnga brgya dang brgyad cu/ zho brgyad/
bkra shis chos sde/ 'phags sde/ she'u grong / rmor dgon sogs su dgung zhag zhe dgu'i bar mang ja gnyis re dang / sku tshigs so sor kye rdor sogs cho ga rigs mi 'dra
ba du ma dang / sku tshigs bdun pa'i thog tu sgrub mchod zhag bdun re/ rab byung grwa tshang nas sku tshigs bdun la sman bla tshar re/ grong mo che/ gong dkar chos sde/ ra
ba smad/ 'phreng 'og gzhi pa/ dwags po grwa tshang / gdung phud chos 'khor/ tshong 'dus tshogs pa sogs

kyis dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod mang po/ dbus gtsang gi sa dgon gtsor gyur gyi dgon khag shin tu mang bar mang skol nyin 'khyongs nas sbyor sbrel bar ci rigs/ yar 'phyong khul
gyi dgon sde che phra phal che bar mang skol sbyor sbrel tshar gnyis/ yar klung khul gyi chos sde che phra phal mo cher ser tshogs gnad 'gro'i khyad chos sde so sor bteg
pa'i mang ja lnga dang bzhes thug re/ gsol ba yon spyi 'bul sogs gzabs rgyas/ lha ldan smon lam chen mo dang dpal gsang phu ne'u thog tu mang skol sne gzhag bcas sgrub pa'i
dgos cha sdom dngul srang stong dang brgyad brgya bdun/ zho dgu/ skar phyed brgyad bcas bsgrubs/ de nas bkra shis chos sder bod 'brug chos rjes gdung rus kyi cho ga sngon
du 'gro ba can gyi gdung tsha dri med kyi snying po can dang / gzhan yang sangs rgyas byang sems rtsa ba gsum gyi snang brnyan phon che spar du btab/ gro bzhin zla nang
der 'di nas dbus su dgongs rdzogs zhal 'debs 'bul ba dang mang skol do dam par bsod nams don chen ched mngags pa 'khor gdong du/ gdung rus thum po gcig 'di khar pheb
pa bzhin nged rang nas sAtstsha dri med kyi snying po can stong dang / chos grwa byang bsnyen song kha shas nas rtsa gsum gyi snang brnyan rigs mi 'dra ba lnga bcu brgal
ba'i gdung tsha khri phrag lhag pa nged rang nas rab gnas bgyis te bkra shis chos sder ched rdzong dang / gser dngul spel ma'i gdung khang byang chub chen po'i mchod rten
rgyab mtho bcu drug pa phra phul gyis phyug pa dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i rje de nyid kyi 'dra sku sku tshad ma gnyis rgyal tshab rin po cher gsol btab bzhin lha ldan
'dod dpal du zla ba bdun pa'i tshes nyer lnga nas

bzo grwa tshugs pa'i 'dod dpal sku tshab blo bzang dpal 'bar gyis 'dzugs ston dang / karma shag /ge ra yab yum sras bcas nas sgang ston/ chos sde bla brang nas grol ston sogs
shin tu rgyas par bsgrubs pa'i zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes dguu la chos sder gdan drangs shing / mgon khang steng du thog 'phar dang sgo 'phyor gsar rgyag gi ar po sogs
dang tshon rtsi ar zhal rnams legs par bsgrubs te/ der sku rten 'dra sku rin po che gser zangs las grub pa khri rgyab na bza' nyer spyad dang bcas pa dang / mkhan chen
gzhon nu blo gros/ rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po/ skyabs mgon dam pa de nyid bcas kyis dgongs rdzogs su srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i bla brgyud chos sde rang gi tshogs 'don
dkyus bzhin la/ mdo khams bla chen sangs rgyas rgya mtshor rmor chen rdo rje 'chang las gsan bzhes ma thub pa'i nag po chen po'i chos skor mtha' klas pa gsan gshis zhal
skong gi tshul du bzhugs pa'i brgyud pa sum cu so lnga'i sku brnyan la rdo rje 'chang mi tshad tsam dang / gzhan rnams byis pa lo brgyad las cung chung tsam sman 'dam las
grub pa/ 'jim pa dang bzo/ lag cha byin rlabs sogs kyang rung bar bgyis shing / sku sha na bza' kun la grang gser gyi byibs byugs kyis gser zangs 'dra cog dang / gsung rten
bstan 'gyur rin po che sde dge'i spar ma shin tu spus gtsang ba bzang gos kyi gdong dar/ kun dga' ra ba dang bcas pa/ thugs rten la'ang sa chog nas bzung ste bum gter/
bang mdzod bca' ba/ dri med rnam pa gnyis kyi cho ga dang srog shing 'dzugs chog /sAtstsha sgrub chog sogs nas rab tu gnas pa'i bar rnams bod

'brug chos rje dang rig 'dzin skal bzang rnam grol sogs dri med kyi dbang lung thob cing / gzhi tshul khrims la gnas pa du mas legs par bsgrubs shing / de dag gi nang bzhugs
la rje nyid kyi gdung tsha dri med kyi snying po can stong tsho brgal ba/ bre nang du thugs dam gyi snying po nA ro mkha' spyod kyi snang brnyan li ser las grub pa khyad
'phags/ bdud rtsi ril bu las grub pa'i dgyes pa rdo rje'i sku brnyan sogs du ma dang / seng khrir bsil ba tshal gyi rdo nag las grub pa'i nag po chen po'i snang brnyan/
bang mdzod du rje de nyid kyi thugs dam rten rgyal chen rnam sras kyi sku sogs rtsa gsum gyi snang brnyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ gsung rten rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis/ lam 'bras
rdo rje'i tshig rkang / 'jam sdud bzang gsum/ yum rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum sogs mdo sngags kyi glegs bam du ma/ gsung ngag bla brgyud sogs dbu zhabs bar gsum gyi gzungs
gzhug chos sku'i ring bsrel phon che ba/ kun la thugs dgongs rdzogs pa dang mchog sprul myur 'byon gyi 'dod gsol spel tshig sbyar ba dri bzang gis legs par byugs shing
na bza' ser po sha stag gis spras pa/ sku gdung sku bal sogs byin rten skor la de bzhin gshegs pa gser thub dang / shAkya'i rgyal po/ shA ri'i bu sogs kyi ring bsrel mang
po/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i tshems yid bzhin gyi nor bu khungs btsun/ rig 'dzin shrI sidha'i dbu skyes sogs dbu skyes dang / tshems phreng mang po/ thams
cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mkhan chen gzhon nu'i mtshan can/ skyabs mgon dam pa de nyid bcas kyi

snam sbyar tshang ma re/ rje nyid kyi dbu rgyan/ dar dpyangs/ phyag phreng sogs gzungs dang nang gzhug bsam gyis mi khyab pa bzhugs pa ni zhib par dkar chag zur gsal yod pa
de bzhin dang / de ltar rten bzhengs lag len rnams bab chol ma yin par shin tu rung bar bsgrubs shing / thugs rten la bzhugs khri/ snyan shal/ sku mdun du dkar shel gyi
spyod pa sogs ngo mtshar ba/ bla brgyud rnams la bzang gos kyi sku ber sogs na bza' dang / sku mdun du zhal dkar stegs bcas/ rdor dril/ gnam rgyan bla re/ dngul gyi maNDal/
dngul gyi mchod kong zhag bco lnga tsam 'khyongs pa sogs mchod rdzas du ma dang bcas pa'i dbus na bzhugs pa'i steng du/ gser zangs kyi ganydzi ra spus legs nang du spyi
sgos kyi gzungs mang po dang bcas pa rnams la/ dpal kye rdo rje dang / byang gter thugs sgrub phur pa sogs kyi sgo nas rab tu gnas pa'ang lan grangs du ma'i bar du legs
par bsgrubs pa'o/ /de dag la rgyu song rags rim bkod par/ mchod rten dang 'dra sku gnyis kyi sku rgyur zangs khal nyi shu rtsa drug dang nyag bco brgyad/ sgo khyim nang
gi thub dbang gi sku rgyur rang byung zangs 'degs nyag bco brgyad/ gser thur 'degs kyi srang lnga bcu tham pa/ dngul lhad med srang lnga brgya dang drug cu re lnga/ maNDal
dang / mchod kong dril bar dngul lhad med srang brgyad cu gya bdun/ sol ba/ shing / star bu/ btsod dang / dngul chu/ bzo rigs pa'i phog yon sogs bsdoms par dngul srang
brgya dang lnga bcu/ 'dod dpal sku tshab gnyis dang bzo rig 'ul mi bcas par grol ston du song bar bsdoms

dngul srang brgya dang bzhi bcu zhe lnga/ rgyal tshab rin po che sogs lha ldan zhabs pad chen por legs 'bul la dngul srang sum brgya dang bco lnga zho bzhi/ bla brgyud rnams
kyi zhal gser na bza' dang bcas par grangs gser thur srang bcu gcig dang zho brgyad/ bzhugs 'bol la zangs btul ma thur srang bdun/ shing rtsi sogs bsdoms par mtshal srang
dgu bcu go lnga/ gser shog che chung bsdoms khri bam gcig dang / stong bam gsum/ rtsi tshon dgos 'tshams bcas/ yar klung du gzungs 'bul rab gnas snga rting gi yon dang
/ dngul bzo pa/ shing bzo ba/ ri mo ba bcas kyi yon sogs bsdoms dngul srang nyis brgya brgyad cu/ zho dgu/ skar phyed brgyad dang / gzungs 'bul skor gyi dgos cha che phra
rmor dgon dang chos sde sogs su gzungs 'bul rab gnas bzo ba sogs la lto chas nar mar bcas song zhing / na bza' mchod rdzas sogs la bzang gos sna tshogs kha nyis brgya dang
dgu bcu go lnga/ ling yug bcu/ bla bre bzhi/ a la cag yug bzhi bcas song ba dang / bkra shis chos sde'i lam 'bras lha khang brgyud pa'i kha skong du sku 'dra sku tshad
ma/ dbu zhwa/ sku ber/ sku pang / rdor dril sogs nyer spyad khri rgyab/ bla bre dang bcas pa/ 'phags sder yang gong mtshungs dang / rmor dgon du rje de nyid kyi sku/ mgon
po'i bla brgyud rnams dang zhe mtshungs khri rgyab yol na bza' dang bcas pa/ bsam gtan chos gling dang rab brtan dgon gsar gnyis su rmor chen rdo rje 'chang dang skyabs
mgon de nyid bcas kyi sku brnyan khru gang tsam na bza' dang bcas pa/

bya sa lha khang gi gtsang khang byang mar sku brnyan rnams la zhig gsos/ tshon rtsi/ zhal gser/ spyan 'byed rnams bgyis shing / gtso bo gsum la snam sbyar/ byang sems bzhi
la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ khro bo gnyis la stod g.yogs/ smad g.yogs/ stag sham/ so sor mdzod btags dang / bsod btags rnying ma'i snyan shal/ ka ba gnyis la bzang gos
kyi 'phan bcas bsgrubs pa'i na bza'i rgyur bzang gos sna tshogs kha brgya dang nyi shu rtsa brgyad bcas song ba/ de lta'i dngos po rnams ni skyabs mgon dam pa de nyid mthong
thos dran reg tsam gyis 'gro kun dad pa'i spu long rang dbang med par g.yos te rang rang gi bdog pa rnams mchod sprin rgya mtshor btab pa de dag log 'tshor mi 'gyur ba'i
bka' khyab mdzad pa bzhin/ yang srid du mar rgya chen smon lam gyi 'brel bas zhabs 'degs kyi rim pa la rtse gcig tu gzhol ba phyag mdzod 'jam dpal rgya mtsho nas phyag
rdzas rnams bar ma dor mi 'gyur ba'i do khur ched gnyer bgyis pa rnams dang / nye dus zhal 'debs kyi rim par yang 'di nas dngul gdung rin po cher dmigs rgya dngul srang
brgya tham pa/ phra rgyan du mo chas sna tshogs/ sgrub mchod thebs su dngul srang lnga bcu/ gos yug bzhi/ rgyal tshab rin po che nas rgya dngul rta rmig ma gnyis/ phra rgyan
du spos shel ngang sgong tsam gcig /dgongs rdzogs thebs su dngul srang lnga bcu/ bzang ja 'khor drug gnyis/ mar khal sum cu tham pa/ chab mdo nas zhi ba lha sprul pa'i
skus gser srang gang / mdzod gos ser po yug /rgya dngul rta mig ma gcig /sde dge sa dbang mchog nas rgya

dngul rta rmig ma gcig /karma shag nas rgya dngul rta rmig ma gcig dang TaM srang lnga bcu/ sde pa zhal ngo lhan rgyas kyis na bza' phon che ba/ phra rgyan du a sgor g.yu hril
che ba cha/ bkra shis mthong smon nas lcam kun skyid mas thod rgyan spus legs 'tsho bcas cha tshang / spor ba yab sras nas/ gser thur zho bdun/ dngul srang drug /phra
rgyan du pad 'dab che ba legs pa gcig /rin spungs pa'i pad 'dab tu grags pa g.yu gru dkar dmar las grub pa'i pad 'dab chung ngu spus legs gcig bcas dang / gzhan yang bkra
shis chos sde/ 'phags sde/ rmor/ she'u grong / gdung phud chos 'khor/ bsam yas rab byung grwa tshang pa sogs/ chos sde khag spyi sger dang / gtsang dbus khams gsum gyi
bla dpon/ grwa rigs/ sbyin bdag /zhal slob/ dad ldan du mas dgongs rdzogs mchod 'bul dang dngul gdung sogs kyi thebs rgya cher phul ba rnams dang bcas rnam dkar gyi bgyi
ba rlabs po che de dag grub par gyur to/ /dge rgyun sbyor 'jags skor la lo bstar sku mchod chen mo'i skabs bkra shis chos sder kye rdor sgrub mchod zhag bdun/ 'di nas grong
mo cher kye rdor sgrub mchod dngos sta bcas nyin bzhi gtong rgyur dngul srang drug cu re gsum sbyar bar/ phyag mdzod 'jam dpal gyis bla brang gsol phog thog nas nas 'dar
khal sum brgya drug cu/ blo gsal rab rgyas nas dus chen nyin mang ja re gtong thebs nas 'dar khal bcu/ rdzong ri dpon slob nas gser sbyangs zho bzhi byung ba grong chen
pas 'brur bsgyur te khal drug cu bcas/ dngul 'bru de thog nas gong

gi sgrub mchod de zhag bdun/ 'phags sder mkha' spyod ma'i cho ga nyin 'khyongs/ gzhan yang rmor dgon bsam gtan chos gling / rab brtan dgon gsar/ shing mang dgon/ grwa phu dgon
gsar bcas la bla mchod nyin 'khyongs re/ de thams cad la zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes bcu drug la bla mchod tshar re/ bsam yas rab byung grwa tshang du lo bstar sku
mchod nyin bla ma gsang ba 'dus pa'i tshes bcu tshar re gtong rgyu bcas ji srid bar chad med 'ong ba'i thebs su zhing 'bru dngul rnams yul babs dang bstun par sbyar zhing
/ rab byung grwa tshang du gu ru mtshan brgyad kyi sku thang grwa mtshungs dgu tshar gcig gsar bzhengs kyi sbyor 'jags byas 'dug go /nged rang nas gong du bshad pa ltar
dgung zhag zhe dgu'i bar la mkha' spyod ma'i sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod bgyis skabs bdag bum gyi sngags bsdoms oM gsum ma drug brgya re dang / rje de nyid kyi sku
bstod shwa lo ka gcig phreng 'khor/ sku bstod rgyas pa dang mchog sprul myur pheb kyi gsol 'debs nged rang nas bgyis pa de tshar re bcas bsgrubs shing / lcags 'brug 'jigs
byed sgrub mchod brgya tshar grangs gsog 'phros lcags sbrul dpyid dbyar gyi khongs su grub par bgyid skabs kyang gsol 'debs kyi rim pa gong ji lta ba bzhin dang / sgrub
mchod la skyabs 'gro/ yig brgya/ uShNI Sha rnams nyis stong chig brgya/ bdag bum bsdoms rtsa sngags chig 'bum chig khri chig stong bdun brgya/ snying po nye snying gnyis
khri re/ 'khor rnams kyi sngags chig khri/ 'jigs byed tshogs brgya bcas bgyis shing / skyabs mgon de nyid gshegs pa nas

bzung srod/ tho rengs/ nyin bar sogs btang snyoms su sdod skabs sems la skyo shas dang / khyad par da ni rje btsun gong ma'i thugs dam chag med kyi rim pa kha gso ba rnams
kyang zhu yul shin tu dkon snyam pa'i 'dun pa dung dung lhang lhang bcas re zhig gi bar la kha 'don dge sbyor rtag 'grus su gyur kyang chos dred can kho la ni gting nas nges
'byung ma skyes pa'i rtags kyis rim pas je lod du gyur kyang / cung zad bgyis pa rnams rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa bka' drin can rnams kyi dgongs rdzogs su dmigs khul dang
/ khyad par rje de nyid kyi dus chen dang bstun 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod zhag bzhi'i khongs ya ma rA dza bzhi stong brgal ba dang
/ rje de nyid kyi gsol 'debs bzhi brgya lhag tsam bgyis shing / dkyil 'khor mchod pa'i yo byad rgyas pa dang / dus chen nyin dpal sa skya'i lha khang chen mo'i mthil g.yab
gtsug lag khang na nged rang nas gsar bzhengs rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi 'dra sku sku tshad lhag tsam/ dbu zhwa/ na bza'/ phyag phreng / phyag cha/ mchod pa'i yo byad
bcas rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid kyi nyer spyod ngo ma kha shas kyis spras te bzhugs pa'i drung du mchod me zhal zas 'bul ba dang / gzhan yang gong gi gsung gi bdud rtsi cung
zad myong skal du gyur pa rnams bstan 'gro'i ched so so'i skal ba dang / mthun par spel ci thub dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba 'khon rigs spel dgos pa'i
bka' stsal sogs ngal ba mtha' dag dang du blangs te dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i dgongs rdzogs su stob khul yin kyang bka' drin gyi cha tsam yang gzhal bar

dka' bas/ skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du bla ma dam pa'i zhabs drung du skyes te/ rnam kun don yod kyi bgyi bas thugs kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs pa zhig byin gyis brlab
tu gsol/ de dag gi don bsdu na/ tshogs gnyis zung 'jug snang ba 'gog med du/ /shar bas sku gsung thugs rten dge rgyun bcas/ /mi nyams dbyar mtsho lta bur rgyas par mdzad/
/gnas gsar 'jam mgon kun bzang thugs bskyed yin/ /zhes so/ /de ltar bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid ni/ re zhig gangs ljongs lnga bdo'i 'gro ba rnams bsod nams
zad pa dang / gdul bya'i dbang gis zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshul bstan mod kyang / mchog gi sprul pa'i sku myur du 'byon par zhal gyis bzhes shing / der ma zad
rang gi dad pas ma bslus na dngos nyams rmi lam sogs su'ang da lta'i sku phreng 'di nyid kyi rnam pa ji lta ba bzhin du pheb nas rjes su 'dzin pa zhig ste/ bka' 'bangs kyi
tha shal za nyal 'chag pa kho bo la'ang / sngon du rang lo nyer gnyis skabs rmi ltas ngo mtshar can de bzhin gyur pa dang / zhing khams brjes nas lcags 'brug khrums zla'i
tshes gsum tho rengs khar rmi ltas su gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang dpon g.yog tshang ma sa skya'i bla brang phun tshogs gling gi dbang khang na bzhugs 'dug par nged rang
nas mjal te/ lha khang rtse'i ga ya dha ra'i bum chu'i snod la skyon byung tshul de zhus song bar skyon med 'gro gsungs shing / rje nyid la dgongs rdzogs 'bul rten yin snyam
pa'i khyad gos kho na phon che ba 'bul nyams dang / zhabs gras sbyin pa rgya mtsho yin snyam pa zhig gis yig brgya mtshal tham

ma zhig gtad nas/ rje bla ma bsnyun skabs pad dkar sprul sku'i lung bstan de 'di yin zer bar/ kha phye nas bltas pas tshigs bcad kha shas 'dug kyang gam la ma zin/ rnam 'dren
dam pa'i yang srid rin po che e waM chos ldan gyi zhabs phyi zhig la nges par pheb rgyu yin zer ba dang / gong sa rdo rje 'chang skal bzang rgya mtsho'i mchog sprul rin
po che'i skor yang rags tsam yod pa zhig byung ba dang / yang skabs shig rmis ltas su phun tshogs gling gi dbang khang na gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang bzhugs te maNDal tshom
bu du ma bkod pa zhig gi mthar mchod gtor bshams nas nged rang la phur pa'i dbang sngar ma thob pa zhig stsal nyams dang / gzhan yang rmis ltas su rnam 'dren dam pa de
nyid yang yang pheb ste rje btsun sa skya ba'i zab chos kha shas la bskyar chos stsol ba dang / sku'i rnam 'gyur zhi khro du ma'i sgo nas lugs gnyis kyi blang dor stsol ba
sogs shar yang / nog lkog shal bdag 'dra la ni brjed ngas gti thom kho na las med pas thams cad gam la ma zin no/ /gzhan yang zhal slob thugs gtsigs che grwas sogs skal
ldan 'ga' re la'ang rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan ma ngo mtshar can byung yod 'gro'ang / da lta go thos cher ma byung zhing / de gras 'dar grong mkhan chen ngag dbang shes rab
kyi mnal ltas la/ mkhan chen nyid rje'i drung nas gtsang la 'byon nye ba'i skabs rje de nyid zhal shar gzigs bzhugs 'bol ha cang mi mtho ba zhig gi khar bzhugs pa gur
gyi mgon po'i skur gyur nas nub phyogs su gzigs pa dang / khong rang nas grong chen du mkha' spyod ma'i khrid 'chad skabs ngom shod phug mo

che'i mdun gyi spang ri de na yar rje bla ma na bza' gzabs 'phyor gyis pheb pa'i phyag na dar phon dang / rdor dril spus legs shig bsnams te pheb pa'i rjes su mkhan chen rang
yang 'byon kyin 'dug pa la phyir bltas su gzigs te/ rdor dril de gnang ba na dges tshor chen po byung ba dang / grong chen gdan sa 'dzin dgos kyi sne sbyor 'ong rgyu'i
snga dro'i mnal ltas su rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid mdun gyi nam mkhar bzhugs te gdung ba'i dbyangs lhang lhang gsung ba snyam byed pa sogs mnal ltas ngo mtshar can kha re
byung 'dug pa dang / yang rdzong ri rab 'byams pa phrin las la zhal bzhugs skabs rmi ltas su/ rje 'di grong chen bla brang phu'i gzims chung na bzhugs nas bka' chos shig
gnang rgyu yin snyam pa la/ gzims chung mdo na chos zhu ba tshogs pa'i khrod du byon te/ spyi bo nas rkang mthil gyi bar la bsrung ba 'dra ba zhig dang mnyam du sdom 'dra
ba'i sems can gsum gnang ba khyur mid byas pa zhig dang / nged rang nas rnam thar zin bris shog dril ston rgyur bskur ba'i zhag gsum tsam nas rdzong ri bla brang gi nub
sgo'i thad kyi bar snang la rje de nyid khri steng du zhal shar gzigs dang / de 'og dge 'dun kha shas bcas 'dug par bzang spyod yan lag bdun pa'i shwa lo ka re re la bskul
mtshams re yod pa bskul bar gnang ba zhig shar 'dug pa bcas/ tshul de lta bu'i sgo nas kyang gdul bya rnams rjes su 'dzin par mdzad de/ de ltar bdag cag gi drin can rtsa
ba'i bla ma dam pa dpal gnas gsar ba chen po 'jam mgon bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas theg mchog bstan

pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bka' drin mtshungs pa ma mchis pa'i zhal snga nas kyi rnam par thar pa tshur mthong byis pa'i snang ngor shar ba re zhig de tsam mo/ /'dir smras
pa/ ngag gi dbang phyug 'gro kun dga' mdzad phyir/ /legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal dang rgyal ba'i sras/ /theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan mkhas dang grub/ /dpal 'byor
bzang po sgyur rgyal la sogs pa/ /sna tshogs sprul pas zhing khams mu med par/ /de snyed gsung gis gang 'dul chos 'khor bskor/ /spros kun nyer zhi thabs mkhas brtse chen
thugs/ /gting dpag dka' ba'i yon tan phrin las sogs/ /gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma'i ngo mtshar gyi/ /rtogs pa brjod pa cha shas re re yang / /bdag 'dra so skyes brjod pa
gad mo'i gnas/ /de dang de 'dra'i skyes chen rnams kyis dgongs/ /'on kyang gser gyi ri la gnas bcas pa'i/ /srog chags rin chen mdog tu snang ba ltar/ /chung ngu'i dus nas
dam pa'i mgon des bskyangs/ /smin grol chos kyi dga' ston ci yang stsal/ /de la brten nas rang gi mthong ba dang / /dad ldan slob bu 'ga' yis gleng ba rnams/ /cung zad
smra ba'i spobs pa thob 'di yang / /rje btsun bla ma'i drin las gzhan du ci/ /'on kyang thog med 'khor bar las nyon gyi/ /bag chags kyis bsgribs don tshig 'gal 'khrul cha/
