/mkha' mnyam 'gro ba'i sdig dang lhan cig tu/ /'dren mchog bla ma'i spyan sngar mthol lo bshags/ /rgyal kun yon tan brjod pa'i bsod nams las/ /bla ma'i rnam thar lan gcig

brjod khyad 'phags/ /mdo rgyud bstan bcos kun las bsngags pa bzhin/ /'dir 'bad dge tshogs byang chub chen por bsngo/ /de ltar gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma yi/ /rtogs brjod ngo
mtshar rab 'byams 'di brtsams tshe/ /bstan pa'i bdag po ston mchog 'khrungs pa sogs/ /bstan rtsis nyung ngu'i rnam gzhag ci zhe na/ /'di la mkhas pa'i bzhed pa mang na
yang / /rang lugs rgya gar rgyal po yongs grags 'gas/ /mnga' 'bangs bu lon mdzod nor gyis sbyangs te/ /zong gsar spyod pa nas bzung lo brtsi ba/ /'di yi khungs ni lugs chen
zhes bya las/ /g.yul bstan 'og tu nyis stong dga' byed 'og /brgyad brgya zhes sogs bshad cing de yi don/ /rtsod dus rgyal po skya seng mched lnga'i gcen/ /g.yul bstan
gyis bcos nyis stong nye ba'i tshe/ /bcom ldan shAkya'i rgyal po sa 'brug bltams/ /brgyad cu bzhes pa me phag lo la gshegs/ /de nas brgya dang so bdun lon pa na/ /dga' byed
byung zhes rtog ge 'bar bar bshad/ /des na slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo dang / /'jam mgon bla ma sa skya paNDi tas/ /'di la brten nas bstan rtsis rtsom par bzhed/ /thub
dbang mya ngan 'das nas sum stong dang / /chig brgya re drug shing pho khyi yi lo/ /'khon ston chen po dkon mchog rgyal po 'khrungs/ /bzhi bcu chu glang dpal ldan sa skya
btab/ /re dgu chu rta lo la zhi bar gshegs/ /'khon ston nga dgu chu sprel sa chen 'khrungs/ /re bdun sa stag gshegs te nga dgu'i lo/ /lcags pho rta la dpal chen 'od po
'khrungs/ /nga bzhi chu phag gshegs de so lnga pa/ /shing 'brug zang tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan

'khrungs/ /nga drug sa phag gshegs te nga lnga pa/ /sa pho khyi la ye shes 'byung gnas 'khrungs/ /so bdun shing khyir gshegs te nyer lnga pa/ /chu khyir bla chen bzang po dpal
pa 'khrungs/ /mgon de drug cu rtsa gsum shing byir gshegs/ /de las gdung rabs mang du 'phel ba las/ /bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs ni/ /bdag nyid chen po zhe
dgu lcags khyi lo/ /don rgyal 'khrungs nas so bzhi chu lug gshegs/ /phyi lo shing sprel de sras kun rgyal 'khrungs/ /don lnga sa khyir gshegs te nga lnga pa/ /sa stag
nam rgyal 'khrungs shing don lnga pa/ /chu 'brug gshegs te zhe bdun shing byi lor/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang blo gros rgyal mtshan 'khrungs/ /nga gnyis shing yos gshegs rnams
rin sgang gdung / /de las lngas gzhon sa sbrul rdo ring pa/ /chos kyi nyi ma don drug shing sprel gshegs/ /de las nyer brgyad kyis gzhon sgo rum pa/ /me byar 'khrungs shing
re brgyad shing 'brug gshegs/ /de las brgyad kyis gzhon pa shing sbrul lor/ /sa lo 'khrungs shing zhe dgu chu sbrul gshegs/ /de las bcu bdun gyis gzhon tshar chen rje/
/chu khyir 'khrungs shing re lnga me stag gshegs/ /de las bco lngas gzhon pa me glang lor/ /bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang chen po 'khrungs/ /re brgyad shing sprel lor
gshegs mgon de las/ /drug gis gzhon pa klu sgrub chu lug lo/ /don gcig chu sbrul lor gshegs rje de las/ /gcig gis gzhon pa mkhyen brtse shing sprel lo/ /zhe lnga sa 'brug
la gshegs de nyid las/ /gnyis kyis gzhon pa me khyi bslab

gsum pa/ /nga gnyis me glang lor gshegs de nyid las/ /gcig gis gzhon pa me mo phag gi lor/ /bod mkhar yol ba rta ra chos rje gsum/ /'khrungs shing bod mkhar re gcig me phag
gshegs/ /yol pa don gsum sa phag lo la gshegs/ /rta ra chos rje don bdun chu yos lor/ /gshegs shing de las so gnyis kyis gzhon pa/ /sa lug 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po
dang / /dbang phyug rab brtan 'khrungs shing bsod nams dbang / /re gsum lcags byar gshegs shing dbang rab rje/ /don brgyad me pho byi ba'i lo la gshegs/ /de las lo bzhis
gzhon pa sngags 'chang rje/ /grags blo chu phag 'khrungs shing nga lnga pa/ /me sbrul lor gshegs de las dgus gzhon pa/ /ngag dbang chos grags chu sprel bdun cu pa/ /lcags
sbrul lor gshegs de las nyer lnga yis/ /gzhon pa me bya 'jam mgon a mes zhabs/ /re gsum sa phag lor gshegs de nyid las/ /lo lngas gzhon pa chu stag zhwa lu ba/ /rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub brgyad cu'i lo/ /lcags byar gshegs shing de las lo gcig gis/ /gzhon pa chu yos khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba/ /nga bdun sa phag lor gshegs rje de las/
/bcu bzhis gzhon pa gong sa rdo rje 'chang / /lnga pa me sbrul lor 'khrungs re drug pa/ /chu khyir gshegs shing de las nyer gcig gis/ /gzhon pa 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang
phyug ni/ /sa stag 'khrungs shing zhe brgyad shing glang gshegs/ /de las brgyad kyis gzhon pa sgro lung pa/ /bsod nams chos 'phel me khyi gya gsum lo/ /sa sprel

gshegs shing de las lo brgyad kyis/ /gzhon pa rdo rje 'chang dbang rmor chen rje/ /shing rtar 'khrungs shing don lnga sa sprel gshegs/ /de las gnyis kyis gzhon pa sa skya pa/
/kun dga' bkra shis me pho sprel lor 'khrungs/ /nga drug lcags mo yos kyi lo la gshegs/ /de las so lngas gzhon pa brag rtsa rje/ /lcags lug 'khrungs shing nga lnga shing
glang gshegs/ /de las bcu gsum gyis gzhon gnas gsar rje/ /shing sprel 'khrungs shing nga bdun lcags 'brug gshegs/ /de las gcig gis gzhon pa'i drin chen rje/ /rdo rje 'chang
dbang bsod nams rin chen zhabs/ /shing byar 'khrungs shing so bdun lcags byar gshegs/ /de nas lo grangs nyer gsum 'das pa yi/ /nyer bzhi shing byar kho bos 'di brtsams
so/ /des na thub dbang mya ngan 'das nas lo/ /sum stong brgyad brgya dgu bcu go brgyad 'das/ /dpal ldan sa skya btab nas drug brgya dang / /dgu bcu go gnyis 'das lo 'khrul
med yin/ /bla ma'i gdan sa gsang chen smra ba'i gnas/ /bkra shis chos sde lcags yos btab nas lo/ /brgya dang don bzhi 'das shing don lnga pa/ /sa skyong zhes pa shing
bya lo 'di'o/ /thub bstan lnga brgya phrag bcur gnas pa las/ /'bras sgrub dus kyi lnga brgya phrag drug dang / /lung dus lnga brgya phrag bdun mngon par 'das/ /lnga brgya
phrag brgyad mdo sde spyod steng nas/ /lo grangs sum brgya go brgyad 'das zin pas/ /kye ma da ni rnam dag bstan pa'i rgyun/ /mdo 'phros brgya gcig lnga brgya phrag dgu
pa/ /'dul ba'i dus

kyi lnga brgya phrag gcig ste/ /sdom pas lo grangs drug brgya gnyis gnas shing / /lnga brgya phrag bcu rtags tsam 'dzin pa bcas/ /chig stong chig brgya gnyis yod brtson 'grus
skyed/ /skye ba kun tu khyed zhal mthong ba dang / /gsung gi bdud rtsi 'thung zhing bgyi ba kun/ /bla ma dam pa mnyes pa'i rgyur gyur nas/ /rang gzhan don gnyis ma lus
mthar phyin shog /gnas skabs rgyal bstan spyi dang sa skya pa'i/ /bstan dang bstan 'dzin sbyin bdag dar ba dang / /de la brten nas gdul bya spyi bye brag /'phral yun phan
bde'i dpal la spyod par shog /rje btsun bla ma'i brtse chen byin rlabs dang / /bdag sogs gdul bya'i dad pas gsol btab mthus/ /gnas skabs mthar thug rten 'brel zab mo kun/
/mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i bkra shis shog /ces rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen gzhan ngor ngur smrig gi bla gos 'chang ba bka'
drin mnyam med gnas gsar 'jam mgon bla ma legs pa'i mtshan can gyi zhal snga nas kyi ngo mtshar rtogs brjod rags rim du bris pa 'di ni/ rnam 'dren dam pa'i zhabs 'bring lhag
bsam can blo gsal rab rgyas nas rje de nyid kyi bka' dngos su pheb pa dang / phyag mdzod 'jam dpal sogs zhal slob du ma'i ngag las thos pa rnams lo tshigs dang bcas pa
gzhir gzung zhing / gdung rus skor la yig tshang rnying ma'i khungs dang rang phyogs kyi ngag rgyun bcas bkod cing / mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan man gsung rgyun dang /
gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen po'i rnam thar go bstun sku bltams pa dang /

/dbus su gdan drangs tshul sogs yum mchog phun tshogs sgrol mas gsungs pa bzhin btsan par byas/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar la'ang zhib tu dpyad/ bka' chos gsan tshul
rnams gsan yig nas kha bskangs/ ljags bsnyen/ chos 'chad/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu bskrun pa sogs gang zin bkod cing / mya ngan 'das byung dang / dgongs rdzogs kyi skor
rnams ni rgyus yod pa bcas rnam thar thog mtha' bar gsum la zin bris zhib mo zhig phyag mdzod 'jam dpal gyis bskul ba bzhin btab 'dug pa gtso bor bzung / nged rang la
rgyus yod pa rnams dang / der ma 'thus pa rnams gzhi dgon mkhan chen bsod nams dpal bzang dang / zangs stan bla ma rdzong ri rab 'byams pa byams pa phrin las/ 'dar grong
mkhan chen ngag dbang shes rab/ ka ye rje drung skyid pa'am/ ming dngos 'jam dpal rab rgyas rnams las zin bris khul bsdus shing / bla ma gong ma rnams kyi rnam thar nas
legs cha blangs te bsgrigs khul bgyis pa 'di'ang / sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po rang nyid rnam 'dren dam pa de
nyid la mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pas 'di lta bu'i rnam par thar pa gzhan gyis sbyar ba'am/ rang nyid kyis las su bya ba gang rung zhig 'grub na ci ma rung snyam pa'i blo
yod khar rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid kyi sri zhu ba'i gtso bo 'jam dpal rgya mtsho nas gong

du bshad pa'i rnam thar zin bris 'phags sde ba'i shog dril rnams bskur ba dang lhan cig rnam thar rtsom dgos kyi bskul ma rten bcas byung don bzhin 'gyangs min legs par sbyar
ba 'di nyid kyi tshe dbu'i mchod brjod rnams brtsams pa'i nub mo rmi ltas su/ dpal sa skya'i dpon po ri'i ldebs la 'brong rgod shin tu gzi brjid can zhig 'ongs nas nged
rang la dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur gyis bltas pa'i tshe/ bsam par sngon dpal ldan a ti sha'i gzigs snang la shar ba de'ang 'di 'dra zhig yin 'dra snyam pa dang / yang nub gcig

ma dang / rtsom grub rgyu'i snga dro rmi ltas su srog chags kyi ra dung yid du 'ong ba zhig nged rang nas bus par chos dung dkar mo rgyang grags kyi gsung dang dbyer
